# **145: Port Town and Departure**

**Volume 10: The Regalia Beastman Kingdom Arc Begins**

---

The Regalia Beastman Kingdom.

As the name suggests, it is a country where more than ninety percent of the population are beastmen, and it is famous for having poor relations with human-centric nations. More precisely, it has poor relations with countries that adhere to human supremacist ideology. That much is only natural.

As an aside, when people say “human supremacism”, for some reason elves are treated as humans and included on the “supreme” side.

Geographically speaking, it lies to the north of the Elgant Theocracy, and one must pass through about two small countries to reach it.

Because it is a nation primarily of beastmen with physical abilities surpassing humans (in many cases), it is also well known as a muscle-brained country that puts heavy emphasis on martial power.

That said, it is not a military state, so do not misunderstand that point.

Of course, the individual soldiers are strong, but when you look at it as an organized military, it is a bit lacking. In short, it relies on brute-force pushes.

This time, an invitation arrived from that very Regalia Beastman Kingdom.

After receiving word from Sakuya, I used Portal to transfer to my private room and heard the details.

“So, can I hear the details?”

“Yeah. An invitation arrived for you, big brother… for Queen’s Knight Gene, from the Regalia Beastman Kingdom. Here, this is the letter.”

Saying that, Sakuya handed me the letter.

Let’s see…

According to the letter, it was not an official invitation from the Regalia Beastman Kingdom, but rather a personal invitation from the queen, Sharon.

Apparently, she had seen Gene during the summit and sensed his strength, and had wanted to speak with him someday. However, during the summit he had been guarding Queen Sakuya, so there was no opportunity.

So, after the summit ended, she decided to formally invite him.

“Isn’t it a bit fast for the letter to arrive, considering it was written after returning home?”

“Oh, that’s because the one who carried the letter was a bird.”

“Come to think of it, there’s a Hero with a Blessing that lets them control animals, right…”

The notice of the summit from the Elgant Theocracy had also been carried by a bird controlled by a Hero.

“It seems to be someone different from that Hero, but with a similar ability. The letter says that if we attach our reply to the bird, it will return on its own, so they want us to give it a little food.”

“That’s a convenient ability. Being able to fly would save a lot of time.”

“When Master says it, it sounds sarcastic, doesn’t it?”

“That’s true…”

As means of conveying information or goods, there are Telepathy, Portal, and Infinite Storage, among other things.

And if we are talking about flying through the sky, a Sky Dragon would be faster than an ordinary bird anyway.

“In truth, it would probably be faster for us to fly there ourselves, but this time I want to try traveling by ship. It’s my first time since coming to this world…”

Let me talk a bit about geography here.

North of the former Eldia Kingdom lies the Kingdom of Sanokia, beyond that the Elgant Theocracy, and further still the Regalia Beastman Kingdom. To the west spreads the Demon territory.

The Eldia Kingdom was originally a landlocked nation, but before it was destroyed by the Castal Kingdom, it was no longer landlocked.

That was because a small country it destroyed and absorbed just before the Hero Summoning faced the sea.

In other words, the current Castal Kingdom, which destroyed Eldia and made it a vassal territory, is also not landlocked (though it originally was).

In addition, the Regalia Beastman Kingdom also faces the sea on its northern side.

What I am getting at is that Castal Kingdom and the Regalia Beastman Kingdom can be traveled between by sea without passing through other countries.

Since the nations are connected by the sea, a graceful sea voyage would be an interesting experience.

“So, does that mean you’re going?”

I nod at Sakuya’s question.

“Yeah. I didn’t dislike that Queen Sharon either. If she’s going to invite us, it’s worth going to see.”

I have never spoken directly with Queen Sharon, but from watching her mock battle with the Hero, I felt she had a personality I did not dislike.

“In the end, it looks like it’s going to turn out just like Mio-chan said…”

“Right. A connection with Queen Sharon, which shouldn’t have existed, is just popping up like it’s normal… It really feels like it’s only a matter of time before Queen Sharon joins as a subordinate.”

Mio responds to Sakuya’s muttering.

That was something discussed back in the Elgant Theocracy.

At the time, Mio had half-jokingly said that Sharon would eventually join as a subordinate.

I thought the possibility was low since I had no connection with Sharon, but… here we are.

“…”

Because of that, I have nothing to say in return.

Still, somehow, Sharon does not feel like the type to be a slave or subordinate. Why is that?

“Jin-kun… I have a constitution that gets really bad seasickness…”

While I was silent, Sakura said apologetically.

I know, but Sakura really has a hard-to-live-with constitution back in her original world…

“Wouldn’t \<Environmental Adaptation> handle it? If it’s still too much, you can join us later.”

“Oh, right… Conditions are different from my original world…”

“And there are your base stats too. There’s a good chance you won’t even get seasick.”

I am not particularly knowledgeable about the causes of seasickness, but it should not be something stats or skills cannot handle. She seems fine with carriage rides, after all…

More than that, Sakura’s ‘Refresh’ magic should be able to cure it. In a sense, it is her specialty. She should have more confidence.

“Understood… I’ll think about it if I actually get seasick…”

“Yeah, that sounds good.”

Leaving Sakura behind is not even an option.

The letter also says that as long as we notify them in advance, we can bring as many companions as we like.

“Sakuya won’t be coming along, right?”

“Yeah, no way. I really want to go, but I am still a queen, after all. I can’t leave the country that often.”

In that case, the main party members and…

“So we should bring Blue and the rest of the dragonewt group, right?”

“What do you mean by that?”

I answer Sera’s question while showing her the letter.

“It’s written here. They would like Dragon Knight Gene to come to the Regalia Beastman Kingdom together with his dragons.”

“Could it be a trap?”

Maria mutters cautiously.

“I won’t say the possibility is zero, but somehow it feels like it will be fine. According to the letter, there is no need to reveal my identity either. It says it is fine to keep wearing the helmet the entire time.”

The letter is written with a great deal of consideration toward us.

If we travel by ship, they will prepare the port reception, and there is also a permit handwritten by Queen Sharon allowing free movement within the Regalia Beastman Kingdom. Of course, there are no restrictions on flying with riding dragons, and city tolls are waived.

Even after arriving at the royal castle, there is no need to show my face, and they will receive us with VIP treatment.

If anything, being treated this well almost makes it look like a trap.

“They really go all out. Just how badly do they want to invite Master?”

“You can feel their sincerity.”

“Well, if it turns out to be a trap, we can just fight our way out. It’s not something to worry too much about. Of course, we’ll stay alert.”

“Yes. We will not let them lay even a finger on Jin-sama.”

Maria’s eyes are as serious as ever.

“So, we’ll go by sea route to the Regalia Beastman Kingdom, then by air route with the dragonewts after that. Can you send that reply?”

“Roger. I’ll write the letter with that content. Ahh, I really wanted to try a sea voyage too…”

Sakuya mutters with genuine regret.

She just returned from a long trip to the Elgant Theocracy. If the queen were to leave repeatedly in a short period, domestic affairs would be in trouble. Especially since Sakuya is the only royal in this country.

Two days after the invitation from the Regalia Beastman Kingdom arrived, we headed to the Meltis Territory.

In this world, travel by sea is actually faster than by land.

The reason is simple. Ships are easy to enhance with magical tools, whereas it is difficult to do the same with carriages.

In the past, a Hero tried to make a vehicle that used magical tools as an engine, but in a world with very few paved roads, there was no way to operate it properly. With monsters and bandits as well, the risks were extremely high.

By contrast, sea routes offer far more advantages.

First, there are fewer monsters at sea than on land, and there are not many particularly strong ones… at least within the range where people send out ships.

Because of that, shipbuilding technology has steadily advanced, and enhancing ships with magical tools is nothing new.

The risk of encountering pirates is not zero, but most ships have escort measures, so attacking them is not without cost. In the first place, if you have shipbuilding technology good enough to be a pirate, you would make more money by running a shipping business.

In short, a country that excels in shipbuilding technology holds a certain level of value by that fact alone.

The Meltis Territory, or rather the Meltis Kingdom, where we are now, was once famous throughout the world for its shipbuilding technology.

For the record, the Meltis Kingdom was a small nation destroyed by the Eldia Kingdom just before the Hero Summoning.

It was only discovered after Eldia was destroyed that Eldia’s purpose in destroying and occupying the Meltis Kingdom had been to seize its shipbuilding technology.

They knew that when transporting Heroes by ship, the Meltis Kingdom would become a key transportation hub, so they planned to make it their own territory in advance.

Realizing this, the Meltis Kingdom focused on letting a small number of royals and engineers escape.

Even though most of the royal family were killed, and many citizens were either killed or enslaved, they made sure that the shipbuilding technology would never fall into Eldia’s hands.

That port town of the Meltis Kingdom was almost completely restored by the time we arrived.

And then…

“Gene-sama! Please take this too!”

“All the fish from our shop! Every last one!”

“Close up for today! Bring everything to Gene-sama!”

An absurd number of people gathered.

Simply put, so many people had gathered that my companions and I could not move even a single step.

And the people who gathered offered every tribute they could.

Amid the clamor, shop owners seemed ready to bring over all their merchandise.

“Um, this is kind of a problem… Oh, nice fish.”

“Fish! He wants fish! Bring more!”

“Ah, crap…”

Mio tried to refuse, but muttered from a cook’s perspective, and in an instant the offerings of fish increased.

Why did we end up in this situation?

There are two reasons.

One is that the Meltis Kingdom harbored a deep grudge against the Eldia Kingdom, and so they feel gratitude, strong admiration, and respect toward Queen’s Knight Gene, who almost single-handedly destroyed Eldia.

The other is that the one who restored the Meltis Kingdom was none other than the Advance Trading Company.

When Eldia was destroyed, the Advance Trading Company prioritized the restoration of the Meltis Kingdom, or rather the Meltis Territory, over the restoration of Eldia itself.

Not only did they restore the town, they also bought back every single person who had been sold as slaves. That includes those sold to other countries, all living slaves.

While they have not been formally freed, they are allowed to live with their families in their original homes, and depending on their work, emancipation is possible.

Those in the know are aware that the Advance Trading Company and Gene are on friendly terms.

The gratitude toward Gene and the gratitude toward the Advance Trading Company combine, and Gene’s popularity has reached an almost absurd level. Specifically, people from all over the Meltis Territory have gathered just to catch a glimpse of us.

Incidentally, the engineers have already returned home as well, and are providing shipbuilding technology to the Castal Kingdom. They did not want to give it to Eldia, but giving it to Castal is apparently fine.

Honestly, I did not expect this level of popularity.

We made it into the port town, but could barely make any progress.

In the end, I had to call the maids and ask them to organize the people and the goods. Of course, there is also a branch of the Advance Trading Company in this town.

And the townspeople are incredibly obedient to the maids’ instructions.

What should have taken ten minutes took nearly an hour before we finally caught sight of the port.

“We finally made it here…”

《I hate crowds!》

Sakura and Dora, who are not used to being the center of attention, are completely exhausted.

As for me, I have had enough experience with it that it does not bother me much. That was true in my original world too, and in this world I am often exposed to believers’ gazes at parties.

“Sakura-sama, Dora-chan, here are some drinks.”

“Thank you, Mio-chan…”

《Thank you.》

“Jin-sama, here you are as well.”

Mio hands drinks to Sakura and the others, and Maria hands one to me.

Since I am wearing Gene equipment, that is, armor, I drink through a straw slipped through a gap in the armor. It was a tropical juice made from a blend of several fruit juices.

A knight in armor drinking tropical juice. That is Queen’s Knight Gene. It makes no sense.

“The ship we’re supposed to board… is that the one we’re seeing right now?”

In front of us is a ridiculously huge ship docked at the port.

At a rough estimate, it easily exceeds two hundred meters in length.

“Yes, that is the ship reserved exclusively for Jin-sama.”

“My… exclusive…?”

Maria just said something I cannot ignore.

Wait, that thing… that’s a passenger ship, right? Not a personal vessel?

I assumed we were borrowing a ship from the Meltis Territory, but…

“Yes. When the Meltis Territory was liberated, on Lucea-san’s orders, the construction maids began building a ship exclusively for Jin-sama. So that they could respond immediately whenever Jin-sama wished to travel by ship.”

What are construction maids?!

“I cannot decide whether to praise Lucea’s foresight, or be amazed that they built a ship of that caliber with no certainty…”

Since I did end up wanting to travel by ship, it was not wasted.

But there was a non-zero chance it would have been wasted. Normally you would hesitate, right? At the very least, you would ask me first… Maids are scary.

“I think it is fine to be amazed.”

“Mio-chan underestimated the maid corps too. At this point, nothing will ever surprise me again.”

《Maids really are amazing!》

“What exactly are maids, anyway…?”

Not just me, everyone’s concept of what a maid is has been shaken.

“By the way, does that ship have a name?”

“It has a provisional name, but we were thinking of having Jin-sama give it an official one.”

“Then, ‘Tita-‘”

“Stop!”

Mio cuts me off. Let me finish.

“Then, ‘Mary Ce-‘”

“Sto-o-op!!!”

That one is no good too… Let’s see, what other tragic ship names are there…

“Master, please stop joking, okay? Please. Especially horror names. I am serious…”

With Mio practically begging, I decide to think seriously.

I am not very good at naming things, though…

There is a fairly common pattern of including the owner’s name in a ship’s name. But I do not want to include Jin or Gene. In that case…

“Then, how about ‘Queen Sakuya’?”

“That’s basically Sakuya-chan’s ship. Is that really okay?”

“Sakuya-sama is almost completely unrelated, though…”

“But it feels more natural to say that a knight is borrowing a ship from the queen, rather than a mere Queen’s Knight personally owning a ship of this size…”

As I said before, it is clearly a passenger ship.

A single knight owning something like this would be extremely unnatural.

“You do have a point…”

Let’s confirm it just in case.

《It’s fine.》

《I have not even contacted you yet.》

Sakuya’s approval came before I even reached out.

《I heard from Alta. If it is just lending the name, you are free to use it. Though, I would appreciate it if you let me use it too.》

《That’s fine as long as I am not using it.》

《Yay! Thank you!》

Castal was originally landlocked, so it never had ships.

But now that it has acquired coastal territories, it would not look right to not have at least one ship.

For Sakuya as well, this proposal was like a godsend. …Yes, that pun landed nicely.

Guided by two maids, we boarded the ‘Queen Sakuya’.

When I checked the interior on the map, there were guest rooms as well as a hall, pool, game room, and more. This is what they call a luxury cruise ship…

“Is this ship a passenger ship?”

I was curious, so I asked a maid.

“Its use is not limited, but it is designed so that it can also be used as a passenger ship.”

“Although few, there is a possibility of damage from monsters or pirates, so it is also equipped with a reasonable amount of weaponry.”

I check again on the map… what is this? Are they planning to go sack a castle?

This ship is loaded with a ridiculous amount of magical tools.

This is an absurd level of armament. …My bad jokes are on a roll today.

“This will be the guest quarters where you will be staying, Master.”

“For this voyage, only the crew besides yourselves are aboard, so you may use any room you like, but this area is the most luxuriously constructed.”

I can tell without even looking.

The spacing between the doors is absurdly wide. Which means the rooms inside are absurdly large.

“Got it. Then let’s assign rooms at random-“

《Together with Master!》

“I would also like to share a room with Jin-sama.”

“I… do not feel comfortable in rooms that are too large…”

“Then, Sakura-sama, shall we share a room? I do not feel comfortable with this size either…”

“Please do not leave me out!”

Despite having such large rooms, we ended up using only two. One room for me, Dora, and Maria. One room for Sakura, Mio, and Sera.

Being treated like first-class luxury guests all of a sudden is just confusing, right?

Not long ago, we were living in temporary housing in the Elgant Theocracy.

After entering the guest rooms and taking a short break, the ‘Queen Sakuya’ departed.

Thanks to magical tools controlling the ship’s condition, there is hardly any sensation of swaying even after it started moving. It really is a luxury cruise ship.

“Maybe I should call Blue and the others now.”

Rather than summoning them after arriving at the Regalia Beastman Kingdom, I intend for them to enjoy the sea voyage with us.

Blue and the others had been with us when we came to the Meltis Territory, but I had them return once they saw how crowded it was. They are definitely not used to crowds.

I used the ‘Summon’ spell and called Blue, Leaf, and Mikazuki.

“So you are already on the ship. It is indoors so it is hard to tell, though…”

“There is a little bit of swaying, isn’t there?”

“It seems we have already departed. We appear to be moving northwest.”

Perhaps finding the ship interior novel, the three of them look around curiously.

“How do you want to handle rooms?”

“Of course, I want to be in the same room as Master.”

“I want to be in the same room as Sakura-chan.”

“And I… what should I do?”

When I ask about room assignments, Blue and Leaf answer immediately. Only Mikazuki hesitates.

“It is fine if Mikazuki uses a room by herself. There are tons of empty ones…”

It might add to the room-making workload, but I doubt they would refuse.

Mikazuki has also been trained by the maids in various ways, so she should be able to handle room-making on her own.

“Um, I will share a room with Leaf-sama.”

“Mikazuki-chan, welcome!”

So in the end, we are still only using two rooms…

When we left our room, Sakura and the others were also coming out.

“Leaf and Mikazuki want to use your room. Is that okay?”

“Yes, that is fine. As you know, it is even more spacious than we expected…”

“I think it would be fine even with three more people.”

“I feel more at ease when there are more people… Maybe it would have been fine if we all used one room…”

Sakura seems uncomfortable with overly large spaces.

“By the way, how is your seasickness, Sakura?”

It comes to mind belatedly, so I ask.

“It seems fine… I do not know what would happen if it swayed more, but for now…”

“That is good. If you start to feel sick, do not push yourself. Deal with it right away, okay?”

“Yes… If it comes to it, I will retreat into ‘Room’…”

‘Room’ is unaffected by outside swaying (depending on settings).

Convenient. Though it also eliminates the charm of a sea voyage.

“I was thinking of heading to the deck now. What will you do?”

“We were thinking the same. It would be strange to head straight to the game room, after all.”

“I am strong at games, you know?”

“Why would we challenge Master in games that involve luck? We would definitely lose.”

We sometimes play cards or board games when we have free time, but when I join, it usually ends with me winning alone, so Mio does not like it.

Since I end up winning regardless of my intent, I have stopped participating much. The \<Handicap> skill is completely useless.

“So this is the sea. It really is a huge puddle of water.”

“It is big. But the wind does not feel very nice…”

When we move to the deck, the dragonewts who are seeing the sea for the first time begin to get excited.

For Leaf, a deep green dragon, the salty sea breeze was unpopular. Excessive salt is bad for plants. Well, Leaf is not a plant.

By the way, Dora also got excited in the same way when she first saw the sea (back in the Meltis Territory).

It is only natural that dragonewts have never seen the sea.

Maria and Sera had apparently been to the Meltis Territory before, so we did not get much of a reaction from them.

Right. Since we are at the sea, there is someone whose reaction I want to see.

I check her status on the map, see that there is no problem, and use Summon.

“Kya!? Eh, what…?”

The one who appeared is, as you all know, the mermaid princess. When it comes to the sea, mermaids are a given.

The giant sea serpent Maple? I do not know about her. That one lives in a lake.

While I was in the Elgant Theocracy, Leila learned some human language, mastered transformation into human form and bipedal walking with Change, and appeared in a swimsuit. A needless, sexy red bikini.

Hey, three-year-old…

“Yo!”

“Ah, Jin…”

Leila flinches slightly when she sees me.

She still has not gotten used to me.

“Did you call Leila?”

“Yeah. Since we came to the sea, I thought I would show it to you.”

“The sea? …Wow!”

Leila looks around, her eyes sparkling.

“It feels nostalgic! Jin! Can I swim!?”

“You can, but we are moving, so you would be left behind, you know?”

Though in that case I could just ‘Summon’ her.

“This much, I can catch up easily.”

“Master, I saw it the other day, but Leila-chan is seriously fast underwater.”

Mio supplements Leila’s claim.

“Are Mio and Leila close?”

“…She seems to like my cooking the most. That led to us talking about various things.”

“I like Mio’s cooking! I want to eat more!”

Well, that settles it.

“She has also gotten along with Princess Cattleya, a regular at the mansion’s dining hall.”

“That one is always in the dining hall, yeah.”

Princess Cattleya of the Kingdom of Estea. She fell in love with our cooking and comes to eat almost every meal.

She eats a considerable amount, but her figure does not change at all.

“Oops, got sidetracked… Even if you can catch up, you still would not be able to get back on the ship, right?”

“Ah…”

She apparently had not considered that, and her shoulders droop.

“Whether you can catch up or not does not matter. You can swim over, and I will just call you again like before.”

“Got it! Thanks! I am going!”

With a delighted expression, Leila starts running (her bipedal walking is not very fast).

“Out of the way! Oof!”

She tosses aside the bottom of her bikini mid-run.

It would get in the way when swimming in mermaid mode, sure, but having a girl who looks to be in her mid-teens running across a ship topless below the waist is not good.

Leila reaches the edge of the ship and dives into the sea without hesitation (I am following just in case).

Given that this is a luxury cruise ship, the height is considerable…

“So refreshing!”

Once in the sea, Leila begins swimming like a fish in water (a perfect joke).

As if to prove what was said earlier, she is swimming alongside the ‘Queen Sakuya’. She really is fast.

Is it just my imagination, or are a lot of fish gathering around Leila?

A: It is not your imagination. Leila is unconsciously using Mermaid Princess.

Leila’s unique skill, \<Mermaid Princess>, is a powerful skill that grants command authority over lower-ranked opponents while underwater.

Since ordinary fish are basically all lower-ranked, most of them fall under Leila’s control.

It seems she is unconsciously charming them and leading a school of fish.

Is this a chance to get seafood?

While I was thinking that, I saw nets being cast toward Leila from below the ship.

Apparently, there is an area for fishing below the guest deck, and the nets were thrown from there.

It seems the maids, knowing Leila’s nature, took action. I take my hat off to the maids who make full use of Leila. Of course, they made sure she would not get caught in the nets.

I thought it was a passenger ship, but it seems it can also function as a fishing vessel. Incidentally, tonight’s dinner is apparently seafood (boneless).

Once Leila was satisfied with swimming, I retrieved her with ‘Summon’.

The sun was already beginning to set, so we returned to the guest rooms.

“We are intruding.”

“Welcome back.”

“Welcome home.”

“Hm? El and Aya were here too?”

When I open the door, besides Blue who had returned earlier, the Progenitor Divine Dragon and Ayato greet us.

“Blue was gone, so I got lonely and Aya came too!”

“I was not lonely, but if Blue and Aya are going, I did not want to be the only one not going.”

For some reason, these three have often been together lately.

Simply put, they are the ones who sleep in my room.

“We will go back when it is time to sleep, so we will not be in the way.”

“I will be manifested for a while, so allow me to do as I please.”

In the Elgant Theocracy, we had them merged with familiars or Great Spirits just in case, but on this trip, since it is not enemy territory, we are not being that cautious.

El is allowed to roam freely in manifested form. Rain, on the other hand, enters my Spirit Stone whenever she has free time… and right now… yes, she is in there.

“You can sleep here too, you know?”

There is still plenty of space in the room.

However, Aya shakes her head.

“It is fine. Also, I have work with the music troupe starting tomorrow morning.”

“Oh right, you joined the music troupe too, didn’t you?”

“I joined quite a while ago. It has been a good source of stimulation.”

Each of the 1024 Gray People has their own individuality, and Aya possesses high singing ability.

After verification of the Gray People’s abilities was completed and they started working as general-purpose helpers suited to their talents, Aya was scouted by our music troupe.

Aya had been interested after hearing from me that we had music specialists, and she seems to participate frequently.

“Leila is staying behind.”

《There, there.》

Leila is being comforted by Dora.

Since Leila is taller, Dora is hovering slightly.

“She still cannot control her skills, and she lacks human common sense, so it cannot be helped.”

Fille, the leader of our music troupe, is greedy for music.

There was no way she would leave a mermaid princess with high singing skill alone, so of course she tried to recruit Leila.

Leila loves singing as much as swimming, so she accepted. However, Leila still lacks human common sense and it is risky to put her in front of people. On top of that, her Charming Voice activates unconsciously, so she is not allowed to participate in the music troupe.

Forcing emotions to sway with something like mental manipulation is heresy, according to Fille (communicated in writing).

“What will you do, Leila? Will you go back after this?”

“Go back… But I might come again tomorrow.”

“Got it. Come again whenever you want to swim.”

“Yeah!”

Good. Letting her swim in the sea seems to have raised Leila’s affection.

Just a little, but it feels like she has gotten more used to me.

---

**Settings**

**– About skills**

There are innate skills and acquired skills.

Innate skills are skills one is born with. In addition to race-specific skills, one may also gain daily-life skills such as \<Cooking>, or combat skills such as \<Swordsmanship>.

Acquired skills are skills gained after birth through one’s actions. They may be obtained by performing actions related to the skill.

Most skills have levels, and they can be raised up to a maximum of level 10.

To raise a skill’s level, one must repeatedly use the skill, in other words, train to raise proficiency and gain skill points.

In fact, performing actions related to a skill in order to acquire it has the same meaning as training through repeated use of a skill.

By performing actions related to a skill, one trains proficiency for a skill they do not yet possess.

However, even if everyone trains in the same way, it does not mean they will all obtain the same skill.

Skills have aptitude depending on race and individual.

Without that aptitude, no matter how much one trains, they cannot obtain the skill.

Let us call that aptitude the growth rate.

Growth rate multiplied by proficiency becomes skill points.

No matter how hard someone with a growth rate of zero tries, it will never be elevated into a skill.

This growth rate is why there are individual differences in the speed of skill level increases.

Additionally, those who are innately born with skills such as Swordsmanship have innate bonuses to proficiency. In most cases, they also have high growth rates.

Incidentally, Shindo Jin has a growth rate of zero for all skills.

In contrast, local Heroes including Maria have uniformly high growth rates for many skills.

Ordinary reincarnators and transmigrators do not obtain skill points when they are born or transferred to another world.

However, talents, techniques, and knowledge they possessed in their original world do not disappear, but instead are added to their growth rates.

In other words, reincarnators and transmigrators can more easily raise the levels of skills related to their Earth experiences.

Furthermore, Jin’s \<Life and Death Authority> allows him to obtain skills regardless of growth rate, and can also grant growth rates, albeit low ones, to those who originally lack them.

The answer to the question, “Since one cannot perform related actions, are spells limited to innate skills?” will be introduced next time in “About Magic.”

---

**AN:** I tried posting some setting information.

Since Jin only talks about things directly related to himself, there are almost no opportunities to explain this.
