# **146: Pirates and a Hungry Mermaid**

**AN:** In a sense, this is a familiar development.

Revised on 2021/09/19:

Since portals cannot be used in midair, this was changed to Warp.

---

Three days have passed since we set out on our voyage.

These three days were a peaceful journey at sea.

The Mermaid Princess swam in the ocean almost every day, providing us with fresh fish.

The Great Sea Serpent also came by, and there were times when the two aquatic monsters swam together.

The ship had a variety of facilities, so there was no chance of getting bored.

There was even a pool, so you could swim leisurely without going into the sea.

That said, since Sera has a high proportion of muscle and does not float, she was always a poolside ornament.

She has a great figure, so she makes for a pleasing decoration to look at.

Those who just want to enjoy the feeling of a sea voyage join us midway using “Portal.”

They will return home by the time we reach the Regalia Beastman Kingdom, but during the voyage it is not a problem.

When Sakuya showed up as if it were the most natural thing in the world, I did wonder about it a bit…

Now then, earlier I said that “these three days” were peaceful.

What I mean is that “right now”, things are not peaceful.

“Pirates, I presume. To set their sights on this ship… they really are an unlucky lot.”

“We are being surrounded…”

As Sera and Sakura said, this ship is about to be surrounded by pirate ships.

Well, it is not like I could go out to sea and expect things to end peacefully…

I said piracy was not worth it, and yet here I am, running into pirates anyway. What a pain.

“You noticed them, but you did not change course at all. That is part of the reason, you know.”

Mio gives her usual wry smile.

《Master does not run away.》

“That is right. You hate going out of your way to change course.”

With a map, you can tell the position of pirate ships even at extreme range.

But just because we know where they are does not mean we have any reason to avoid them.

So we continued on and ended up being surrounded by pirates.

Needless to say, every single pirate is marked red (enemy). They are preparing their weapons even now.

Alright, let us kill them.

“I am going to wipe out the pirates.”

“Does your policy of killing all bandits apply to pirates too, Master?”

“Yeah. Pirates, bandits, thieves. All of them get exterminated.”

“Oh my… how unfortunate.”

“They truly are an unlucky bunch…”

Basically, I have decided to exterminate anyone with “bandit” in the name.

Besides, fighting pirates is part of the appeal of a sea voyage. Battling some captain-whatever atop the mast is one of a man’s dreams.

Is there a captain-whatever here?

A: No. They are state-affiliated pirates, so they differ greatly from the pirates you are imagining, Master.

Pirates affiliated with a state?

A: Yes. Pirates belonging to one country attack the ships of other countries. Ships from other nations pay that country to avoid being attacked. Ships without a contract are attacked without mercy. Since the state backs them, their equipment performance is reasonably high.

My excitement at hearing the word “pirates” plummets.

What the hell. Farm-raised pirates?

Even though fighting pirates should be the highlight of a sea journey, just hearing that they are state-affiliated makes my interest evaporate.

Normally I would deal with them as Queen’s Knight Gene, but I do not even feel like that.

Spending time on boring opponents is a waste. They are enemies regardless…

“Did something happen? You suddenly look less excited…”

“Yeah, a little…”

“Jin-sama, if you are not feeling up to it, shall I wipe them out instead?”

Should I leave it to Maria? No, that would just be another waste of time.

“No, I will finish it quickly. Actually, it is a hassle, so I will end it right away.”

I activate \<Life and Death Authority> on the crews of nearly ten pirate ships.

I strip all the pirates of their status entirely and reduce their HP to 1.

Then, using \<Omnipotence> (the unique skill of the Yellow Dragon I defeated earlier), I whip up strong winds around this ship.

The pirate ships suddenly rock, and the pirates inside fall over.

The pirates die.

This was my first time using \<Omnipotence> in actual combat, and it is surprisingly easy to use. It seems handy when I want to unleash unnecessarily large-scale attacks.

“It has been a while since I last saw Master steal statuses… this is terrifying…”

“This truly embodies the phrase ‘it is not even a fight’…”

Mio and Sera say this with shivers.

“You activate an ability on the map to drain HP, then use a weather-manipulation skill to shake the ships and finish off the remaining HP… When you put it into words, that is all it is, but… is there any way to stop this?”

“No… I do not think so. The pirates probably did not even understand how they died.”

“I do not really want to say this about Jin-kun, but… this is completely the work of a god…”

Sakura says it hesitantly, but honestly, I cannot really deny it.

This was far too one-sided to even call it a battle. Being called divine is not unreasonable.

In fact, after strengthening \<Life and Death Authority> through \<Expanded Interpretation>, I can now steal skills from anyone on the map.

I have no interest in stealing skills or statuses from non-enemies, and using it normally yields no experience, so I rarely had a chance to use it. But in situations like this, where I can deal with many enemies without causing collateral damage, it is just right, as long as they are opponents I do not care about.

“What is really nice is that there is no damage to the pirate ships, so we can capture them as-is.”

They are high-performance ships built by a maritime nation.

If we can obtain them intact, they will make good souvenirs for Sakuya.

“Jin-sama, the maids are already heading out to collect them.”

“Our maids really are excellent.”

The maids approach the pirate ships in small boats and store them away into \<Infinite Storage>.

Since all the pirates inside are dead, they can be collected just like that.

This is a bit late to say after exterminating the pirates, but from the start, there were two reasons why ship-to-ship naval combat was never an option.

First, naval combat would damage both sides. I obviously do not want the ‘Queen Sakuya’ to be damaged, and we would not have been able to obtain the enemy ships in such pristine condition either.

Second, killing enemies with ship-mounted “weapons” yields nothing.

Let me explain a bit about how this world works.

One of this world’s rules is that “weapons unaffected by physical strength or magic power grant no experience.”

Furthermore, you cannot steal skills or statuses with \<Life and Death Authority> either.

More precisely, if physical strength or magic power does not influence the attack at the moment of impact, you gain no experience.

Simply put, bows are OK, crossbows are not.

Generally speaking, most “weapons” have nearly the same attack power no matter who uses them. Personal physical strength or magic power usually does not factor in.

In other words, simply using “weapons” grants no experience.

If you are not using physical strength or magic power, it does not count as fighting.

Conversely, there is also a rule that “weapons unaffected by physical strength or magic power do not receive any attack power beyond the weapon’s own performance.”

For example, under the same conditions and with the same draw length, a bow can be stronger than a crossbow.

This is because the act of “a person drawing the string” is counted toward attack power.

If you think about what this implies, you will realize something interesting.

While I was thinking about that, it seems the collection of the pirate ships finished.

Earlier, I said that all the pirates inside the ships were dead, but in fact, there was another living being inside.

Naturally, we did not kill anyone other than pirates.

When collecting the ships, we also collected that being.

Here she is.

Name: Myule

Gender: Female

Age: 255

Race: Mermaid

Skills:

\<Aquatic LV9> \<Diving LV9> \<Charming Voice LV4>

As you can see, she is a mermaid.

Encountering another mermaid while traveling with the Mermaid Princess feels like fate. That said, she does not seem to be a princess.

She has no unique-class skills and is overall quite plain, but her swimming-related skills like \<Aquatic> and \<Diving> are outstanding.

She looks to be in her mid-twenties, with blue hair and scales, a beautiful woman. Naturally, she is topless.

She was unconscious, brought in with handcuffs on her arms and weights attached to her legs.

It seems she struggled, as there is blood on her restraints.

What kind of situation is this?

A: I listened to the pirates. This mermaid apparently appeared defenselessly before them. She seemed to be trying to appeal to them, but the pirates did not understand and captured her. She was supposed to be sold after returning to their base, but they encountered this ship on the way back.

I see. It is like a duck bringing green onions with it.

The irony of pirates being treated as the duck is amusing.

So, what does this mermaid want to appeal about?

Based on the pirates’ story, communication is impossible without magic, so “Translation” will be necessary.

Myule is currently… not sleeping in a bed in the infirmary.

She was thrown into the pool on the ‘Queen Sakuya’. Apparently, her body was too dry, leaving her in a faint-like state.

According to Alta, mermaids need to enter water periodically. A kappa?

After removing her restraints and treating her, we decided to toss her into the water.

One hour after throwing her into the pool.

A poolside maid contacted us to report that Myule had woken up.

Sakura, Maria, Mio, and I went to check on her.

Sera stayed behind because she is too intimidating. We were also uneasy about showing Leila right away, so she stayed behind too, along with the Dragonewts playing with her.

When we arrived at the pool, Myule was appealing to the maid about something.

At some point, she had put on a bra.

“Ruuraaru-ruu!?”

As expected, I still cannot understand her.

So, I activate “Translation.”

“Ruuraaru-ruu!? (You cannot understand me!?) Ruu-ruu! (Help!)”

“What is wrong? What do you want?”

“Ruuraaru!? Ruu-ruu! Raaru-ruu! (You understand my words!? Help me! Please help us!)”

When I called out to her from poolside, Myule immediately reacted once she realized we could understand each other.

As expected, mermaid language is different from human language. Considering Leila, it seems you could learn it if taught from a young age, but no one ever thinks to do so.

…Or rather, can communication really work with just “ru” and “ra”?

A: Strictly speaking, the pitch is finely differentiated. Would you like to examine the linguistic system?

No, even if I learned it, I would not use it. There is no need.

“Calm down. Calm down and explain properly.”

“Ruuraaru! (There is no time for that!) Raaru! (Hurry!) Raaru-ruu! (Please help us quickly!)”

If she really wants help, she should explain the situation first, but she is only shouting meaningless things.

You cannot communicate with someone in a panic through words alone.

So, I lightly release killing intent.

“Calm down.”

“Ru… (Yes…)”

Myule quiets down instantly. Hey, do not wet yourself in the pool. This is not a kiddie pool.

… Oh, my killing intent leaked toward Mio!

“Pii!? W-why me too…”

If you ask why… collateral damage?

After that, we listened to Myule’s detailed story once she calmed down.

Mermaid language or not makes no difference, so I will omit it.

“Please… help our mermaid kingdom. Our country is currently in a critical situation.”

There is a mermaid kingdom. Truly fantasy.

What kind of fantastical crisis are they facing, I wonder? I feel guilty, but I am kind of looking forward to it.

“What happened?”

“A food shortage.”

“A food shortage!?”

That is so ordinary. Such an ordinary crisis.

A fantasy word like “mermaid kingdom” dragged back into reality by a normal crisis.

Well, in a way, it is a fitting crisis for a medieval-style world…

“Right now, in our country, we can barely catch any fish, which is our staple food. Many of our people are already so weakened that they cannot move. I am the best swimmer, so I was given a small amount of food and sent out to seek help.”

Mermaids eat fish.

Well, fish eat other fish too, so it is not exactly cannibalism.

“We did not know because we never leave our country, but humans did not understand our language.”

“Do you have no interaction with humans at all?”

“Yes. At least, I have never heard of any interaction with humans since I was born.”

Myule answers my question.

Since she is 255 years old, that means there has been no contact for at least that long.

“Humans have been passed down as fairy-tale beings for a long time. We are told never to approach them unless absolutely necessary, because they are terrifying beings who capture mermaids. Some children with strong curiosity leave the country to observe humans. When they return, we hear their stories.”

So something truly serious happened, and she approached humans, only for the fairy tale to come true…

Still, it is amusing to think that from a human perspective, mermaids are fairy-tale creatures, while humans are fairy-tale creatures to them.

“The first humans I asked for help could not understand me. I was shocked, lost my composure, and was captured.”

As I listened, one question came to mind.

“This affects our actions too, so I want to ask. What exactly were you planning to ask humans to do?”

“Of course, I was going to ask them to save the mermaid kingdom.”

“What would saving you from the food shortage entail?”

“I was thinking of having them bring a large amount of food.”

“How?”

“Humans go out to sea on ships, right? I thought they could transport large amounts of food by ship.”

So they know about ships.

That knowledge probably came from curious mermaids who left the country.

“What would you offer as payment?”

“Payment?”

Myule tilts her head.

I suspected as much, and it seems the concept of compensation does not exist for them.

I had that feeling. After all, Myule did not have anything that looked valuable. Apparently, the pirate ships did not either.

So, I gave her a brief explanation about compensation.

“Then… how are we supposed to get everyone to help us…”

Myule looks crushed.

Even if communication worked, there are not many people who would provide massive amounts of food without any guarantee.

Or perhaps they would pretend to bring food, then capture weakened mermaids instead?

“Payment afterward is possible, but without collateral… without a guarantee, it would be difficult.”

“Payment… payment…”

As Myule desperately racks her brain, I offer some advice.

Honestly, I am very interested in the mermaid kingdom, so I do not mind going to help.

But as always, compensation is required.

“If you cannot think of anything right now, how about guiding us to the mermaid kingdom first? If there is compensation I want, I will provide food aid.”

“You will… help us…?”

Myule looks at me with pleading eyes.

The labyrinth-grown crops made by the maids are piled up in mountains (literally, not figuratively), so providing food aid itself should be easy.

And as usual, the top priority for compensation is rare skills.

If there are rare skills, I will take one point, and then demand other valuable items as compensation.

“If there is compensation I want. Well, if you call yourselves a kingdom, it is unlikely that you have absolutely nothing to offer. Also, just to be sure, are you in a position to demand compensation from your country?”

I do not want to be handed a blank check.

Well, if that happens, things will just turn ugly…

“Y-yes. Seeking help was the queen’s order, so I think it will be fine.”

Oh? The mermaid kingdom is ruled by a queen?

…Come to think of it, what position is our Mermaid Princess in?

Should I reveal it here? Or should I keep it secret?

…Alright, I will keep it secret.

《We will proceed with the policy of not disclosing Leila. That is all.》

I conveyed this policy to the members present.

Could you have Alta inform the others?

A: Understood.

I will subtly probe the situation as we go.

“If you are willing to pay compensation, then guide us to the mermaid kingdom first.”

“Yes! Understood!”

And so, we decided to head for the mermaid kingdom.

Thirty minutes after we decided to depart for the mermaid kingdom.

“The fastest swimmer in the mermaid kingdom, huh. Pretty quick”

I murmured while riding on the back of the Sky Dragon.

“Not impressive at all. I am not even going full power,” Blue replied.

“That’s only fair. Comparing you to Blue would be cruel. She’s my mount, you know.”

“Good, then.”

Said Blue, her voice betraying her excitement.

Currently, we were heading toward the mermaid kingdom guided by Myule.

The party consisted of four members me, Sakura, Maria, and Mio. Three additional companions: Blue, Leaf, and Mikazuki were acting as mounts.

The ‘Queen Sakuya’ was still heading toward the Regalia Beastman Kingdom, and only the members going to the mermaid kingdom rode on the dragonkin, following the swimming Myule.

Since the mermaid kingdom is underwater, there was no advantage to going there aboard the ‘Queen Sakuya’.

Incidentally, Sera and Dora were absent for their usual reasons.

Sera exhibited an aversion to the underwater kingdom.

Being muscular and unable to float, she apparently dislikes the feeling of sinking in water.

Dora prioritized staying on the ‘Queen Sakuya’ to play with Leila.

Though it seems inconsistent, she calls herself Leila’s older sister and doted on her.

For Dora, who had no playmates of similar age or situation, this may be good stimulation.

“Jin-sama, the area has shifted, and we can see the mermaid kingdom.”

“Let’s see…”

I checked the map after receiving the report from Maria, who was riding Blue with me.

Searching for mermaids three areas away revealed more than I had expected. Approximately 5,000 lived there.

Though small as a kingdom, that is a decent number for an underwater nation.

“Looks like only starving mermaids are here. Just as Myule said.”

“Rations seem sufficient… I will ask Lucea to add them into \<Infinite Storage> just in case.”

Since the mermaids were starving, we prepared rations in the form of energy balls created with the \<Energy Ball> magic instead of regular food.

Apparently, feeding normally to starving beings could be fatal, as Mio taught me.

According to Alta, energy balls remove that risk, so we planned to distribute the stored ones. Sera seemed slightly flustered upon hearing the stock would decrease.

…Looking back, feeding Sera a massive amount when she was on the brink of starvation may have been risky.

A: In Sera’s case, she was not starving entirely, so there were no problems. Malnutrition would be a more accurate description.

Good, then.

With ‘Recovery’ and \<Healing Magic> available now, it would never have been a real problem anyway. Worst case, ‘Resurrection’…

To avoid being depressed by staring at starving mermaids, I looked outward from the mermaid kingdom.

I decided to leave the mermaid kingdom itself as a surprise for later.

No land exists near the mermaid kingdom.

For two areas, there is nothing, and no fishing ships appear.

As Myule said, there are almost no fish in the waters, leaving the sea lifeless.

The reason quickly became clear. This is what we found:

Ghost Captain Jack

LV100

\<Swordsmanship LV6>\<Leadership LV8>\<Physical Enhancement LV6>\<Sorcery LV5>\<Undead LV6>

Notes: Leader of the Undead Pirates

Undead Pirates × Many

LV50

\<Swordsmanship LV3>\<Physical Enhancement LV3>\<Sorcery LV3>\<Undead LV3>

Notes: Pirates of the Undead Pirate Crew. Skill sets vary, this is representative of one.

As expected, the Undead Pirate Crew existed in the area adjacent to the mermaid kingdom.

Alright! Real sea enemies have appeared!

“‘Warp’!”

“‘Summon’!”

Mio tried to flee using ‘Warp’ the moment she detected the undead, so I promptly called her back with ‘Summon.’

“Please, let me go home…” she pleaded.

“No.”

I took Mio’s \<Unique Magic> away.

Now she could no longer use ‘Warp’.

Returning to the topic of the undead pirates:

Like the immortal king we defeated before, they contaminate the surrounding area with \<Sorcery>-based miasma.

Miasma affects smaller creatures more severely, similar to poison. Fish left the surrounding waters to avoid it.

Larger-bodied mermaids likely did not notice the minor miasma and continued their lives unaware. Thus, the mermaids fell into a food shortage.

We understood the cause, but providing food support to the mermaids took priority, so we left the pirates alone for now.

One disappointment is that, although the undead pirates are interesting as enemies, they possess no rare skills. Fighting them is fun, but the reward for defeating them is minimal.

Despite being called pirates, they carry little treasure, which emphasizes the point.

Nonetheless, pirates must be exterminated regardless of rare skills or treasure, if they claim the pirate name.

There are about ten pirate ships, all stationary.

Their sails are folded; what exactly are they doing?

Is their goal to just release miasma? For what purpose?

After a short while, we received a signal from Myule, and I instructed the dragonkin to approach the sea surface.

We were close enough to say we were essentially at the mermaid kingdom; all that remained was to dive.

Before arriving, we had set up underwater-oriented skills including \<Diving> and \<Environmental Adaptation>, and worn swimsuits, so we were fully prepared.

“Alright, Blue and the others, head back first.”

“Understood. Will you use ‘Portal’ on the way back?”

I nodded at Blue’s question.

“Yeah, that’s the plan.”

“I really wish you could come back with us too, but it can’t be helped.”

“You really love your master, don’t you, Blue?”

“…Yes.”

Leaf said with a fond smile.

Blue blushed but would never deny it.

“When we reach the Regalia Beastman Kingdom, there’ll be another chance to ride, so be patient until then.”

“Absolutely, right?”

“Yes, count on it.”

I jumped from Blue and splashed into the sea.

Maria followed immediately.

“Thank you too, Leaf…”

“Not at all, I’m fine.”

Sakura jumped in as well.

“Mio, do your best too.”

“Thanks, Mikazuki…”

Even the unenergetic Mio plunged in.

Once everyone entered the water, we began diving according to Myule’s guidance.

Maria swam quickly, as expected; she is skilled at everything she does.

Mio was not as skilled, moving at a slightly slower pace… though perhaps weighed down by the undead issue.

Surprisingly, Sakura swam effortlessly.

Later, I learned she had learned swimming out of necessity. She was particularly good at swimming fully clothed… I did not ask for details. And I dare not.

Sakura’s abilities vary greatly.

As far as I know, her weaknesses are gore, physical activity, and cooking. Cooking I can’t criticize, though…

《Sakura, besides gore, exercise, and cooking, do you have other weaknesses?》

《What is it…?》

《Just curious.》

I decided to ask her telepathically.

I know. This is a potentially sensitive topic.

《Jin-kun, you are abrupt as always… Well… motion sickness… is cured, so otherwise… Oh, I am bad at conversation and social interaction… Please infer why…》

《…》

No need to ask, really.

《Mio-chan is afraid of ghosts…》

《I know.》

Mio tried to appeal with lifeless eyes, but I ignored her.

---

Settings

– About Magic

Those who possess magic-type skills can use magic in exchange for consuming MP.

When magic is used, a magic circle appears, and the caster enters a chanting state (actual verbal chanting is not necessary).

After a set time specific to each spell passes, consciously focusing on the magic will trigger it. Saying the spell’s name produces a similar effect and can also activate the magic.

This chanting requires considerable concentration, and MP gradually decreases during the process. The chanting time is almost equal to the MP consumption time (except for Sakura’s magic). Even if concentration breaks and the magic fails, the consumed MP is not returned.

There are two ways to acquire magic-type skills.

The first is to inherently know a magic-type skill from birth. The second is to use magical tools designed for acquiring magic.

These magical tools, which allow the acquisition of magic, can be created by skilled users of high-level \<Magic Tool Crafting> and are called “Grimoires.” Naturally, they are high-grade items, but they are not completely out of reach for ordinary people.

Unlike skill orbs (introduced in Volume 5: Dragonfolk Hidden Realm), Grimoires do not guarantee that the user will acquire a skill.

Grimoires have the effect of increasing proficiency, as explained in the previous “About Skills” section.

In other words, even someone with a growth rate of 0 cannot acquire a skill using one.

Moreover, Grimoires are single-use. This leads to complaints like “I used it but couldn’t learn the magic-it’s a scam,” or causes people with actual talent to give up on the path of magic because they were sold a fake.

When purchasing a Grimoire, it is recommended to buy from a reliable shop and sign a certificate acknowledging “I will not complain even if I cannot acquire the magic” before use.

Incidentally, all of these topics are irrelevant to Jin, so they never came up in the main story.

This is because Jin’s growth rate is 0 in every case.

Magic-type skills allow the use of several spells per level.

However, not all spells are usable depending on racial traits. Generally, the spells a user can employ depend on their race’s intelligence level.

Elves, who can use all spells fully, tend to become arrogant, mistakenly thinking their racial intelligence is superior.

Among magic-type skills, there are also several that assist in magic usage, such as \<No-Chanting>.

These are almost exclusively innate skills, as they lack Grimoires and are difficult to obtain through related actions.

---

**AN:** This is the usual detour. However, it is a short detour, so it does not consume a full chapter. Really!

I’ve just bought a game, so my remaining lives are a bit low.

Well, the real challenge starts when lives reach 0 anyway (though I’m the type who can’t actually handle that).

+++

# **147: The Mermaid Kingdom and Food Aid**

**AN:** My progress has gotten dangerously bad, regardless of the game.

Volume 11, Adventurers Guild Arc, please look forward to it.

---

The mermaid kingdom was covered by a gigantic dome-shaped barrier.

Those who hear that opening line can probably already guess, but as everyone knows, the mermaid kingdom was a dungeon.

Using dungeon functions to deploy a barrier was the same method used by Dora’s homeland, the “Dragonkin Sanctuary.”

I remember saying that Dora and Leila had similar circumstances, but I never thought it would extend to something like this. Well, it is not yet confirmed that this place is Leila’s homeland either.

Unlike the “Dragonkin Sanctuary”, this barrier is not completely sealed. There are several entrances.

We are heading toward one of those entrances under Myule’s guidance, though honestly, I already confirmed them on the map.

To prevent sea creatures from accidentally wandering inside, the entrances appear to be located near the seafloor.

Myule, who is leading the way, crosses the barrier, and we follow after her.

“Whew. Looks like we made it inside the barrier.”

“Just as Jin-kun said, I can breathe normally…”

In fact, this barrier has several special functions.

One of them is this.

Surprisingly, humans can live normally inside this barrier.

We can breathe, and we can talk. Even if you open your mouth, water does not rush in. Instead, only air flows in. It is probably impossible to convey that sensation properly with words.

Thinking about it normally, mermaids can already breathe and converse underwater thanks to the \<Aquatic> skill, so this function is clearly unnecessary for them.

It is almost as if it was designed with humans coming here in mind.

That said, even though humans can function here, this is still the sea. Swimming is faster than walking when it comes to movement.

Anyway.

As we entered the barrier, five male mermaids holding spears approached us from a short distance away.

They were probably gatekeepers, but they were so emaciated from starvation that they honestly looked weak.

“Myule, you made it back safely. That is a relief.”

“The humans behind you… we can assume we are saved, right?”

All of the gatekeeper mermaids looked visibly relieved.

As expected, the situation must be quite dire.

“Yes. I am back. Please grant us an audience with Her Majesty the Queen. And then…”

Myule briefly reports everything that happened up to now.

“I understand. I will go ahead and make preparations.”

One of the gatekeepers, after hearing Myule’s report, swims off at a speed that belies his emaciated appearance.

Ahead of him is a particularly magnificent building where the queen resides. It is almost certainly the royal castle.

“Jin-san, the queen needs time to prepare, so let us take things slowly as we head to the palace.”

“Yeah, that works. I want to take a look around the city anyway.”

I do think it is not ideal to take too much time when so many mermaids are starving, but if the mermaid side says it is fine, it is not my place to complain.

All right then, let me explain the mermaid kingdom as we proceed slowly.

The mermaid kingdom does not seem to have barrier expansion facilities like the “Dragon Gate”, so it is not as vast as the “Dragonkin Sanctuary.”

Even so, with a diameter of ten kilometers, it is more than large enough for about five thousand mermaids of human size to live comfortably.

Every building in the mermaid kingdom is made of stone.

At a glance, you would not notice it, but I can tell. Every building in this country was created using dungeon core functions…

Well, it is not like mermaids would normally have construction know-how.

We can see the mermaids themselves, but every single one of them is emaciated, and hardly any are moving properly.

The gatekeepers and those stationed at the palace seem to be in slightly better shape, but the general populace is practically devastated. This is probably due to food distribution priorities.

“Normally, it is much more lively… but right now, it is like this…”

Myule says sadly.

Even I cannot go into sightseeing mode while seeing suffering mermaids out of the corner of my eye.

“Once the food shortage is resolved, let me come sightseeing properly. Will you all join me?”

After resolving the food crisis, we should be able to tour the place without anyone complaining.

“I shall accompany Jin-sama wherever you go.”

“I will go too… It is a rare country, so I want to look around…”

“I want to go home…”

Mio is not doing so well.

Maybe I teased her a bit too much just because her reactions were funny. I should reflect on that.

“I will send you back to the ship before we make contact with the Ghost Pirate Crew.”

“Come on! Let us go! Hurry up and solve the mermaid kingdom’s crisis!”

Mio’s swimming speed suddenly increased after that. What a straightforward girl.

After swimming through the city for a while, we finally arrive at the castle, the core of the mermaid kingdom.

Like the other buildings, the royal castle is made of stone, but it is enormous enough that anyone can tell at a glance.

Mermaids seem to have little desire to decorate things, so there are hardly any ornaments or furnishings.

“That is a shame. If only it were Japanese-style, I could call it a Dragon Palace…”

That was my honest impression upon seeing the largest building in the mermaid kingdom.

When you hear about a castle under the sea, it is only natural to imagine a Dragon Palace.

But calling a simple stone structure a Dragon Palace does not feel right.

“Does this building have a name?”

“? No, it is only called the royal palace.”

I asked Myule with a faint hope, but the result was disappointing.

How unfortunate.

We proceed into the royal castle.

As an aside, none of the buildings in this country have doors.

From a mermaid’s perspective, opening and closing doors is probably a hassle (they cannot brace themselves properly, after all).

“So it is the same inside… Maybe I should have brought the maids?”

Inside the castle, just like outside, there are many mermaids suffering from starvation.

Originally, I planned to have people come pick up ration balls themselves instead of distributing them, but seeing mermaids who do not even have the energy for that makes me reconsider.

Maybe I should have the maids help and distribute them using sheer manpower?

“Why not save the ones closest to death first, then have the recovered mermaids help?”

An energetic Mio offers some advice.

“That should be more than enough. Still, we should secure a guarantee of compensation from the queen first.”

“I do not want to work for free.”

“I will never forgive anyone who tries to take advantage of Jin-sama.”

I feel bad for the starving mermaids, but I have no intention of handing over ration balls without a guarantee of compensation.

Unfortunately, there are hardly any holders of Unique Skills here either.

“Myule has already informed Her Majesty, so it should be fine. We are almost at the room where Her Majesty resides, so please be sure not to be disrespectful.”

“…”

I was asked that by Myule, but unfortunately, I cannot promise to be respectful, so I will maintain silence.

After all, there is a possibility I might classify her as an enemy because of mermaid princess-related issues…

A princess who lived alone outside the country overlaps with Dora’s situation. If she went through the same thing Dora did, there is no way I could remain polite.

Beyond this point lies a particularly large room, probably the audience chamber. The queen should be there.

Here are the queen’s status details.

Name: Mestialka  

Gender: Female  

Age: 570  

Race: Mermaid  

Titles: Queen of the Mermaids, Usurper King  

Skills: \<Aquatic LV10> \<Diving LV10> \<Transformation LV10> \<Alluring Voice LV9> \<Luck LV5>

The skill levels are fairly high, but the lineup is unimpressive.

There are almost no skills befitting a queen.

Looking at her titles, the reason becomes clear. She was probably not originally a candidate for the throne.

I cannot be certain, but I feel there is some involvement with Leila.

“Jin-san, we have arrived.”

Not long after Myule says that, we arrive at the audience chamber (temporary).

The mermaid queen sat on a throne, just like a human king. She did not have to imitate humans in that regard…

She looks like a beautiful half-naked woman in her late twenties.

Blonde hair, blue scales. Her facial features are completely different from Leila’s. The queen is not Leila’s parent.

We land at a spot a short distance from the queen.

Many mermaids surround her, all of them emaciated without exception. The only one who is not is the queen herself.

“Welcome, human guests. I am Mestialka, the queen of this mermaid kingdom.”

“Nice to meet you. My name is Jin.”

It has been a while since I last used polite speech.

However, the queen looks at us with a suspicious expression.

“… Why do you not kneel before me?”

As expected, we are standing while facing the queen.

She seems displeased that we did not kneel.

“There is no reason for us to kneel. We came here because we were asked. We will treat you with respect, but we have no reason to abase ourselves to the point of kneeling.”

That is why I am at least using polite speech.

When I meet the head of a state for the first time, I use polite speech out of respect for the fact that they lead a country. Of course, if that respect disappears, so does the polite speech.

The “Dragonkin Sanctuary” was an exception.

I could not respect a chieftain who would not even search for a lost imperial princess.

The relationship between Leila and the mermaid kingdom is also suspicious, but it is not confirmed yet, so I am still being polite.

“J-Jin-san!?”

Myule lets out a panicked voice beside me, but I do not care.

The queen glares at us with overwhelming pressure. Given her long life, it is quite an imposing presence. I can physically feel the tension in the air.

That said, sorry, but I have not lived such a gentle life that I would be shaken by this alone.

We exchange silent stares for a while. … I am bored.

“If you have no business, we will be leaving.”

It seems like an interesting country, but it is not worth bending myself for.

I feel sorry for the mermaids, but they will have to follow the path chosen by their country’s leader.

“… Very well. Speak while standing.”

Perhaps she sensed my seriousness. The queen reluctantly yields.

Ah, the queen has turned red (enemy) on my display.

Just from that? How petty.

“Do you truly possess enough food to distribute to all of this country’s people?”

“Yes. Here it is.”

I take out about five ration balls from my \<item box> bag. This is underwater, so they float gently.

“They are small.”

“They are small, but one is enough to fill most people. There are over five thousand of these in this bag.”

“Your Majesty, what Jin-san says is true. I ate one myself, and a single one filled me up. With these, this country can recover from starvation!”

I had Myule eat one beforehand, so she can attest to it from experience.

“Hm. If that is true, then this country’s situation should improve. … And you want a reward in return, correct?”

“No. That is not quite right. We are not asking for a reward, but for compensation as an equal transaction.”

A reward is something given from above to below, with the giver having the final say over what is given.

That is not appropriate for an equal transaction like this.

“Do not phrase things in such an irritating way.”

The queen says so without hiding her displeasure.

This queen is naturally condescending, so my respect points are dropping fast.

“… Fine. There is no time, so a transaction it is. What do you desire? Speak.”

“If there are rare magical tools, I would like those. Or if there are items of value obtainable only in this country. Additionally, I would like the right to tour this country.”

I would really like rare skills, but there are hardly any rare skill holders here, and the few that exist are ones we already have.

The rarest skill holder among the mermaids is our own mermaid princess.

“Very well. Take whatever you like from the treasury. Tour the country as you please.”

I have already confirmed the location of the treasury and listed noteworthy items.

If she tries to cheat us on compensation, I will make her regret being born.

“I understand. Then, this is for you.”

“Myule. Take the bag and distribute the food.”

“Yes. Jin-san, excuse me.”

I hand the item box bag to Myule as she approaches under the queen’s instruction.

“Myule. Feed it to someone suitable first.”

“Yes.”

Myule takes out a ration ball and feeds it to the most emaciated mermaid.

“Uooooooo!!! Power is surging through me!!!”

The revitalized mermaid lets out a roar.

For the record, it is a woman (topless). Her shriveled chest regains its fullness.

“T-The effect is disturbingly strong…”

The queen recoils at the sight. I do too.

The revived woman takes ration balls from Myule and feeds them to others. There are plenty, so no one should go without.

“Uooooooo!!!”

“Haaaaaaa!!!”

“Gooooooo!!!”

Mermaids all over are surging with energy after eating ration balls.

This is different. This is not the mermaids I know. The mermaids I know swim gracefully underwater.

“Myule. Have them distribute food to those outside the palace.”

“Yes! Leave it to me, Your Majesty.”

Under the queen’s orders, Myule and several other mermaids leave the audience chamber with food.

Once Myule leaves, the queen speaks to me again.

“Go to the treasury and choose your compensation.”

“Yes. Understood. Are there any conditions? Quantity, value…”

“I do not know the value of the treasures. Take however much you deem equivalent. They are not things we need anyway.”

That is surprisingly generous.

“Understood. I will do so.”

That said, I do not intend to take everything.

I plan to keep it roughly equivalent to the ration balls provided with a bit extra (as a handling fee).

We are led to the treasury by a guide mermaid.

“Please choose from the items inside. I will wait outside. Call me when you are finished.”

The guide mermaid says in front of the treasury.

“All right, thank you.”

“Please take your time.”

Now then, it is time for treasure hunting.

Well, I had already decided on the items I absolutely had to take with me.

《Jin-sama, the queen is showing as an enemy. Is that acceptable? Shall I strike?》

Just as I was thinking that, Maria asked through telepathy.

Since a mermaid was nearby, she was checking via telepathy.

《Do not strike, do not strike. Even if the queen appears as an enemy, it poses no real problem. If she harbors hatred in her heart, she can still interact without showing it externally. Any queen should be able to do that. As long as there’s no direct action, there’s nothing worth getting worked up over.》

《If Jin-sama says so, I will continue to maintain caution.》

It wasn’t enemy territory like the Elgant Theocracy, but since the queen at least disliked me, caution was necessary.

Still, hostility and harmful intent were different. Hostility alone didn’t justify an attack from our side.

…It’s a shame that I haven’t been able to go sightseeing without caution lately. I wonder how it is in the Regalia Beastmen Kingdom?

《Do as you will. But if she takes direct action, that changes everything.》

《Understood.》

With the telepathy conversation concluded, the search for treasures had also come to a close.

Since I had a map, there was no need to search deliberately.

“Mio-chan, this one is for you. I can’t believe it’s actually part of a series…”

What Mio had wanted was armor.

Mermaid Treasure Circle Shield

Category: Shield  

Rarity: Legendary  

Notes: Complete Heat Control

…Correction. It is labeled as a shield, but to my eyes, it looks like nothing but a pot.

There is a handle in a position unlike a normal shield…

It is probably the same category as the kitchen knife we got in the “Dragonkin Sanctuary.”

A knife sword and a pot shield. Clearly joke equipment. A pot would fit better as a helmet, honestly.

“Mio, next time, could you hold that knife from the sanctuary and wear that pot on your head for me?”

“Eh… Why would I wear something so weird…?”

“I think joke equipment suits you.”

“That is terrible! Do not treat me like a joke character!”

Eh? Mio is a joke character, though?

“Jin-kun is teasing Mio-chan again…”

“Jin-sama, if you wish, I can equip it.”

“Maria, huh… The gap appeal might be interesting once in a while… But I cannot accept covering your cat ears with headgear. Mio, can I make holes in that pot for cat ears?”

“That would defeat the purpose of it being a pot!”

After Mio’s desperate persuasion, I give up. What a shame.

Maria also looks disappointed.

All right, that is enough teasing Mio. Next treasure.

Dungeon Core

The core that serves as the source of a dungeon’s power. Unregistered Dungeon Master state.

Yeah.

No.

Leaving this alone is not okay, is it!?

It is the heart of the dungeon!

This country is safe thanks to the dungeon barrier, yet the dungeon core is treated like this!?

For reference, the dungeon core was placed in a box and left carelessly in a corner of the treasury.

Clothes and ornaments are piled messily nearby.

It is treated completely differently from the other treasures.

There is no way I can take the dungeon core.

Should I inform the queen about this?

I pick out other suitable items so that the total is (roughly equivalent) to the ration balls, that is, lives.

Back to the audience chamber again.

By the time mermaids across the country had been revitalized and Myule returned, we also returned to the audience chamber.

No one died. We made it just in time.

“Your Majesty, we have successfully saved all of our citizens.”

“Good. Well done.”

“Thank you for your gracious words.”

The queen nods in satisfaction at Myule’s report.

However, Myule’s expression remains clouded.

“However, the lack of food, the absence of fish, remains unresolved. What should we do?”

“Hm…”

The queen ponders Myule’s words.

Yes, this food aid is only a temporary measure.

It does not solve the root problem.

If conditions were right, we could solve it ourselves. We know both the cause and the countermeasures.

“An investigation is necessary. I will leave the selection of personnel to you. However, food will still be scarce during the investigation.”

“The food Jin-sama provided is almost gone. We must take some kind of action.”

“Hm…”

The queen thinks again, then turns her gaze toward us.

“You there, Jin, was it? Is it possible to request continued food aid from you?”

“Providing food is possible, but do you have something to offer as compensation? I saw the treasury earlier, but I do not think it is sufficient for ongoing support.”

More precisely, there are still valuable items left.

But if they do not interest me or my companions, I do not want them, no matter how valuable.

If I do not want them, they are not compensation.

I am a man who does not move for money alone.

“There is nothing left that has value and that I want.”

“Hmm… That reminds me. What did you choose as compensation?”

The queen asks as if she just remembered. She truly has little interest in treasure.

“Well, these, and these, and…”

I line up the items I plan to take, one by one.

I also place the boxed dungeon core there. I did not bring it to take it, but to ask about it.

“The last one is something I would like to ask Your Majesty about…”

“… You bring something unpleasant.”

The queen makes no effort to hide her distaste.

“Do you know what this is?”

“I do not. But it is something the former queen cherished dearly. It disgusted me, so I had it thrown into the treasury.”

So she does not know it is a dungeon core.

And the former queen may have been the Dungeon Master.

“May I ask why it disgusted you?”

“It belonged to the woman I cast aside to take the throne. Of course it disgusts me.”

I see. That is why it was placed carelessly in the treasury.

That means everything in that area belonged to the former queen.

The relationship between the former queen and the current one. Judging by her expression when speaking of her, it seems the current queen harbored one-sided jealousy.

That was probably the reason she overthrew her.

And the method was likely close to an ambush. Otherwise, it is hard to imagine a dungeon ruler falling so easily inside their own dungeon.

“May I ask one more thing?”

“Speak.”

“Do you know anything about the mechanism of the barrier surrounding this country?”

Given how she treated the dungeon core, the odds are high that she does not know.

But I want to ask to determine future actions.

“I do not know. It has always been there and will remain so. No one investigates it.”

“Jin-sama, according to an ancient royal decree, investigating the barrier is forbidden. All we know is that when the royal bloodline ends, the barrier will disappear.”

Myule supplements the queen’s statement.

Considering that the former queen cherished it, she likely understood the dungeon core and the barrier. A royal secret.

Unlike the “Dragonkin Sanctuary”, this kingdom did pass down knowledge of the dungeon core to those who should know.

…Well, that did not help when a rebellion occurred.

Also, the barrier disappearing when the royal bloodline ends is one of the settings revealed by examining the dungeon core.

This dungeon core has been modified, with various restrictions imposed.

First, no one outside the royal family can become the dungeon ruler.

More precisely, even if they become one, they do not receive the information needed to operate the dungeon core.

Furthermore, even if a royal becomes the dungeon ruler, the information they receive is limited, so they cannot change those settings.

Additionally, the dungeon ruler’s immortality setting is disabled, so rulers are replaced generationally.

Put bluntly, the queen is a generational barrier maintenance device.

While thinking about this, the queen stares at Maria and Mio beside me.

“I have a question for you as well. Do you desire a mermaid girl?”

“Your Majesty!?”

Myule cries out.

“Myule, be silent.”

“…”

Myule falls silent under the queen’s glare.

“Humans capture mermaids. That means mermaids have value. Then, offering mermaids as compensation for food aid is reasonable, is it not?”

I see. Logically speaking, perhaps?

Selling one’s own citizens is problematic, but if there is no other option, I cannot completely deny it.

“I would rather not be hated by their parents…”

I generally only buy orphans or slaves (Exception: Unique Skill Village).

Slaves abandoned by parents, or orphans who lost theirs. Those who have already lost blood ties.

It is less troublesome in many ways. I also dislike severing parent-child bonds with my own hands.

“Rest assured. Conveniently enough, there are many girls without parents now.”

That may be convenient, but it is not a good thing.

“So you intend to…”

“Myule, I told you to be silent.”

Myule falls silent again.

Ah. I get it now. Everything connects.

If the former queen and Leila were mother and daughter, everything fits.

Leila is currently three years old. That means the queen changed around three years ago.

The current queen, who purged the former queen’s belongings, likely purged the mermaids around her as well.

If that ‘purge’ meant execution, what happens? Children become orphans.

Three years ago, most children would still be children.

That is cruel.

She orphaned them herself, then sells them off because they are orphans.

And I would be the buyer… No. Absolutely not.

A: Master. Would it not be better to buy them and save them?

What do you mean?

A: Do you believe children orphaned under such circumstances are living decent lives? In this food crisis, those closest to death were those orphans.

I see.

---

**AN:** I understand that there are many points to question about the underwater dome.

Is it in the deep sea? If so, does light reach it? If not, how is the sea structured?

I thought about many things, then gave up.

As a provisional setting, the sea in this world is not that deep, and due to refraction and such, light reaches a certain depth. Let us leave it at that.

+++

# **148: Transactions and the Ghost Pirates**

**AN:** My writing pace has finally started to recover a little.

---

“Could it be that they are… children of those connected to the former queen?”

When I asked, the queen nodded.

“Hmm, you are perceptive. That is correct. All of the former queen’s close attendants were executed, but at the earnest pleas of my vassals, only the children’s lives were spared. To me, they are beings whose presence or absence makes no difference. Would they not make an appropriate price to pay you?”

“Your Majesty…”

It seems the children of the former queen’s attendants are not even counted as citizens.

Hearing this, Myule looks extremely sorrowful.

Perhaps Myule herself was among the vassals who begged for the children’s lives.

“So then, do you desire mermaid girls? Will they suffice as payment for food?”

“Yes. They are acceptable as compensation. How many are there?”

If the head of the organization is the one selling them, and they are children with no parents who have been treated poorly, then there is no problem or obstacle in purchasing them.

Any objections about human, or fish, trafficking will not be accepted.

The next thing to confirm is the number.

“Myule, answer.”

Well, there is no way the queen would bother to remember the number of orphans.

Ordered by the queen, Myule answers reluctantly.

“…Yes. Among the children who have lost their parents, those not currently working amount to twenty-five girls.”

“Only girls?”

If they were children shunned by the queen, I was prepared to buy them regardless of gender, but it sounds like there are only girls to begin with.

“As for boys… given the gender ratio of this country, we cannot sell them…”

In fact, the mermaid country has a gender ratio of roughly three to seven, with females being more numerous.

If they were to sell boys here, it could cause trouble in the future.

In other words, surplus orphaned girls can simply be sold off.

“I understand. I will purchase them all. The question is how many days worth of food to exchange for them, but I have one proposal.”

“Speak.”

I want to finish troublesome matters in as few turns as possible.

“How about this: we will provide food aid until the food shortage is resolved?”

“Hmm, that would certainly help us, but if things go poorly, you could end up providing aid indefinitely. What is it you want?”

Even the queen seems suspicious.

With just this, we would be taking all the losses.

“It is simple. We are saying that we will eliminate the cause of the food shortage.”

“What…?”

The queen gives me a puzzled look.

“We already have a good idea of what is causing the food shortage. The moment we resolve it, the contract ends. Even if we never distribute food even once.”

“The cause of the food shortage? What could that be?”

“If I tell you, the meaning of this proposal will diminish, so I will explain after it is resolved.”

Even if I told her, it does not mean she could resolve it anyway.

“Hmm… But if I think about it carefully, this proposal poses no disadvantage to us. If you resolve it, we will no longer need food aid. If you cannot, the food support will continue until we resolve it ourselves. Either way, all we lose are unnecessary orphans.”

“…”

At the queen’s phrasing, Myule’s expression clouds over.

Setting aside the queen’s wording, this proposal carries no disadvantage for the mermaid side.

It is simply a matter of where our effort will be spent.

I intend to crush the ghost pirates for my own peace of mind. I do not want the food aid to last long. I will take the orphaned mermaids.

Considering all of these together, this seems like the most efficient option.

“There is also a benefit for me. If we resolve it, I can obtain the mermaids in the shortest time possible without giving any food. And we already have a plan.”

“I understand. If you are that confident, I will accept your proposal. Myule, accompany them and determine the cause of the food shortage.”

“Yes!”

Thus, we set into motion to resolve the cause of the food shortage.

The queen does not intend to leave the resolution solely to us. She will also proceed with organizing a mermaid investigation team. In addition, she is organizing an expedition force to secure a minimum amount of food.

Leaving everything to us would be dangerously risky from a risk management standpoint, so this is only natural.

For these reasons, the castle has become quite busy.

Since there is no reason for us to remain in the royal castle, we decide to head out immediately to hunt pirates.

As we leave the castle with Myule in tow, we notice a city that has regained some vitality.

However, since the threat of food shortage still looms, many mermaids wear expressions filled with a sense of desperation.

Perhaps because we are unusual, I can feel gazes directed at us, but no one approaches to speak. Some of the looks seem fearful, likely due to the reputation humans have.

In no time at all, we arrive at the barrier, speak to the guards, and exit through the gate.

We do not plan to swim underwater to reach the ghost pirates, so we surface to the sea first.

“Master, sorry to keep you waiting.”

“Sorry we took so long!”

“We apologize for the wait.”

After floating for a while, the three dragonkin girls used for transport arrive.

“Huh? Weren’t they supposed to have gone back already?”

“I sent them back once, but since we are moving to resolve the food shortage, I called them again.”

“Called them? Huh, how did you…?”

“Trade secret.”

I answer Myule’s question, but she seems even more confused now.

Of course, I have no intention of answering the additional questions.

“Mio is…”

“I’m going back! Mikazuki-san, please!”

“Y-yes…”

She has no intention of participating in the fight against the ghost pirates, and quickly mounts Mikazuki.

“Mio-chan really is bad with ghosts, isn’t she…”

“Not just actual ghosts, but even undead classified as monsters. That’s pretty severe.”

“Scary things are scary!”

Since it is a clear weakness, part of me wants her to overcome it someday, but the part of me that finds frightened Mio cute also wants to leave it as is. It is a dilemma.

To begin with, I think it would be difficult to overcome. If her mental age matched her appearance, I could believe she might grow out of it, but in reality she has lived twenty-four years. Fixing something that has not been fixed in that time would be tough.

“Seems like it. So as promised, Mio, you can head back first.”

“I will do that.”

An immediate answer.

“Maria… goes without saying. Sakura, what will you do? Will you follow me, or do you want to go back first? I will not force you.”

“I will follow Jin-kun to the end… Ghosts do not bother me…”

“All right.”

And so, Maria rides Blue, and Sakura rides Leaf.

“Now then, the problem is how to bring Myule along.”

“You all fly through the sky, correct? Should I not simply chase after you?”

Myule does not seem to understand what I am worrying about.

“Hmph, so I am being underestimated.”

“Blue, do not say that. She does not know your top speed, so it cannot be helped.”

“If Master says so…”

Blue is a tsundere in a dere state, so she is very dere.

Myule swims fast, but it cannot be compared to the flight speed of a sky dragon.

Matching her swimming speed would be a waste of time, except when she needs to guide us.

If only she had the \<Transformation> skill, I could have her ride behind Leaf, but I want to avoid that since mermaid form would make balancing difficult.

“Let me see…”

I wear the “Undead Wings” as a cloak over my swimsuit. A swimsuit cloak is highly perverted, but this is no time to be picky.

I manipulate the cloak to scoop Myule out of the water, lifting her up like a princess carry. That said, since I am holding the reins, it is actually part of the “Undead Wings” that is supporting her.

“W-what is this!?”

Myule shouts, but I ignore her.

Thus, the image is complete: riding a sky dragon in a swimsuit, holding a mermaid in a black cloak.

“Perfect.”

“What is!?”

Mio’s retort comes in, but I do not mind.

This is probably the fastest way.

“Well then, we are heading out.”

“Take care. I am heading back first.”

“Please excuse me.”

We bid farewell to Mio and Mikazuki and head toward the extermination of the ghost pirate crew.

“H-hieeeeeee!”

Myule, who has never flown before, lets out a pitiful scream.

And naturally, she soils herself, soaking the “Undead Wings.”

This is, for the record, a rare boss drop from the Estea Labyrinth…

I activate “Purify” while making sure the dripping golden liquid does not splash onto Blue.

After flying for a short while, we arrive in the area where the ghost pirates are located.

Now then, how should we exterminate the ghost pirate crew…

To add some context, this is less about planning a battle and more like deciding on a dinner menu.

In other words, we can cook them however we like (a masterpiece of a joke).

The fastest method would be to use \<Life and Death Authority> to steal the \<Undead> skill.

If we take the \<Undead> skill, even tens of thousands of enemies could be wiped out in an instant. It would not even be a fight.

When speed is required, this is sometimes the option.

Come to think of it, do those ghost pirates even have consciousness? More importantly, can they talk?

A: They cannot. They have no consciousness.

As expected.

Looking at the map, they are all rotting, tattered wrecks with not a shred of intelligence.

If possible, I wanted to confirm their motive for spreading miasma, but there is no way words would get through to them.

Sigh…

I had two chances to fight pirates on this voyage, but neither seems like it will turn into the kind of fight I want.

Even if I charged in and challenged the captain to a duel, they would not accept.

It would just be a horde of undead attacking.

The pirate ships are in shambles, and there is no treasure, so there is no reason to capture them.

No rare skills and no duel means my motivation does not rise.

Maybe I should just steal the \<Undead> skill…

Ah, but it would be smoother to let Myule see the moment of extermination.

《Once we reach the pirates, the three of us will use magic to wipe them out.》

《I thought Jin-kun would board and fight them…》

Sakura says, sounding surprised.

《If the ghost pirates had consciousness, I would have done that. Since they do not, extermination is just work.》

《I understand…》

《I acknowledge.》

There is little to learn from fighting undead that do not act intelligently.

Spending time on battles with nothing to learn is a waste. I have no intention of putting in effort.

As mentioned earlier, there is nothing of value, so wiping them out along with their ships using flashy magic that anyone can understand is best.

And then, we draw close enough for the pirates to be visible.

“Are those ominous ones the cause of the food shortage?”

“Yeah. They are the ghost pirate crew. A group of undead that scatter miasma. Because of that miasma, the fish fled, and the mermaid country ended up with a food shortage.”

I answer Myule’s question.

“So they were here… Because of them, our country…”

Myule glares at the ghost pirates with resentment.

Naturally, she must have ten or twenty grudges against them.

However, unfortunately, if they fought properly, the mermaids would have had no chance of winning.

First, mermaids are generally low level. Since they are not a race meant for combat, their levels are abnormally low despite their long lifespans.

In addition, the undead have no consciousness, so \<Charming Song> does not work. At that point, it is almost checkmate.

“You may have grievances, but I will defeat them. I will not allow any complaints.”

“I understand…”

Causing unnecessary casualties among the mermaids would only leave a bad aftertaste.

It is best for me to quickly wipe them out.

“All right, let us annihilate them at once.”

“Um, how will you do it?”

“Simply. We will bombard them with magic from here.”

High firepower from long range. Simple, right?

“There is quite some distance, though…”

“No more questions. Watch quietly and you will understand.”

“Y-yes, understood.”

If I answered all of Myule’s questions, the day would be over.

I will have her understand only the process and the result, and overlook the logic.

Blue, whom I am riding, moves to the center. Leaf with Sakura moves to the right, and Maria, standing in midair with \<Barrier Arts>, moves to the left.

Once we take some distance, we activate magic simultaneously without chanting.

“‘Fireball’” x3

Well, you could call it a classic.

-GOOSH!!!-

Three enormous “Fireballs”, super-enhanced by \<Expanded Interpretation>, streak forward at tremendous speed and instantly blow ten pirate ships to smithereens.

The sheer firepower causes the sea around the impact points to evaporate, and surrounding water rushes in to fill the void.

After waiting a bit, by the time the sea calms, there is not even a trace left of the pirate fleet.

The wreckage of the ships is swallowed by the sea.

“A-ahgah…”

Myule’s face is pale with fear, and meaningless groans leak from her mouth.

Incidentally, something is leaking from her lower mouth as well. “Purify.”

Still, Myule’s reservoir had not emptied yet. Larger capacity than I expected.

Now then, since we have wiped out the ghost pirates, let us check the state of the sea afterward.

With the ghost pirates gone, the miasma polluting the sea dissipates. This kind of miasma disappears once the monster causing it is gone.

If contamination persists for a long time, like the case of the Undying King Sera fought in the At Confederation, ecosystems can collapse and take time to recover.

However, since this was short-term contamination in a fluid environment like the sea, it should quickly return to normal.

As I am thinking this, fish begin to swim in from outside the affected area.

“Myule, could you go into the sea and confirm that the fish are returning? Otherwise, we will never be able to complete the request.”

“I-I understand. Come to think of it, that is why I came along.”

I lower Myule into the sea and wait in the air for a while.

Myule swims around, confirming that fish have begun to return.

“Jin-san, it seems fine! It looks like the sea will return to normal!”

Myule shouts up to us.

“Then, can we say the request is complete?”

“Yes! Of course!”

When I ask, Myule answers with a beaming smile.

“All right, then this quest is successfully cleared.”

I nod in satisfaction.

If three ‘Fireballs’ can tame a large catch of mermaids, it is a bargain.

“Since we only fired magic from a distance, it is only natural that everyone is safe…”

“Well, that is true…”

This battle had zero danger since the enemy had no long-range attack methods.

The pirate ship cannons were rusted and unusable.

“As long as Jin-sama is safe, nothing could be better. Of course, the same goes for Sakura-sama.”

“Yes… Everyone being safe is best…”

Since “safe equals boring” tends to be the case, I cannot say I welcome it.

“Still, Master really is amazing.”

“Of course. He is my Master, after all!”

“Blue-chan really loves Master, doesn’t she?”

“W-well, yes.”

Blue blushes but does not deny it.

Even Leaf’s slightly vacant eyes make it obvious that Blue is completely smitten with me.

Vacant Leaf and lovestruck Blue. The phrasing is nice.

To report the quest completion and receive the reward, we head back to the mermaid country.

As before, the two dragonkin are sent back to the ship ahead of us.

As we approach the barrier entrance, about ten mermaids are exiting the barrier.

They are probably either the investigation team or the expedition force.

One mermaid (male) notices us and approaches.

“Myule, what happened? Did you forget something?”

“No. We simply returned because the cause of the food shortage has been resolved.”

“Huh?”

The mermaid (male) looks stunned by Myule’s reply.

Myule does not know this since she spent most of the travel time unconscious, but it has not even been an hour since we left the mermaid country.

“We have also confirmed that fish have begun to return. I believe the sea will soon return to normal.”

“I-is that true?”

“Yes. I understand it is hard to believe, but it is true.”

“You do not look like you are joking… Myule, go report to Her Majesty. We, the investigation team, will verify this.”

The mermaid (male) returns to the group and begins discussing their next steps.

They will likely head out to confirm the cause and the return of fish.

We enter the barrier through the gate and ask the guard mermaid to announce our audience with the queen.

Since preparations are needed, we swim leisurely toward the royal castle.

And then, once again, the audience chamber.

“Oh? You have already resolved the cause? Then what was the cause?”

“It was miasma emitted by undead. It dissolved into the sea and drove away the fish. We have exterminated the pirates, so there should be no more problem.”

I answer the queen’s question.

As I said during the first audience, since it is after the fact, it is fine to explain in detail.

“Myule, is what he says true?”

“Yes… As Jin-san said, we have confirmed the disappearance of the undead. I believe the fish will return in time.”

“Then that concludes our transaction.”

The queen nods in satisfaction.

Resolving a nation-threatening food shortage for twenty-five unwanted mermaid girls is a cheap deal.

We consider it cheap, and the queen also considers it cheap. This is truly a win-win relationship.

“Yes. It seems the investigation team has also begun confirmation. Shall we wait until they verify it?”

“No, there is no need. If Myule has confirmed it, there should be no issue. …You, bring the promised girls. Ah, do not let them enter the castle. Gather them in front of it.”

The queen gives instructions to what appears to be her attendants.

“I have no intention of letting the girls into the castle. You may take them from in front of the castle on your way out.”

“…Understood.”

I have my thoughts about how poorly the mermaid girls are treated, but there is nothing to gain by criticizing it here.

“One more thing, if I may?”

“Hmm, what is it?”

“In our previous deal, I believe we were granted the right to tour this country.”

“That is correct. Will you be sightseeing now?”

I shake my head.

“No, I would like to postpone that sightseeing. The country has not yet settled down, so I would like to come again once things are calmer. Would that be acceptable?”

To be honest, sightseeing a chaotic country has no meaning.

I would like to come back after the fish return and things settle.

“Indeed, in its current state, it would not be very interesting. Very well. I will inform the gatekeepers. You may sightsee the next time you come.”

“Thank you.”

Having completed our purpose, we thank the queen and leave the throne room.

In front of the castle stand twenty-five mermaid girls, looking rather listless.

“Please take good care of them. Truly, please.”

“Yeah, leave it to me.”

As expected, Myule likely has strong feelings toward the orphaned mermaid girls.

She pleads with me repeatedly.

I begin taming the mermaid girls.

“If you accept this, I will let you eat your fill of food.”

The mermaid girls are initially confused, but with this one line, they seem to make up their minds.

One after another, they are tamed by me.

I could tame them by force, but if possible, I want them to follow of their own will.

Thus, we leave the mermaid country together with twenty-five mermaid girls.

We teleport to the Estea Labyrinth with the twenty-five tamed mermaid girls.

More precisely, we returned via “Portal”, and the others were pulled over via “Summon.”

Using “Summon” by the lake on the fifty-second floor of the labyrinth, I drop the mermaid girls directly into the lake.

“Welcome home.” x many

“Yeah, I’m back. Could I leave the education of these girls to you right away?”

“Yes, please leave it to us.”

I entrust the education of the mermaids to the maids who greet us.

The plan is to give the mermaid girls maid training.

First, we will give them \<Transformation> and have them learn human form.

At last, my long-awaited mermaid maid squad pun is about to be completed.

…I know it is stupid.

With the cleanup regarding the mermaid country complete, we return to the ‘Queen Sakuya’.

“My homeland…?”

I explain the mermaid country to Leila, but she tilts her head.

It seems she cannot quite grasp a homeland she does not remember.

“Just think of it as a place where many of the same race as you live.”

“Then I might want to go… maybe.”

For Leila, who has never seen other mermaids besides Maple’s (mermaid form), the mermaid country must be an unknown world.

She also showed a sense of kinship with Maple’s mermaid form, so I am curious how she would react.

《Then Dora will go too!》

“Dora-oneechan, is that okay?”

《Yeah!》

“If Dora-oneechan is with me, I feel safe!”

Despite appearances, Dora is in the dependable big sister role for Leila. How heartwarming.

“But if you take Leila-chan to the mermaid country, would it not cause trouble over succession…?”

Sakura raises a concern regarding Leila’s homecoming.

“Of course it would if we took her as-is, so I plan to disguise her or something.”

“If that is the case, then it is fine…”

“At worst, even if it is discovered, as long as I am there, it will not be a problem.”

“…That is true… Jin-kun, even if there is trouble, you could resolve it by force, couldn’t you…”

“Sakura, the way you say that makes me sound like a brute… Though it is true that I have the power and authority to do so.”

Most disputes can be resolved with force, authority, and wealth. A truth.

“While we are at it, Sera, would you like to go sometime too?”

This time, Sera had no role at all.

She is completely a land combat unit, so it cannot be helped that she had no role in a sea field.

“I am not particularly inclined, but it might be good to see it once.”

“I will not force you. If you feel like it.”

“Yes, I will do that.”

Even Sera, who dislikes sinking into water, seems to want to see it at least once.

Several days after the events in the mermaid country.

As I leisurely dote on Dora in the cabin, one of the maids comes to report.

“We are scheduled to arrive at the Regalia Beastkin Kingdom around this evening.”

“All right.”

《Okay!》

It seems we will arrive at the Regalia Beastkin Kingdom today.

After the mermaid country, nothing particularly unusual happened.

No pirates came, the weather did not worsen, and no giant sea monsters attacked. …Boring.

A: If you wish, I can guide you to giant sea monsters.

That does interest me, but the charm is being attacked during the voyage.

Going out of my way to find them feels different.

A: Understood.

…Still, could you at least tell me what kind of monster it is?

A: Yes. We also sent scouting units to sea areas we were not planning to pass through, and during that, we discovered a monster called an island whale. It is about five kilometers long and constantly floats on the sea surface, making its back resemble an island. Its blowhole area is shaped like a mountain, and because it blows salt, it is called a sea mountain.

That sounds extremely interesting. I really want to go.

However, even if we went now, it would be difficult to fully enjoy it before reaching the Regalia Beastkin Kingdom.

It cannot be helped. Regrettable, but we will visit the island whale another time.

《Master, are we eating the whale? Is it tasty?》

Perhaps having heard the explanation from Alta, Dora asks such a thing.

“No, we are not eating it. We will play on top of the island whale.”

《That’s too bad…》

“Do you not want to play with me?”

《I love you!》

But is whale meat tasty?

I have heard it was served in school lunches before, and it seems it is still sold today, but I have never eaten it myself.

A: A maid has gone to secure it.

Fast! Too fast!

At this rate, whale meat will be on the dinner table tonight.

“You might get to eat whale meat soon.”

《Yay!》

“Yay!”

The one rejoicing along with Dora is Leila.

Seeing me play with Dora, Leila gradually lost her wariness, or rather her discomfort toward me, and now she lets herself be doted on alongside Dora.

She looks like a beautiful woman, but inside she is a little girl, so I am not doing anything problematic.

At first, she approached hesitantly after being invited by Dora, but now she actively comes over to be petted. It seems stroking her scales feels good.

“Leila, you play in the sea, but have you ever seen a whale?”

“What is a whale?”

“You were happy without even understanding it…?”

Well, that happens often with small children.

They do not understand the topic but match the reactions of those around them.

A: Leila plays only around this ship, so she should not have encountered a whale.

That makes sense.

“A whale is a really big fish that lives in the sea. Probably an edible fish.”

Yes, I understand that whales are mammals.

Explaining that to a little girl would be a hassle.

“Then Leila will catch one!”

“Oh right, you have \<Mermaid Princess>.”

Leila’s unique skill \<Mermaid Princess> allows her to command sea creatures.

Using that, she could easily capture a whale.

A: \<Mermaid Princess> does not work on higher-ranked beings. The whale is higher-ranked than Leila.

An unexpected fact is revealed. Whales are strong.

Leila has raised her level somewhat and undergone underwater combat training, but still…

“Leila cannot help Dora-oneechan…”

《There, there.》

Leila slumps, having been eager to please Dora but told it was impossible.

Dora comforts her.

“I decided! Leila will become stronger!”

《Do your best!》

“But if you want to level up, you will have to fight on land. There are fewer monsters in the sea.”

I feel bad for Leila, who has resolved to become stronger, but leveling up is far more efficient on land.

Mainly due to encounter rates.

“Ehh…”

And Leila is very bad at fighting on land.

《Do your best!》

“O-okay… I will try.”

However, being cheered on by Dora, she seems unable to refuse.

Well, asking a child who has only been walking on two legs for a few weeks to fight is quite a tall order.

If possible, I want her to at least be able to protect herself.

**AN:** The mermaid queen safely crossed the minefield.

It is rare to see an arrogant character who does not cross Jin’s unacceptable line. Incidentally, it is also rare for someone who becomes an enemy marker to survive without becoming a subordinate and exit the stage like this. There are plans for her to reappear.

There is no guarantee she will be safe when she does.
