# **149: Arrival in the Beastman Kingdom and the Crimson Princess**

**AN:** For various reasons, the island whale’s body length has been changed to 5 km. Ten kilometers was a bit inconvenient.

---

At last, we arrived in the Regalia Beastman Kingdom.

Since the sun was already starting to set, we planned to stay the night in the port town where we docked the ship, and then continue our journey from tomorrow.

The ones who came to welcome us in that port town were a dozen or so beastmen wearing butler and maid outfits.

“Welcome. We have been expecting you. Dragon Knight Gene-sama and your party. By order of Her Majesty Queen Sharon, we have been instructed to escort you, Gene-sama.”

Following the lead of the foremost butler, we were shown to the most luxurious hotel in the port town.

And, naturally, we were guided to the most luxurious room.

…This is VIP treatment!

“Phew. If we’ve come this far, it’s fine to take off the helmet, right?”

“Yes. I believe it should be all right.”

After confirming in the guided room that we could not be seen from outside, Sera and I removed our helmets.

“We only need disguises, but it’s tough for the two of you who have to wear helmets.”

“I’m really glad it’s just a disguise… I never want to wear that mask again…”

《Dora actually liked it, though…》

This time, aside from Sera and me, everyone else is disguised, as Mio said.

And those disguises are created by magical tools.

The previous disguise equipment, the “Mysterious Nobleman’s Mask”, was unpopular, so Sakuya prepared new ones. Sakura really hated it.

It only changes hair and eye color, but that is enough to significantly alter one’s impression, so it should be sufficient as a light disguise.

Incidentally, the dragonkin group is staying on the ship.

We have no intention of showing their human forms within this country.

“Keeping a helmet on would make eating difficult, after all.”

“I can eat ration balls. I toss them in when I’m a little hungry.”

“Only Sera and Scarlet can casually eat ration balls.”

Unless you possess the \<Proof of the Hero> skill like Sera and Scarlet, eating even one ration ball will make you completely full.

For ordinary people, it’s impossible to eat one just to satisfy a light hunger.

“If you like ration balls that much, should you just have ration balls for dinner, Sera? We’ll eat normally.”

“W-w-wait a moment! That’s too cruel!”

Sera shouted with tears in her eyes.

Being the only one eating bland ration balls in a luxury hotel.

That hurts.

For dinner, we had the food brought to our room, like room service.

You can probably guess that the purpose was to eat without showing our faces, but it seems Sharon’s orders were thorough, as the hotel suggested this before we said anything.

“As expected of a port town, there’s a lot of seafood. And the fact that it looks boneless is a big plus. Yeah, it’s good.”

“Yes, Master does dislike fish bones. Certainly, a high-class hotel wouldn’t make guests remove bones themselves.”

As Mio said, for someone like me who hates removing fish bones, the consideration shown by a luxury hotel feels very comfortable.

Incidentally, what I put into my mouth was red-fleshed sashimi. Sashimi seems to be a rather rare culture, but did it come via the Hero? Or is it native to the beastman country?

“Still, we had a lot of seafood on the ship too, so I can’t deny that I’m getting a bit tired of it.”

《Fish is tasty, though?》

“No, of course it’s tasty.”

Just because something is tasty doesn’t mean you never get tired of it.

“Jin-sama, shall I take out food from the \<Infinite Storage>?”

“No, I wouldn’t go that far…”

I stop Maria as she tries to bring out different dishes.

Maria tends to overreact the moment she sees an opening.

“We’ll be heading inland from tomorrow, so I think there will be fewer fish dishes.”

“That’s true. This much fish is probably because it’s a port town. Since we came by ship, I guess it’s inevitable…”

As I was nodding in agreement, Mio stopped me.

“Master, wait a second. Normally, people who arrive by passenger ship wouldn’t be eating fish continuously, you know? On normal passenger ships, they eat food that was loaded in advance. It’s unlikely that all of that food would be biased toward fish. Our ship is the strange one for acting like a fishing boat despite being a passenger ship.”

“That’s true… Normal passenger ships wouldn’t procure food locally, would they…”

“In that sense, it is convenient. Though it doesn’t feel very passenger-ship-like…”

The “Queen Sakuya” is a luxury cruise ship, but also a luxury fishing boat.

…What even is a luxury fishing boat?

“And probably, if we’d asked, they would have served non-fish dishes too. I checked the map, and they have normal ingredients available… They probably wanted you to try the fish of this country. They wouldn’t have thought you’d already been catching and eating fish on the ship.”

“Seriously… So it was just normal consideration… We did something abnormal, and complained about normal consideration. That wouldn’t be right. All right, let’s accept it gratefully.”

If they were responding appropriately, we shouldn’t complain.

Let’s say nothing unnecessary and savor the food.

“By the way, what will the maids be doing now?”

I said I wouldn’t say unnecessary things, but I didn’t say I wouldn’t talk during meals.

Only now did I start thinking about the maids, and the “Queen Sakuya”.

Come to think of it, I don’t think we talked at all about what would happen after they delivered us.

“To conceal the ‘Portal’, the ‘Queen Sakuya’ will remain docked at this port. Management will be handled responsibly by the Regalia Beastman Kingdom, so some of the maids will remain on the ship, while the others will apparently go sightseeing in this country.”

The one who answered my question was Maria, who is in close communication with the believers.

“Sightseeing by the maids, huh… They won’t just be sightseeing normally, will they? There’s no way the maids would do something that doesn’t benefit Master…”

“They’ll probably increase the number of maids. And also set up ‘Portals’.”

Mio and Sera also seem to understand the true meaning of Maria’s “sightseeing”.

Most likely, the maids objectives are visiting slave traders and setting up ‘Portals’. Depending on the situation, they might also consider establishing a branch of the Advance Company.

If I say I like it, a branch will be established with high probability.

“Well, it sounds like we don’t need to worry about the ship or the maids. And after the talks are over, we can return to this port.”

“Yes. If Jin-sama does not desire to travel by ship, I think you could return immediately via ‘Portal’ after coming back to the ship.”

“If we have nothing planned, returning by ship might be nice too.”

A leisurely ship journey both coming and going isn’t bad.

In most cases, the standard is normal travel on the way there, and ‘Portal’ on the way back…

Huh? You say the trip here wasn’t leisurely to begin with? Ha ha ha.

The day after arriving in the Regalia Beastman Kingdom.

We left the hotel and returned briefly to the “Queen Sakuya”.

We came to pick up the dragonkin girls, who would serve as our means of transportation.

“Sorry for not taking you to the hotel yesterday.”

“It’s fine. Even if we went into a human inn, we’d just get mentally tired anyway…”

When I spoke to them in the room where the dragonkin girls were staying, Blue, in her human form, replied with a happy smile.

“Sorry. We can’t have you in human form from now on, so I think it will be inconvenient for you, but please bear with us.”

“I told you not to worry about it. More importantly, what’s important to me is that Master rides on me.”

Within the Regalia Beastman Kingdom, we intend for them to remain in dragon form at all times, and not publicly reveal that they are dragonkin.

They will be treated as riding dragons, in other words, not as humans, but Blue doesn’t mind at all.

“Blue-chan is right. Please don’t worry about us!”

Leaf seems to share the same opinion.

“Yes. This time, we will be accompanying you as riding dragons, after all. We were prepared for that from the start. Though the downgrade in meal quality is a little… No, quite disappointing…”

Come to think of it, Mikazuki was tamed by me because she lost to her appetite.

Despite her appearance as a beautiful older sister type, she’s one of the perpetually hungry characters.

Being treated as a riding dragon means there’s a high chance she won’t be able to eat proper meals, so it seems she had some internal conflict.

“Well then, let’s depart right away.”

When I declared that, Blue and the others began busily removing their clothes.

Their clothes would tear when they transform into dragon form, so it can’t be helped.

And so, I head through the ship with the three of them, now naked except for a single towel each.

We’ll depart from the small boat access point used for fishing. We can’t exactly transform and take off openly on the deck.

Near the small boat access point, the dragonkin girls change into dragon form.

The towels flutter down.

I caught a glimpse just for an instant before the transformation! …If I asked, they’d probably show me anytime, but situations like this are important.

After the three transformed, Maria and I rode on Blue, Sakura and Dora rode on Leaf, and Sera and Mio rode on Mikazuki.

Sera is using ‘Float’ to reduce her weight. It’s not that she couldn’t ride without it, but she uses it at her own request.

Sera and I are in knight attire, but the other members are in maid outfits. Since riding in skirts would be difficult, they’re wearing pants that look like skirts.

In Sakura and Dora’s pairing, there’s no one in knight attire, but we’re planning to push through with the explanation that they’re maids who can ride dragons. …Will that be all right?

“Please have a safe journey, Master” x many

Naturally, many maids have come to see us off.

“Yeah, I’m off.”

“All right, let’s go. Hold on tight.”

After saying that, Blue began flapping her wings and took off into the sky in an instant.

Leaf and Mikazuki followed behind.

Since there’s too much difference in their maximum flight speeds, Blue has slowed down considerably, allowing the other two to keep up with ease.

“This direction is fine, right?”

I nod in response to Blue’s question.

“Yeah, just keep going straight. There’s no need to hurry, so I plan to stop at a suitable town and rest after we’ve made some progress today. Sightseeing.”

“Again? Master really does that a lot.”

“It’s my hobby.”

“Thanks to that hobby, you ride on me sometimes, so it’s not a bad thing for me.”

Blue really seems to love flying through the sky with me.

I also prefer riding on Blue to flying myself with the ‘Wings of the Undead.’

“I’ve been told about some towns suitable for sightseeing, so I’m thinking of choosing one of those.”

“Let me know when you decide, okay?”

“Yeah, got it.”

“Jin-sama, please inform me as well. I will check the details in advance.”

“That’s fine, but…”

Even if Maria doesn’t do it, Alta probably will…

A: It’s a careful multi-layered check. It offers unexpected perspectives, so it’s quite useful. The information is passed to the maids at the base, and they also verify it.

Isn’t that… a bit too careful?

About an hour has passed since we started flying.

《Whenever I travel like this, something usually happens, doesn’t it?》

Since my voice wouldn’t reach other dragonkin during flight, I use party telepathy to speak to everyone.

《Now that you mention it, that’s true. Well, you could call it a template, I guess…》

《Tempura?》

《Dora-chan. Close, but not quite. …Could it be that you’re hungry?》

《A little…》

It’s still a bit before noon, but Dora seems to be getting hungry.

《So Jin-sama, are you going to save her?》

As you can tell from Maria’s line, this event is a “woman in distress”.

As Mio said, it’s a template if you call it one.

《Yeah. It’s not like we have no connection. If she asks for help, we’ll help her. Sera, could you go and call out to her in my place?》

《Of course I can, but you’re not going yourself this time?》

She seems to find it strange that I’m leaving it to Sera instead of going myself.

《Yeah. Technically, the top of this group is ‘Queen’s Knight Gene’. Wouldn’t it be more natural to stand firm at first and leave it to subordinates? That gives a sense of importance.》

《No, with the mobility to go almost single-handedly to a distant foreign country, there’s no sense of being imposing or important at this point… Hey! That’s terrible…》

《Um… Something feels wet, though…》

Since Mio cut me down so bluntly, I carry out a light retaliation. Mikazuki gets caught in the crossfire.

《We don’t have much time, so I’ll be going now.》

《Yeah, I’m counting on you.》

Mikazuki, carrying Sera, flew off toward the woman in distress.

We’ll approach slowly.

Incidentally, this is the status of the “woman in distress.”

Name: Strawberry Crimson

Gender: Female

Age: 17

Race: Human

Title: Crimson Empire Imperial Princess

She’s an Imperial Princess of the Crimson Empire, meaning she’s a relative of Rouge and Scarlet.

That counts as a connection, right?

Now then, let me briefly explain the princess’s current situation.

1. The suspension bridge on the cliff has collapsed.

2. She’s holding onto a rope with her right hand.

3. With her left hand, she’s holding onto what appears to be her attendant maid.

4. Below the cliff, a horse that must have fallen earlier lies dead, and the carriage is completely wrecked.

See? A dire situation, right?

Judging from her status, Princess Strawberry alone could probably climb the rope.

However, climbing the rope while holding onto the maid is impossible. Furthermore, the maid lacks the status to reach the rope on her own from that position. In other words, the maid’s death is guaranteed.

If nothing is done, it comes down to two choices: Princess Strawberry abandons the maid and lets go, or they both fall and die together.

《Master, she says she wants to be saved. She says she’ll pay a reward.》

《Well, that’s to be expected. Sera, save her.》

《Understood.》

Mikazuki moved beneath the maid, and Sera received the maid who was about to fall.

The moment the maid was gone, Princess Strawberry easily climbed up the rope.

As expected of Scarlet’s relative, she has something special.

Rouge? Her \<Experience Gained Increase> skill must be shining brightly, right?

While Sera was lowering the maid, we also landed on the ground.

The maid seems to have reached the limits of her stamina, collapsing on the spot and lying there limply, but Princess Strawberry still seems to have plenty of energy, and she walks toward us.

Princess Strawberry has pale crimson hair styled in vertical curls, and is wearing a deep red dress. …It’s been a while since I’ve seen vertical curls.

“Please excuse my appearance. Thank you very much for saving us. The fact that the two of us are unharmed is thanks to you.”

“I’m glad you are safe. If you don’t mind, may I ask your name?”

Having imagined a haughty character due to the vertical curls, I actually felt a sense of dissonance at her polite thanks. You shouldn’t judge people by their appearance.

Still, I think vertical curls have too strong an image.

Incidentally, by saying “my appearance”, she is likely referring to the fact that her dress is torn in places, probably from being caught when she fell from the cliff.

“I apologize for the late introduction. I am Strawberry Crimson, Second Imperial Princess of the Crimson Empire.”

“An imperial princess of the Crimson Empire. I am Sara, a knight of the Castal Kingdom.”

Sara is Sera’s alias. Since we’re in disguise, everyone will be using aliases.

“A Castal knight who rides a dragon other than a Wyvern… Could it be that you are the party of Gene-sama, the Queen’s Knight of the Castal Kingdom?”

“You know of us? Yes, that is correct. He is Gene.”

Sera said that as she introduced me.

So much for standing firm.

“Pleased to meet you. I am Gene, a Queen’s Knight of the Castal Kingdom.”

“I have heard about you from my father. That you are very strong. It left a strong impression on me, because it was the first time I had ever seen my father praise someone without reservation.”

“Your father?”

Who is she referring to?

“Yes, my father is Scarlet Crimson. You met him in the Elgant Theocracy, did you not?”

Princess Strawberry is Scarlet’s daughter!?

Um, Scarlet is 34, and her younger sister Rouge is 22, so I assumed she was another sister, but she was a daughter?

So the previous emperor wasn’t the one who worked hard.

“Yes, I did me–“

“Wait just a moment! What do you think you’re doing, not even removing your helmet before a princess of a nation?!”

The one who interrupted was the maid who had been lying limply until just a moment ago.

She’s 15 years old, a girl with slightly sharp eyes and chestnut-colored short bob hair, giving off a somewhat harsh impression.

“Milfy, I do not mind such things.”

“But, my lady! Allowing such rudeness would stain the name of the Crimson Empire!”

Milfy is the maid girl’s name.

Strawberry and mille-feuille. My mouth is starting to feel sweet.

Huh? Tiramisu, maple, chocolat? Ha ha ha.

“They are our saviors. Is it not also improper to order them to remove their helmets from such a superior position?”

“And besides, Gene-sama did not show his face even at the Elgant Theocracy’s summit conference, where the leaders of all nations gathered. If there is a reason he does not wish to show his face, you must not make unreasonable demands.”

“But–“

-Gon!-

“Gup!”

Princess Strawberry’s answer to Milfy’s continued resistance was a knuckle strike.

After a very nice sound, Milfy crouched down silently, holding her head.

“My attendant was rude.”

“Is that all right?”

“Yes. She is stubborn, so this is the best way to make her behave.”

A stubborn maid feels like a lot of things are wrong with that…

Also, as expected of Scarlet’s daughter, she’s a martial type. She didn’t hesitate at all to punch her.

“Milfy, say you’re sorry.”

“…I-I am very sorry.”

Milfy apologizes with tearful eyes from the pain of being hit.

Judging from her status, a martial imperial princess’s knuckle strike is effective on an ordinary person like Milfy.

“I don’t mind. It is true that hiding one’s face is rude.”

“I’m glad to hear you say that.”

Not that I have any intention of stopping just because it’s rude, though…

“By the way, Gene-sama, what brings you to such a place?”

This isn’t something we need to hide, so I’ll answer.

“We were invited by Her Majesty Queen Sharon of the Regalia Beastman Kingdom, and are on our way to the royal capital.”

“Oh my, is that so. I’ve heard rumors that Queen Sharon also favors strong individuals.”

“Then may I ask why Lady Strawberry is in this country, if you don’t mind?”

“Yes, I don’t mind. It is to apologize for an incident in which my father caused harm to Lady Sharon in the Elgant Theocracy.”

Come to think of it, something like that did happen.

The incident where Scarlet interrupted Sharon and the Shippouin during their mock battle.

“It would be improper for my father himself to go, so I have been sent as his representative.”

“Just the two of you?”

It’s one thing for an imperial princess to go as a representative, but having only one maid as an attendant seems questionable.

Not in terms of combat strength, but in terms of personal care and negotiations.

“Yes. For most opponents, I alone would be sufficient. I actually intended to go alone, but…”

Indeed, with Princess Strawberry’s status, there would be no problem unless something extraordinary happened.

If there were an opponent she couldn’t defeat, escorts would be mostly meaningless anyway.

“That would not be permitted, so I ended up accompanying her as a maid.”

Milfy says with a composed face.

“Oh? Wasn’t it Milfy who threw a tantrum and insisted on coming because she wanted to go to a foreign country?”

“O-Ojou-sama! You mustn’t say that!”

Milfy’s composed face crumbles.

It seems Princess Strawberry and Milfy have quite a close relationship.

Given that she didn’t let go even when about to fall off the cliff, and that she casually punched her, it’s easy to imagine…

“Milfy may be dressed as a maid, but she is actually my younger sister.”

Princess Strawberry explained before I asked.

“Sis– Strawberry-sama! No! That’s not correct! I am not your sister! I am not permitted to bear the Crimson name!”

“You share the same father, do you not? Then you are my sister.”

So she’s a half-sister. Probably something to do with their mothers’ status.

Even so, Princess Strawberry said she was the Second Imperial Princess, so Scarlet has at least three children.

Well, he’s royalty, so that might be normal.

“By the way, if you include children in similar positions to Milfy, we are a family of twenty siblings.”

That was far more than I expected.

Scarlet-san, you worked too hard!

“So if, at worst, the two of us were to die, it would cause no significant pain to the Crimson Empire. That is why I was sent to apologize this time, as a representative of my irreplaceable father.”

I doubt it would cause no pain at all, but…

However, while I understand Princess Strawberry’s explanation, there’s something that bothers me.

“By the way, why did you try to cross the suspension bridge with a carriage?”

Judging from the remains of the suspension bridge, it didn’t look very sturdy.

If they hadn’t tried to cross it with a carriage, it probably wouldn’t have broken. Also, there was a sturdier bridge several kilometers away, so they could have used that.

Why take such a risk to cross a flimsy suspension bridge?

“Huh? Was there some problem?”

“The bridge collapsed because we were unlucky, right?”

They don’t understand at all…

“No, crossing such a flimsy suspension bridge with a carriage is dangerous. It wouldn’t be strange for it to break.”

“Oh, is that so? Since it was a bridge, I thought it could handle at least a carriage. Milfy, did you understand?”

“No, it did not occur to me. That explains why they recommended we take a detour in the previous town.”

“Ah, so that was what the danger referred to. I thought it meant there might be bandits…”

Hey, who was it that allowed a sheltered two-person journey like this?!

“I thought we could manage bandits, but if the suspension bridge collapsed, there was nothing we could do. I was barely able to grab Milfy’s hand, but…”

“The carriage fell into the ravine. The luggage was in an item box, so that’s not a problem, but moving forward from here will be difficult…”

Unfortunately, the distance from this cliff to another town is quite long.

A road that would be trivial by carriage would be extremely harsh on foot through these mountains. It might take more than a few days.

“Gene-sama, this is a shameless request from someone you have already saved, but could you take us to a nearby town? Of course, I will provide compensation separate from the reward for saving us.”

Well, I could imagine such a request coming.

“Lady Strawberry, wouldn’t it be better to take us all the way to the royal capital?”

Oh! Milfy is even more shameless!

“Milfy, that would be far too convenient. There is a limit to the trouble we can impose on Gene-sama. Or are you telling me to be shameless?”

“…Lady Strawberry, I am sorry.”

Milfy apologizes to Princess Strawberry, then turns back toward me.

“Gene-sama, please forgive my earlier rudeness. And would you please take us to a nearby town?”

If someone apologizes sincerely and makes a polite request, I can’t just brush it aside.

If it were “to the royal capital”, I’d refuse without hesitation, but “to a nearby town” isn’t that unreasonable.

“Very well. I will take you to a nearby town.”

“Thank you very much.”

“Thank you.”

Knight Gene is a gentleman who is kind to women.

He kicked women in the Eldia War? Enemies and obstacles are different.

And so, Princess Strawberry rode with me on Blue, while Milfy rode with Sera on Mikazuki.

“This view is amazing. My father’s riding dragon, Kuroa, won’t let anyone but my father ride…”

Scarlet’s riding dragon would be the black dragonkin who was at the summit conference.

So its name is Kuroa now. I think its real name was something like Yoiyami?

A: Yes. That is correct.

Like Dora, it is a stray dragonkin, but it seems to have lost its memory.

I don’t know the circumstances, but it must be under Scarlet’s protection.

I heard about it in the “Dragonkin Hidden Land”, but Yoiyami’s family was killed by a dragon that attacked the hidden land, leaving no one behind.

If it’s living happily under Scarlet, there’s no need to forcibly take it away.

“Will these ones also take on human forms…”

To Princess Strawberry’s muttered words, I replied only in my heart, “They will.”

After about ten minutes of flight, we arrived at a nearby town.

What would take days on foot is over in an instant for dragonkin.

It’s a moderately sized town, with a population of several tens of thousands.

We couldn’t land in the middle of town, so we landed on the road near the town.

“Gene-sama, thank you very much.”

“Thank you.”

Princess Strawberry and Milfy bow their heads.

“No, please don’t worry about it. I have received proper compensation.”

As promised, I have received a reward from Princess Strawberry.

Since it’s an apology to the Regalia Beastman Kingdom, it seems she brought considerable treasures.

Among them were magical tools, which I accepted without hesitation.

“What will Gene-sama and the others do next?”

“…Let’s see. Since we’re here anyway, I think we’ll have lunch in this town.”

Passing through a town we came all this way to would be a waste.

We’ll have a meal here, and then think about what to do next.

Since it’s still around midday, we could continue on to the next town if we wanted, and it’s not a journey that requires haste, so staying overnight in this town is also an option. We can act according to how we feel at the time.

Incidentally, Princess Strawberry and the others will need to arrange a carriage in town, and depending on how things go, they may have to stay in this town for several days.

“Then, shall we have lunch together… Ah… Never mind.”

“…”

Princess Strawberry seems to have realized mid-sentence.

Since I hide my face with a helmet, I can only eat in private rooms.

In other words, eating together is impossible.

Alta, could you find a place to eat with private rooms?

A: It has already been confirmed. There are over ten such places, so if you tell me your preferences, I will pick suitable ones.

Phew… There seem to be quite a few places where we can eat in private rooms.

We entered the town together, but since our objectives differed from there, we parted ways with Princess Strawberry.

Incidentally, the three dragonkin girls, Blue and the others, were entrusted to the stable for carriage horses at the town entrance. Showing Sharon’s permit was enough.

Given the Queen’s permission, I’d like to believe no one would harbor ill intentions. Even if they did, it would just end with those ill-intentioned people dying…

“Then, if fate permits, let us meet again.”

“Yes. Farewell.”

After raising such obvious event flags, I doubt we’ll never meet again… We’ll definitely meet again…

After parting with Princess Strawberry and the others, we also began walking through the town to get lunch.

“Since we’re here, I’d like a place with menus that feel like the beastman kingdom. Alta found places where we can eat in private rooms.”

Enjoying local cuisine is the essence of sightseeing.

There may be differences between regions, but first, I want to eat food that feels like the beastman kingdom. The port town was mainly seafood, which felt less beastman-like.

Apparently, crops grown in the Regalia Beastman Kingdom are tastier than those grown elsewhere.

Additionally, livestock raised on good feed also tastes better, so as a result, both meat and vegetables are delicious in this land.

《Yay!》

“I’m looking forward to it.”

“The beastman kingdom, huh. I wonder what kind of seasoning they use?”

Following Alta’s directions, we enter a slightly upscale-looking restaurant.

Using a private room requires a usage fee, but it’s not a large amount, so we reserve one without hesitation.

“I see. So this is beastman kingdom style…”

Looking at the menu handed to us, I nod in understanding while also being surprised by its extremity.

“Hmm, it seems they don’t know the words nutritional balance. It’s either meat or vegetables…”

It’s no wonder Mio, a cook, frowns.

The menu was a choice between vegetable dishes (no meat) or meat dishes (no vegetables).

“Probably for carnivorous beastmen and herbivorous beastmen.”

“In other countries, there are many beastmen who eat normal dishes, so it’s not that they can’t eat a mix of meat and vegetables.”

If Sera, who has eaten in many places, says so, it must be true.

“I’ve also heard from beastmen, but even if they can eat it, they are somewhat influenced by the preferences of their original animals. And since there are many beastmen in this country, the restaurants probably adapted their menus to those preferences.”

“I see. If the majority of the population is beastmen, then even such a biased menu wouldn’t be a problem. …How about you, Maria? Do you have any beastman-specific episodes from your diet?”

At the estate, there are other beastman subordinates, but Maria is the one I can ask readily.

“None in particular. I lived in a human village, so I ate the same things as humans.”

Incidentally, it seems cats overseas are strictly carnivorous, while Japanese cats have evolved into omnivores.

I once had a cat… Well, I took care of one, and researched it at that time.

If we investigated whether cats (beastmen) in this world are carnivorous or omnivorous, we might be able to tell whether this world is Japan or overseas. Saying this world is Japan sounds strange.

“I’m not very fond of sour things, though…”

“It’s hard to tell whether that’s because you’re a cat beastman or just a personal preference…”

Cats are said to dislike citrus fruits, but what about cat beastmen?

There are plenty of people who just don’t like sour things.

《Master, I’m hungry.》

“Oh, sorry. Let’s order quickly.”

Since Dora complained of hunger, we quickly placed our orders.

Perhaps because there are many dishes with few preparation steps, the food was brought out relatively quickly.

《Looks tasty!》

“It really feels like meat.”

Dora and Sera ordered meat dishes. Very straightforwardly, steaks were brought out.

Perhaps because the Regalia Beastman Kingdom is rich in food, even large steaks were reasonably priced.

“I can’t finish that much meat…”

“Same here. Mio-chan eats small portions…”

Sakura and Mio ordered vegetable dishes, vegetable stir-fries without meat.

Since there are also unprepared raw vegetables, there weren’t many easy-to-eat options among the vegetable dishes.

“It looks good, but it’s a bit disappointing that there’s no staple food.”

“I’ll ask the staff if bringing our own is allowed.”

Maria goes after the staff member who brought the food.

Maria and I decided to split the meat and vegetable dishes between us. If we want to eat both meat and vegetables, that’s the only option.

“I asked. It’s fine for private room guests.”

“Then, without hesitation, rice!”

Saying that, I take out bowls of rice from the \<Infinite Storage>.

Yeah, it’s surreal.

The food is tasty, but the meat dishes were quite strongly seasoned.

To the extent that Sakura and Mio, who each took just one bite of the meat dish, didn’t ask for a second bite.

“Too many spices! It ruins the good ingredients!”

Apparently.

**AN:** The food culture of the beastman kingdom has a wild image.

The \<Proof of the Hero> has an additional effect that makes it easier to have children.

Bearing children is also a hero’s job.

Please look forward to Volume 12, the Crimson Empire Arc (tentative)!
