# **150: The Eight Vassal Beasts and the Ninja**

**AN:** This chapter has a bit of an explanatory bent. Yeah. Extremely late.

---

It’s sudden, but I think I will explain about beastkin.

Beastkin are a staple of fiction, but since interpretations vary widely depending on the work, let us clarify how beastkin are understood in this world.

First, beastkin in this world basically possess the traits of a single animal.

In Maria’s case, a cat… though I am not that knowledgeable about cat breeds, so I do not know exactly what kind. Ah, the beastkin girl in the adventurer group is easy to understand. She is clearly a golden retriever dog.

What is important is that they are “humans with animal traits (ears and tails)”, not “animals that walk on two legs”.

And there is no individual variation in how these traits appear. If someone is a cat beastkin, then they have both ears and a tail.

Only when using the skill \<Beast Transformation> does the entire body (the proportion of beast can be adjusted to some degree) transform into that animal.

Even if a small-animal beastkin uses \<Beast Transformation>, their size remains close to their human form. In other words, when transformed, it is hard to tell the difference between a tiger cat beastkin and a tiger beastkin.

Also, the animals that serve as the basis for these traits are limited to land-based mammals. There are no bird, fish, or reptile beastkin. Harpies, mermaids, and lizardmen (they actually exist) are treated as monsters, so that is a different story.

Furthermore, even among land-based mammals, there are no beastkin of animals with hard outer bodies. Examples include elephants, rhinos, and hippos. I do not know the reason. They are not fluffy, so I am not interested.

Because they possess animal traits, their physical abilities are generally higher than those of humans.

On the other hand, it is easy to understand that many of them are poor at thinking things through. For better or worse, they are probably being pulled along by animal instincts. There are many muscle-brained types.

As a race, it is not that they are unsuited to it, but there are extremely few who can use magic.

Since status talk and \<Beast Transformation> came up, a brief aside.

For example, if a wolf and a wolf beastkin using \<Beast Transformation> were to fight, and they were in the same level range and status range, the wolf beastkin would win.

That is because it is not simply a beastkin turning into a beast, but rather a change in form as one method of status enhancement.

Maria is abnormal in that she has high physical ability, learns quickly, is dexterous, and can also use magic.

When you list it out like this, you can clearly see that Maria’s specs are quite high. Yet, why does she not really give that impression?

…Ah, because her impression as a believer is far too strong.

This is not limited to beastkin, but among the human-type races (humans, beastkin, elves, and other races treated as people), they can have children together.

The child’s race will basically be the same as the mother’s (in the case of beastkin, the animal traits are also inherited).

However, in rare cases, the child will be the same race as the father, but there is no atavistic inheritance.

This trait is widely known, and if by bad luck a child of a different race from both parents is born, the mother’s infidelity is immediately exposed. Apparently, it happens fairly often.

Also, only in the case of elves, if the mother is an elf, a half-elf is born.

Incidentally, beastkin do not have a mating season… no, like humans, they are in season year-round.

Their lifespan is about the same as humans, but their growth during childhood is slightly faster.

Perhaps it is more accurate to say that they become adults more quickly.

Basically, compared to humans, animals have a shorter period until they become fully grown. Animal living environments are full of danger, so if they do not become adults quickly, the chances of being killed increase.

Humans, who take over ten years to reach adulthood, are the strange ones.

Beastkin also possess animal traits, so their growth is slightly faster. And yet, they also age more slowly, so it is no wonder that humans find this enviable.

Even if beastkin grow quickly, there are individual differences.

Additionally, differences also arise depending on the living environment, so it is not an absolute rule.

Maria and Coco grew up poor, so their development was not very good.

After becoming my subordinates, their diets improved, and the two of them have been growing rapidly, as if making up for lost time. Their chests as well.

Maria’s current appearance would probably correspond to that of a fourteen-year-old human beauty. For beastkin, she is already a fully grown adult.

I have gone on at length, but what I really want to say is…

“Bet her freedom and duel me!”

In other words, things like this can happen.

The duel event that everyone knows. Of course, the thing being wagered is Maria.

The incident began around the time we stopped for lunch in the town where we delivered Princess Strawberry.

This was not a rushed journey, so we decided to stay one night in this town. Following Alta’s instructions, we made sure to secure lodgings for the night while the sun was still high.

We had arrived in the town without much thought, but it seemed to be a transportation hub, and there were more people than expected.

If you have a desired inn, it is best to secure it early.

Since I do hold the position of a knight of a country, we selected a fairly high-class inn, but unfortunately, that seems to have been a mistake.

As we were walking along the main street toward the inn, one gentle-looking man approached us.

I probably do not need to say it, but this guy is the duel opponent (tentative).

Since an unknown person approached, Maria (expressionless) stopped in her tracks.

Seeing Maria like that, the gentle-looking man must have mistaken it for interest in him, as he offered a soft smile and held out his hand to Maria.

“Lovely young lady, would you care to have some tea with me?”

The one who tried to pick her up with a line straight out of a template was a beastkin with yellowish brown hair grown to his shoulders.

Checking his status, he seems to be a jackal beastkin. And surprisingly strong.

Still, to think he would try to hit on a maid (Maria) who is with people wearing knight armor (me and Sera)… he is quite the challenger.

Unfortunately, I can only say that he picked the wrong opponent.

“I refuse.”

Maria firmly declined and started walking again.

Left behind was only the gentle-looking man, frozen in place with his hand still outstretched.

“W-wait a moment!”

The rebooted gentle-looking man moved at a speed too fast to follow with the eye and blocked our path.

Everyone knows \<Shukuchi>. Using \<Shukuchi> now, of all times…

“Miss, although the ‘Eight Vassal Beasts’ hold noble rank, I myself was originally a commoner. There is no need to be reserved out of concern for appearances.”

The gentle-looking man says this while striking a needlessly cool pose.

Alta!

A: ‘Eight Vassal Beasts’ is one of the noble titles of the Regalia Beastkin Kingdom, granted to the eight beastkin considered the strongest in the country. Because even commoners can become ‘Eight Vassal Beasts’ if they are strong, the title is especially popular in the Regalia Beastkin Kingdom, which values strength.

Ah, so that is why the surrounding beastkin are looking at him with eyes of admiration.

Ah, so that is why the gentle-looking man is misunderstanding himself as an object of admiration.

A: Incidentally, the sheep beastkin secretary who was with Sharon in the Elgant Theocracy also held the same ‘Eight Vassal Beasts’ title.

Is that so?

There were so many outrageous people in the Elgant Theocracy that a slightly rare title did not surprise me at all. It probably did not even register.

A: They also possessed a unique-class skill, just in case.

I was probably only paying attention to Sharon standing next to them at the time.

If even a unique skill did not catch my eye…

Now that I think about it, ‘Eight Vassal Beasts’ sounds like the kind of title given to some pompous group in manga. The kind that shows up when they cannot use ‘Four Heavenly Kings’ because of the number.

Ah, the demon race used the ‘Four Heavenly Kings’ template. I can give them credit for that.

“No, it is not a matter of being reserved. I truly am fine.”

There was a bit of sharpness in Maria’s words.

It was probably because he was standing in front of me, blocking my way.

However, it seems true that this gentle-looking man is a famous person, as beastkin gradually begin to gather around us.

“How modest. But if modesty goes too far, it becomes sarcasm.”

Ah, the type of beastkin who does not listen.

The fact that someone like this holds a noble rank lowers my evaluation of the Regalia Beastkin Kingdom a bit.

“Such a lovely lady as yourself is unsuited to a lowly job like being a human maid. Quit it at once and enjoy tea with me. If you come to my estate, you can live a far better life than you do now… hm, what was that killing intent just now!”

Receiving the killing intent released by Maria, the gentle-looking man instantly reached for the dagger at his waist.

At this point, it was confirmed that he has no eye for things.

Once again, my evaluation of the Regalia Beastkin Kingdom dropped.

He seems to have eyes so bad that he cannot recognize the quality of our equipment, nor our strength.

…This is one of the eight strongest in the country? You have got to be kidding me…

“Hey now, just because the girl you were with fell for me, it is not good to be jealous like that. Leaking killing intent like that is unsightly. Haha, but I am generous, so I will forgive you. Come on, I have no business with you, so you should hurry up and go somewhere else.”

On top of that, he has mistaken the source of the killing intent as me.

That killing intent came from the girl you just called ‘lovely young lady’.

For the third time, my evaluation of the Regalia Beastkin Kingdom dropped.

“Haa…”

I could not help but sigh.

To have someone with such a grand title as ‘Eight Vassal Beasts’ be like this is deeply disappointing.

If he were the weakest among the Four Heavenly Kings type of position, there might be some saving grace.

Can I hope for the other seven?

“What is it? Why the sigh? Do you have some complaint?”

“I do not know about ‘Eight Vassal Beasts’ or whatever, but is it not uncool to keep pestering someone after being rejected?”

“…What are you saying? There is no way I could be rejected by a beastkin girl.”

The atmosphere of the gentle-looking man changes as he glares at me. …Pathetic killing intent.

“I am the seventh seat of the ‘Eight Vassal Beasts’. There is no beastkin woman in this country who dislikes me.”

“Second from the bottom, then. So that means you are less popular than the six above you, right?”

“Y-you really say that. Even for magnanimous me, there are l-limits, you know?”

The gentle-looking man says this with his cheek twitching.

“Maria, tell him honestly.”

“I am sorry, but to be perfectly clear, you are a nuisance.”

“Guha!?”

Maria’s finishing blow strikes the gentle-looking man.

“Ku, I see. So you are the one making her say such cruel things. Because she is usually oppressed, she cannot be honest with her heart in front of you. How pitiful… This is why humans are…”

Listening to him, I notice that he keeps making remarks that look down on humans.

But this country does not exactly lack humans, does it…?

Huh?

“I will not forgive scum like you!”

Saying that, the gentle-looking man draws his dagger.

Are you sure?

“Bet her freedom and duel me!”

– Crack! –

The next moment, the gentle-looking man’s neck rotated one hundred and eighty degrees on the spot. Simply put, his head ended up facing downward, with his jaw pointing up.

The gentle-looking man died.

The surrounding beastkin are frozen, unable to move due to the sheer shock.

Standing behind what had been the collapsing gentle-looking man was a female beastkin clad in black.

Her short black hair and the cat ears perched on her head give her a charming look.

“I apologize for showing you something unsightly, gozaru. We were on the verge of allowing discourtesy toward my lord’s important guest, gozaru.”

In plain terms, she is a ninja.

There were ninjas in the Izumo Wa Kingdom as well, but this ninja scores extra points for using a ‘gozaru’ speech pattern.

However, one unfortunate thing is that the black outfit is designed so that nothing but her face is visible. Even though she is a kunoichi, there is zero sex appeal. This is a major deduction.

“And you are?”

“Oh, my apologies for the late introduction, gozaru. I am called Kuroneko. I serve Queen Sharon of this country as the eighth seat of the ‘Eight Vassal Beasts’, gozaru. Sir Gene, thank you for answering my lord’s request and coming all this way, gozaru.”

The eight strongest in this country. The second one has appeared in a short span of time. Hooray. Not that I am happy…

Incidentally, Kuroneko is apparently a false name, or rather, a codename. Well, she actually is a black cat beastkin.

She did not give her real name, but since I myself am currently using an alias, it would not be appropriate to complain.

Since she serves Queen Sharon, it would not be strange for her to know who I am. Rather, it is stranger that the gentle-looking man seemed not to know me.

“It seems the seventh seat caused you great trouble, please accept my deepest apologies, gozaru.”

With that said, Kuroneko performed a jumping dogeza on the spot.

It was unnecessarily beautiful.

“Please forgive us, taking the seventh seat’s life as compensation for his discourtesy, gozaru. If there is any other apology required, please say so, and I will do my utmost to accommodate, gozaru.”

I desperately restrained myself from saying, “Then strip”.

Even if it is natural law to demand sex appeal from a kunoichi, right now I am Gene, the Queen’s Knight. I must refrain from such things…

“There was no actual harm, so forgiving it is fine, but was it really okay to kill him? He was still a noble of this country, was he not?”

Moreover, this was the killing of a noble whose rank was determined by strength, in a manner close to assassination.

And by someone of lower rank, at that.

“Oh, thank you for your forgiveness, gozaru. There is no problem at all regarding the seventh seat, gozaru. Ignoring my lord’s summons, acting freely, and showing discourtesy to my lord’s guest are absolutely unforgivable, gozaru.”

According to Kuroneko, Queen Sharon had summoned the hot-blooded ‘Eight Vassal Beasts’ and strictly ordered them not to show me any disrespect.

However, the seventh seat ignored the summons. After repeatedly refusing to respond, he was about to forcefully summoned when news arrived of Gene’s arrival.

Unfortunately, the gentle-looking man was positioned along my travel route, so Kuroneko was dispatched in great haste.

Kuroneko finding the gentle-looking man and the gentle-looking man trying to challenge me to a duel happened almost simultaneously, and she decided without hesitation to assassinate him.

“The moment he challenged Sir Gene to a duel, it was tantamount to defying my lord’s command. I have also obtained permission to strip him of his ‘Eight Vassal Beasts’ title and execute him, gozaru.”

“You are the eighth seat, yet you can execute the seventh seat? Not in terms of authority, but in terms of ability.”

Looking at their statuses, it is clear that Kuroneko is stronger than the gentle-looking man.

Then why is Kuroneko ranked lower?

“Ah, that matter, gozaru. I do not fight by standing face-to-face and trading blows, gozaru. In this country, those who do not fight head-on tend to be looked down upon, gozaru.”

I see. So behind-the-scenes types are looked down on among muscle-brains.

If it were an anything-goes fight, Kuroneko would go quite far.

“In a one-on-one duel in the arena, fighting head-on, I would likely lose to the seventh seat. But in any other situation, I would not, gozaru.”

Kuroneko says this while letting a bit of fighting spirit leak out.

After seeing that clean assassination earlier, it is obvious that those words are not a lie.

However, considering that Sakura looks slightly unwell after witnessing an assassination right in front of her, I do wish there had been a bit more consideration.

“Hey! What are you doing there!”

As we were talking, it seems guards who heard the commotion arrived.

Dog beastkin. Dog policemen.

“The eighth seat of the ‘Eight Vassal Beasts’… and the seventh seat? Why is the seventh seat dead?”

It is hard to accurately grasp this situation at first glance.

Also, Kuroneko is famous despite being a ninja. Try to be stealthy. Or at least lean into the sex appeal.

“Do you not understand what it means that I have acted, gozaru?”

The guard freezes, sweating coldly under Kuroneko’s glare.

It is a technique where you release killing intent for just an instant, intimidating only the target.

“…I see. If the eighth seat, ‘Black Shadow’, has acted, then the seventh seat must have defied Queen Sharon’s orders or committed treason against the country.”

Ah, so Kuroneko really does occupy that kind of position. That makes sense.

‘Black Shadow’ must be Kuroneko’s epithet. Ninja plus shadow is natural. Still, try to be stealthy.

“That is correct, gozaru. The seventh seat defied Queen Sharon’s orders, so I punished him, gozaru. Of course, I have permission from Queen Sharon, gozaru.”

Saying that, Kuroneko took a document from her bosom and handed it to the guard.

The guard checked the letter and nodded.

“I apologize for causing a death in the middle of the city, but there was a reason to act quickly, gozaru.”

That reason being that the gentle-looking man was bothering us, right?

“If the eighth seat, directly under Her Majesty, is acting under Queen Sharon’s orders, then that takes absolute priority. We have no standing to question it.”

After that, the guards asked Kuroneko a few questions and then left.

Incidentally, Kuroneko will take the gentle-looking man’s body back in ‘Storage’. It will be treated as the head of a traitor.

To think that simple flirting would be treated as treason. The gentle-looking man really had bad luck.

After the gentle-looking man’s pickup incident and Kuroneko’s assassination incident ended, we decided to head to an inn recommended by Kuroneko.

Due to her position, Kuroneko moves between major cities in the country, so she is well-versed in recommended inns and eateries in a city of this size.

When I asked why she was so knowledgeable about such things…

“A ninja’s work covers many areas, gozaru. I have developed a habit of gathering as much information as possible, gozaru. Any information can provide some advantage just by having it, gozaru. Showing my lord’s guest around the city, like this, is also ninja work, gozaru.”

That is not ninja work. Be stealthy.

“Please also recommend some places to eat.”

Mio politely asks Kuroneko.

In addition to lodging, we plan to have her introduce recommended eateries. By the way, since I cannot remove my helmet in public places, I will not be eating. I will have them buy food and eat it at the inn.

“Leave it to me, gozaru. The food in this country is famous for not suiting humans, so there are tricks to ordering meals, gozaru.”

Apparently, ordering straight from the menu was not the right approach.

If you ask for human-oriented food, they will surprisingly adjust the seasoning. Although the country does not get along with the human-supremacist nation, it does not actually hate humans themselves.

After walking a bit, we arrive at a magnificent hotel facing the main street.

No matter how you look at it, it is a high-class hotel.

“This is the place, gozaru. I will go call the owner, so please wait a moment, gozaru.”

Saying that, Kuroneko went into the hotel.

…Is there really a need to call the owner?

“Welcome. I am the owner of this establishment…”

In less than five minutes, a well-dressed man who appears to be the owner came out and began introducing himself with an extremely low bow.

I look at Kuroneko…

“I have a small favor owed to me by the owner, gozaru. I have conveyed Sir Gene’s circumstances, but please feel free to say anything if something is lacking, gozaru.”

“A small favor? Lady Kuroneko is our benefactor!”

It seems he is one of Kuroneko’s connections. Kuroneko does not seem to be stealthy at all.

On Kuroneko’s recommendation, the owner offered to waive our lodging fee entirely.

“I did not intend to go that far…”

“Please do not worry, gozaru. Consider it an apology for the seventh seat’s misconduct, gozaru.”

With both the owner and Kuroneko insisting, we reluctantly decided to stay for free.

“There is one thing I would like to ask, gozaru. Around when do you plan to arrive at the royal capital, gozaru?”

Kuroneko asks, so I recall our schedule.

“Our plan is to leave this city tomorrow and stop by other cities along the way, so… I think we will arrive within four days.”

That should be about the same schedule we gave at the first port town.

Since letters are carried by something like carrier pigeons, the royal capital should have received that report.

“Hmm. If that schedule has not changed, then I may be able to return to the royal capital slightly before Sir Gene, though it will be tight, gozaru.”

“Wouldn’t that be difficult by land?”

Traveling by air via dragonkin is incomparably faster than land routes.

Even with detours, carriages would not compare.

“Not by land, gozaru. I also have a means of traveling through the air, gozaru.”

“A bird monster?”

Kuroneko actually has the \<Monster Taming> skill.

I could see on the map that there was a bird monster familiar of Kuroneko’s present. Still, I have to pretend not to know.

“Correct, gozaru. It does not compare to Sir Gene’s flying dragons, gozaru, but being an aerial route, it is very useful, gozaru. The drawback is that it is not very large, so frequent rests are required, gozaru.”

It apparently takes about two days if she departs now, so she plans to leave immediately.

It was so hectic that I suggested she take her time and arrive at the royal capital more slowly, but she has various tasks left, so returning early was necessary anyway.

Additionally, since Queen Sharon is waiting, she would prefer not to arrive later than scheduled.

“I have marked recommended eateries on this map, gozaru. If you present this paper and my name, you can also order from the secret menu, gozaru. Please enjoy this city, gozaru.”

《Woo, secret menu, yay!》

As promised, Kuroneko handed Mio a paper with recommended eateries written on it and departed.

Incidentally, Dora’s delighted voice does not reach Kuroneko.

Guided by a staff member, we enter an excessively luxurious room.

After resting for a while, we plan to go out into the city again.

“After all, ninjas and butlers give off an unnecessarily strong character vibe.”

I mutter as I remove my helmet.

Ninjas aside, there is no need for butlers to be strong characters, but they give that impression anyway.

“Master, you have defeated both butlers and ninjas.”

“I remember the butler, but did I ever defeat a ninja?”

I tilt my head at Mio’s retort.

“Jin-sama, during the Castal war, one of the heroes had the \<Ninjutsu> skill.”

“…Ah, right. That did happen.”

Maria’s explanation jogs my memory. One of those mass-produced heroes.

I remember being impressed that there were ninjas even in that world.

Well, the world is full of strange things. It would not be that surprising for ninja descendants to exist.

“To be instantly killed and then treated like that, that ninja hero was pitiful.”

“That is Jin-kun for you…”

《That’s right.》

It has been a while since I heard that template line.

“The butler barely qualified as a strong character, but the ninja was a weak character.”

“Or rather, his compatibility with the map was just too bad. If he had fought normally, he would have been quite strong.”

As Mio says, maps are fundamentally about stealth kills. They are also strong against ambushes.

The exception would be absurd ambushes like Orihara’s.

“To begin with, ninjas should not stand openly on the battlefield. Be stealthy.”

“That is true. But on a battlefield, there could have been jobs like assassinating the enemy commander. Even without that, they could have been useful as scouts…”

“At that time, it was just me, so no matter what, there was no place for a ninja to shine.”

Although ninjas would have had opportunities to shine in a normal war, the Castal-Eldia War was not a normal war.

It is called the Castal-Eldia War, but in reality, I was the only one who fought the Eldia army. Against an overwhelmingly powerful individual on the battlefield, there is no role for a ninja.

The advantage of fighting one against many is that no matter where you attack, there is no risk of harming allies.

Honestly, when the power difference reaches a certain level, fighting alone can be more comfortable.

“In that sense, this time’s ninja was very active. She fulfilled the ninja’s main duties of assassination and acting as an information source.”

“I wish she would not have done that kind of killing right in front of us…”

“It was not pleasant to watch…”

Sakura and Mio look drained.

Dora seems fine. It is bad for education, though…

“There were some dangerous aspects, but at least she seemed loyal to Sharon, and as long as we are Sharon’s guests, she is unlikely to become an enemy.”

“It is good that she is not an enemy, but the danger is a bit much…”

“I do not think it is just a bit…”

Rotating a neck one hundred and eighty degrees for an assassination is, in my opinion, only ‘a bit dangerous’…

When I argued that, Mio muttered in an exasperated voice.

“Maybe your sense is numb because you are basically the embodiment of danger, Master.”

Was I dangerous? That is news to me.

“Guhh… sniff…”

For the time being, I decided to make Mio cry for her slip of the tongue.

If you say unnecessary things to the embodiment of danger, it cannot be helped.

Ah, I did properly ‘Purify’ the wet floor.

---

**AN:** The usual template crushing.

Kuroneko is in the Erincia position. A key person friendly to the protagonist. And also the part where she kills the template target.

**Editor’s Note:** Not sure the ‘gozaru’ really comes across properly…

+++

# **151: The Clown and the Message**

**AN:** Koda-style overpowered character ranking

1st:　 Butler  

2nd: Ninja  

3rd:　Clown  

---

“At this pace, it looks like we’ll reach the royal capital by tomorrow morning.”

I muttered that while looking over the map atop Blue as we flew.

“Yes. I believe we’ll arrive with plenty of time to spare.”

The one who answered my muttering was Maria.

Well, since we’re in flight, she’s the only one who can answer anyway, seeing as she’s riding Blue with me.

Three days had passed since we parted ways with the black cat of the ‘Eight Vassal Beasts’.

As planned, we were continuing through the Regalia Beastman Kingdom toward its royal capital, Granleon, traveling by dragonkin transport while sightseeing along the way.

Since my Ability map only provides information up to four areas ahead, I compared it with a map we bought in the port town to estimate when we’d reach the capital.

The sun was still high, and we had plenty of time, so once we reached the next area, I figured we’d choose the town we’d stay in for the night.

After moving on for a while, we reached the boundary between areas.

Just as we crossed the boundary and confirmed the new area, a message came in from Alta.

A: Emergency situation. We have discovered a Hero wielding anomalous weapons.

Following Alta’s guidance, I checked the status displayed on the map.

This is the Hero.

Name: Kurauchi Hiroe  

LV: 99  

Sex: Female  

Age: 18  

Race: Human (Otherworlder)  

Skills: \<Throwing Arts LV9> \<Physical Enhancement LV3> \<Acrobatics LV9>  

Blessing: \<Clown’s Ogre Tag +19>  

Titles: Transmigrator, Hero of Another World  

And this is the weapon.

Magic-Devouring Arm: Eating Knife  

Category: One-handed sword  

Rarity: Fantasy Grade  

Notes: Unbreakable, Owner-bound  

Magic-Devouring Arm: Eating Fork  

Category: Spear  

Rarity: Fantasy Grade  

Notes: Unbreakable, Owner-bound  

Ugh…

This is absolutely someone connected to Orihara. I really don’t want to deal with this…

That said, now that we’ve found her, not going isn’t an option.

If she’s connected to Orihara, then all the more so.

Kurauchi, a (provisional) Orihara affiliate, happened to be in a town that was just right for us to stay in tonight.

Orihara really is meticulous about setting things up, isn’t he? Of course, that’s not praise.

Left with no choice, we decided to head for the town where Kurauchi was. Honestly, playing into Orihara’s schemes is extremely unpleasant, but…

“If possible, I’d like Lord Jin to stay back…”

“I can’t really do that, can I?”

After we arrived in town and started walking toward Kurauchi, Maria murmured that.

Ever since the incident where Orihara played us for fools, Maria’s level of caution seems to have risen.

Still, if this involves Orihara, I have no intention of staying somewhere safe by myself.

“Yes. That is why, this time, I will protect you, Jin-sama.”

“Maybe we should have brought Rico-chan with us?”

Mio said that as she looked at Maria, who had a resolute expression on her face.

With Rico’s precognition, it would probably work even against Orihara. Even if the future itself gets changed, she can still predict the timing of the first strike.

“Honestly, I don’t think that level of caution is necessary this time…”

“Is there some reason for that…?”

“Yeah. Two big reasons.”

As I answered Sakura’s question, I raised one finger.

“First, it hasn’t been that long since our last fight with Orihara. If he were going to reappear, it would be at a more meaningful timing. Simply put, it wouldn’t be interesting for him to show up now.”

“And once again, we’re getting some incomprehensible logic that only you and that person understand, Master.”

“I kind of get what you’re saying, but actually doing that in real life is still weird.”

Mio and Sera both refused to fully accept it. Well, Mio didn’t really refuse, I guess…

That guy is the type who’s obsessed with his entrance scenes.

There’s no way he’d show up during something as minor as an attack while we’re traveling, instead of during a major event.

“The second reason is similar to the first. Orihara doesn’t have any strong ties to the Regalia Beastman Kingdom. For one of his associates to show up here would be far too abrupt.”

“I don’t really understand what you mean…”

《Dora doesn’t get it either…》

“So this is the ‘logic only two people understand’ part two, huh.”

Seriously, can you stop talking like Orihara and I are close?

“During the Eldia War, Orihara was, by title, a Hero affiliated with Eldia. That means he was involved in the events happening at the time. He had a motive and a reason to appear. But Regalia is different. If he showed up here again, the only reaction would be, ‘Huh? Why are you here now?’”

“Oh, so his motive for fighting you would be weak. Seriously, he really is like a manga character…”

Exactly as Mio said, he’s a man who feels like he stepped out of a manga.

‘Orihara, who obsesses over his entrances’ wouldn’t show up in a situation like this.

“So the likelihood of Orihara appearing here himself is extremely low. Since he went out of his way to clearly indicate that this is one of his associates, there’s probably some kind of message involved.”

It’s a pretty dangerous messenger, but Orihara himself is dangerous, so it can’t be helped.

I feel like I was called dangerous myself a few days ago, though…

“We should be arriving soon, but… there’s quite a crowd.”

Around Kurauchi, there was a crowd of several dozen people.

It looked like she was performing acrobatics in the middle of town.

“Hey! Ho!”

She was juggling while standing atop a large ball.

What she was throwing included knives (not those weapons), bananas, small balls, and more. Over ten items of different sizes, shapes, and hardness. It was impressive.

It didn’t seem to be some cheat from her Blessing. It looked like genuine skill.

《So cool!》

Dora was watching Kurauchi with sparkling eyes.

She’d probably only seen this kind of entertainment from Akindo in the Izumo Wa Kingdom, so it naturally caught her interest.

Kurauchi was quite small. If you weren’t careful, you might mistake her for an elementary schooler.

As you’d expect from her Blessing and skills, she was dressed like a clown.

Clowns are famous for makeup that hides their facial features, but she wasn’t wearing makeup. Instead, she wore a mask. A mask with asymmetrical expressions, white on one side and black on the other.

While dozens of spectators were completely absorbed by her acrobatics, I watched openly without hiding myself.

“…!”

I didn’t miss the moment when Kurauchi glanced at me for just an instant and her expression stiffened.

-Thunk!-

“Ugyah!”

The next moment, Kurauchi fell off the ball.

Yeah, that was definitely intentional.

-Clonk! Thump! Gosh! Splat!…-

Then, one after another, the items she’d been juggling struck her head as she lay there.

Naturally, the knife hit with the handle.

The way she failed was convincing enough, and laughter rose from the crowd.

“Ahahaha, looks like I messed up. That’s all for today.”

With a friendly smile, Kurauchi bowed to the audience.

Tips flew through the air.

“Thanks so much!”

She bobbed her head as she collected the tips.

If you only saw this, she’d look like nothing more than a street performer.

No one would ever guess that she had such absurdly dangerous weapons in her Item Box.

《Ei!》

Ah, Dora’s throwing a tip too.

Once the crowd dispersed and Kurauchi finished packing up her tools, we approached her.

“Ahaha. Sorry to keep you waiting, Jin-sama. Or should I call you Shindo-sama?”

She asked in a tone completely free of malice.

…Well, there’s no way she wouldn’t know.

Hey…

《Maria, there’s no point in being on guard. Take your hand off your sword hilt.》

《…Understood.》

She took her hand off the hilt, but Maria was still on full alert.

“Just call me Jin. I’m an unidentified Queen’s Knight, after all.”

“Understood. Then, once again, my name is Kurauchi Hiroe. I have a message from Orihara-sama for you, Jin-sama. It won’t take long. Would you like to hear it here?”

Just as I expected, she was a messenger from Orihara.

“A message from Orihara isn’t something to hear out in the open like this. Let’s hear it somewhere else.”

“Understood. Orihara-sama really is disliked, huh. In that case, would you like to come to the house I’m renting?”

Despite her unrealistic outfit, the words “the house I’m renting” suddenly made her feel very real.

“Jin-sama! There could be a trap. I don’t think you should go to such a place…”

Maria’s caution was at maximum.

“Oh dear, you’re really wary of me. I guess that’s Akari-chan’s fault, huh. Honestly, what a pain.”

By Akari-chan, she meant Nojiri Akari, the Hero who sent me to the gray world during the Eldia War. Given that they’re both connected to Orihara, it wouldn’t be strange for them to have crossed paths.

Still, the reason for our caution wasn’t Nojiri. It was Orihara, who gave the order.

I don’t really think there’s a trap, but there’s no need to burden Maria’s mind either.

“Alright then… We’ll take an inn, and you can come there.”

Before even coming to this town, we’d already picked out a good-looking inn.

Apparently, it’s a high-class place that will also take care of cleaning up after violent incidents, as long as you pay. A place that swallows both purity and filth.

“Understood again. Want to hear my recommended inn?”

“If we go to your recommended inn, then there’s no point in being cautious.”

“Yeah, that’s true.”

Kurauchi is… kind of light in a lot of ways.

“So, so, Jin-sama. What brings you to this country anyway?”

As we headed toward today’s inn together, Kurauchi kept asking questions.

Normally, you might think it’s enemy reconnaissance, but there’s a zero percent chance Orihara would order something like that. She was probably just genuinely curious, or acting on her own.

She’s not asking anything that would be a problem to answer, either.

“I was simply invited by the queen of this country. She apparently took an interest in me during the summit.”

“As expected of you. I’m just a humble clown myself, but someday I’d like to perform before a king too.”

By the way, a court clown who performs before a king is called a jester.

Dressed as a clown, with the \<Clown’s Ogre Tag>, a Blessing that literally bears the word clown, and a dream of becoming a court jester.

It’s an absurdly consistent character setup.

“In that case, wouldn’t it have been better to perform before Eldia’s former royalty?”

“Huh? No way. Performing before the king of a country that’s guaranteed to fall soon would be nothing to brag about. Total waste of time.”

Kurauchi has a surprisingly sharp tongue.

“…Besides, if I performed at Eldia’s royal castle, there was a chance those idiots from that stupid school would see me. Absolutely not.”

A dark shadow settled in the eyes behind her mask.

If she follows Orihara, then it’s a given that she has her own circumstances.

I mean, her Blessing even has a +19 attached…

As we talked, we arrived at our destination.

We call it an inn, but it was more like a high-class hotel. Not to brag, but I have money.

“This is the place.”

“Oh dear. So it really was here. …This is actually the inn I was about to recommend.”

Kurauchi said that awkwardly.

…Yeah. Since Kurauchi lives in this town, it makes sense that the inn she’d recommend could overlap with the one I thought was good.

“Jin-sama, let’s choose another inn.”

With her caution cranked beyond maximum, Maria made that suggestion.

“…No. We’ll stay here. Mio, go book rooms for six.”

“Okay.”

Mio jogged into the high-class hotel.

We followed after her and waited at the front desk.

I feel bad for increasing Maria’s anxiety, but backing out just because Kurauchi’s recommendation overlapped with my own doesn’t sit right with me.

“Sorry, Maria.”

“No. Since you chose it, Jin-sama, I will simply support you with all my strength.”

“Jin-sama, you’re really loved, huh.”

Hearing Maria’s devotion, Kurauchi teased her.

“Please don’t joke. Hearing that from someone I’m wary of is nothing but unpleasant.”

“Oh dear. But I get how you feel. I’m pretty much the same.”

“The same…?”

Maria asked back with a confused expression.

“Yes! I feel the same way about Orihara-sama.”

“Don’t lump us together!”

Maria shouted angrily at Kurauchi for treating Orihara and me as the same.

“Room 304 is booked. …Bad timing?”

Mio returned just then.

Maria was getting emotional, and it seemed best not to continue the conversation here.

“Let’s head to the room first. Maria, that’s fine, right?”

“Yes…”

She didn’t seem happy about me being compared to Orihara, but she didn’t object to changing locations.

To be honest, I don’t like being told I’m similar to Orihara either, but it’s also true that there are some similarities. Setting aside emotions, I can’t completely deny it.

The main party plus Kurauchi, seven of us in total, headed to room 304.

Along the way, we passed other guests, but every single one of them had their face hidden.

…Aren’t there way too many shady people here?

After walking a bit, we entered room 304. Once Kurauchi was inside, I locked the door.

She could probably break it if she wanted to, but just in case.

“Alright then, let’s hear Orihara’s message.”

“Understood. Now then, I will announce Orihara-sama’s message! Ta-dah!”

She even did the sound effect herself.

“‘I do not recommend going to this country’s royal capital.’”

…Yeah. I have no idea what that means.

“Could you explain a bit more?”

“Huh? I don’t know. I’m just the messenger. I wasn’t given the role of explaining the message, and I didn’t hear any details.”

“…”

Kurauchi answered my question with a carefree expression.

What the hell do I do with this…

“Master, based on how that Orihara person thinks, what do you think it means?”

“Well… let’s see…”

As Mio said, if I trace Orihara’s thought process, I should be able to infer the meaning.

I really don’t want to, but I’ll try thinking as if I were Orihara. Ugh…

“First, Orihara doesn’t fixate on whether something benefits him or not. And considering the wording ‘I do not recommend,’ which doesn’t sound like a high-priority warning, I’d guess that whether I go to the royal capital or not won’t change the overall situation of a future confrontation with him.”

“He’s your enemy, right? Why would he send a message that doesn’t affect the situation?”

To be precise, it’s ‘someone who could become an enemy’.

“Yeah. That’s just how Orihara is.”

“I truly cannot understand it. What in the world is he thinking?”

Not just Sera, but the others looked equally confused. Dora wasn’t even trying to understand.

Kurauchi, on the other hand, was visibly grinning behind her mask.

I traced Orihara’s thoughts a bit deeper. Bleh…

“Well. Like I said before, Orihara is a fan of my story. And he’s the type of fan who directly interferes with the work. …If I go to the royal capital as things are now, it’ll probably turn into a development he doesn’t find very interesting. He’d prefer I not go, but from an entrance-timing standpoint, it’s awkward for him to stop me directly, so he had no choice but to send a messenger. Something like that.”

I can’t verify it, but I think I’m probably right.

“You really do understand Orihara-sama so well.”

Kurauchi muttered, sounding genuinely envious.

If I could trade places, I would.

“You didn’t hear any details from Orihara, right? There’s no guarantee I’m correct.”

This is only at the level of ‘probably right’.

But Kurauchi shook her head.

“Orihara-sama told me to pass along a message once Jin-sama, no, Shindo-sama, traced his thinking and inferred the meaning. ‘That’s correct.’”

“Ugh…”

He completely read me.

Since coming to this world, this might be the single biggest mental blow I’ve taken. This is rough…

“May I ask one question?”

“Sure. What is it?”

At that point, Maria asked Kurauchi a question.

“Did you come to this country solely to deliver that message?”

“Yes. I’ve been waiting in this town for nearly a month for you, Shindo-sama. Is there a problem?”

Even Orihara shouldn’t have been able to predict exactly when I’d come to this country.

For an entire month, Kurauchi had apparently been making a living in this town by performing street acts.

“I don’t know much about this Orihara person. But is it really necessary to risk your life just to be his messenger? Coming to see Jin-sama, whom he’s clashed with before, surely puts your life in danger.”

Normally, a messenger to an enemy would be someone you’d expect to be killed.

And if the message itself isn’t even that important, all the more reason to refuse.

“You ask such a silly question. I think I said earlier that you and I are similar. If you were in my position, what would you do? If it wasn’t a big deal, but Shindo-sama asked you to risk your life, would you refuse? Would you complain and say it’s ridiculous?”

“…I would gladly risk my life.”

Apparently, there’s another abnormal person among our allies.

A look of understanding appeared on Maria’s face. She looked a little frustrated, but still.

“Perhaps Shindo-sama truly is the greater person. If roles were reversed, maybe Shindo-sama would handle things better. But when I was truly suffering, the one who reached out and saved me was Orihara-sama. Not Shindo-sama. …That is why I can risk my life for Orihara-sama.”

Kurauchi said that without hesitation.

In Orihara’s inferior copy of my Ability \<Eye>, Kurauchi is probably marked in yellow, a believer.

“I understand now what you meant when you said we are similar… We truly are similar…”

Maria nodded, finding much to empathize with in Kurauchi’s words.

“Well, I don’t intend to die pointlessly either. Orihara-sama told me that Shindo-sama isn’t the kind of person who would casually kill a messenger.”

When it comes to outright enemies, I show no mercy, but messengers are a gray area.

As long as they don’t commit a clear act of hostility, I’d let them go almost every time. Spies are a different story.

“I think I have a nine-to-one chance of surviving.”

“So, a ninety percent chance?”

Kurauchi shook her head at Maria’s question.

“No. I think there’s a ten percent chance I’ll survive. Normally, you’d kill me.”

The chance of dying pointlessly is way higher, isn’t it?

“Besides, if Shindo-sama kills me, that gives Orihara-sama a reason to fight you, so it wouldn’t be a complete waste.”

Nojiri, whom I killed in the gray world, looked satisfied at the end too.

“If you’re that prepared, then a little payback should be fine.”

Of course, I have no intention of killing Kurauchi. But that doesn’t mean I’ll do nothing either.

A normal messenger is one thing, but Orihara’s messenger is another. Just being reminded of Orihara feels like an act of hostility.

“Huh?”

I closed the distance to Kurauchi in the blink of an eye (at a speed that even a typical S-rank adventurer could barely perceive) and stored her mask into \<Infinite Storage>.

For now, let’s reveal her true face.

I’m Shindo Jin, the man who mercilessly reveals the faces of masked characters. Nice to meet you.

Hmm. She’s short, with droopy eyes that evoke a protective instinct.

She doesn’t look bad, but there’s something undeniably plain about her…

I’d already confirmed beforehand that she didn’t have the stereotypical ‘facial scar’ common to masked characters.

Even I wouldn’t do something as heartless as ripping the mask off a girl with a scar on her face… I think.

…By the way, which is worse, heartless or cruel?

Now then, how will a masked character react when their mask is stripped away?

Kurauchi patted her face, confirming that the mask was gone.

“Ka, kame…”

“Turtle?”

A meaningless word slipped from Kurauchi’s mouth, and her eyes quickly filled with tears.

“Ka, mask, ka, mask… mask, mask, mask, mask aaaaaah…”

Ugh…

Kurauchi collapsed on the spot, crouching down and covering her face with her hands.

“Aaaaah… mask, mask, mask, mask… ah… ah…”

She groaned for a while, then, once she calmed down a bit, looked up at me pleadingly.

“Pl, mask… p-please… give it… back…”

This wasn’t just pleading-like. It was genuine pleading. And she was slurring her words.

“Alright…”

Her reaction was stronger than I expected, so I judged that the payback was sufficient.

…Or did I overdo it?

I took the mask out of \<Infinite Storage> and handed it to Kurauchi.

She snatched it back and immediately pressed it to her face.

“Haa… haa… Just like Orihara-sama said… you really… show no mercy…”

Kurauchi muttered, looking utterly exhausted as she finally regained her composure.

“Were you expecting mercy from me?”

You came here prepared to be killed nine times out of ten, right?

“Our Master is a genuine sadist, you know. He really doesn’t show mercy, regardless of whether you’re a woman or a child. Pssh! …If he were merciful, he wouldn’t casually leak killing intent during a conversation like this and make people wet themselves…”

Verbal disaster. Sorry, but Mio will have to suffer a little accident.

It was light killing intent, so she probably didn’t wet the floor.

“Mio-chan, when are you going to learn…?”

“Given how things are, I think Mio-san does it on purpose.”

Sakura criticized her, but Sera offered a different take.

When I looked at Mio, she quietly averted her eyes. So it really was on purpose…

“You really are loved. But our love for Orihara-sama isn’t inferior either.”

“‘Our’? You mean that girl Nojiri who was with Orihara before?”

There was something in Kurauchi’s words I couldn’t ignore.

“Akari-chan too, yes. We call ourselves the Gourmet Club. Akari-chan, me, and two other guys. The four of us are the Four Heavenly Kings of the Gourmet Club.”

Orihara’s group had turned into a ridiculous organization.

“Oh, the two guys’ love is more like reverence, so don’t get the wrong idea.”

I don’t need that clarification.

“All of us were in Class C, and Orihara-sama saved us when we were being bullied by the malignant factors.”

“Class C… bullying… malignant factors… What does that mean…?”

A familiar set of words came up, and Sakura reacted without thinking.

…That was unnecessary.

“Huh? According to Orihara-sama, Kinoshita-san, you were in the same position as us in 2-C, right? Did Shindo-sama not tell you?”

Kurauchi asked back, looking genuinely surprised.

“Hey, don’t talk about unnecessary things.”

“But I think she has the right to know. She’s directly involved, after all.”

If we’re talking about rights, then yes, Sakura has the right to know.

But think about it. Is it really okay to tell Sakura? Compared to when we first came to this world, she’s more mentally stable now. She’s gotten over a lot, and she doesn’t really bring up dark topics anymore.

Still, hearing or talking about it will only leave a bad taste. If she doesn’t know, maybe it’s better that way.

“Jin-kun, what are you talking about…? This is something related to me, right…? Something about our school in the original world…”

“…Yeah. There’s one thing about our school in the original world that I never told you.”

“Will you tell me…?”

Sakura clearly wanted to hear it.

If she wants to know, then maybe it’s better to tell her.

“Shindo-sama, since we have the chance, let’s talk about it here.”

Kurauchi said that casually, even though it wasn’t her problem.

“Was that an order from Orihara?”

“No. This is just advice based on experience. Even if you hear it, nothing will really change, and I don’t think it’ll lead in a bad direction.”

I don’t think Orihara ordered this either, but experience, huh…

Alright.

“It might be a painful truth for you, Sakura, and it won’t change anything now, but do you still want to hear it?”

“Yes… If it’s something related to me in the original world, I want to hear it…”

At that point, I couldn’t refuse.

“Alright. I’ll explain briefly first. The school we attended was a facility that gathered children with special talents. And in Class C, the school deliberately created an environment where bullying was likely to occur. Sakura, you were a victim of that environment.”

---

**AN:** The story of Jin’s school is something I’d been thinking about since early on.

It’s also the answer to the question of why there were so many unhinged people at Jin’s school. Tsukishin Academy, Hakoniwa Academy, Hope’s Peak Academy.

Those are the kinds of images in mind. The details will come next time.
