# **152: The Truth About the School and Cancellation**

**AN:** Even though he only came up in conversation, Orihara’s presence is seriously overwhelming.

According to Kurauchi’s information, Orihara is still listed as missing, with his life or death unknown.

---

“That school was run under national supervision, gathering children with special talents from all across Japan. Of course, not every single student was like that. There were plenty of ordinary students too.”

From all over Japan, they actively scouted those who had surpassed the limits of humanity, those on the verge of doing so, and those who were just a little outside the norm. In some cases, they even arranged things so that such students would enroll by coincidence.

“That sounds like a manga-style setting. An academy for supernatural battles?”

“If anything, it was closer to an animal testing facility. Just to clarify, it wasn’t an organization that conducted human experiments. Their recent main research theme was ‘investigating the influence and reactions of humans with special talents’.”

Unfortunately, there were hardly any battles like Mio was hoping for. There were a few, but not many.

Since observation was the primary goal, there wasn’t much direct interference with the students. There was some, but not much.

“So, Master really wasn’t normal even back in his original world…”

Mio muttered in understanding, but I didn’t comment on that and continued.

“Of course, the school didn’t mess up in a way that would make the students realize any of this, so it’s only natural that Sakura didn’t know.”

“Then… how did Jin-kun find out about it…?”

“Oh, that’s easy. My best friend hacked the school’s network.”

My best friend Azuma showed me the materials he found by hacking into the school’s internal data. All I did was guess the password to cancel it, which was a trivial contribution.

Really, you should treasure talented friends.

Incidentally, those documents detailed the research conducted within the school. There were all kinds of unpleasant things written there.

“”…””

After my criminal confession, Sakura and Mio both pulled back a little.

Hey, I wasn’t the culprit, okay? Azuma did everything.

Selling out my treasured best friend immediately.

“Anyway, back to the point. As an approach to observe the influence students had on their surroundings, it seems they gathered ‘students with special talents’ into Class B, and surrounded them with ‘slightly special students’ and ‘ordinary students’.”

Assuming one class has 40 students, let’s generously estimate 5 ‘students with special talents’.

Of the remaining 35, 10 were assigned as ‘slightly special students,’ and 25 as ‘ordinary students’.

Within that setup, they studied the influence of the ‘students with special talents’. That was the purpose of Class B.

For the record, I was also in Class B as one of the ‘students with special talents’. Totally unnecessary, if you ask me.

“Why B? Normally, wouldn’t that kind of class be A?”

Mio asked, but I shook my head.

“Class A had its own separate purpose. And of course, Class C had one too.”

“That would be… what you were talking about earlier… right…?”

Sakura, who used to be in Class C, asked timidly.

I nodded.

“The purpose of Class C was to investigate negative influences and reactions. It was a nasty class where they surrounded ‘students with special talents’ with ‘students with bad conduct’ to observe what happened.”

It was similar to Class B, but Class C was far more malicious.

They formed a class with several ‘students with special talents’ ten ‘students with bad conduct’ and twenty-five ‘ordinary students’ and observed how things turned out.

What Kurauchi called ‘malignant factors’ earlier was a derogatory term for these ‘students with bad conduct’.

“Could it be that… I was…”

“Yeah, you were probably one of the ‘students with special talents’ in Class C. From what I’ve heard about your past, Sakura, you were unnaturally disliked by people.”

“Mio-chan felt that way too for a long time. Sakura-sama’s treatment in her original world was way too harsh…”

I’ve known Sakura for a while now, and she isn’t a malicious person.

At the very least, the treatment she received was clearly excessive.

She has some negative tendencies, but those aren’t innate. They were likely shaped by her environment.

Naturally, Sakura bears no blame that should be held against her.

“I don’t remember the details clearly, but when I looked at the documents before, I think there was a description of a student with the trait ‘unnaturally disliked by others’. It caught my interest, so it stuck in my mind. Now that I think about it, that fits Sakura perfectly.”

I only skimmed through the documents Azuma lent me, but I do remember that description.

I didn’t remember the specific name, but it couldn’t have been anyone other than Sakura.

“Now that I think about it, it was strange that I even got into that school… Every other school rejected me before I even got to the interview stage. They turned me away just when I went to submit my application… Only that school accepted me, and it was by recommendation. No matter how you look at it, it was unnatural…”

“Is ‘being disliked’ really enough to describe that?”

“Yeah… that’s way beyond what I imagined…”

Mio and I, who understand how high school admissions work, were completely put off.

Being rejected just for submitting an application goes far beyond what can be brushed off as ‘being disliked’.

“On the flip side, since that school was gathering special students, there’s no way they would have rejected Sakura. Whether you’d be happy after enrolling is another matter…”

“I wasn’t… happy…”

Yeah, figures.

“By the way, I was also a ‘student with special talents’ in Class C. Apparently my physical abilities were abnormal compared to my height and weight. Was I in those documents?”

Kurauchi cut in there. Apparently, she was like a modern-Japan version of Sera.

Looking closely, her stats were unusually high for her level. Probably something she was born with.

“…Sorry, but I don’t remember that.”

“That’s unfortunate.”

I searched my memory, but I couldn’t recall anything like that.

If I remember right, those documents only covered students in the same grade. Kurauchi was technically our senior.

“Kurauchi-san, you were bullied too, right…?”

“Yes, I was. If you can tell me why a shy, small-framed girl with super strength who can’t even talk properly without wearing a mask wouldn’t be bullied, I’d love to hear it.”

Kurauchi answered Sakura’s question as if it were nothing.

So that reaction when she took off her mask wasn’t something caused by this world. It was how people had always reacted.

“Well, compared to you, who had the ‘talent of being hated by others’ I might have had it easier.”

“That’s… true… My talent, no, my curse feels like it exists just so I can be bullied… But high school was the worst…”

At Kurauchi’s merciless follow-up, Sakura’s expression darkened.

“I do have a theory about why that is… Do you want to hear it?”

“Please…”

She didn’t really want to, but there was no avoiding it.

Sakura nodded with a gloomy expression.

“According to the report my friend hacked, in Class C, where ‘students with bad conduct’ were present, ‘ordinary students’ tended to become more easily tainted by malice. Simply put, their behavior worsened.”

“Wouldn’t that eventually mean there were no ‘ordinary students’ left?”

“There wouldn’t be. And there probably weren’t. If almost everyone in the class became a ‘student with bad conduct’ it’s only natural that the bullying escalated.”

I answered Sera’s question without hesitation.

Someone like Sakura, who is easy to dislike, surrounded by nearly forty ‘students with bad conduct’ wouldn’t stand a chance. And malice only escalates over time.

“That’s why Sakura’s bullying was ignored by the teachers. No, by the observers. Observers aren’t allowed to intervene arbitrarily with their subjects.”

I had heard before that teachers ignored Sakura’s bullying. All the teachers assigned to Class C knew the school’s true purpose and also served as observers.

To obtain accurate data, it’s highly likely they deliberately left things alone.

“That’s… awful…”

“What do they think students are, anyway?!”

Sakura muttered with tears in her eyes, and Mio, who heard her, exploded in anger.

“Test animals, probably… Even we felt sick reading that report, so we decided to destroy the school.”

“Huh? But it was an important research facility run by the state, right?”

“You think that kind of reason would stop me? Or us?”

“Yeah, not even a little.”

As Mio said, the three of us didn’t stop.

It started with a small trigger. We investigated the bullying at the school (mostly Azuma did), and that investigation led us straight to the school’s hidden face.

Being treated like test animals was disgusting, and so was creating an environment that encouraged bullying.

Once we judged them as a clear enemy, there was no reason not to act.

So we destroyed it.

In the end, everyone received punishment befitting their actions.

“Kinoshita-san, didn’t you think there were an unusual number of self-study periods on the day we were transferred?”

Oh, Kurauchi, you’re even saying that…

“Now that you mention it… There were hardly any classes that day…”

“That’s because the upper management of the school had been wiped out and classes were the least of their concerns.”

Yes. Exactly.

We completely destroyed the school the day before we were transferred to this world.

That’s why so few teachers were transferred here.

As for Class C’s homeroom teachers, not a single one was transferred. They weren’t even at the school.

“With requests from Shindo-sama and others, class reassignment was supposed to happen as early as the next day. Naturally, it was meant to protect those being bullied in Class C and prevent further bullying.”

“Jin-kun… you were doing things like that…?”

“Well, it was in front of my eyes, it was unpleasant, and I had the power to change it.”

I don’t think of it as a good deed.

I just couldn’t stand unpleasant things happening within my reach. If it didn’t take much effort to change that situation, lending a hand was fine.

It was the same kind of ‘small help’ I gave to believer heroes like Kino and Shichihouin.

“In that sense, we would’ve been saved as early as tomorrow. Fortunately or unfortunately, we got caught up in the otherworld transfer before that.”

“I feel conflicted… Whether I was transferred or not, Jin-kun would have saved me… Maybe I would’ve ended up in the same position as Shichihouin-san and the others…”

Sakura murmured with a complicated, yet slightly happy expression.

Come to think of it, my ‘small help’ had increased the number of believers…

“If that had happened, I probably would’ve believed in Shindo-sama instead of Orihara-sama.”

“…I understand now. You really are similar to me.”

Maria, who had stayed silent because this was about the original world, spoke up.

Kurauchi resembled Sakura in being bullied in Class C, Sera in her constitution, and Maria in temperament.

As for Mio and Dora… not exactly, but they do feel similar to our group.

Did Orihara think that far ahead when he chose her as a messenger?

It’s possible. Though it doesn’t seem like he told Kurauchi that much.

“Hey, Master. Listening to all that, I started wondering. Why are we able to interact with Sakura-sama normally? I’ve never disliked Sakura-sama even once since we met.”

“Yes, we owe Sakura-sama a great debt. Disliking her would be unthinkable.”

“Indeed. She is the second most precious person after Jin-sama.”

《Sakura, like!》

Starting with Mio, everyone looked at Sakura with eyes full of affection.

“Everyone… thank you… But now that you mention it, it is strange… Since coming to this world… except for Eldia Royal Castle at the beginning, I haven’t really suffered…”

Sakura thought for a moment, then spoke as if something had clicked.

“Could it be because I’ve been traveling with Jin-kun…?”

“””《That makes sense!》”””

Everyone nodded in agreement.

Is it really okay to accept that so easily…?

“That’s quite possible. Shindo-sama’s talent is an extremely strong positive one. By being together, it likely canceled out Kinoshita-san’s negative-leaning talent.”

“Kurauchi, you sure know a lot about our situation, don’t you?”

Honestly, she knows things even my close companions don’t.

“Of course. I heard all about the original world from Orihara-sama.”

“That bastard… I’m going to punch him next time I see him.”

“P-please be gentle…”

No mercy.

“If that hypothesis is correct, then I’m really glad I came to this world… Even in my original world, Jin-kun might’ve helped me, and things might’ve been better than before… But I don’t think I would’ve made close friends like this…”

Overall, Sakura sees coming to this world in a positive light.

But my view is slightly different.

“I don’t think that would’ve been the case.”

“What do you mean…?”

Sakura asked, puzzled.

“First, let’s assume that hypothesis is correct. The reason you were bullied was a ‘mere constitution’ that would disappear just by being with me. You yourself have no faults at all. You’re not someone who deserves to be bullied.”

“I want to believe that… I don’t want to think that it was my fault…”

What happened to Sakura was something beyond her control.

And there’s more.

“If class reassignment had happened in your original world, you would almost certainly have ended up in the same class as me. And if someone with such a strange talent were in my class, do you think I wouldn’t be interested?”

“Yeah, Master would definitely be interested.”

Being told I have the opposite kind of talent, there’s no way I wouldn’t be curious.

In fact, even skimming the documents left an impression on me.

“I probably would’ve dragged you around with me even in the original world. Sakura, do you think you could refuse if I forced you along?”

“I absolutely couldn’t…”

I wouldn’t easily let go of something I found interesting.

If she truly hated it, that would be different, but Sakura likely wouldn’t have refused. At the time, she wouldn’t have been able to reject someone’s positive feelings toward her.

“Being with me would cancel out your constitution. Sooner or later, you would’ve made ordinary friends. I’m pretty sure of it.”

“You think so…?”

“Probably. In either world, you and I would’ve formed a connection.”

And once that connection formed, her constitution would’ve been canceled.

“Let me say it again, based on that premise. You have no faults at all, and you’re not someone who deserves to be bullied. Once that curse-like constitution is canceled, you’d have friends in either world. There’s no need to think ‘because it’s this world’. You can hold your head high without worrying about anyone.”

There’s no need to think you were saved because of this world.

You were saved because you’re a decent person who deserved to be saved. That’s enough.

“You’re right… It doesn’t matter which world it is… If I’m saved either way, then the one I should thank isn’t this world, but Jin-kun…!”

Huh? That’s where you landed?

“I was trying to say that you yourself deserve to be saved…”

I added timidly, but Sakura shook her head.

“Even if I deserve to be saved, the one who saved me is Jin-kun, right? I think it’s fine to direct my gratitude to you… I’ve been grateful ever since you reached out to me after I was driven out of the royal castle, but after hearing this, I’m sure the decision I made back then wasn’t wrong.”

“The decision you made when you were driven out of Eldia Royal Castle?”

That’s news to me.

“Yes… From the moment I was driven out and you extended your hand to me, I decided that unless you rejected me, I would stay by your side…”

Now that she mentions it, she did say she wanted to keep traveling with me back in the Dragonkin Sanctuary.

So she decided that all the way back when she was driven out of Eldia.

“That’s probably why Kinoshita-san’s ability awakened the way it did. According to Orihara-sama, abilities awaken to fulfill the strongest wish at that moment.”

Kurauchi butted in again with unnecessary commentary.

This is getting annoying. Maybe I should silence her for a bit.

…I instantly snatch Kurauchi’s mask away.

“Aah! My mask, m-mask!”

“Sera, throw her into the bathroom or something.”

“U-understood…”

Sera carried the panicking Kurauchi toward the bathroom.

…Phew. That should quiet things down.

“Y-you’re ruthless…”

Mio was trembling, but I ignored her.

“When my ability awakened… I think I was wishing not to be a burden to you, Jin-kun, to be useful to you… and at the same time, not to be separated from you… Magic Creation fulfills both of those.”

“Yeah. It’s an ability that’s close to omnipotent, yet premised on my presence.”

“I always thought your ability awakened at the most convenient times, Jin-kun, but mine was the same…”

The ability to create one’s own magic is incredibly powerful. No one would call someone with that ability a burden. Yet it can’t reach its full potential with her MP alone, requiring my presence. It perfectly reflects Sakura’s wishes at the time.

“Well, even if Magic Creation hadn’t manifested, I don’t think I would’ve abandoned you.”

Sakura’s ability awakened sometime after we started traveling together, around when we found Dora.

By then, I had already judged her as a companion. I wouldn’t abandon someone without good reason.

In the first place, I didn’t side with Sakura because her ability was useful.

“But if my ability hadn’t been useful at all, or if I’d been too weak, maybe I would’ve been removed from the main travel party once we bought the mansion…”

“Yeah, I can’t say that would absolutely never happen.”

I wouldn’t abandon her, but if traveling together was impossible, I might have refused to let her accompany us. For someone who wished to stay by my side, that wouldn’t have been desirable.

“Jin-kun, I’ll prove that I can be useful to you, so please keep me by your side…”

“That sounds like a proposal.”

“I don’t mean it as a proposal, but I have resolve on that level…”

If she’s saying that much, I have to respond seriously.

“…Alright. Then unless you say you don’t want to, you can stay by my side and accompany me on my journey. Is that okay?”

“Yes, thank you…”

Sakura bowed deeply.

Honestly, I was worried about telling Sakura the truth about the school, but in the end, it seems to have worked out in her favor.

When she raised her face, there was no darkness in her expression.

If there’s one complaint, it’s that Orihara’s messenger was the trigger.

After wrapping up things with Sakura, we brought out the person in question, Kurauchi.

Thanks to Sera’s consideration, Kurauchi had her hands and feet bound with sturdy wires (made of mithril) so she couldn’t move.

She was also gagged, preventing her from casting magic.

“Mmmph! Mmmph!”

Kurauchi groaned, her face smeared with tears and snot.

“So, Master, what are we doing with this girl?”

“She is a member of a hostile faction. For safety, I recommend killing her.”

Maria spoke up before I could answer Mio.

“Orihara could be considered hostile, but this one is just a messenger. She hasn’t shown any malice or hostility, and she hasn’t gotten in my way. That’s not enough reason to kill her.”

She’s annoying, sure, but not enough to kill (though I am taking the mask).

She was probably thoroughly instructed by Orihara on that point.

In other words, Orihara hasn’t decided on his next move yet.

If he had decided to oppose me again, Kurauchi’s behavior would have been different.

…What we did to Kurauchi was also partly to see whether she’d become hostile after being treated like this. Really!

But Kurauchi’s indicator is still green (neutral, indifferent). It hasn’t turned red (hostile).

That makes it even harder to kill her.

“However, while it’s not a reason to kill her, there’s also no reason to do nothing.”

Thud!

“Mmph!? Ugh…”

I delivered a solid punch to Kurauchi’s stomach, knocking her unconscious.

“Sera, remove the wires. Maria, strip her.”

“”Yes.””

And thus, Kurauchi became my slave through Slave Arts.

Just in case, I used \<Multiple Existence LV6> to disguise and erase the title ‘Jin’s Slave’.

I also had Alta thoroughly examine Kurauchi to ensure there were no traps from Orihara. It was unlikely given his personality, but better safe than sorry…

“Master, why make her a slave? So she can’t take hostile actions?”

“That’s part of it, but the main purpose is bait. By enslaving Kurauchi and then releasing her, we can investigate Orihara’s movements.”

Now I finally answered Mio’s question.

As a slave, \<Contract Bond> makes it easy to track her location.

If things go well, we might even find Orihara’s hideout.

“Do you think such a petty scheme would work on someone like Orihara?”

“I don’t expect it to. This is just in case.”

If Orihara makes a huge blunder, maybe we’ll get lucky.

If we do find his location due to a blunder, I plan to mock him mercilessly.

Think about it.

A guy whose hideout gets exposed because his messenger came back.

Whether he shows up as an enemy or an ally, he’d just look ridiculous.

Yes. If this plan works, we can steal Orihara’s spotlight.

If there’s even a small chance of making him disappear from the stage, it’s worth doing, no matter how petty.

After explaining that…

“Master, you really understand that Orihara person too well.”

“You’d have to be extremely close to read someone’s actions that deeply.”

“It’s a strange thing to say, but I’m jealous that Jin-sama understands you that much.”

Those were comments from the three slave girls.

《Master! Hungry!》

Dora’s comment had absolutely nothing to do with Orihara.

That’s only natural, since she’s never met him and has no interest…

“Let’s eat soon. As for Kurauchi… we can just leave her.”

We talked quite a bit, so it was a good time for dinner.

“Leaving a girl unconscious after punching her in the stomach… Master, you’re seriously cruel… pii!”

Since Mio’s comment (slip?) was clearly intentional, I made her leak without hesitation.

Hey, don’t make me do something that requires a change of clothes right before we go out.

“Mio-san, do you have masochistic tendencies?”

“That’s not it! I was trying to communicate with Master!”

Mio shook her head vigorously, her crotch soaked, as she replied to Sera.

“Communication involves wetting yourself and crying…? Mio-chan, you’re really putting your body on the line…”

Mio looks like a child, but her mental age isn’t that different from mine. Despite that, she kept making frequent slips without learning, so I suspected she was doing it on purpose.

That’s why I went along with teasing her a bit…

But I didn’t expect it to be for communication.

…Well, in a sense, it is the easiest kind of communication?

In terms of being able to talk nonsense casually, Mio is the closest to me…

“I understand your resolve, Mio. In that case, I’ll be even more merciless from now on.”

“Master, please, spare me.”

Mio prostrated herself while still wet.

Apparently, prostration is also a form of communication.

After accepting Mio’s plea, I cast ‘Purification’ and headed to dinner.

Kurauchi took a good hit, so she probably wouldn’t wake up for about an hour.

…Lately, I’ve gotten pretty good at estimating how long someone will be unconscious based on how solidly I hit them.

I can’t acquire skills naturally in this world, but I guess I can still develop techniques like this. First time I realized that.

A little over an hour later, after finishing dinner, we returned to the inn.

The dining area (private room) was more crowded than expected, so it took longer than planned.

“Well, if she woke up, there’s no way she’d still be here.”

Kurauchi, who had been unconscious, was no longer in the room.

I had removed the wires and left the mask nearby, so I figured she’d leave on her own once she woke up.

“So, where is Kurauchi now?”

A: She is at the house she has rented in this town. Also, there is a message from Kurauchi.

A message? Does Kurauchi know about Alta?

A: No, that does not appear to be the case. However, she realized she was being monitored. More precisely, it was not a message but a monologue. She said, “I apologize, but I never intended to return to Orihara-sama in the first place. I do not know Orihara-sama’s location, and all bases I knew of have already been abandoned. Orihara-sama told me that if I lost consciousness even once in front of Shindo-sama, there was a high likelihood I would be enslaved. Assuming I have been enslaved and am being monitored, I wish to inform you that I have no value as an information source.”

Annoying…

Kurauchi aside, Orihara is just plain annoying…

The fact that he’s completely reading us is what’s most irritating…

So basically, Kurauchi has been completely cut off by Orihara.

Or rather, she was cut off with her consent…

Most likely, Orihara won’t make contact with Kurauchi from here on.

She’s useless as an information source, can’t really be treated as an ally, and I don’t feel like killing her as an enemy… What an annoying person to have left on my hands.

---

**Behind-the-Scenes Story**

_* Backstory and extra tidbits from the main story._

– The high school Jin and Sakura attended

It didn’t come up in Jin’s account, but many of the heroes who participated in the war between Eldia and Castal were ‘students with bad conduct’ from Class C.

Strictly speaking, some were ‘ordinary students’ who became ‘students with bad conduct’ but by Jin’s standards, they were equally guilty.

Also, Kusakabe and Sano, who appeared earlier in the main story, were candidates for Class C. Due to numbers, Kusakabe was placed in Class A and Sano in Class B, but in terms of treatment, they were considered ‘students with bad conduct’.

Even outside Class C, some ‘students with bad conduct’ were mixed in to observe reactions.

This should mostly explain why the students in the main story were said to have such strong personalities.

---

**AN:** Incidentally, Orihara and Mizuhara were in Class A.

And Jin’s family composition still hasn’t even been mentioned.

I want to give him a little sister, but no matter how I look at it, Jin really feels like an only child kind of personality.

That’s it. I’ll make her a stepsister. Or maybe suddenly give him about twelve little sisters. Sounds familiar somehow…

+++

# **153: The Beastkin Kingdom’s Royal Capital and the Reverse Scale**

**AN:** Since this is a new land, there are a lot of new characters popping up needlessly.

Well, more than half of them are disposable for this arc anyway.

---

《It looks like we can see it now. Is that the royal capital, Granleon?》

The day after encountering Kurauchi.

As scheduled, we arrived at the royal capital of the Regalia Beastkin Kingdom, Granleon.

Judging by the scale of the city alone, it is bigger than Castal Kingdom’s royal capital.

And out of a population of over a hundred thousand, more than ninety-five percent are beastkin (according to Alta).

And I could also guess why Orihara did not want to let me go to the royal capital.

Of course, this was information I had already read off the map once we got close to the city…

《According to information from Kuroneko-san, she said it was recommended to enter from the south gate, right?》

《Yes. It seems the south gate alone is prepared so that we may enter at any time.》

《Right. Well, if we head straight like this, we will reach the south gate anyway, so there is no particular problem.》

The title ‘Eight Vassal Beasts’, granted to those with the strongest-class abilities in the Regalia Beastkin Kingdom.

From Kuroneko, who holds the eighth seat among them, we had received various information about the royal capital as well.

The fact that we were coming to this country at the queen’s summons is not confidential information.

However, it is also not something being loudly advertised everywhere.

It is, at its core, Queen Sharon’s personal hospitality.

Therefore, there is no guarantee that every gate can fully handle our reception.

To put it plainly, there is no guarantee that unnecessary trouble will not occur.

However, it seems the south gate alone has been thoroughly informed about us and fully prepared.

After hearing that, there is really no choice but to enter from the south gate.

Trouble outside of nobles is basically welcome, but I am not so starved for it that I would deliberately scatter sparks myself. If I get dragged into something, I will consider it lucky.

《I see. They really have prepared thoroughly.》

Granleon has gates to the east, west, south, and north, but the south gate alone had no pedestrian traffic at all.

A: There are people who wish to pass through, but all of them are being guided to other gates.

In other words, the south gate has become a passage exclusively for the Gene-sama party.

It seems unlikely that unnecessary trouble will occur, but it also feels like it might earn us unnecessary resentment.

Since taking more time only increases the burden on others, we brought Blue and the others as close as possible and landed so we could enter the city quickly.

Shortly after landing, a single man approached us from the south gate.

He was an elderly wolf beastman, immaculately dressed in a butler’s outfit.

…I see. They matched the reading with an old butler and a wolf butler.

“Welcome. You must be Gene-sama, correct?”

“Yeah. This is the letter I received from Queen Sharon.”

I hand the letter to the butler.

“Allow me to take a look. …Thank you very much. I am Sein, and I have been tasked with guiding you, Gene-sama. I hope you will remember me.”

The old butler’s full name is Sein Barse.

Being so close to the archetypal butler name earns high marks.

“Alright, I will be counting on you. So, what should we do now?”

“Whatever you wish, Gene-sama. Her Majesty the Queen has placed top priority on meeting with you. If you desire, we can prepare the meeting at once. If you wish to rest, please relax as long as you like. Naturally, lodging expenses will be covered by us.”

So they are willing to give us at least that much time if we want to sightsee.

Honestly, I do want to look around, but sightseeing leisurely while keeping someone waiting does not sit well with me. Sightseeing must be free. Of course, one must still observe proper etiquette at tourist spots.

“No, it would be rude to keep her waiting, so I would like to have the meeting as soon as possible, within reason. Could you convey that to Queen Sharon?”

“That would be most appreciated. In fact, Her Majesty has already finished preparing for the meeting. It seems she has been eagerly awaiting Gene-sama’s arrival.”

“I-is that so…”

I cannot imagine the usually taciturn Queen Sharon waiting impatiently like that.

“Then, please excuse me for a moment.”

Saying that, Sein took out a blue tube from his chest pocket.

“What is that?”

“A device to launch a smoke signal. I will signal Her Majesty that Gene-sama will be heading over immediately.”

When Sein pulled the cord attached to the tube, blue smoke hissed upward into the sky.

“Then, I will lead the way. May I ask that you follow me to the royal castle while remaining mounted on your riding dragons?”

“Hm? What do you mean by that?”

Are we going to stomp through the city streets while mounted on Blue?

“I mean this.”

With that, Sein started running and sprinted straight up the south gate wall, which was over ten meters tall.

Wall running…?

If I had to put it in one phrase, it would be, “Old man runs up”.

“I will travel along the rooftops to the royal castle, so I would like Gene-sama and the others to pursue me while mounted on your riding dragons! You may enter the castle grounds directly!”

Since he had gotten some distance away, Sein shouted this loudly back to us.

“Both of those methods sound like they will cause all sorts of problems. Will this really not become an issue later!?”

I shout back just as loudly.

“There will be no problem! It may be a bit unseemly, but this seems the fastest way, and we have already obtained Her Majesty’s permission!”

It does not seem like he is lying.

In that case, let us enjoy the rare experience of flying over a royal capital.

＊Normally, permission would never be granted.

“Alright, Blue. I am counting on you again.”

《Leave it to me. We are taking off!》

We take flight again while mounted on the dragonkin.

“Here we go!”

With that, Sein began running, so we mounted the dragonkin and followed after him.

Well, a royal castle is a magnificent structure. It is not like we could mistake it anyway.

You know, that Western-style castle standing in the city center, looking the most important?

A: Yes.

Naturally, the most important person resides in the most important-looking building.

Sein, who is ahead of us, runs lightly across the rooftops of the buildings.

Even when leaping from roof to roof, his jumps are so light they do not convey any sense of weight.

If I had to put it in one phrase, it would be, “Old man becomes the wind”.

“If you are going to flaunt such an impressive title as one of the ‘Eight Vassal Beasts’, you really ought to be able to do at least this much. It is not a title someone who gets instantly killed by Kuroneko should be allowed to claim.”

As you can probably guess from the flow so far, Sein is also one of the ‘Eight Vassal Beasts’.

I do not know which seat he holds, though.

A: He is the second seat. People in the city were muttering as they saw Sein leaping.

That is practically top-tier. As expected of the old man. It makes sense that his various skills and stats are all high-level.

That said, the vertical wall movement and rooftop jumps he showed earlier are not feats achieved purely through skills and stats.

Simply put, they are only possible with the assistance of a rare skill.

\<Wild Traversal>

A beastkin-only skill. Allows high-speed movement regardless of terrain.

As you can see, Sein possesses a movement-type unique-class skill.

With sufficient stats and a certain level of \<Body Enhancement> and \<Jump> skills, similar feats are possible, but whether one could move that lightly is questionable.

Also, the sight of a well-aged old man leaping around on rooftops is surreal beyond words.

I could do the same thing if I wanted to, but I absolutely do not want to.

This is a good example of how being capable of something in terms of ability and actually being willing to do it are completely different matters.

After about ten minutes of flight, the royal castle had drawn quite close.

“Even if the royal capital is large, Blue makes reaching the center almost instantaneous.”

《Of course. Even now, I am flying slowly to match the old man running below, you know?》

Even with movement skills, a ground-running old man cannot begin to compete with a flight-specialized sky dragon.

Compared to our usual travel, Blue is moving quite slowly.

That said, an old man who can cross half the royal capital in ten minutes (with the castle being at the center) is impressive in his own way.

“I know. Blue at full power is nothing like this, right?”

《Yep!》

At full power, Blue should be able to fly from one end to the other in under a minute.

As an aside, with Warp, you could cross from end to end in under a second as long as it is within line of sight.

If I said that, Blue would probably cry.

While we were talking like that, Sein, who had been leading, arrived at the royal castle.

An old man running straight up the outer wall of a large Western-style castle.

He reached a very wide balcony at a height equivalent to the fourth or fifth floor, then waved his hand to signal us.

I had Blue and the others reduce speed and land on the balcony where Sein was.

“Is it alright to leave the riding dragons here?”

“Yes. There are stables here for Kuroneko’s familiars, specifically bird familiars, so please entrust them there.”

At the edge of the balcony was a structure that looked like a stable, inside which several monsters were being kept.

Kuroneko, one of the ‘Eight Vassal Beasts’ whom we met before, possesses the \<Monster Taming> skill and said she uses them for communication and transport.

So this balcony also serves as their landing and departure point.

“See you later.”

《Yes. Please enjoy yourselves at your leisure.》

After greeting Blue, I hand the reins over to a castle maid.

Inside the stable, there seem to be fairly large bird monsters, and it looks like there is plenty of space even with Blue and the other two (in dragon form) inside.

Having parted ways with Blue and the others, we were about to enter the castle at once and visit Queen Sharon.

…But we were unable to do so.

“So you are Gene, huh? I am the first seat of the ‘Eight Vassal Beasts’, the King Beast, Leopardo. Sorry, but you will be sparring with me now.”

Standing in our way was a gigantic lion beastman over two meters tall. Another ‘Eight Vassal Beast’, seriously…?

Moreover, behind Leopardo were two male beastmen and one female beastman. They are apparently the fourth, fifth, and sixth seats of the ‘Eight Vassal Beasts’. Yet more ‘Eight Vassal Beasts’…

They are supposedly the eight strongest in the Regalia Beastkin Kingdom, but since coming to this country, it feels like I have only properly interacted with the ‘Eight Vassal Beasts’.

Their encounter rate is higher than that of ordinary people, and the ‘Eight Vassal Beast’ density in this space is fifty percent.

“Leopardo-sama, Her Majesty the Queen has forbidden any interference with Gene-sama.”

Sein stepped in front of Leopardo, as if to shield me.

“No, you got it wrong. Sharon said not to be rude to Gene. If we both agree and have a light spar, that would not be a problem, right?”

Leopardo grins, eyes fixed on me like he is looking at prey.

This does not look like it will end as a light spar.

“Yes, yes. That is exactly right. In fact, it would be more rude not to witness the ability of such a promising individual, someone Her Majesty deemed worthy of summoning to this country.”

“That is right. Think of it as the Regalia Beastkin Kingdom’s welcoming greeting.”

“DeathDeath.”

The fourth seat, a male hyena beastman. The fifth seat, a male gorilla beastman. The sixth seat, a female hamster beastman, each chime in.

…A hamster beastman!?

The sheer unexpectedness of the species made my reaction lag behind.

It is amazing you managed to become one of the ‘Eight Vassal Beasts’ with that species. Seriously impressive.

“Is that not an excessively arbitrary interpretation?”

“…Tch, you are noisy. You are not in a position to give me orders, are you? Do you understand?”

Sein tries to admonish him, but Leopardo snaps back irritably and shows no intention of backing down.

By the way, judging from his title, Leopardo seems to be a member of the royal family.

In terms of skills and stats, he is quite strong, so being the top of the ‘Eight Vassal Beasts’ is… well, just barely convincing. The fact that Sein seems stronger is a secret.

More importantly, why is this guy picking a fight with me in the first place?

What is the point?

A: First, Leopardo is aiming for the throne. He intends to stage a coup eventually.

A traitor!

A: As groundwork before that, he is plotting to diminish Sharon’s authority. You were summoned by Sharon because your ability was recognized. By thoroughly beating you, he intends to spread the idea that Sharon lacks discernment.

That plan is roundabout!

A: Those behind Leopardo are known as the Leopardo faction, a group that recommends Leopardo as more suitable to be king of this country.

A power struggle!

Huh?

I heard this was a country full of muscleheads, but there is someone pulling sneaky tricks here.

This is nothing but a nuisance.

“Indeed, I am not in a position to command Leopardo-sama, but at least I have the right to voice criticism toward someone attempting to violate a royal order, do I not?”

“Tch, persistent. I am royalty! If I say it is fine, then it is fine!”

Leopardo shouts at Sein, who refuses to back down.

Alright. Leopardo has now been categorized as the type of noble I hate most, the kind who hides behind status to force irrationality.

…And on top of status, he has combat power too, which makes him especially unpleasant.

Leopardo has some interesting rare skills, so I had a bit of interest in him, but now that he is classified as a noble I despise, that interest has almost completely vanished.

“Sein-dono, do I have any obligation to deal with him?”

“No, you do not. Leopardo-sama’s actions go against Her Majesty’s orders. Moreover, even if it were Her Majesty’s order, Gene-sama, as a knight of another country, has no obligation to comply.”

When I ask, Sein shakes his head in response.

Good. Sein seems to possess a sensible mindset.

“Then there is no point in wasting time arguing. Let us go to Queen Sharon at once.”

“Yes, exactly. Let us do so. Leopardo-sama, please excuse us.”

Sein nods, clearly fed up with dealing with Leopardo.

“Hey, are you running away!?”

As we tried to pass by Leopardo, he snapped directly at me this time.

Running away… running away, huh…

“Do not drag me into your petty power struggle. Also, rejecting a claim that lacks legitimacy is not called running away.”

When I said “power struggle”, the air around Leopardo and his group changed.

They must be wondering how someone who just arrived in this country could know that.

“You… what do you know…?”

“I will give you one piece of advice. If you are aiming higher anyway, it is more constructive to think about raising yourself rather than dragging others down. It will serve you better in the long run.”

Trying to lower the opponent’s evaluation to raise your own by comparison is far too pathetic for a so-called Beast King.

“I see! It seems you know things you should not know! In that case, I cannot let you go!”

Killing intent leaks from Leopardo.

Apparently, from Leopardo’s perspective, this was something that even warranted silencing me.

The next moment, killing intent so intense that it drowned out Leopardo’s erupted from deeper down the corridor where he stood.

“T-this is… could it be…!”

“Th-that is impossible…! Why is she here…?”

Both Sein and Leopardo seem to recognize this killing intent.

Incidentally, I already knew from the map.

“Hey, Leopardo. What exactly do you think you are doing?”

Walking slowly down the corridor, overflowing with killing intent, was Sharon, dressed in a pure white gown.

Her tone differs from when we met at the summit. Is that because of a split personality?

“I told you, did I not? Do not be rude to Gene-sama. I even used a royal order that I rarely invoke. …I am not so conceited as to claim that I am adored by all of you. But at least follow a royal order. Otherwise, what is the throne even for?”

Her tone is calm, but her killing intent shows no sign of subsiding.

In fact, Kuroneko had been hiding on the balcony.

I know that when she saw Leopardo confront me, she hurried off to report it to Sharon.

“W-wait… There is a reason for this…”

“Even though it looks like our two wishes might finally be fulfilled, why would you deliberately do something that lowers Gene-sama’s evaluation?”

Ignoring Leopardo’s excuse, Sharon continues advancing.

After closing some distance, she then turned her gaze toward me.

“Gene-sama, welcome. I extend my heartfelt greetings. And I offer my sincerest apologies for the grave rudeness committed by my subordinates.”

With that, Sharon bowed deeply, without regard for onlookers.

Allowing her subordinates to act freely is a demerit, but the fact that she can properly apologize even in public is a major plus.

Normally, for the ruler of a nation to bow in public to a noble of another country (technically, a knight) is difficult and not something easily done.

“No, it was before things escalated, so I am not particularly bothered.”

The first polite speech I have used in several days.

Since there was no actual harm in the end, forgiving Sharon is not a problem.

“I will make a formal apology later. I am terribly sorry, but for now, could you please proceed to the room prepared for our meeting?”

“Will Queen Sharon not be coming?”

“Yes. It will not take long, so please wait a little.”

Ah, she is going to punish Leopardo and the others.

Her killing intent has not subsided at all, after all.

“Understood. Then we will go on ahead.”

“Gene-sama, this way, please.”

At last, we left the balcony, guided by Sein.

— Third-Person Perspective —

After Gene and the others proceeded down the corridor and disappeared from sight, Sharon once again faced Leopardo and his group.

“Now then, Leopardo. You disobeyed a royal order. That means you are suspected of high treason. Do you have anything to say in your defense?”

Still brimming with killing intent, Sharon questioned Leopardo.

“W-wait! I only did that to Gene… ghbuh!?”

Sharon closed the distance in an instant and punched Leopardo in the stomach, sending him collapsing to the ground.

“It is Gene-sama. You were not granted the right to address Gene-sama without honorifics.”

“Guh… I had no intention of being rude to Gene-sama. He is someone Sharon herself summoned, a person of ability. I was just curious and challenged him to a spar. If both sides agree, that is not rude, right?”

Leopardo continues his excuse while crouched on the floor, utterly devoid of dignity.

“I see… So an order like ‘do not be rude’ gets interpreted that arbitrarily… I learned something today. I should have ordered you from the start to not approach him, not interact with him. This is truly disappointing…”

Sharon mutters, sounding deeply disappointed.

“It is unfortunate for Faron, but this one is beyond saving. …Leopardo, I am placing you under arrest for high treason. Of course, I will also strip you of your post as one of the ‘Eight Vassal Beasts’.”

“What!? Do not screw with me! Do not give orders to me, the grandson of the previous king, when you are just from a branch family!”

Leopardo roars in protest, but in truth, that status holds no value.

In the Regalia Beastkin Kingdom, the throne is not a simple hereditary position.

When the previous king passed away, those of royal blood competed in martial prowess, and the most outstanding became the new king.

Therefore, being a direct descendant of the previous king carries no inherent meaning.

Sharon became king three years ago at the age of just twelve by winning the martial tournament.

In the finals, she fought Leopardo, who was twenty-two at the time.

At that point, there was no great difference in their abilities.

Because Sharon won by a narrow margin, Leopardo refuses to concede, believing himself more suited to be king.

“Do you not feel empty boasting about such meaningless past glory?”

“Do not mock me!”

When Sharon sneers, Leopardo, whose pride is immense, boils over.

Despite having lost to Sharon in the martial tournament, Leopardo continues to look down on her even now, and being mocked by Sharon is something he absolutely cannot tolerate.

“No more roundabout nonsense! Right here, I will beat Sharon to death and prove that I am stronger!”

“Stop! Stop! Leopardo-sama, you must not give in to rash anger!”

“Shut up! You all help me too!”

The hyena beastman, one of Leopardo’s subordinates, tries to stop him, but Leopardo, having crossed his boiling point, cannot be stopped.

“Well, well… I suppose it cannot be helped. You two, support Leopardo-sama.”

“Y-you are serious…?”

“Serious DeathDeath!?”

Thus began the battle of Sharon versus four of the ‘Eight Vassal Beasts’.

Strictly speaking, Sharon’s side also has two ‘Eight Vassal Beasts’, but…

“Merci, Kuroneko. Do not interfere, alright? This also doubles as stress relief for me.”

“Understood.”

“As you wish.”

Though they had not participated in the conversation until now, Merci, Sharon’s aide, and Kuroneko, who had reported Leopardo’s actions, had followed Sharon here.

Merci is Sharon’s secretary and bodyguard, a female sheep beastman who also accompanied her to the summit.

She is particularly exceptional in defensive techniques, and combined with her sharp intellect, she is said to “protect the king in both letters and arms”.

Kuroneko is Sharon’s intelligence agent, in other words, Sharon’s eyes and ears.

Though she is an intelligence agent, being one of the ‘Eight Vassal Beasts’ means her combat ability is by no means low. That said, she seems to be better at chaotic melees where anything goes than at one-on-one combat.

Among the ‘Eight Vassal Beasts’, Merci holds the ‘third seat’, and Kuroneko the ‘eighth seat’.

It might even feel insufficient to face the ‘first seat’, ‘fourth seat’, ‘fifth seat’, and ‘sixth seat’ simultaneously, but Sharon declared that no assistance was needed.

“Uooooooooh!”

The skill Leopardo activated was \<Divine Beast Transformation>.

An ultra-rare skill that brings the body closer to that of a beast and greatly increases physical abilities.

Though far rarer than simple \<Beast Transformation>, it is not entirely unique, as others possess it as well.

With Divine Beast Transformation, Leopardo’s form became a golden, shining lion.

Both \<Beast Transformation> and \<Divine Beast Transformation> allow adjustment of how far one approaches a beast form, but Leopardo had transformed into a fully complete lion at one hundred percent.

“Not yettttttttttttttttttttttt!”

Leopardo then activated his unique skill, \<Lion’s Rampage>.

\<Divine Beast Transformation> alone is sufficiently powerful, and \<Lion’s Rampage> can be used in conjunction with it. These two together are Leopardo’s trump cards.

Incidentally, he could not use this combination back when he fought Sharon in the martial tournament, which is part of why he now believes himself stronger and looks down on her.

“You all, let us gooooooo!”

“Yes, yes! We will follow Leopardo-sama!”

The hyena beastman’s unique skill is \<Survival of the Fittest>.

“At this point, we have no choice!”

The gorilla beastman’s unique skill is \<Three Faces, Six Arms>.

“DeathDeath!”

The hamster beastman’s unique skill is \<Cornered Mouse Bites Cat>.

Each of them activates their unique and rare skills at full power and assaults Sharon.

“‘Hard Fist Barrage’!”

“Guwaaaaaah!” x4

Including Leopardo, all four ‘Eight Vassal Beasts’ were defeated.

Not a single speck of blood, not even dust, marred Sharon’s white dress.

**AN:** Using strong characters as disposable pieces is fun (distorted).

In response to the reaction to the previous afterword, I put together a profile.

Name: Rin Shindo

Gender: Female

Age: 13

Race: Human

Notes: Jin’s younger sister. An ordinary girl, for better or worse. Specifically, she always scores exactly the overall average in every subject on tests. Naturally, she is not his biological sister, but a younger sister with no blood relation. She should have been left behind in the original world, yet Jin shows no concern at all about her. The reason is…

An introduction for a (potential) character whose appearance is undecided might be a bit too early.
