# **154: The Beast King and a Wish**

**AN:** This is a dialogue-heavy chapter, but a lot of things move forward.

What surprised me was that someone actually guessed Sharon’s true identity in the comments.

I only reply to comments when I feel like it to begin with, but as a rule, I never respond to plot predictions.

No matter how you look at it, it would just turn into spoilers. That said, writing predictions is perfectly fine. At least, Koda thinks so.

---

Led by Sein, we waited for Sharon in the room prepared for the meeting. Ten minutes passed.

Sharon, having finished purging Leopardo and the others, soon entered the room as well.

“Gene-sama, sorry to keep you waiting.”

“No, not at all.”

I had been checking Sharon’s movements on the map, so I had plenty of ways to kill time.

It was an amusing bit of entertainment, and it really showed how strong Sharon was.

“Sein, sorry, but could you leave us alone? There are some things I don’t want other people overhearing.”

“For safety reasons, I would prefer to have guards present, but considering that you trust this guest so deeply, Sharon-sama, and that guards would be completely useless anyway… I suppose it cannot be helped.”

If we intended to harm Sharon, the number of guards present would make no difference at all.

Leopardo hadn’t understood that at all, but Sein seems to have grasped our combat power to some extent. Experience, perhaps?

“Then please excuse me.”

With that, Sein left the room.

“Here, the soundproofing is solid, and even intelligence-gathering techniques won’t reach us. We can talk freely. It really has been a long time…”

Sharon muttered, sounding deeply moved.

I checked just in case, but the walls were thick and the soundproofing excellent.

There were no windows or proper vents either. It was a room where outside surveillance would be extremely difficult.

“So, may I ask why you summoned us here?”

When I asked, Sharon made a bitter face.

“Could you stop using polite speech with me? When Jin talks to me like that, my skin crawls.”

“So you really are someone connected to me…”

Sharon casually called me Jin.

Just as I thought, she must be someone who had been connected to me in my previous life.

Since there was no longer any reason to hide it in this space, I removed my helmet and showed my face.

“It’s been so long, Jin… But you don’t look surprised at all. How did you figure it out?”

Sharon tilted her head, looking puzzled.

I had already shared my guess with the others, so no one was surprised.

Yes. This is an excerpt from Sharon’s status.

Name: Sharon  

Gender: Female  

Age: 15  

Race: Beastkin (White Tiger, Reincarnator)  

Title: Queen of the Kingdom of Regalia, Dual Personality

A reincarnator who invited me to her country, with a blue marker on the map, of course I would assume she was connected to me in my previous life.

Incidentally, at the leaders’ summit, her marker color had been green. I suspect it has something to do with the title “Dual Personality.”

“Well, if it’s Jin, then nothing that happens, or that he can do, would surprise me.”

“Ah, that’s exactly how someone who knows Master well would react.”

Seeing Sharon’s reaction, Mio nodded in understanding.

…So that’s how I’m seen.

“So then, who were you in your previous life?”

“Hahaha, even Jin can’t tell that much, huh? Well, we never spoke even once in our previous lives, so it can’t be helped.”

“We never talked?”

Someone connected to me, but whom I never spoke to even once.

…I can’t think of anyone.

“There’s no point hiding it, and I want you to know as soon as possible, so I’ll just say it. My previous life’s name was Shiro. The white cat you kept.”

That must have been about eight years ago.

Back when I was in the middle grades of elementary school, I picked up a white kitten that had been abandoned in a cardboard box one day.

It was so weak it looked like it might die, so I helped it, and kept it under my care for a while. In other words, I raised it.

Of course, I was the one who named it Shiro. Everyone I knew said it was unimaginative, but it couldn’t be helped.

At the time, I didn’t have any other pets, so I remember doting on it as my second pet.

Incidentally, Igarashi, also known as Lassie, the Hero, was my first pet. Dora is my third pet.

…The fact that the only “true” pet, meaning non-human or non-humanoid, was the white cat is a secret.

Shiro was a very smart cat.

With the caveat “for a cat”, of course, but there were many times when it really did seem to understand what I was saying.

I spent about a year with Shiro, but to cut to the chase, I eventually had to give Shiro up.

I entrusted it to a reliable acquaintance.

The reason was that my surroundings were getting a bit dangerous, and I could no longer guarantee Shiro’s safety.

At first, Shiro resisted like crazy when we parted, but it seemed to understand my situation. After that, it never came near me again.

Of course, I remember Shiro.

Even after giving it up, I exchanged photos with its new owner from time to time.

“Wait, seriously? You’re really Shiro?”

The status display is convenient and powerful, but even it doesn’t show information about previous lives.

The possibility is incredibly low, but there’s still a non-zero chance that this was someone else pretending to be Shiro.

Well, either way, it would have to be someone connected to me…

“Yeah, it’s me. Proving it is hard, but… ah, that’s right!”

Sharon moved closer and whispered something in my ear.

…

“I see. Only Shiro and I would know that.”

I had no choice but to accept that Sharon really was Shiro.

“Mm-hmm, I’m glad you believe me.”

“I really want to know what you said!”

Sorry, Mio. That’s not something I can tell people.

《I sense a powerful rival…》

And just like that, Dora had recognized Sharon as a rival.

She hadn’t reacted at all to Igarashi (the first pet slot), but Sharon made it into the rival slot…

“So, I’m fine with you being Shiro, but there are a few things I want to ask.”

“I know. Ask me anything.”

Then I won’t hold back. I’ll ask what’s been bothering me the most.

“Why did you die, Shiro? If you reincarnated, that means you died in the original world, right?”

“That’s the first thing you ask?”

“Yeah. If I’m told a precious pet died, of course I’d want to know why.”

I never heard from the acquaintance I entrusted Shiro to that Shiro had died.

Based on what I’ve heard about other reincarnators’ timing, it seems it was the same day we were transferred to this world, so I probably just didn’t know yet, or hadn’t been able to get in touch…

“…I didn’t think just being called a ‘precious pet’ would make me this happy.”

For some reason, Sharon blushed and started fidgeting.

《Hmph…》

And for some reason, Dora was sulking. Jealousy as a pet, perhaps?

I smoothly lifted Dora onto my lap and stroked her as much as I could.

《Ehehe~》

Naturally, Dora immediately cheered up.

“…Hmph.”

This time, Sharon looked slightly displeased as she watched Dora.

“That child… is she your pet now, Jin?”

“Yeah. Her name is Dora. She might not look it, but she’s a dragonkin.”

“The one from the rumors… So she really was connected to Jin.”

It seems word about the dragonkin has spread to some extent.

“But I thought your wyvern was your pet. Looks like my prediction was wrong. That’s unfortunate.”

“Could it be that asking us to come on wyverns was…”

“Yeah. I don’t really want to go back to being Jin’s pet at this point, but as a former pet, I’m technically her senior. I was curious about my junior.”

So that was the reason behind the invitation specifying “please come by wyvern.”

There was no way I could have guessed that.

“Back to the story. As you guessed, I died in the original world. I was hit by a truck.”

“Oh, the classic.”

Mio reacted instantly.

“I saved a child who ran into the road chasing a ball by tackling them out of the way.”

“Oh, it deviated slightly from the classic…”

There are patterns like “saving a cat” or “saving a child”, but “a cat saving a child” feels pretty rare.

“When I came to, I had been reincarnated as a beastkin in this world. At least it was instant death, so I didn’t feel any pain. I don’t regret it.”

“I see. Since you died, I can’t say it’s good, but I’m happy we could meet again.”

“I’m happy too. Talking with Jin like this has been my dream for many years.”

Sharon said that with genuine happiness.

“Since we have the chance, would you listen to my story? I think it will answer several of the questions you have.”

“Yeah, I’d like to hear it.”

There were plenty of things I wanted to know. It was better to hear everything first.

“I was run over by a truck in the previous world, lost consciousness once, and then received a second life in this world as a beastkin. My name was Sharon. As you know, that’s the name of a white tiger beastkin.”

At that point, Sharon’s atmosphere changed.

And the color of her marker on the map changed from blue to green.

“My name is Faron. Sharon’s twin sister.”

Then the atmosphere and marker color returned to normal.

“I was born as Sharon’s twin, but Faron was stillborn. No, to be precise, Faron’s soul entered my body instead of her own.”

“I’m currently living in Sharon’s body.”

I see. That explains the title “Dual Personality.”

It’s less a personality issue and more like having two souls…

“Not long after birth, I realized that, and I decided to hand control of the body over to Faron. Even though I was a cat, I had already lived one full life. I thought it would be better for Faron to live hers.”

“In a sense, my name is also Sharon. Faron was the name our parents gave to my body, which died. To tell us apart, we call each other Sharon and Faron between ourselves.”

So because it wasn’t her actual name, the name in the status didn’t change even when the personality switched.

“I decided to give my life to Faron, but there was one wish I still wanted to fulfill. As I said earlier, it was to talk to Jin.”

“I’ve heard that so many times…”

Faron said, sounding utterly exhausted.

“Ever since my previous life, when I was a cat who couldn’t speak, I wanted to talk to Jin.”

Sharon then shook her head and said, “No…”

“There was just one thing I wanted to say. ‘Thank you for saving me.’ …I finally got to say it.”

Sharon looked completely satisfied.

Being thanked like that doesn’t feel bad, but…

“…Sure, you couldn’t talk because you were a cat, but I knew you were grateful. I mean, you were incredibly attached to me. People used to tell me, ‘Cats normally don’t get that attached.’”

“I-is that so…?”

Sharon fidgeted shyly.

Animals generally didn’t warm up to me easily, but Shiro was a clear exception.

Something acquaintances often said was, “Cats normally don’t shake hands, do high-fives, or stand up.”

…I trained it thoroughly.

“…W-well, anyway. About that dream, I asked Faron to help me fulfill it… but…”

“When she realized it was a different world from her previous life, Sharon’s despair was intense. It was like the end of the world. Literally, since it was another world.”

It’s been a while since I heard one of Sharon’s, or rather Faron’s, lukewarm puns.

“No, Faron’s puns are bad, so let’s drop that.”

“!?”

“And then, after being depressed for a while, I learned about hero summoning from other worlds.”

Ignoring Faron, who momentarily switched personalities just to be shocked, Sharon continued.

“That’s when I thought, ‘Ah, Jin will come.’ So I wished to become strong.”

“That feels like a sudden leap in logic?”

Why would thinking I’d come to another world make her want to become stronger?

“It’s not a leap. My greatest dream was to talk to Jin, but if possible, I wanted to talk to him as an equal. I didn’t want to just be someone protected by him anymore, so I sought power.”

Did that lead to the treatment of “inviting me to the country as Knight Gene”?

Was the overly generous hospitality because she prioritized “being equals” above all else?

“And that was the beginning of grueling training…”

“Fortunately, we had two souls. That meant if one soul slept, the body could stay awake the whole time.”

“It really was… the beginning of grueling training…”

A true black training regimen, literally sacrificing sleep.

That must have been what blossomed Sharon and Faron’s talents.

Faron, in particular, looks a bit traumatized by it.

“Our efforts paid off, and after becoming queen of the Regalia Beastkin Kingdom, we learned that a hero summoning would take place. Knowing Jin, I figured he’d become famous right away.”

“At that time, Sharon was noisy around the clock.”

“That’s why I apologized, right? I admitted I got carried away.”

“She’s usually calm, but when Jin is involved, she goes out of control. I wish she’d stop that.”

Was the punishment of Leopardo earlier part of that out-of-control behavior?

“Really, I’m sorry. …Anyway, back to the story. Even after the hero summoning, Jin’s name didn’t reach us for a while. Then there was the war between Castal and Eldia, and that’s when I first heard the name Queen’s Knight Gene. The moment I did, I knew. ‘Ah, that’s Jin.’”

Every time, people immediately see through my alias.

“After that, we didn’t hesitate to attend the leaders’ summit.”

“The main purpose there was to confirm whether Gene really was Jin.”

“That’s mixing public and private matters.”

If anything, the older sister seems like the airhead, and the younger one the straight man.

Faron’s puns are usually weak, too… Oops, boomerang. …Failed!

“Since I became king for purely personal reasons from the start, it’s a bit late to worry about that, right? I figured having some authority would make it easier to fulfill my dream, so I became king for now…”

“I can’t deny it.”

You don’t just become king “for now.”

“Once we were sure Gene was Jin, all that was left was to set up an environment where we could sit down and talk properly. …Though Leopardo interfered at the very last moment.”

“Stopping an enraged Sharon was the hardest part.”

“At least it seems Leopardo and the others are still alive.”

All four of the ‘Eight Vassal Beasts’ are alive.

That doesn’t mean they’re unhurt. They’re in tatters.

“Since he’s still royalty, killing him would cause all kinds of trouble. But having our reunion with Jin ruined was just unforgivable… Should I go kill him now?”

“Sharon, stop.”

Faron stopped Sharon, who was radiating killing intent from dredged-up memories.

Since Sharon only has one body, it feels like watching a one-person play.

Their voices are slightly different, so it’s possible to tell them apart.

“We gave Leopardo and the others severe punishments. I knew Leopardo was aiming for the throne, but now it’s impossible to prop him up anymore.”

It seems Sharon had seen through Leopardo’s roundabout schemes.

“That’s right. We cut off his tail. …Ah, Jin, you might not know this, but for beastkin in this country, losing your tail after a defeat is the greatest shame.”

I didn’t know that.

In that case, magic or secret medicines that can heal lost body parts would skyrocket in value here.

A: After it became public knowledge that the ‘Divine Medicine Soma,’ which heals lost body parts, drops from a labyrinth boss in the Kingdom of Estea, the number of beastkin challenging the labyrinth suddenly increased. It’s believed to be related.

So that historic discovery (self-staged) affected beastkin as well.

“A warrior who loses their tail is treated as a pathetic loser. Even though Leopardo is feline.”

“Yes, yes. …So Leopardo’s authority has fallen to the ground. As long as he has no tail, he can never become king. For someone as power-hungry as Leopardo, it’s the ultimate punishment.”

Ignoring Faron’s pun, Sharon continued.

“At least while Jin is in this country, we’ll keep Leopardo and the others locked up. I promise we won’t let them make you uncomfortable again. …And if Jin absolutely can’t forgive him, we could force the issue and execute Leopardo. What do you think?”

“Of course, that would definitely cause trouble.”

As Faron added, forcing it would guarantee complications.

And I have no desire to deal with noble-related headaches.

Honestly, since Sharon crushed Leopardo before he accomplished anything, I don’t feel any grudge at all. I can barely even remember his face.

“No, ignoring Leopardo is fine. I don’t hate him enough to want him executed.”

“Is that so? If Jin says so, then we won’t kill him.”

“Honestly, that’s a relief.”

For some reason, Faron looked visibly relieved.

And so, Leopardo narrowly escaped execution. Happy ending? Maybe?

“By the way, there’s one thing I’ve been wondering. Can I ask?”

“Sure, ask anything.”

Anything…

Then tell me your measurements.

A: Starting from the top…

Stop! I’m kidding!

I see. From map information, that kind of thing would be easy to know…

Wait. Does that mean underwear color too?

A: White. It matches the dress.

She answered without giving me a chance to stop…

“Is something wrong?”

Sharon, wearing white underwear, asked when I froze for a moment after that exchange with Alta.

“No, it’s nothing. What I want to ask is about the difference in strength between you two. Sharon, when you fought Leopardo, you were far stronger than Faron when she fought at the leaders’ summit, right?”

I composed myself and asked what I’d wanted to know.

In fact, Sharon and Faron have identical base stats, but only when Faron’s personality is active do her abilities get negative modifiers, like Strength: 255 (-100).

I was a bit surprised when I first saw it. She wasn’t using cursed equipment, nor did she have any skills with negative modifiers.

“As expected, Jin is abnormal in any world. You even noticed that…”

“Just ‘amazing’ doesn’t cover it. It’s scary.”

The two of them didn’t answer my question and instead shared their impressions.

“In a way, it’s obvious. Faron isn’t the original owner of this body. There are many restrictions when she uses it. Simply put, she can’t go all out.”

Having two souls in one body probably isn’t a normal state.

Those negative modifiers must be the side effect.

“Even so, she became strong enough to become king of this country on her own merits.”

“Did you know about the martial arts tournament that decides this country’s king?”

“Yeah, I’ve heard about it. A battle where the entire royal family participates to decide the king, right?”

I answered Sharon’s question.

I learned about it after coming to this country.

“Yes, that tournament. Faron fought from start to finish. She defeated Leopardo, who was slightly stronger than her at the time.”

So it was Young Sharon > Young Leopardo ≥ Young Faron.

“Now, even I could easily defeat Leopardo. Sharon could do it with even more ease.”

So it’s Sharon >>> Faron >>> Leopardo.

“In other words, because he had such a close match with Faron back then, he misunderstood the gap in ability and kept acting selfishly.”

In short, Leopardo equals an idiot who overestimated himself.

“After losing to me in the tournament and failing to become king, Leopardo slackened in his training. If he had kept training, he might have become about as strong as me. His personality is problematic, but I acknowledged his strength. That’s why it’s a shame.”

“It seems Faron grew attached to Leopardo. I said we should crush him early since he looked like he’d rebel, but Faron hesitated…”

“I hoped he would reform someday.”

It seems Faron didn’t hate Leopardo that much.

Perhaps feelings developed through battle.

“But you understand now, right? That this time, you can’t protect him.”

“…I know. With such an obvious rebellion, I can’t protect him. And reform is no longer possible…”

Simply put, Leopardo went too far.

“Well, whatever. Let’s stop talking about someone so unimportant. More importantly, our story is about done. If you have any questions, we’ll take them.”

Harsh toward Leopardo, Sharon wrapped things up.

I understood their history well enough.

Except for one issue that hadn’t come up at all…

“Then I’ll ask one thing. Was the only reason you summoned me to this country because Sharon wanted to see me? Or was there another reason… say, something related to that?”

I pointed to the ground as I spoke.

More precisely, deep beneath the castle. To what exists there…

“Ah, you noticed that too… But watching Jin until now, I can believe you’d notice. That’s what makes you scary.”

“Sharon’s former master, are you really human? Or are people from other worlds all like this?”

“That’s impossible. Jin is the weird one.”

The way Sharon put it, she seemed to be denying my humanity too.

“That’s harsh. …So what’s the answer?”

“Sorry, sorry.”

Sharon’s apology was light.

“The answer is obviously yes. Wanting to see and talk to Jin is my wish.”

“And wanting to save her is my wish.”

Sharon and Faron each had one wish.

“I couldn’t think of anyone but Jin who could do something about that.”

“After hearing Sharon’s story, I thought we had no choice but to bet on that.”

“Please, lend us your strength.”

“Please. We’ll pay anything we can.”

I listened as Sharon and Faron kept switching tones.

“Anything?”

“Anything. Even our chastity is fine. Though we’d appreciate it if you spared our persons. At least until the transfer of the throne is complete. Or would you like to become king, Jin?”

“I don’t want the throne. And shouldn’t you be saying there’s no need for compensation…?”

They’re treating the position of king incredibly lightly.

“We won’t say that. If our wish is fulfilled, neither the throne nor our bodies matter. We won’t act irresponsibly, but it’s not something we’re attached to.”

It was clear they sought the throne only as a shortcut to their wish, not out of attachment to the position itself.

“But is that really okay? Sharon, your wish included being ‘equal’ with me, right? This is clearly a plea from below.”

“Hahaha. Honestly, that part is a bit disappointing. But Faron’s wish is something I can’t ignore either. It’s not important enough for me to insist on it out of stubborn pride.”

Now then, what should I do…

Don’t misunderstand. I’ve already decided to accept their request.

Even I can’t ignore that thing, and it’s not unrelated to me.

The problem is what kind of compensation to ask for.

There’s nothing in this country that’s an appropriate price for dealing with that.

Despite what Sharon said, I have no intention of doing anything to the two of them.

If Sharon wants to stand as my equal, forcing her into subservience would just leave a bad taste.

Naturally, that also goes against my principles.

…Yeah, let’s put that off.

“I’ll accept your request. But I can’t think of compensation right now, so can we decide it later?”

“Jin, thank you so much. Of course, compensation can be decided later. I said we’d pay anything, after all.”

“I thank you as well. Thank you. If this goes well, she can be saved.”

I don’t know what relationship Faron has with the woman sealed beneath the castle, but as I said, I’m not unrelated either.

If possible, I want to gather as much information as I can…

Name: Ulysses  

Gender: Female  

Age: 6810  

Race: High Elf  

Title: Elf Princess Priestess, Elf Royalty, Living Sacrifice  

Skills:

Magic  

\<Spirit Arts LV10> \<Spirit Magic LV10> \<Sealing Arts LV >  

Techniques  

\<Magic Tool Creation LV10> \<Wisdom of the Forest LV >  

Other  

\<Astral Projection LV10> \<Ageless LV > \<Priestess Succession LV > \<Memory of the Earth LV >

No matter how you look at it, she’s the same type as Yuria, who belongs to my subordinate Castal adventurer group.

The same type as that high elf whose background is still unknown.

Stats that clearly indicate involvement.

And above all, I can’t believe this one is unrelated to the strange display on the map.

Earthquake Dragon

Race: Calamity Dragon  

Title: Anti-Existence, Sealed Calamity

What’s strange is that this is all I can read.

No stats. No HP or other parameters are displayed at all.

Even Alta can’t acquire information on it.

In other words, it’s an unknown existence, like the “gray world”.

No wonder Orihara hates it. It’s like a spoiler-killer.

---

Side Story

_* Behind-the-scenes notes and extra stories._

・Dual Personality

In the royal castle of the Regalia Beastkin Kingdom, it is not hidden that the king, Sharon, has a dual personality. More precisely, almost no one in the castle actually recognizes it as a dual personality.

People do notice that her manner of speech changes at times, but her overall behavior and policies never change, and she retains full awareness even of things said to the other personality. As a result, most people just think, “She changes her way of speaking sometimes.”

Sharon and Faron are not truly a dual personality, but possess two souls. However, no one knows this.

As mentioned in the main story, by alternating sleep between the two souls, the body can remain awake with relatively few issues, even without physical sleep. Compared to resting the soul, physical sleep has lower priority.

---

**AN:** It took a long time. Really, a long time before the calamity dragon finally appeared. The calamity dragon had already been planned from the draft stage of the first arc. Details next time!

Since Sharon’s dual personalities share the same voice, if this were an anime, the voice actor would have to work incredibly hard.

+++

# **155: The Calamity God and Subspace**

**AN:** Just because something was considered back in Volume 1 does not mean it will necessarily be active or have a major impact on the main storyline, so please keep that in mind.

---

The seven of us, the six of us plus Sharon, continued to descend endlessly, just endlessly, down the staircase that led deep beneath the royal castle.

“Seriously, it’s so long…”

“And we’re only about two-thirds of the way down, it seems.”

“That can’t be helped. For ordinary people, just getting close to that thing is apparently a tremendous burden.”

In response to Mio and Sera’s muttering, Sharon dutifully replied.

At the end of this staircase exists the “Earth Calamity Dragon: Earthquake”, which emits something like miasma.

In this world, “miasma” refers to a type of magical energy.

However, this “miasma” is a pure aura, or rather a presence, that does not contain magical power. When ordinary people are exposed to it, they feel sick and suffer various adverse effects.

The range of influence of this “miasma” is quite wide. Even though the main body exists deep underground, its effects already begin to manifest around the castle’s underground chambers.

The reason we are unaffected is mental defense from \<Multiple Existence>… that’s not it. There are many categories of beings who are exempt from the effects of this “miasma.”

Transmigrators, reincarnators, Dungeon Masters, dragonkin, those with \<Hero>, those with \<Proof of the Hero>, those with \<Holy-Demonic Smith>, and so on.

In other words, all of us were completely fine.

Huh? High elves? Apparently they’re somewhat better off than ordinary people, but the effects are still far from negligible.

The three members of the ‘Eight Vassal Beasts’ tried to follow Sharon, but once it came to the underground, it seemed to be a domain beyond even the ‘Eight Vassal Beasts’, so they gave up and came to see us off.

“This staircase isn’t hidden. When I looked through the records, it seems to have existed even before the royal castle was built, and there isn’t even a lock on it. Rather, it was apparently as if it were inviting anyone who could enter to do so… and for some reason, I, or rather we, could enter.”

Leaving Faron aside, Sharon is a reincarnator.

Since it’s Sharon’s body, she seems fine even when Faron’s personality is the one at the forefront.

“I don’t really remember the reason anymore, but when Faron was little, she threw a tantrum and ran away from the castle staff. By chance, she found this staircase and just kept going down.”

“I really didn’t want you to tell that story…”

Faron said, looking embarrassed.

“Wondering why no one was chasing her, she kept going further and further down, and then she found her. Ulysses was there.”

“Ulysses was sealed inside a crystal. But her astral body was outside the crystal.”

Deep underground are the completely immobile “Earth Calamity Dragon: Earthquake” and Ulysses, sealed inside a crystal-like mass.

Considering the title “Human Pillar”, she must be serving as the human sacrifice sealing the “Earth Calamity Dragon: Earthquake.”

“Her body was semi-transparent, so at first I thought she was a ghost.”

“And at that time, Faron was so scared she wet herself, right?”

“…It’s Sharon’s body.”

“Huh? Isn’t it a bit cruel to push the responsibility onto me there?”

She must have left her body using the \<Astral Projection> skill.

Incidentally, \<Astral Projection> has a time limit. Roughly speaking, it’s about one hour per level.

The cooldown is 24 hours.

“After we learned that her real body was nearby and only her consciousness was outside, a lot happened and we became close.”

“A lot really did happen…”

That’s a pretty rough summary.

Well, it strays far from the main thread of the story, so it’s not like you have to hear it…

“So basically, you want us to save your close friend Ulysses.”

“Well, to put it simply, yes. To go a bit deeper, I want Ulysses to be rewarded. Because I learned just how unimaginably long she has devoted herself for the sake of this world.”

“The calamity sealed here is called ‘Earth Calamity Dragon: Earthquake.’ A calamity god that governs earthquakes. As long as Ulysses lives, it remains sealed.”

Starting from my question, the conversation shifted toward the topic of the seal.

“I don’t know the detailed history either, but apparently some high elves have the ability to seal Earthquake. However, fundamentally, the seal is only effective while the high elf is alive. If the high elf were to die in an accident or something, there’s a chance the seal would be undone.”

“And so, people long ago came up with something terrifying.”

Faron said this with an extremely unpleasant expression.

I can already guess the rest. Just looking at Ulysses as she is now makes it obvious.

“Sealing her inside the crystal and keeping her alive as a human pillar…?”

“Exactly. Because she can’t move, she can’t kill herself, and she can’t die of old age either. An eternal prison. It’s horrifying that anyone could even come up with something like this.”

It’s as expected, but that doesn’t make the revulsion toward such an act any weaker.

After becoming close to her and then hearing such a story about her circumstances, it’s only natural to sympathize.

“For an ‘Earthquake’ that has to be sealed by such means. Is it really that dangerous?”

Of course, having lived in earthquake-prone Japan, I know well how terrifying they are.

But to be honest, even when told it’s a “calamity god that governs earthquakes”, it’s hard to grasp just how overwhelming it is.

“…Actually, ‘Earthquake’ isn’t in this world right now. By offering herself, Ulysses has isolated and sealed it in a place called subspace.”

Subspace, huh.

In a sense, it’s another world. It has a similar feel to the “Gray World.”

Could this have been Orihara’s next move?

“Its body is still in this world, right?”

“Yeah. If you tried to send all of ‘Earthquake’ to subspace, the burden on the sealer would be far too great. If only the soul is sent, the body won’t go on a rampage, so it’s probably to reduce the load. Although, even when we tried to destroy the remaining body, we couldn’t even leave a single scratch on it…”

So that’s why the body of ‘Earthquake’ doesn’t move at all.

“If Ulysses wants to, she can also send people into subspace. She sent me once, but…”

“You were sent back after three seconds. You really couldn’t do anything.”

“What happened to you?”

To put it bluntly, people don’t die from earthquakes themselves.

An earthquake is merely the trigger. It’s what happens as a result that injures or kills people.

“‘Earthquake’ didn’t do anything to me. It was really just there. And yet, the ground shook, rose, shattered, and then solidified again. Around ‘Earthquake’, the ground is constantly cracking, shattering to pieces, and then solidifying again as ground.”

“If it were just cracks, you might be able to climb out. But if it solidifies immediately after splitting, you’d just get crushed to death. Crushed by rising rock, falling into cracks and dying, or getting pinched by cracks and dying. I think I lasted three seconds pretty well. I really thought I was going to die.”

I can only imagine it, but it truly sounds like a natural catastrophe.

In other words, for creatures that live standing on the ground, there’s basically no chance of winning.

…Hmm?

“There’s one thing I want to ask. When you told us to come riding wyverns, was that so we could fight Earthquake in aerial combat?”

“Huh? …Ah!?”

Sharon looked like she had just realized it.

“Don’t tell me you didn’t actually think that far when you called us?”

“…Yeah, I was only thinking about my own convenience.”

I had assumed that calling the wyverns was meant to fulfill the wishes of both Sharon and Faron, but apparently not.

“I see. If we had wyverns, we might have been able to fight ‘Earthquake’. Should we go back now and get them… Ah! But going down this staircase would be difficult!”

“It’s not that wide a passage.”

In human form it would be fine, but it would be difficult for sky dragons in dragon form to pass through.

“Well, it’s not a big problem, so it’s fine.”

“Huh? It is a big problem, right?”

“No, even without wyverns, flying through the air is easy enough…”

“That’s ridiculous… Ah, right, it’s Jin we’re talking about…”

It’s always a killer phrase, ‘because it’s me.’ When did that happen?

The ‘Undead Wings’ are a labyrinth-produced magical item, so if anything, it’s Higashi’s fault…

Also, if Blue finds out she wasn’t called to a fight we knew in advance would be aerial, she’d either get sulky or cry, so I’d like to call her if possible.

“More importantly, what do you think I should do? Should I go to subspace to kill the soul, or should I do something about the body in this world?”

“It seems the soul is more important. Even if you could destroy the body, the soul wouldn’t disappear, and when the seal is undone, it would rampage even without a body. That alone would easily throw this world into chaos.”

If it were just the body, there was a chance we could have resolved it by putting it into \<Infinite Storage>.

Winning by storage against a calamity god might have been amusing… but no, it’s still kind of questionable.

“Ulysses spent thousands of years in solitude to seal such an existence. She has been saving this world for thousands of years, all while having her mind eroded by ‘Earthquake’s’ miasma… That’s why she deserves to be rewarded. I want to stop living on the sacrifices of Ulysses.”

Faron spoke of her feelings.

I do feel a bit guilty about taking our time before coming to the capital.

Of course, we didn’t know about any of this, so we didn’t do anything wrong…

Still, if they had at least said “hurry”, things might have been different. But if you get an invitation saying “sightseeing is OK”, then of course you go sightseeing. There’s no reason not to.

After continuing down the stairs for a while longer, we finally reached the space where Ulysses is sealed.

It’s only about the size of a small school gymnasium, and at one end we can see the crystal sealing Ulysses.

“Ulysses! It’s me! Sharon!”

After walking a bit and getting reasonably close to the crystal, Sharon called out loudly.

Then, something like hazy smoke emerged from the crystal and quickly began to take on a human shape.

So this is what the activation of \<Astral Projection> looks like.

Mio flinched for a moment, but quickly regained her composure.

Given Mio’s weakness to scary things, I was a bit worried, but it seems to be just barely okay.

The smoke took on the same form as Ulysses’ true body inside the crystal.

Ulysses had the same smooth silver hair as Yuria, reaching down to her waist (a high elf trait?), and wore only a thin, robe-like garment.

Her apparent age looked to be around twenty, and she had a well-proportioned large bust (not monstrous like Sera’s).

Incidentally, since the clothes are thin, it’s kind of dangerous in various ways.

“Oh my, Sharon-chan, it’s been so long!”

Ulysses spoke brightly, like a friendly neighborhood older sister.

…I had imagined a woman with a bit more of a tragic air.

“Ah, it’s been a while.”

“Ulysses, it’s been a while.”

“Faron-chan, it’s been a while too. Are you both doing well?”

“We were doing well. Are you okay, Ulysses?”

The way Faron asked assumed that she wasn’t doing well.

And was checking how bad it was within that context.

“Yes, I’ve been feeling pretty good lately. So I think we can talk until the time runs out.”

Ulysses answered, her expression clouding slightly.

“Sorry. We didn’t come here just to talk today.”

“Oh? That’s a shame… Ah? Now that I look more closely, it’s awfully lively today, isn’t it? Come to think of it, it’s the first time anyone other than you girls has come here, right?”

Ulysses, who until now had only had eyes for Sharon and the others, finally recognized us and looked confused.

She really might have spent thousands of years alone.

There probably weren’t many eccentric people who would go all the way down such an eerie and needlessly long staircase.

“They’re rare people I called, people who aren’t affected by ‘Earthquake’.”

“That’s amazing! So there were others besides you and Faron-chan who could enter!”

Ulysses smiled, looking genuinely happy.

“And they might be able to save you, Ulysses.”

“…”

When Faron continued like that, the smile instantly vanished from Ulysses’ face.

“Faron-chan. I’ve told you many times, you mustn’t think about trying to save me.”

What came from her mouth this time was not the affectionate words she had used before, but a clear rejection.

“But you’ve suffered alone for so long. I want to help you somehow.”

“It’s impossible… You saw it too, didn’t you? ‘Earthquake’ isn’t an opponent humans can defeat. Disasters aren’t something humans should think about defeating in the first place… If peace comes to the world through my sacrifice, then that’s what’s best for everyone.”

Ulysses wore an expression of complete resignation.

“That’s what you say. But we haven’t been thinking about this without a plan. ‘Earthquake’ is certainly an existence beyond common sense. Then all we have to do is prepare an existence beyond common sense on our side. Fortunately, I had someone in mind.”

Sharon said this while looking in my direction.

An existence beyond common sense, Shindo Jin at your service.

“So Ulysses, please. Send them into subspace.”

“I won’t… Defeating ‘Earthquake’ is impossible. If I send your acquaintances into subspace and they die, I couldn’t face either of you. Even when I sent you two before, sending you back was really down to the wire.”

Hmm, this is probably going to take some time to persuade her.

Just as I was thinking that, a report came in from Alta.

A: Analysis of Earthquake and subspace has been completed.

Oh, finally done.

Actually, ever since I recognized “Earthquake’s” existence on the map, I had tasked Alta with analyzing it.

Just like with the ‘Gray World’, it was clear that unknown laws were at work.

A: Sorry to keep you waiting.

No, it’s nothing to worry about.

During the ‘Gray World’ incident, it was an obvious crisis, so I had her analyze it at full capacity. This time, since the urgency seemed lower, I had asked for analysis on the side.

It wasn’t something worth cutting off other support for.

Alright, then. Please explain.

A: Yes. First…

…

I understand.

The ‘Earth Calamity Dragon: Earthquake’ is nothing more than pure malevolence.

In that case, there’s nothing to hesitate about. Let’s crush it with everything we’ve got.

“Ugh…”

Almost at the same time I made my decision, Ulysses, who had been arguing with Sharon and Faron, suddenly let out a groan.

“Don’t tell me! Already!?”

“We put too much burden on Ulysses! We failed!”

“What’s going on?”

Since the two of them seemed to have an idea, I asked.

“Ulysses has been constantly exposed to ‘Earthquake’s’ miasma, and her mind is being eroded. To put it simply, the time she can remain sane isn’t very long.”

“M-miasma, so…”

Faron forced in a joke.

“She said she was feeling good, so we tried asking, but it ended up being more of a burden than we thought, shortening the time she could stay sane.”

“Uaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaah!!!”

Ulysses began screaming, her face contorted in agony.

“Ugh! Uwaaaaaaaaah!!! Uwaaaaaaaaaaaah!!!”

Though in astral form, she flailed her body wildly and rolled around.

Ah, she’s really not wearing panties.

“Ugh… uuu…”

After a while, she went limp and quieted down.

Her astral form slowly began to fade.

“Jin, sorry. We couldn’t persuade her. We won’t be able to meet Ulysses for a while, so let’s come back tomorrow.”

Sharon apologized, but this was unavoidable.

However, I had no intention of waiting quietly.

“No. We’ll finish everything today.”

“Huh? But without Ulysses, we can’t enter subspace.”

“Then we’ll wake Ulysses up.”

Saying that, I approached the crystal sealing Ulysses’ real body.

“W-wait! Jin, what are you planning to do with that crystal!? We couldn’t even put a single scratch on it with our power!”

“Did you try to damage it?”

I stopped and asked.

“Y-yeah. After hearing Ulysses’ story, Faron insisted that we at least destroy the crystal imprisoning her. Even though it would be dangerous if we didn’t do something about ‘Earthquake’, she wouldn’t listen…”

“Sharon helped in the end.”

“…Well, regardless of whether we were going to break it or not, we thought we should at least know how strong it was.”

If they had some basis for trying to break the crystal, that would be one thing, but doing something so risky on a moment’s emotion is dangerous.

“Relax. I don’t plan to break the crystal. If necessary, I’ll put Ulysses back in later.”

With that said, I touched the crystal imprisoning Ulysses.

\<Infinite Storage> activated.

“Maria.”

“Yes.”

The crystal vanished, and Maria caught the falling Ulysses.

“Huh?”

“Maria, strip her.”

“Yes.”

Ignoring Sharon’s dumbfounded voice, I gave Maria my instruction.

While Maria was lifting Ulysses’ clothes, I took out a small vial of my blood from \<Infinite Storage>.

I then dropped a single drop of blood onto Ulysses’ back, which Maria had stripped bare.

\<Slave Art> activated.

Contaminated by miasma and weakened, Ulysses became my slave with barely any resistance.

Alta, I’m counting on you.

A: Yes.

\<Multiple Existence> activated.

Through the mental defense of \<Multiple Existence>, the effects of the miasma vanished from Ulysses.

“U-uhn…”

“Huh?”

Ulysses woke up immediately, while Sharon failed to keep up with the situation.

“W-where am I…? I…?”

“I used my power to take you out of the crystal.”

“What have you done!? If I die now, ‘Earthquake’ will…”

Ulysses shouted, her face pale.

“More importantly, how do you feel?”

“Huh? Ah…? The nausea from the miasma… it’s gone? This is… it’s been six thousand years… My body… This can’t be…”

She looked over her own body in disbelief.

“Sorry, but I’ve made you my slave. And I can protect my slaves. That’s the effect.”

Put simply, the choice is between eternally enduring near-infinite loneliness while being mentally contaminated, or becoming my slave.

I haven’t explained it yet, but there’s telepathy, so the loneliness can be alleviated to some extent.

Even if I fail to defeat ‘Earthquake’, most of Ulysses’ problems will be solved by becoming my subordinate. Except in the case that I die.

“Slave… My head… it’s all mixed up…”

“Sorry, Jin. Please explain.”

Ulysses was confused, and Sharon rebooted and asked.

“Sorry. I only explain this side of things to my slaves or subordinates. Even pets from my original world aren’t exceptions.”

“…Maybe I should swear loyalty to you too, Jin?”

What happened to “equal footing”?

“And now you can no longer refuse my orders. You’ll send me to subspace.”

I thought it was a good tactic to solve Ulysses’ problem while moving the story forward.

“No! Not that! If I do that, Sharon-chan and Faron-chan, my only friends, will hate me!”

“Lord Jin, I will accompany you.”

“If it’s a battle, I would like to go as well.”

“I… I’ll wait so I don’t get in the way… But if Jin-kun wants me to go, I will…”

“For long-range combat, Mio-chan’s bow might get some use?”

《Dora will do her best too. But if Sakura isn’t going, Dora will stay too.》

Ignoring Ulysses’ refusal, the five of them continued speaking as they pleased.

“Sorry, but this time I’m going alone.”

“Again? Master really does like fighting alone…”

As Mio said, I do choose to fight alone fairly often.

I don’t dislike party battles, but fundamentally, I find one-on-one fights more relaxing and preferable.

However, this time there’s a slightly different reason.

“Lord Jin, am I a hindrance?”

“It’s true we can’t deny that we’ve fallen quite far behind Master. But couldn’t you at least take Maria with you?”

Maria wore a pained expression, and Sera asked on her behalf.

“I don’t think you’re a hindrance. It’s just that I’m planning to go all out this time and finish it instantly. If it’s going to be over in an instant, I thought it would be pointless to bring everyone along… Maria, will you come?”

“Yes! I will follow you anywhere!”

In that case…

《Blue, there’s a fight that looks like it’ll be an instant aerial battle…》

《I’m going!》

And with that, I ‘summon’ Blue.

“…Something beyond common sense happened again. Well, it’s fine. It actually gives me more confidence in Jin’s strength. But this is just too…”

It would be quite a shock if Blue suddenly vanished from the stables. I’ll follow up later.

For now, I’ll ignore Sharon’s grumbling.

Thus, the preparations of me, Maria, and Blue in dragon form were complete.

“Ulysses. I’ll let you choose.”

“W-what…?”

Ulysses looked anxious.

“When you send us to subspace, will you believe in our victory and wait as you are, or will you doubt our victory and wait sealed inside the crystal?”

“You can put me back in the crystal!?”

“Yeah.”

I took out the crystal without Ulysses from \<Infinite Storage>.

“A-amazing… Without even an item box…”

“If you think about emergencies, waiting inside the crystal would be safer. However, if I die, there’s no telling when you’ll be able to come out next. Hopefully next time six thousand years will be enough?”

“E-eh…”

Without the protection of the crystal, we can’t prevent Ulysses’ sudden death.

Considering my possible defeat, it would be better for Ulysses to remain sealed.

“Choose. It’s your future.”

“…I’ve had enough.”

After pondering for a while, Ulysses muttered.

“I don’t want to be alone anymore! I don’t want to suffer from miasma! I don’t want to be in pain! I don’t want the feeling of losing myself! Why do I have to go through this!? What did I do wrong!? I didn’t do anything! I was sealed in a place like this without even a chance to do anything! It’s dark! Creepy! I can’t even eat food! Inside the crystal, I can’t sleep, so my consciousness just keeps going on and on! What kind of torture is this!? I told you I didn’t do anything wrong! I couldn’t even make friends for six thousand years until Sharon-chan and the others came! And since the ones who came were girls, romance was just a dream! What is eternity!? When does it end!? Someone! Someone help me!”

Ulysses vented as if a dam had burst.

Even six thousand years’ worth of frustration probably isn’t enough, but let’s end it here.

“Fine. I’ll help you. So send me to subspace.”

“I don’t care anymore! Do whatever you want!”

In her desperation, Ulysses cast \<Sealing Art> to send us into subspace.

We accepted Ulysses’ \<Sealing Art> without resistance and were transferred into subspace.

It seems Ulysses was considerate enough to transfer us into the air, allowing Blue to fly as is.

“It’s exactly as Sharon described.”

I muttered while looking down from Blue as he flew.

However, my muttering was drowned out by the surrounding roar and didn’t reach anyone.

Directly below us was the ‘Earth Calamity Dragon: Earthquake’.

Let’s see, its total length is about ten kilometers?

A: 12.3 kilometers.

Of course Alta would know the exact value.

Unlike the ‘Gray World’, this space has already been analyzed.

Despite having “earth” and “dragon” in its name, its form looks more like a gigantic iguana.

Well, if you consider dragons to be related to lizards, it’s not entirely wrong…

Around this colossal iguana, the ground over an area several times its length, possibly even ten times, was repeatedly rising and collapsing.

The ground would rise and shatter, and the deafening roar would continue unabated, making conversation impossible.

And yet, ‘Earthquake’ itself did not move at all.

Only the ground directly beneath “Earthquake’s” feet did not rise.

Indeed, if something like this were unleashed upon the world, any civilization would collapse in no time.

It’s truly an existence that could be called a living disaster.

Unlike the somewhat underwhelming final trial opponents, its very existence can be said to be a threat to the world.

In other words, it’s no exaggeration to say that Ulysses has been saving the world.

Incidentally, this subspace is a spherical place about ten thousand kilometers in diameter, essentially like a planet.

Within it, there is nothing but ground and sky. There are no people, nor anything that could be called a living creature. Even the sky is obscured by dust clouds created when the ground shatters…

Well then, now that observation is done, it’s about time to send Earthquake on its way.

《Alright then, I’m going to go punch it once.》

《Take care.》

《Do your best.》

Sorry.

I don’t have any personal grudge against you, but your very existence is incompatible with the world.

I don’t know if you have consciousness or ego, but if you do, you can hate me if you want.

I clenched my fist and leaped down from Blue.

The ‘Earth Calamity Dragon: Earthquake’. An attack from directly above, its greatest blind spot.

“Disappear.”

My full-power strike.

If a mere calamity god can withstand it, then go ahead and try.

---

**AN:** Next time: Earthquake dies.

Other planned ones include Volcano, Tempest, and Tidal Wave (major spoilers).

+++

# **156: The Princess Shrine Maiden and the Return**

**AN:** Previously: Jin-kun, unusually, went full protagonist mode. “Earthquake” died somewhere between Chapter 155 and Chapter 156.

---

After finishing the job and returning under my own power, Ulysses was completely spaced out.

Her mouth hung slack in a dumbfounded gape, as if she were embodying the phrase “not all there” with her entire body.

“What’s with her?”

I asked Mio, who was acting as the explainer.

“After she sent Master into subspace, and then calmed down a bit, Ulysses-san completely lost it.”

“She was lamenting that she’d sent you all into subspace in the heat of the moment, and that she should have at least sealed you in a crystal instead”, Sera added.

“Yeah, that figures.”

With Sera’s explanation included, it all made sense.

Acting out of desperation is never a good thing.

“After that, Ulysses-san kept apologizing profusely to Sharon-chan and the others. For some reason, she was panicking because she couldn’t even bring you back.”

“Well, I did resist.”

In fact, I had been hit by Ulysses’ \<Sealing Art>-based return magic, but I intentionally ignored it because it was a hassle.

Or rather, I canceled it.

“Then, after a while, she started panicking again because she said the reaction from ‘Earthquake’ suddenly disappeared.”

“Well, I killed it.”

Since I’d observed it for a bit, it might have taken longer than expected.

“She reflected on her entire life up to now, understood just how absurd Master is, and it seems she completely exceeded her mental capacity.”

“Oh, so that’s why the return magic suddenly cut out. Because of that, I had to come back on my own.”

It wasn’t a big deal for me, but if it had been someone without a way to return, they’d have panicked.

“At least the ‘Earthquake’ that was threatening Ulysses is gone, so there shouldn’t be any problem leaving her alone. If she doesn’t come back after waiting a while, we can just carry her back.”

“By the way, your Special Power level went up again, right? Tell me about it in detail later, okay?”

“Yeah, sure.”

This time, defeating the ‘Earthquake Disaster Dragon: Earthquake’ gave me several things.

One of them was an increase in my Special Power level.

However, there were also many things I didn’t get.

For example, experience points. I didn’t get any at all. None whatsoever.

For example, skills. ‘Earthquake’ apparently wasn’t causing earthquakes via skills, and it didn’t have a single skill.

For example, status. Like the ‘Gray World’ it seemed to be an existence that operated under different rules, and didn’t have normal status values.

It really was exactly what the information shown on the map indicated.

“Sharon, Faron. Can we say that the two of you have had your wish fulfilled now?”

“Of course. After having our wish granted this easily, there’s no way we could complain.”

“I’m truly grateful. Thank you.”

Alright, that completes the request.

Now then, what should I ask for as compensation?

As I was counting my chickens before they hatched, the previously spaced-out Ulysses had somehow regained her senses and started walking toward me. Sharon and the others didn’t try to stop her.

“You’re Jin-san, right?”

“That’s right. My name is Shindo Jin. Just call me Jin.”

Come to think of it, I don’t think I’d properly introduced myself.

“So, Jin-san, I have something I want to talk to you about. An apology, my thanks, and a question. Is that alright?”

“Yeah, that’s fine.”

“First, my apology. I’m sorry for yelling at you with such harsh words earlier.”

With that, Ulysses bowed her head.

Was she talking about when she’d been ranting?

“To be honest, I’ve been enduring something painful for a very long time. It wasn’t something anyone could solve, so I thought there was no helping it, that I just had to give up. …But then, Jin-san, you presented a possibility right in front of me that I didn’t have to give up. I was happy, and sad, and confused, and I ended up acting out of desperation. I’m truly sorry.”

Ulysses bowed again, but being apologized to like that just left me at a loss.

“You don’t need to apologize. To be blunt, I acted that way expecting things to turn out like that.”

“I-is that so?”

“Yeah. I could tell just by looking that you’d been bottling things up. So I deliberately spoke in a way that would corner you a bit, to make you explode.”

Just as I thought, Ulysses had been enduring things right up to her limit, and she exploded.

“For what purpose?”

“For afterward. Ulysses, how do you feel now?”

“…Now that you mention it, I feel a lot lighter in many ways, and refreshed.”

She seemed aware that her mood had cleared to that extent. Good, good.

“After venting all that pent-up frustration at the top of your lungs, and then immediately afterward having the root cause, ‘Earthquake’ be destroyed, of course you’d feel better. If ‘Earthquake’ had been destroyed before you vented anything, I don’t think you’d feel as good as you do now. It’s hard to vent after it’s all over…”

After all, that was six thousand years’ worth of pent-up frustration.

Leaving that bottled up would just cause trouble later.

By venting it and then having the cause disappear at that timing, any later negative effects should be minimized.

“Now that you say it, you might be right. I certainly have grudges against ‘Earthquake’ but more than that, the feeling of having a weight lifted off my shoulders is stronger.”

“Excellent.”

I’m not very good at intricate schemes, but I’m glad this worked out.

“Yes, thank you. Truly. For saving me from six thousand years of hell. For removing suffering that I thought might last forever. …But, I’m so grateful that I can’t even put it into words. What should I do to convey it?”

Ulysses looked genuinely troubled.

Even if she says that, I don’t know what to do.

“That’s it! I should become Jin-san’s wife!”

Nani?

“I was saved by Jin-san, I’m grateful to Jin-san, and when I look at Jin-san my heart starts pounding! This must be love! If I become Jin-san’s wife and devote myself to you until you die, then my gratitude will be conveyed and my feelings of love will be satisfied! Even after Jin-san passes away, if I bear your child, I can continue to devote myself to your descendants forever! How wonderful!”

Uh…

“Human lifespans are only a few decades, so if we’re going to do it, sooner is better, right? But it’s my first time, so will I be able to do it properly? If I say I’ll devote myself but I’m too bad at it, won’t you be disappointed? I don’t want to practice with anyone but Jin-san… Oh! That’s it! I should learn from a professional in that field! If it’s a professional of the same sex, they can teach me how to practice on my own, right?”

…

“Jin, is it really okay to just leave her like that?”

As I moved away from Ulysses and started preparing to return to the surface with Sakura and the others, Sharon asked me.

“She’s your friend, right? You guys deal with it.”

“Well, we’ve never talked about love with Ulysses before. I never imagined she’d turn out like this. It’s a new side of a friend.”

“I said I wanted the love-crazed high elf to be rewarded, not that I wanted her to break.”

This state of Ulysses must have been unexpected for them too.

Neither of them said they’d “deal with it.”

She’d been sealed for six thousand years, after all. She probably ended up with all sorts of hang-ups.

“Isn’t that a bit harsh for a best friend?”

“I wonder where the Ulysses we knew went.”

“That’s, that bad, isn’t it…”

At Mio’s question, Sharon answered with a distant look.

《Master, she’s coming back》

At Dora’s voice, I turned around, and there stood Ulysses, who seemed to have regained her sanity. Or so I thought.

“Jin-san, wait! I’m sorry. It’s my first love, and I got a bit carried away. I really do want to become your wife, but I know it would trouble you to suddenly be told something like that, right?”

“Yeah, it would. And wanting to become my wife doesn’t change even when you’re sane?”

Can you really call that sane?

“That won’t change. Until I die.”

“That’s heavy… Yandere-san, that’s heavy…”

Stop it, Mio! I can kind of tell already, so don’t slap an explicit label on her!

Incidentally, I have absolutely no intention of settling down and starting a family right now.

Even in another world, I don’t intend to bind myself to Japanese law, but I think it’s too early for various reasons, and I haven’t even decided to be buried in this world.

Of course, I’d also have trouble if she just wanted my seed.

I hate irresponsible parents. I don’t want to become one.

“Let’s set aside the wife talk. Since the apology and thanks are done, let me ask my final question.”

“Oh yeah, that was still left.”

The impact of the thanks had been so strong I’d completely forgotten.

“What do you think I should do from now on? Right now, I’ve become Jin-san’s slave, haven’t I? So I thought I should ask you…”

“If you want, Ulysses, you can stay in my country.”

“Ulysses is the benefactor of this country, of the world. We’ll treat you with the utmost respect. You could bow to Jin and ask him to cancel your enslavement.”

Before I could answer, Sharon and Faron asserted themselves.

This time, enslaving Ulysses wasn’t because I wanted to add her as a subordinate, but because it was convenient in various ways.

I hadn’t told her anything that would really be a problem if it got out, so if Sharon and the others wanted her freed, I wouldn’t mind.

“Sharon-chan, Faron-chan, I’m very happy about how you feel. …But honestly, I don’t want to stay in this country. Even though I vented my frustrations, this country, this land, has too many unpleasant memories.”

“That hurts to hear.”

“Yeah. Considering Ulysses’ peace of mind, it might be better for her not to stay in this country.”

If she lived here, especially on top of ‘Earthquake’ there was a chance her frustrations would build up again.

By the way, the basement floor we’re standing on right now is also part of ‘Earthquake’s back.

Oh right, I didn’t mention it, but the body of ‘Earthquake’ underground is being left as is for two reasons.

The first reason is safety.

Removing a giant body ten kilometers in diameter without any preparation is far too dangerous. In the worst case, the surface might collapse.

The second reason is food-related.

The reason crops grown in this country were so delicious was actually because of ‘Earthquake.’ Just by existing, ‘Earthquake’ seemed to enrich the soil with nutrients.

There’s no way I, of all people, would do something that ruins a tourist attraction’s specialty products.

“And I don’t intend to stop being Jin-san’s slave either. Being a slave who can stay by the side of the person she loves and devote herself to them is a wonderful position. There’s no way I’d give that up easily!”

She hadn’t regained her sanity at all.

Hey, Maria over there. Don’t nod along in agreement.

“Hahaha, it seems the Ulysses we knew is gone.”

“That’s sad. Truly sad.”

Faron looked genuinely sad.

“Ulysses, it’d be difficult for you to stay by my side.”

“Eh? Why?”

“I have several bases, but basically I travel and do sightseeing all over the place.”

“Then I’ll travel with you.”

“I have many slaves and subordinates besides you, but I only treat those five over there as special. My policy is to not increase the number of regular travel companions.”

There are many people I act with temporarily, but the fixed members are only those five.

“In that sense, we’re quite fortunate, aren’t we?”

“Yes… We get to stay with Jin-kun all the time…”

“I’m truly happy.”

《With Master!》

“I do feel a little sorry toward the others.”

“I’m envious that you can stay together all the time, but as a riding dragon, I’m still better off than most.”

Incidentally, the Sky Dragon is my riding dragon, but not a fixed member. I always call her when traveling through the air, though…

“No! I want to go with Jin-san too!”

Ulysses refused to give up.

“There’s no actual hard limit on numbers, so it’s not that I absolutely can’t add anyone… But if I did, there’d be a lot more subordinates who’d want to travel with me.”

Even if they don’t say it openly, the number of potential applicants would be absurd.

“…Then if I become overwhelmingly the number one among those many slaves, will you consider taking me with you?”

“I wouldn’t say I won’t consider it, but there are so many that it’d be difficult.”

“It’s fine. I’m actually quite multi-talented.”

Yeah, looking at her skill list, I can tell she’s multi-talented.

She has Unique-class skill-type abilities, after all.

“Ten or twenty people? Or a hundred or two hundred? Becoming the best among uneducated slaves isn’t that difficult!”

“No, there are like ten thousand, twenty thousand subordinates.”

“Huh?”

Sorry. The scale’s different.

Just my believers alone number ten thousand. Adding those sent to the Brown Wall Kingdom puts it over twenty thousand.

“And just so you know, all ten thousand of those can read, write, and do arithmetic, and they all have some kind of skill.”

“Huh!?”

The believers are highly motivated, and many learned reading, writing, and arithmetic after becoming my subordinates.

Most of my subordinates possess some kind of skill-type ability and contribute to the expansion of my power.

They’re far removed from the image of “ordinary slaves” that Ulysses has.

“Sera-chan, what are slaves again?”

“A collective term for specialists who serve Master.”

“Hasn’t the concept of slaves completely collapsed for you two…?”

A group with architectural maids and construction maids, running a trading company independently of me, with each individual possessing combat power on par with S-rank adventurers.

Slaves…!?

“…Th-that’s a joke, right?”

“I do joke around, but I rarely exaggerate small things into big ones.”

I love joking, but I don’t make things sound bigger than they are.

“…I-I’ll do it! Ten thousand or twenty thousand, I’ll produce results, rise to the top, and prove I’m worthy to stand beside you, Jin-san!”

“If you’re prepared, I won’t stop you. I won’t play favorites, though. Do your best.”

“Yes, I’ll do my best! I’ll make you acknowledge me through my own power!”

Ulysses truly doesn’t give up.

Honestly, it’ll be a harsh and difficult path, but it’s probably better than six thousand years of loneliness and suffering?

Since there was no longer any reason to remain here, we left the basement and started climbing the stairs.

As expected, six thousand years of sealing was no joke. Ulysses had difficulty even moving her body, and we had to take many breaks on the way back.

Speaking of returning, the number of people going and coming back differed by about two. Blue and Ulysses.

How should we explain that…

“Sharon, I’ll leave it to you.”

In times like this, it’s best to dump responsibility on the person in charge.

“Eh… just dumping it on me like that… Well, we’re the ones who asked you to save Ulysses, so I guess it can’t be helped.”

“Sharon, I’ll leave it to you.”

“Faron, you too…?”

And so, Sharon alone ended up drawing the short straw.

Is Faron just more capable, or is Sharon naturally someone who attracts hardship…

We finished climbing the stairs while chatting idly.

“Welcome back, Sharon-sama. Sein-sama asked me to pass on a message that he has something he’d like to report once you returned.”

A soldier who’d been waiting at the entrance because Sharon had gone underground spoke.

“Oh, got it. I’ll head over now. The office, right?”

“Yes, he’s waiting in the office. He also said it concerns Jin-sama and the others, so he’d appreciate it if you could come together. Apparently it’s about Jin-sama’s riding dragon…”

Ah, probably about ‘summoning’ Blue.

“Jin-sama, would you come as well?”

“Yes, I’ll go.”

In front of unrelated people, I have to speak politely.

“…Excuse me, but it seems there are people here whom I didn’t see on your way down.”

“Oof…”

A diligent, excellent soldier, noticing even the small details.

Alright, Sharon, what are you going to say?

“By royal order! This matter is to be kept confidential!”

“Yes, sir!”

She forced it through!

She used the royal order she said she “rarely uses” in her conversation with Leopard!

“…”

“…”

“…”

“…”

“…”

“…”

“…”

“…”

“I couldn’t help it! I couldn’t think of a good excuse!”

On the way to Sein, Sharon finally made excuses after succumbing to our silent pressure.

“I won’t say it was bad, but I’m a little disappointed.”

“Sharon-chan, couldn’t you have tried a bit harder?”

“As your twin sister, I’m ashamed.”

“T-that’s cruel…”

“Oh, she retreated.”

It seemed Sharon had transferred control of the body to Faron and shut herself away.

“Still, the surface after six thousand years feels wonderful. Even without the miasma, being underground all the time really weighs on you.”

Stretching, Ulysses enjoyed being back in the open world.

“By the way, why were you sealed underground in the first place, Ulysses? It’s not like you were born inside a crystal. There must’ve been some reason.”

“Ulysses, I want to know too.”

“Faron, you didn’t hear? You’ve known her for a long time, right?”

Given how much they cared about Ulysses, I thought they might know the details, but…

“I heard a little. But before the seal was broken, I couldn’t ask anything too deep.”

“Now that you mention it, that makes sense.”

They say talking about painful things makes it easier, but for Ulysses, who had no hope of relief, it’d be cruel to deliberately make her recall them.

She didn’t talk about it herself either, so not asking was the right call.

Of course, now that it’s over, I’ll ask without mercy.

“If Jin-san and Faron-chan want to hear it, I don’t mind talking, but it’ll be long, so I think it’d be better to do it later when things have settled down.”

“If it’ll be long, summarize it briefly.”

Preferably in about three lines.

“Th-that’s a bit difficult…”

“Then explain it in detail later.”

“Alright. Then let’s talk later.”

“I’ll listen too. We’re already at the office.”

And so, we quickly arrived at the office where Sein was waiting.

“Oh, welcome back, Sharon-sama. While you were away, several matters requiring reports have arisen. …By the way, who are those two? I don’t believe they were present when you went underground.”

Of course an excellent butler like Sein would notice.

Alright, Faron, what kind of explanation will you give?

“Do not pry into those two. Treat them as my guests, just like Jin and the others.”

“Understood.”

Well, at least she didn’t use a royal order like Sharon did.

Not exactly a skillful explanation, though…

“Now then, I will proceed with the reports. First, one riding dragon that was entrusted to us by Jin-sama has gone missing.”

“No problem. Jin-sama knows its whereabouts. No action or inquiry is necessary.”

“Understood.”

Sein didn’t pry any further.

From the perspective of someone like me with many secrets, he’s very easy to deal with.

“Second, Leopard-sama has escaped. Members of the Leopard faction were manipulating things behind the scenes. We are currently searching, but several castle personnel have already been killed.”

“What!? Is that true?”

“Yes, regrettably…”

Actually, Alta had already told me the details.

After Sharon went underground, members of the Leopard faction saw it as an opportunity and bribed the jailer.

They freed Leopard and planned to have him lie low for a while.

However, when one subordinate noticed Leopard’s tail had been cut off, they looked at him with disappointment.

That enraged Leopard, who killed the subordinate on the spot, then killed the jailer.

He killed soldiers who rushed over after hearing the jailer’s scream and fled, rampaging through the castle…

-BANG!!!-

“Foouuund yooouuu!!! Shaaaaron!!! I’ll kiiill yooouuu!!!”

And that’s how he ended up bursting through the office door.

Leopard had transformed into a golden lion via the \<Divine Beast Transformation> skill.

On top of that, the simultaneously activated \<Lion’s Rampage> caused black stripes to appear on the golden lion.

\<Divine Beast Transformation> and \<Lion’s Rampage> are a composite skill that’s difficult to activate simultaneously, but incredibly powerful if successful.

As a result, his speech has become somewhat incoherent.

Furthermore, he’d consumed a secret stash of doping drugs, granting him tremendous power for a short time. Naturally, the side effects are severe. Very severe.

In other words, he’d thrown all caution aside and focused solely on killing Sharon.

In Leopard’s beastly eyes, only Sharon was reflected, filled with hatred.

However, there was someone just as enraged as Leopard, if not more so.

“Like, I, already, saiddddd! Why do you always get in my way!? I declared I wouldn’t let Leopard-related matters make Jin uncomfortable! Why do I have to go back on my word the very same day!?”

It was Sharon.

She’d retreated deep within Faron, but her anger had forced her back out.

Indeed, Sharon had said she’d lock Leopard up and never let him appear before me.

Because of Leopard, Sharon was forced to go back on her word to me twice.

And this was right after Ulysses had been saved and everything felt like a happy ending.

“Shut uuup!!! If yooou weren’t heeere…!”

“You’re the one who should shut up!!!”

Enraged, Sharon attacked without letting Leopard finish.

Sharon’s form had changed into that of a beast, similar to \<Beast Transformation> or \<Divine Beast Transformation>.

However, rather than becoming a complete beast like Leopard, she was in a bipedal, beast-like state.

Her overall silhouette remained humanoid, allowing her to move as usual while greatly enhancing her abilities. It was the most practical transformation state.

To clarify, this was neither \<Beast Transformation> nor \<Divine Beast Transformation>.

The skill’s name was \<White Tiger>.

An ultra-rare, race-exclusive skill that manifests only in extremely, extremely, extremely rare cases among White Tiger Beastmen.

Simply put, it’s far stronger than \<Divine Beast Transformation>.

This should’ve been Sharon’s trump card, but in her rage, she’d lost the ability to judge properly.

She even called me “Jin” earlier…

-KRUNCH!!!-

“Gubeh!?”

-BOOM!!!-

In short, \<White Tiger> Sharon’s punch hit Leopard square in the face, sent him flying, smashed through a wall, and dropped him onto the balcony.

Ah, the balcony from when we first entered the castle. Is this what they call karma?

“Don’t let him escape!!!”

Sharon jumped down after Leopard through the hole he’d made.

Well, escape or not, you were the one who sent him flying…

Looking down through the Leopard-shaped hole, I could see Leopard collapsed and Sharon approaching to deliver the finishing blow.

This was bad.

“Maria! Stop her!”

“Yes!”

I gave Maria instructions.

Maria’s more dexterous, so she’s better suited to stopping Sharon while protecting Leopard. Me… my actions tend to have collateral damage…

Maria jumped down through the Leopard hole.

Wearing a maid outfit, she firmly held down her skirt as she leapt.

-SLAP!!!-

She caught Sharon’s punch aimed at Leopard with her palm.

She was also subtly protecting Leopard with \<Barrier Arts> so he wouldn’t die.

“Sharon-sama, please stop.”

“You’re… Mari… Maria-san, right? Why are you stopping me?”

Sharon asked Maria, her anger still present.

“This is a message from Jin-sama. If you’re going to kill him anyway, he says to let us do it.”

“Huh?”

Sharon’s rage dissipated completely.

Well, I’m not saying we absolutely have to kill him, but if we do, we want the rare skills, right?

---

Ulysses-san is an easily infatuated, easygoing heroine.

She fell in love just from being released from a mere six thousand years of sealing.

Next time, the duel event. The title is “Public Execution and the Sword of Light.”
