# **157: Public Execution and the Sword of Light**

**AN:** A duel event. To put it bluntly, it is playing around.

---

In a sense, it has become something quite rare.

“Oy, if I really beat the hell out of that little brat, my sentence will be reduced, right?”

“Yeah. I swear it as the king of the Kingdom of Regalia Beastmen. However, in this duel, you have no right to surrender. Of course, she does have the right to surrender, so if you attack her after she surrenders, you will be judged the loser, and your execution will be confirmed.”

“Tch… So you’re planning a public execution rather than a duel. Still, having such a little brat as my opponent means you’re really underestimating me.”

“I’m a little brat too, you know. Leopardo-kun, who lost to me.”

“You bastard…”

The ones talking on the balcony are Sharon and Leopardo.

Leopardo is restrained, but he has been given \<Healing Magic>, so he has recovered considerably.

However, the nose that was crushed by Sharon’s Punch has not returned to normal.

What is about to begin is the duel between Leopardo and Maria.

No, that’s wrong. It is the public execution of Leopardo by Maria.

One hour earlier.

Just after Maria stopped Sharon.

“Are you serious? You’re going to use the price for rescuing Ulysses on something like that…”

“Yeah, I’m serious. If possible, I’d like to ask for a bit more, too.”

“Of course that’s fine. I don’t think the price can be fully paid with just that anyway…”

After descending to the balcony, I asked Sharon to let me duel Leopardo as part of the price for rescuing Ulysses.

Due to the series of events starting with the jailbreak, Leopardo is now in a situation where nothing but the death penalty is possible.

Royal blood or backing does not matter. After going that far, anything other than execution is impossible.

Therefore, even if Sharon were to kill Leopardo here, there would be no one who could openly complain.

However, since his death is already confirmed anyway, it would be a waste to let Leopardo, who possesses multiple rare skills, die as is.

It would be only natural to want him to be killed by me or someone connected to me, and become valuable skill points.

I also considered making Sharon my subordinate and then having Leopardo executed to obtain the skill points, but I rejected that since I have no intention of making Sharon a subordinate against her will.

Sharon seems to want an equal relationship with me, and I want to respect that.

I also considered obtaining skill points as the executor of the execution, but I rejected that since it’s not my hobby.

In the end, I decided to finish Leopardo in a duel and obtain the skill points.

The question was who would fight him.

“Jin-sama, please leave it to me.”

While Sharon was running around to fulfill my request, we discussed who would fight Leopardo.

Since it was only insiders, we used real names.

“Alright, let’s leave it to Maria.”

“Yes!”

We decided to leave it to Maria.

“You’re leaving it to her there!? …Ah? Come to think of it, Maria-san seems to handle quite a lot of duel-related things. Rather, I’ve hardly ever dueled at all.”

Now that it’s mentioned, Maria has kind of become the one in charge of duel events.

Of course, Sera is strong as well, but Sera is tall, so she has a certain imposing presence.

If we’re going to have a duel anyway, it makes for a better picture if someone without visual impact shines. If Sera fights, there’s little surprise, but if Maria fights, there is surprise.

Because of that, it’s also kind of unfortunate that Sera’s duels, which lack surprise, never happen…

“There’s also a serious reason. Since we’re killing Leopardo in a duel, some resentment will probably be directed our way, and there’s a possibility of more trouble. In that case, it would cause less backlash if he’s killed by a fellow beastman, even if from another country, rather than by a knight of another country. A perfectly valid reason.”

Even if onlookers try to say something after the match, if they’re told it was the result of an unarmed fight between beastmen, they would have no choice but to shut up. It’s much better than a knight doing it.

That said, Leopardo’s faction is practically annihilated, so whether there’s even a need to worry about it is debatable…

“I’m sorry if this causes more trouble for Maria…”

“Please don’t worry about it.”

She even seems to be happy to take on trouble for my sake.

Since this was my idea in the first place, she seems extra motivated.

“Come to think of it, this is the first time I’ve proposed a duel myself.”

Even though the purpose is execution in the form of combat rather than showing off power, this really is the first time I’ve proposed a duel myself.

Of course, that’s only if calling a public execution, where the final outcome is already decided, a duel is allowed.

“By the way, given your philosophy, you’re usually not interested in events involving arrogant nobles, right? Then why are you deliberately starting an event yourself?”

“No, Leopardo is already a criminal whose execution is decided. There’s no reason to treat someone like that as a noble, right? In other words, the current Leopardo is just skill points. And this isn’t a duel with a noble, it’s just an event solely to obtain skill points.”

I answer Mio’s question with my reasoning.

“Master is treating a person as skill points.”

“There’s no need to treat someone properly if they’re not decent, right?”

“Master, you’re incredibly harsh toward those you consider below the standard of ‘decent.’”

Someone who is neither decent as a person nor interesting, and whose only slightly interesting aspect is the skills they possess, gets treated as skill points.

Leopardo fits that perfectly.

In the Kingdom of Regalia Beastmen, duels are not particularly rare.

Originally, it is a nation led by beastmen, a muscle-brained race, so there is a tendency to value physical strength over debate.

Duels were held to stake things neither side could give up, to clearly determine who was stronger, or to force the other side to listen through strength.

As such, in this country, duels are recognized as “relatively major spectacles.”

Naturally, a duel that may be the last for Leopardo, the former ‘Eight Vassal Beast’, draws attention.

Sharon said that there were an extremely large number of requests to watch, but I have no intention of turning killing into a spectacle, so I flatly refused everyone.

As a result, only the minimum necessary personnel, besides those involved, are present on the balcony.

“Don’t worry. As you requested, Jin, I’ve issued a royal command completely banning entry into this area.”

“You say that, but there were already two violations of royal command just today.”

Since Sharon said it so confidently, I decided to interrupt.

Also, whatever happened to that declaration about rarely using royal commands?

We are currently preparing for the duel, with the balcony divided between Leopardo and us.

On the side where Sharon and I are, there are no unrelated people, and they are mostly there to monitor Leopardo.

“Ugh…! D-don’t worry. Taking Leopardo’s case into account, I made sure to threaten that anyone who violates a royal command next time will have their entire family executed.”

“Without me noticing, Sharon has become a tyrant…”

A tyrant-type beautiful girl with a split personality beast king. This might be a new character archetype.

“Sharon is seriously bothered by the fact that she ended up lying to Jin.”

Faron offers some follow-up.

Faron and follow-up look similar in writing. Completely irrelevant.

“When Jin goes back, I plan to crack down on Leopardo’s faction with full force. They went too far. And frankly, I’ve reached the limit of my patience.”

“All I can say is good luck…”

Sharon is smiling, but her eyes are not.

Joking or not, Sharon will carry out what she said.

Of course, it’s outside my sphere of interest.

“More importantly, can Maria-san really beat Leopardo? I declared in the king’s name that if Leopardo wins, his sentence will be reduced…”

At that point, Sharon’s interest shifts to Maria.

Despite the fact that the duel is about to begin, Maria shows no sign of tension and remains in her maid outfit.

Seeing that, Sharon seems to feel a bit uneasy.

“That level of opponent poses no problem at all. Borrowing Mio-chan’s words, it’s ‘a piece of cake.’”

《Dora, is getting hungry.》

It’s almost time for dinner.

“You’re very confident. …You stopped my fist while I was beast-transformed. I know you’re strong. But was it really necessary to heal Leopardo beforehand?”

Leopardo has been given \<Healing Magic>. We also properly removed the side effects of the doping. One cast of ‘Refresh’ was enough.

After waking up from unconsciousness, Leopardo was puzzled at first, but once he heard about the duel, he stopped caring about that.

Doping in a duel is nothing but tasteless.

“If we’re going to call it a duel, I want to do it under conditions as fair as possible.”

“I get how you feel.”

“Hmm, I don’t really get it. If you have an advantage, I think that’s fine…”

It seems Faron and Sharon have different sensibilities.

In Sharon’s case, since she is originally a cat, she has almost no concept of fair play, and she seems to have trouble understanding the act of giving up an advantage.

On the other hand, Faron, as she showed in the mock battle with the Hero in the Elgant Theocracy, tries to fight under conditions as equal as possible. She does not hold back, but instead tries to match conditions.

“By the way, what do you do when the two of you disagree?”

The one who answered my question was Sharon.

“Basically, we prioritize Faron’s opinion. Right now, Jin is with us, so I’m taking the lead, but normally Faron is the main one. I don’t intend to do anything that deviates greatly from her way of thinking.”

“If it were the usual me, I wouldn’t have beaten Leopardo so badly.”

“That’s because Leopardo was the one who broke a royal command. I’m not apologizing for that.”

Sharon seems to cherish Faron, but when it comes to Leopardo, she shows no mercy.

“Oh, looks like preparations are almost done.”

Preparations refer to things like deploying personnel to prevent Leopardo from escaping, and moving the monsters that Kuroneko has tamed and that are being kept on the balcony to another location.

“Seems so. Maria, it looks like it’s almost your turn.”

“Yes.”

《By the way, Jin-sama, may I finish that person instantly? Or should I lower my status as much as possible and use it as training?》

Since Sharon is present, we discuss status-related matters via telepathy.

Given the overwhelming difference in status, if she fights normally, it will end instantly.

In such cases, sometimes one lowers their status to be closer to the opponent’s, or even lower, in order to learn techniques that do not rely on status.

《Leave it to you. If it seems like good training, lower your status. Otherwise, an instant kill is fine.》

《In that case, I intend to decide it in the initial exchange.》

《Yeah, do that. …If you want, you can even use that as practice.》

《Is that really okay? You won’t keep it secret?》

As Maria says, that is probably something that should normally be hidden, but for some reason, I don’t feel that way this time. Why is that?

《Yeah. Rather, using it in public might be beneficial later. …Probably.》

《Understood.》

What is that, you ask?

Well, that.

“Then, we would like to begin the duel between Lady Marie and Lord Leopardo.”

The one managing the proceedings is Sein.

Somehow, he really looks like he fits the role of moderator. Like he’s used to it…

Leopardo’s restraints have already been removed, and he is facing Maria one-on-one.

“Are the rules confirmed?”

“Yes, no problem.”

“Yeah, I get it. Only that little brat can surrender. Weapons are prohibited, beast transformation is allowed, magic is allowed, no time limit… right?”

Weapons were prohibited so that if Leopardo attempted to escape, there would be no additional casualties. Even if he doesn’t look skilled with weapons, even throwing one randomly would be enough to make it a deadly weapon.

Maria was also checked, and it was confirmed that neither side was carrying weapons.

“Yes, that is correct.”

“Then let’s get started already. …But before that, let me say one thing. Hey! You, little brat!”

Saying that, Leopardo points at Maria.

“Yes?”

“You’re probably strong, right? This isn’t some situation where a joke kid would come out.”

“Please use your imagination.”

“Hah! If that weren’t the case, there’s no way you’d come out as the opponent of someone whose execution is already decided!”

He’s surprisingly able to judge things calmly.

Even if my evaluation of him goes up a little now, it changes nothing.

“But! Don’t think you can kill me that easily!!! GUGAAAAA!!!”

Leopardo activates his specialty skills \<Divine Beast Transformation> and \<Lion’s Valor> simultaneously, transforming into a golden lion. A 100% beast state.

He must have judged that there would be no time to leisurely transform after the match began.

“Now, start already…”

Due to the effects of the combined skills, Leopardo urges them on with distorted intonation.

“…Very well. Are both of you ready?”

“Yes.”

“Yeaah.”

“Then… begin!”

“GUGAAAAA!!!”

At Sein’s signal, Leopardo roars and leaps at Maria.

Leopardo swings his claws down at Maria.

-DOOOOM!-

As expected, Maria evades, and the claws shatter the stone pavement.

It’s an attack with enough power to create a crater where the claws struck. If it hit directly, it would be disastrous (generally speaking).

“You’re a nimble one! But I’m confident in my speed too. GURUAH!!”

Saying that, Leopardo approaches Maria again.

This time, instead of leaping, he moves his legs quickly, apparently aiming for a series of attacks.

“GAA! GURUAH! GOAA!”

He swings his claws, tries to bite, and aims for a body slam.

Each strike seems weaker than the first, but given Leopardo’s high physical ability as the base, it would still be disastrous if any hit (generally speaking).

“You’re not even using a single feint?”

“What!?”

Maria slips inside while avoiding the claws swung at her.

Then, grabbing Leopardo’s arm (foreleg), she throws him with a powerful shoulder throw.

“GYA!”

-THUD!-

Leopardo slams into the ground on his back and lets out a groan of pain.

“Guh… damn it…”

Leopardo staggers to his feet.

It looks plain, but that shoulder throw just now had tremendous power. Rather than throwing him away, it was a clean vertical slam aimed at smashing him into the ground.

“You didn’t even take any ukemi… There’s nothing to be learned from this fight.”

Maria says calmly, and honestly, I agree.

When Leopardo was thrown, he couldn’t react at all and was simply slammed.

Someone trained in martial arts, or even a wild beast, would try to take ukemi and reduce the damage as much as possible.

According to what Sharon told me, Leopardo climbed this far purely on his raw physical ability. He did strength training, but never trained in martial arts.

Because of his tough body, even taking attacks resulted in little damage, and he could brute-force most things with power alone, so he never realized the importance of ukemi.

On top of that, since he lacks the wild instincts of a normal beast, he couldn’t react instinctively either.

The half-baked Leopardo is “not accustomed to preventing large damage.”

For a martial artist or a beast, this would be training, but against a half-baked opponent who only has high status, there is very little to be gained.

“There’s no reason to drag out a fight that offers nothing in front of Jin-sama. Let’s end this.”

Maria has decided there is nothing more to gain from fighting Leopardo and moves to finish it.

“Don’t underestimate me!!!”

Leopardo leaps again.

Beast attacks are troublesome in terms of speed and power, but since their attack methods themselves are limited, they are easy to deal with for someone with technique.

That said, Leopardo’s attacks are more compact than before, showing that he is wary of the shoulder throw.

He does seem to learn something, but it’s still not enough.

Originally, he should cancel the 100% beast transformation and shift to something like 80% beast transformation, which is almost humanoid. That would increase his attack variety and make it more of a fight.

Of course, that would be betting on Maria not pursuing him during the transformation…

Maria, who has completely lost interest in fighting Leopardo, mutters.

“\<Kusanagi Sword>”

With Maria’s murmur, shining swords of light appear from both of her hands.

-GAKIN!-

“What!? Guh!”

She blocks Leopardo’s claws with the swords and then kicks his exposed abdomen.

“A weapon!? You checked for weapons! Don’t tell me you tricked me!”

Leopardo roars after creating distance.

“This is a weapon created by my magic. I did not bring it in.”

\<Kusanagi Sword LV >

Creates a sword made of light (indestructible, effective against demonkind and monsters). The number is unlimited. However, it disappears if not held by the user. It can also be activated layered over a normal weapon, in which case it increases attack power and grants effectiveness against demonkind and monsters.

\<Kusanagi Sword> is a skill that appeared when Maria’s \<Hero> skill reached LV7.

Unlike the skills that appeared with previous \<Hero> level-ups, it seems to be a unique skill without a level.

Even by my estimation, I thought it was about time for a decisive, Demon King-killing skill to appear.

The \<Hero> skill leveled up when we defeated the “Earth Calamity Dragon: Earthquake.”

I thought we still lacked skill points, but they suddenly increased and caused a level-up. Perhaps that counts as “hero-like behavior”.

For the record, regarding the \<Hero> skill, I do not allocate points to raise its level, instead leaving it to Maria to raise it naturally.

Special skills like \<Hero> are best left untouched as much as possible.

“That’s still cheating!”

“The use of magic is not prohibited. And what was prohibited was bringing weapons in. Their use was not prohibited from the start.”

“You bastard! You planned this from the beginning!”

Yes, of course.

We didn’t prohibit magic so that we could use \<Kusanagi Sword>, and in case someone argued that weapons created by magic were still weapons, we only prohibited bringing them in.

There was no real need for such trickery, but I wanted to try it. Can’t be helped.

“D-damn…”

\<Kusanagi Sword> radiates a presence worthy of a legendary-class weapon or more.

Even Leopardo, with his low beastly instincts, cannot ignore it.

“Damn it!”

And then, Leopardo ran away in the opposite direction from where Maria was.

…He ran.

Well, it’s a duel with his life on the line, so it’s not impossible.

Leopardo runs toward the edge of the balcony, intending to jump down.

The personnel deployed to prevent escape raise their weapons… no, they don’t.

Ah, right. Those deployed there are soldiers of Leopardo’s faction.

From the start, they intended to assist his escape if it came to that.

They had been leaking information to Leopardo’s faction as Sharon’s personnel for a long time.

But sorry.

“I said I would end it.”

There’s no way you can escape Maria?

-SLASH!-

“Ga… ah…”

Leopardo is split into upper and lower halves by Maria’s \<Kusanagi Sword>, which had gotten ahead of him.

Leopardo died.

I gratefully accept the skills.

As promised, we left the cleanup after the duel to Sharon and the others of the Kingdom of Regalia Beastmen, and returned to the soundproofed room we were initially led to. Ulysses and Blue came with us.

“Master, that was the skill Maria-chan got from her \<Hero>, right!? It was insanely cool!”

Mio says with sparkling eyes.

“Yeah. That’s \<Kusanagi Sword>, obtained when \<Hero> reached LV7. The sharpness is quite good, and usability is excellent. If there’s a problem, it’s that we can now predict the skills that will be obtained in future \<Hero> level-ups.”

“Well, it will almost certainly be the Three Sacred Treasures.”

Probably at LV8 and LV9.

“Mio-chan, please explain later.”

“Ah, yeah. Got it.”

Another piece of Japanese knowledge will be added to Maria.

“Um! What are you all talking about?”

At that point, Ulysses, who couldn’t follow the conversation at all, spoke up.

Even though she became my slave, I had forgotten that due to all the commotion and Sharon’s presence as an outsider, we hadn’t explained anything to Ulysses.

“It’s my secret. A story I haven’t told anyone but my subordinates.”

“Then you’ll tell me too!?”

“I don’t mind, but if you hear it, I’ll never be able to free you from slavery again.”

“I don’t care!”

That was an impressively immediate decision.

Then, Alta, I’m counting on you.

A: Leave it to me.

“Eh? A voice directly in my head…”

Yes, promise received.

“Not only Maria-chan’s \<Hero>, but Jin-kun’s powers also leveled up, right…?”

“Yeah. All my level-based powers leveled up.”

Among my powers, the ones with levels are \<Life and Death Authority>, \<Expanded Interpretation>, and \<Multiple Existence>.

All of them leveled up, which is surprising.

Also, incidentally, Blue’s \<Dragon Magic> went up to LV4. A shocking two-level increase.

Well, I’m not really looking for attack power from my riding dragon.

“In game terms, do they give insanely high skill experience?”

“No, I didn’t get skill points for \<Martial Arts>, so it probably only affects certain things like \<Hero> and abilities.”

To begin with, the level-up conditions for abilities aren’t well understood.

At first, it seemed like my own level-up was the condition, but that’s no longer the case…

At present, the most promising candidate for the level-up condition is “defeating a strong enemy (lol)”.

“I see. …Then if there’s another similar opponent in the future, it might be better to bring Cynthia-chan or Rico-chan along too.”

“Yeah. It seems like a chance to significantly raise the \<Hero> skill level, so if possible, I’d like to actively aim for it.”

I nod at Mio’s suggestion.

Since it deliberately calls itself an “Earth Calamity Dragon”, there’s a possibility that other calamity dragons exist.

If things go well, we can further level up \<Hero> and abilities.

“Jin-kun… Listening to that, there’s one thing I was wondering. May I ask…?”

“Yeah, what is it?”

“Jin-kun, did you perhaps beat the ‘Earth Calamity Dragon: Earthquake’ to death with your fists in subspace? You mentioned \<Martial Arts> as a candidate for skill level increases…”

Right, on Sakura’s flat map, detailed combat scenes aren’t visible.

Those with high processing ability, like Alta or Kate from the explorers, use maps with 3D information. With those, the details of combat can be seen…

“Yes, he beat it to death with his fists.”

“He beat it to death with his fists.”

Maria and Blue, who saw my fight, answer Sakura’s question.

“Master, as always, you use insane methods.”

“From what Ulysses-san said, it didn’t seem like something you could deal with by punching…”

“But Jin-kun did deal with it by punching, right…”

Since I’m about to be treated like a monster, I should offer some self-defense.

“No, Earthquake didn’t attack upward, and there were safe zones and an easy-to-punch back, so I just punched it. I didn’t do anything that difficult.”

Sakura and the others give wry smiles.

“Well… that’s Jin-kun for you…”

《That’s why I said so!》

They’ve given up arguing.

For the record, Dora, who hadn’t been listening, hurriedly said a template line.

“Putting aside the talk about Master no longer being human, what effects did you get from the ability level-ups?”

Mio is treating me as a complete monster.

I could make her wet herself again…

…Probably not a good idea in someone else’s house. Mio, you got lucky.

“I’ll start with the simple one. \<Expanded Interpretation> reached LV10, expanding the enhancement slots to 1000.”

\<Expanded Interpretation LV10>

Effect targets expanded to 1000.

It was originally LV8 and went to LV9, but then immediately to LV10, so LV9 had no meaning.

Also, I secretly hoped that reaching LV10 would make the effect targets unlimited, but it wasn’t that generous.

“That’s just plainly useful.”

“Yes, I think Lusea-san will be pleased.”

According to what I heard from Maria before, the enhancement slots of \<Expanded Interpretation> are managed by the head maid.

More precisely, excluding what I need, Lucea holds onto the remaining slots that have been arranged, and assigns them to subordinates as needed.

Lucea, how much work are you carrying…?

A: The work is subdivided and each has a leader, so her main duty is final approval. I don’t think the burden is that heavy. Vega also assists her.

Good. It doesn’t seem like an excessively black work environment.

“It’s just a simple effect increase, so it’s hard to comment.”

“It’s not something you can really comment on much to begin with.”

It definitely helps, but there’s nothing to say.

“Alright, next. Well, \<Life and Death Authority LV9> and \<Multiple Existence LV7> are essentially a set. You can’t use them alone.”

“You said something like that before. What can you do this time?”

I continue while trying to remain as calm as possible.

“Simply put, I can do something extremely dangerous.”

“Having Master say ‘dangerous’ to my face is really scary…”

A gulping sound can be heard.

# **158: The Princess Shrine Maiden and the Stay in the Royal Capital**

**AN:** Regarding the matter of Special Powers spoilers, avoiding them in the foreword and afterword would honestly be stepping on a landmine (guaranteed to cause flames), so I will put them in the activity report instead (probably sometime this week).

I am personally fine with almost any kind of spoiler, but I think people like that are probably a minority.

This chapter marks the end of Volume 10.

---

It’s sudden, but I think I should explain about elves.

Elves are a staple of fantasy, but since interpretations often differ depending on the work, let us make the understanding of elves in this world clear.

This is actually the second time, following beastmen.

First, elves are broadly classified into three types.

Pure elves, half-elves who are mixed-blood with other races, and the superior race known as high elves.

In fact, there is no way for other races to distinguish between these three types of elves (map aside).

They all share the general elf traits of long lifespans, long ears, and proficiency with magic and bows, so they cannot be immediately judged by appearance or ability.

However, elves themselves can apparently tell at a glance. That said, half-elves cannot tell whether the other party is a ‘high elf’ or a ‘pure elf’. To put it simply, those below cannot judge how far above the other is, only that they are above.

I heard before that Iris, a half-elf from the Castal adventurer group, thought that Yuria, who is a high elf, was a pure elf.

Rather, if it had been known that she was a high elf, Yuria’s treatment would probably have been different. The value difference between elves and high elves is on a completely different order of magnitude.

Each of the three elf types has their birth conditions more or less fixed.

Pure elves are only born when both parents are elves.

If the mother is an elf and the father is not an elf race, if the mother herself is a half-elf, or if the father is an elf race and the mother is not an elf race (cases where the father’s traits manifest), a half-elf is born.

High elves are born in cases where a pure elf would be born, but they are said to appear extremely rarely. Roughly one every several hundred to several thousand years.

Naturally, there are also differences in lifespan and growth among the three types.

Half-elves live about 500 years, pure elves about 1000 years, and high elves have no lifespan.

In addition, the further along you go, the slower their apparent growth becomes.

Of course, during infancy they grow like humans, but from around age ten, their growth suddenly slows.

Half-elves reach an appearance equivalent to a human adult at around 50 years old, elves at around 100 years old, and high elves at around 1000 years old.

Also, aging begins around lifespan minus adult age, but their memory seems to be good, and they do not become forgetful until death.

High elves do not age, and their apparent age completely stops at around 20. When they die, it is said that suicide and homicide make up about half each.

Because mixed blood produces half-elves, maintaining pure elves requires forming communities of the same race.

As far as I know, there is the “Elf Village” deep within the Crimson Empire.

Pure elves apparently do not have much interaction with human society, so encounters with half-elves are far more common.

In that sense, the Goddess Church of the Elgant Theocracy stands out, with many elves among its clergy and a high elf serving as the Pope.

The reason for bringing all this up is as a refresher before hearing Ulysses’ story.

After finishing our explanation about Special Power level-ups, we decided to listen to Ulysses’ background story together with Sharon, who had returned.

“The elf settlement I belonged to was a clan that sealed ‘Earthquake’ for generations. Apparently, long, long ago, the goddess directly asked them to perform the sealing.”

So there really is some kind of connection between the goddess and ‘Earthquake’.

“Only high elf women can perform the sealing, so high elf women born into the clan were called ‘Princess Shrine Maidens’. The sealing was maintained just by the ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’ being alive, so back then there was no need to imprison them in crystals.”

“High elves have no lifespan, so why did they pass on the role? Back then, they didn’t need to approach ‘Earthquake’ and be exposed to miasma either, right?”

Mio raised her hand and asked.

As expected, Mio’s comprehension is high when it comes to fantasy topics.

“Simply put, even just maintaining the seal has some negative effects, and in order to maintain it, there was also the need to periodically approach the Calamity Dragon’s body. When the next ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’ was born, the previous high elf would always wish to pass on the role. And after the handover was safely completed, the previous ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’ would always commit suicide, or so I’ve heard.”

We ended up glimpsing the high suicide rate of high elves in a strange place.

Incidentally, the handover of the ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’ is done through \<Shrine Maiden Succession>. It is a skill that transfers the Title ‘Human Pillar’, \<Sealing Arts>, and various other things required of a ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’.

In a world that does not recognize skills, it can be said to be an extremely rare skill.

“The role was passed down for a long time, but as times changed, clan members who feared the risk of a ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’ suddenly dying devised a method in my generation to confine her in crystal. And as you know, that resulted in me being sealed in crystal and left there for over six thousand years.”

“Did Ulysses accept being sealed?”

Faron asked, her voice tinged with anger.

“Faron-chan, you’re kind. …I accepted inheriting the role of ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’, but I was never told I’d be sealed in crystal. I remember clan members speaking proudly to me while I was trapped inside the crystal.”

“That clan… crush them.”

Faron is completely furious.

“Unfortunately, I don’t know what my clan is doing now. After a while, no one came to check on me anymore, and before I knew it, the royal castle of the Regalia Beastman Kingdom had been built on top. But I was never given any information.”

“When we looked at the founding records, we found that elves were involved in the establishment of the royal family, but there weren’t many details. It doesn’t seem unrelated.”

This time Sharon spoke.

“Are there elves within the Regalia Beastman Kingdom? They might be related.”

“I’ve never heard of any. In addition to the land being originally dominated by beastmen, it’s said to be incompatible with elf constitutions, so they are extremely few.”

“Come to think of it, we haven’t seen a single elf since entering this country…”

Even checking the map, I cannot find any elf race at all.

It’s possible there really isn’t even one.

If the ‘Elf Village’ we plan to visit someday is involved in this matter, we’ll have to think about how to respond.

At worst, they might not be a party we can build friendly relations with.

“Ulysses, do you harbor resentment toward that clan? Do you want to avenge that resentment?”

“…I do feel resentment. But I also understand their sense of crisis. …If I had to name someone I want to resent, it would be a man named Gired who devised the method of sealing me in crystal.”

In response to my question, Ulysses named one man as the object of her resentment.

“That man stood in front of me while I was sealed in crystal and unable to move, boasting arrogantly about the brilliance of the spell and his own excellence. …Endlessly. It was truly annoying and hateful.”

“Ugh…”

“What an unpleasant person…”

“I can’t believe it…”

“That guy, kill him.”

From the top, those were the reactions of Mio, Sakura, Sera, and Faron.

Faron’s killing intent is intense.

“That said, considering his lifespan, that guy is probably already dead, so the chance to get revenge…”

“Gired is also a high elf, so the chance that he died of old age is zero. And since he’s a man, he couldn’t become a ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’ either…”

“…If you get the chance, want me to punch him once?”

“By all means.”

Ulysses’ eyes are serious.

I categorized Gired as a person of concern in my mind.

Talking about dark topics for too long is just depressing, so we moved on to other subjects.

“The preparations to crush the Leopardo faction are going smoothly. Once Jin and the others return, I’m planning to deliver the finishing blow, but when do you plan to return?”

Asked by Sharon, I thought a bit about the length of our stay.

“Well. Staying too long would be a bother…”

“That’s not true! If anyone tries to obstruct Jin’s stay, I’ll eliminate them with all my might!”

“It’s scary how serious you sound.”

Ulysses, who knows Sharon’s personality, gives a wry smile.

“Then let’s stay for about three days. In the meantime, we’ll do some sightseeing around the country.”

“Moving to other cities is fine with dragonkin, after all.”

Blue muttered “Yes!” in a small voice.

Are you really that happy?

“Of course, if any problems come up, feel free to use my name as much as you want.”

The king’s name feels… light.

“More importantly, if you’re sightseeing domestically, do you need a guide? If you’d like, I could…”

“Sharon, think about it rationally.”

Faron stopped Sharon’s outrageous idea.

“J-joking. But I do think it’s better to have a guide…”

“Being assigned someone half-heartedly would just be a hassle.”

It would only restrict our actions.

“Then how about Kuroneko? You’ve acted together before, and she won’t say unnecessary things.”

“Sharon, Kuroneko will be busy too, so that’s difficult.”

I’ve gotten used to it, but when Faron interjects while Sharon is talking, it can be a bit confusing to watch.

“Ah, right. Jin, sorry. Please forget what I just said.”

“By the way, what are you going to do about the ‘Eight Vassal Beasts’? Two dead and three arrested, they’re in shambles.”

I had little interest and forgot about it, but since we’re here, I’ll ask.

“Well, it’s an internal affairs matter, so I shouldn’t really talk about it with outsiders, but with Jin it’s too late for that. To get straight to the point, we’ve decided to have the three arrested continue as ‘Eight Vassal Beasts’. Of course, it’s not like they’ll go unpunished.”

“Is that really okay?”

Ulysses asked with concern for Sharon and the others.

It’s a valid concern. Betrayal, betrayal, and more betrayal.

“Yeah. The three of them happily agreed to become my slaves.”

“Ah, I see…”

In that case, unless something goes terribly wrong, it shouldn’t become a problem.

“The slots of the two who died, or rather were executed, need to be filled somehow. We wouldn’t have trouble even with six, but it’s tradition, so it can’t be helped. …By the way, Maria-san, are you interested in becoming one of the ‘Eight Vassal Beasts’? It’s treated like nobility, so the pay is generous.”

I understand the sentiment, but she boldly tried to recruit Maria.

Mio muttered leisurely, “Maria-chan is popular in this country.”

“I’m very sorry. My place is only by Lord Jin’s side.”

“Well, yeah. Trying to lure someone under Jin with money is fundamentally impossible.”

Sharon can only give a wry smile at Maria, who refuses without even considering it.

“To begin with, easily placing importance on people from another country is problematic.”

Why is the reincarnator playing the fool while the native is the one delivering the straight man retort?

In this case, shouldn’t Sharon be the stopper?

“If you think it’s impossible, then don’t ask in the first place.”

“Just in case. I know Maria-san has the ability to become one of the ‘Eight Vassal Beasts’. And if she’s connected to Jin, there’s less worry about her harboring ill intentions. If we purge all the talented people from the Leopardo faction, it could reduce national strength, so we desperately want capable people.”

It seems the Regalia Beastman Kingdom is in quite a tight spot.

“In that case, why not stop the purge and make them slaves like the other ‘Eight Vassal Beasts’?”

“That’s impossible. There are too many to manage properly, and… an example is necessary, right?”

“Sharon’s anger hasn’t cooled at all.”

Faron sighed.

Yeah. Since Sharon’s policy is not to subordinate people, maybe I’ll make a suggestion while we’re at it.

“Whether they can become ‘Eight Vassal Beasts’ or not, I could lend you capable people.”

“Eh? Are there beastmen here besides Maria-san? Or do you mean the others? Non-beastmen can’t become ‘Eight Vassal Beasts’, you know?”

“No, I’m calling them now.”

I’m thinking of asking Lucea to dispatch capable beastman maids.

Through \<Contract Bond>, as long as I have even one subordinate, I can grasp the situation of that land on the map.

In every country I’ve visited so far, at least two subordinates live there, allowing information to gather. However, at present, I have no subordinates in the Regalia Beastman Kingdom.

My maids are excellent, so if I call them, they’ll come immediately and start building a life foundation on their own.

But if Sharon is suffering from a lack of personnel, I’m fine with lending her capable maids.

“Call them? How…? Ah, well, if it’s Jin, you can probably do that. You summoned Blue-san earlier too, right? Can you call people from even farther away?”

“Yeah. I’ll do the same as with Blue and call beastmen from Castal.”

I did use ‘Summon’ right in front of them once.

“That would be a huge help. If they’re people Jin recommends, they should benefit the beastman kingdom.”

“Don’t proceed assuming acceptance. For self-defense reasons, borrowing personnel from another country is not good.”

Faron was the one who stopped Sharon from accepting.

I understand what she’s getting at. Simply put, it’s like having spies.

“But Faron, the other party is Jin, you know? Someone who has means to grasp our circumstances and can crush ‘Earthquake’ head-on. Don’t you think talking about self-defense against someone like that is rather hollow?”

I am Shindo Jin, an existence for whom self-defense is meaningless.

“That’s… true, but…”

“I don’t intend to accept just anyone either. I’m accepting because it’s Jin’s introduction. Jin doesn’t need petty tricks, and I don’t believe for a second that Jin would harm me.”

“…All right. I’ll accept them too. I trust Jin.”

“It wasn’t meant to be such a big deal…”

And so, I asked Lucea, and it was decided that two desired maid beastmen would be dispatched to the Regalia Beastman Kingdom.

The first day was consumed by the battle with ‘Earthquake’ and Leopardo, so from the second day onward, we enjoyed sightseeing in the Regalia Beastman Kingdom for three days.

First, the second day was sightseeing within the royal capital.

At Sharon’s request, wanting to at least provide a guide for sightseeing within the royal capital, especially the lower districts, someone knowledgeable was assigned.

“This way is a recommended diner, DeathDeath.”

One of the ‘Eight Vassal Beasts’, a hamster beastman girl named Papit.

Yes, she’s the hamster beastman girl who, as part of the Leopardo faction, attacked Sharon and was defeated. While she wasn’t publicly punished, her life was only spared by having her become Sharon’s slave.

She’s around the same age as us, and has a transistor-glamour physique.

Why was someone from the Leopardo faction deliberately chosen as a guide?

“Hey, isn’t that Papit-sama of the ‘Eight Vassal Beasts’?”

“Why is she dressed like she’s in underwear?”

“Who’s that knight over there? Papit-sama is obviously fawning over him…”

You might be able to guess from the voices of the town. As you can tell, Papit is currently wearing underwear-like clothing with very little fabric, smiling with all her might as she fawns over us while guiding us around.

Her purpose can be summed up in one word…

“I’ll listen to anything, Death! Please cooperate to improve Queen Sharon’s impression of me, Death!”

She’s ‘begging for her life’.

Papit attacked Sharon under Leopardo’s orders.

Although her position as one of the ‘Eight Vassal Beasts’ remains, Papit is currently Sharon’s slave.

Normally, becoming the slave of the person you attacked would not lead to good treatment afterward.

To improve Sharon’s impression of her even slightly and secure her own safety, she decided to fawn over me, who Sharon favors.

Fortunately, Papit is a self-made ‘Eight Vassal Beast’ from the lower districts, so she’s knowledgeable about the area and was well-suited as a guide. When recruitment for a guide went out, she applied without hesitation.

Incidentally, “listening to anything” apparently includes nighttime companionship.

If she can secure her safety with just her chastity, it’s cheap, or so she says.

To that, I replied, “A mysterious knight revealing his identity through an affair is impossible.”

Well, it was a trivial joke.

As a result, as a second-best measure, Papit reduced the amount of fabric in her clothing.

Despite her short stature, she has a large chest, so her scant outfit is, put simply, erotic. It seems she shifted her objective to being eye candy.

However, unfortunately, fawning does not earn evaluation points, only the guiding does.

That said, being knowledgeable about the lower districts, the shops Papit introduced were quite good.

Unfortunately, since there were no private rooms, all the food ended up being takeout…

“Papit was useful, so I’ll report properly to Sharon.”

“Yay, Death! Thank you, Death!”

Papit jumps around in joy.

She was helpful for sightseeing, so my evaluation of her isn’t low.

“Ah!”

In her enthusiasm, her chest popped out of her underwear-like outfit.

As a kind of classic trope, I decided to raise Papit’s evaluation by one more level.

Just to be clear, I did not evaluate her out of lust, but in appreciation of the big-breast trope.

…Come to think of it, Sera has a big chest, but she never has slips like that.

“W-what is it? That look is scary, could you please stop?”

Day three of the stay.

Today we promptly left the royal capital and strolled around the cities in the surrounding area.

Rather than thoroughly sightseeing in one place like the royal capital, this was a style of picking out famous spots from several cities.

Since we’re traveling by dragonkin today, there is no guide.

Therefore, we can do whatever we want.

“Well then, I’m going to go to the slave trader for a bit.”

“I will accompany you.”

The first thing I do in a new land is go to the slave trader to secure slaves with valuable skills. For me, the slave trader is also one of the sightseeing spots.

Recently, slave maids have been securing slaves in new lands, but since there is no Advance Trading Company in the Regalia Beastman Kingdom, I need to secure them myself.

Incidentally, knight attire stands out, so we’re touring the town lightly disguised.

Blue and the others are also acting together in human form. Ulysses is in the royal capital with Sharon.

“Then we will go around the food stalls first.”

“We’ll make sure Master can eat only Mio-chan’s selection, so look forward to it. After that, we’re heading to the arena, the specialty of this city.”

As usual, the food group centered around Sera and Mio also gets moving.

This city is apparently famous for having relatively mild flavors (by our standards), making it easy to eat.

“Yeah, arenas are a staple sightseeing spot in fantasy worlds.”

Being a country full of muscle-brains, there are many cities with arenas.

Even so, it’s not slave-on-slave fighting, but contests between people confident in their skills.

Basically, killing is prohibited, and they use training weapons with magical tools like those in the adventurer guild that don’t deal damage to opponents.

Well, in underground arenas, there are illegal matches where anything goes, including killing.

Since this is sightseeing, we plan to stay away from the underworld.

“If it’s training weapon matches, Sakura can watch too, right?”

“Yes, I’m fine…”

The biggest reason we can’t go to underground arenas is that Sakura is not good with bloodshed.

It’s also bad for Dora’s education. …Don’t say that just being by my side is bad for her education.

After deciding on a meeting place, we split into the group going to the slave trader and the group going on a food tour.

“I’ll go with Master.”

“I’ll choose food, please.”

“I’ll go that way too.”

Among the dragonkin riders, it’s easy to see: only Blue comes with me, while the big eaters Mikazuki and Leaf head toward the food tour.

There are slaves in quite terrible conditions, so I won’t bring Sakura or Dora. Dora was originally in the food group anyway…

We spent the third day repeating the routine of slave traders, food tours, and wandering sightseeing spots in several cities.

“Master, you really only watch and don’t jump in or bet.”

While watching matches at the arena, Mio asked curiously.

Even outside underground arenas, betting is done, and jump-in participation is possible, so I could have taken the stage.

“I basically don’t gamble on things with a strong luck element. Plus, I don’t like disrupting ‘tourist spots’. Whether betting or fighting, if I participate, it will definitely disrupt things. That’s not what I want.”

When it comes to tourist spots, I prefer to enjoy them as they are.

Whether betting or fighting, my participation would mean disrupting the place.

Unless there’s a compelling reason to fight, I don’t want to casually drop by and disrupt things on a whim.

“When Master gets involved, most things turn into big deals. Did you know? Queen’s Knight Gene is called the ‘Knight of Turmoil’ in this country.”

Sera told me about the public evaluation of Queen’s Knight Gene.

“Seriously?”

“Seriously.”

This is the first I’ve heard of it…

“Ah, I’ve heard that too. Wherever Master appears as Gene, there’s inevitably an incident that shakes the nation. The Kingdom of Eldia, the Elgant Theocracy, and the Regalia Beastman Kingdom.”

“Now that you mention it…”

With Mio’s addition, even Sakura nods in agreement.

I find myself agreeing too.

When acting under the name Queen’s Knight Gene, major incidents that shake nations are usually bundled together.

Even when we exposed Fake Sakuya in the Castal Kingdom, it was done under Gene’s name.

Well, it’s no wonder the nickname ‘Knight of Turmoil’ stuck.

Day four of the stay.

Having sufficiently enjoyed normal sightseeing, today we decided to wander monster territories.

On a remote mountain, a stray upper-class fire dragon that hadn’t gone to the ‘Dragon Forest’.

“GYAOOOOOOO!!!”

《Take that!》

-Whack!-

“GYA, GYAO…”

Dora, who hates dragons, delivers a solid blow and takes it down.

In a remote forest, a flock of harpies living in the woods.

“So the harpies around here live in forests instead of mountains.”

“Munch munch, the egg flavor is slightly different from the ones from the mountains. There might be dishes that suit these eggs better.”

Harpies lay delicious eggs, so if they aren’t massacring humans, they’re tame candidates.

Fortunately, people don’t approach this forest, so it seems there have been no massacres, and we were able to tame them safely.

According to Mio, the eggs of these harpies are also delicious, so even though we only tamed about 20, it was a good outcome.

Day five of the stay.

Today, instead of sightseeing, we enjoyed casual conversation with Sharon over tea until noon.

After lunch, we plan to depart the royal capital and head home.

“Are you really sure it’s fine? I want to talk with Jin more, and you could stay a bit longer.”

“I’m grateful for your feelings, but I’ll pass. I’m affiliated with Castal, after all. I can’t stay in another country’s care forever.”

Sharon says regretfully, but I shake my head and decline.

“And with the two new ‘Eight Vassal Beasts’, they can contact me, so if you need anything, or even if you don’t but want to say something, let me know.”

“Thank you. I’ll ask the two of them if there’s anything to convey. …Still, even if it’s Jin’s introduction, I didn’t think you could become ‘Eight Vassal Beasts’ in just one day.”

Around noon on the third day of our stay, we received word from head maid Lucea that the selection of maids to send to the Regalia Beastman Kingdom was complete. I then ‘Summoned’ the two beastmen and introduced them to Sharon.

The two fought against two ‘Eight Vassal Beasts’ selected as mock battle opponents (excluding Papit from the Leopardo faction) and instantly defeated them.

After that, various things happened, and by the end of the day, they were added to the ranks of the ‘Eight Vassal Beasts’.

As an aside, the two selected maid beastmen both possessed Unique Skills. Moreover, they weren’t acquired later through my abilities, but were innate Unique Skills.

“I tried giving them some simple tasks, and their administrative abilities seem fairly high too. It’s a huge help. Now I can crush the Leopardo faction without holding back.”

“Crushing the Leopardo faction is fine, but in another two or three days, the Crimson Empire’s princess will arrive.”

“What? …Ah! Right, she’s due to arrive soon!”

Looking at the map, the Crimson Empire’s princess, Strawberry Crimson, is already near the royal capital.

It’s an apology for Scarlet hitting Sharon… or rather, Faron, in the Elgant Theocracy.

I assumed it wouldn’t be an unannounced visit, but it seems Sharon simply forgot.

“Jin, I’m really sorry, but could you advance your plans a bit?”

“What are you planning to do?”

“…Today and tomorrow, wipe out the Leopardo faction.”

Sharon’s eyes are serious.

She intends to settle things before Princess Strawberry arrives.

“…Do your best.”

“Yeah, I will.”

And so, after finishing preparations in a bit of a rush at the end, we decided to leave the Regalia Beastman Kingdom.

Naturally, we took off by dragonkin from the balcony where so much had happened.

“Sorry. It ended up feeling like we chased you out at the end…”

For the sake of private conversation, only Sharon saw us off directly, with Sein and the others at a distance.

“Don’t worry about it. I can come again, right?”

“Of course! You’re welcome anytime. Faron too, right?”

“Of course, welcome anytime. Except during bath and toilet times.”

“That’s just being a pervert.”

I retort to Faron’s odd joke.

“Ulysses, take care.”

This time Faron calls out to Ulysses.

“Yes, thank you for everything. Sharon-chan, Faron-chan, take care too.”

“The one who should be thanking you is us. Ulysses, thank you for everything up to now. If possible, I’d like you to visit this country again someday. I know you have bad memories here, but it would make me sad if you continued to dislike the country we govern.”

“I’ll try once I’ve sorted out my feelings and settled down.”

Even if she dislikes the land, she likely likes Sharon and Faron.

Considering everything that happened, it’s quite a positive response.

“I’d be happy if you did. Jin, please take care of Ulysses.”

“…Even if you say that, I’m fairly hands-off.”

I don’t recall doing much hands-on care after adding people as subordinates.

Put positively, I leave it to the maids. Put negatively, I don’t feed the fish after catching them. …Both sound bad.

“Ah, I’m not asking you to do anything special for Ulysses. I just want you to keep Ulysses in your heart a little. And when the time comes, extend a hand to her…”

“If she’s my subordinate, that’s only natural, right?”

I won’t do anything particularly special, but I won’t treat her badly or forget her.

Keeping her in mind and lending a hand when needed is something I welcome.

“Haha, is that so… The kids under Jin are lucky. I’m jealous, maybe I’ll become your underling too?”

“Equal standing.”

“Ugh… I know that without Faron telling me.”

It seems Sharon’s desire to be in an ‘equal standing’ with me hasn’t changed.

Though, it feels like it’s wavering slightly.

“Well then, it’s about time we depart.”

“It’s really a shame, but I have various plans too.”

I mount Blue in dragon form. Maria and Ulysses ride behind me.

The other members also begin mounting their respective dragons.

“See you again.”

“Yeah, see you.”

The dragonkin flap their wings and take off from the balcony.

We landed somewhere deserted and returned using ‘Portal’.

---

**AN:** Recently, there has been a period where my writing has not progressed at all, and Volume 11 is not finished yet. At this rate, there is a risk I won’t make it by the 30th (due to mental reasons, I want to have at least one volume’s worth of stock).

I expect about one or two more chapters, so I will post the character introductions once it’s complete. If the character introductions are not posted by the 30th, that means it didn’t work out, and on the 30th I will post the character introductions and a small short story to tide things over.

I sincerely apologize.

# **Characters Appearing in Volume 10**

**AN:** As for tomorrow’s update, it has not yet been officially decided whether it will be the main story or a short story.

For now, I will just list the characters. The discussion about the activity report and such will be postponed a bit.

---

Main story only. Basically, only people whose names are shown. Skills are excluded.

Information that is not explicitly stated is excluded.

**Protagonist Side**

Name: Unknown (Girls from the Mermaid Country)

Gender: Female

Race: Mermaid

Title: Jin’s Familiar

Notes: Twenty-five girls who were oppressed in the Mermaid Country. They were tamed by Jin and are currently studying to work as maids on land. There is suspicion that they were tamed just for the pun of “mermaid maids.”

Name: Hiroe Kurauchi

Gender: Female

Age: 18

Race: Human (Otherworlder)

Titles: Transferee, Hero from Another World, Jin’s Slave

Notes: A hero who possesses the Blessing \<Clown’s Demon Card>. One of the students who was bullied in her original world. As a subordinate of Orihara, she delivers a message to Jin. She wears clown-like clothing and a mask. She is forcibly enslaved by Jin, but even so, she accepted the role of messenger with full understanding. Since her time in her original world, she has been small in stature but monstrously strong. Unlike Sera, her weight matches her appearance, yet only her arm strength is excessive, an unbalanced trait.

Name: Ulysses

Gender: Female

Age: 6810

Race: High Elf

Titles: Elf Princess Shrine Maiden, Elf Royalty, Living Sacrifice, Jin’s Slave

Notes: A High Elf princess shrine maiden who sealed the Earth Disaster Dragon “Earthquake” for over 6000 years deep beneath the royal capital of the Regalia Beastkin Kingdom. She is completely worn down mentally and falls for Jin, who saved her from a hellish situation. In truth, rather than love, it is more like imprinting born from being at the absolute limit of her mental state. She is on good terms with Sharon and Faron and has known them for nearly ten years.

**Mermaid Country**

Name: Myule

Gender: Female

Age: 255

Race: Mermaid

Notes: She came from the Mermaid Country to the human lands to seek help in order to save them from food shortages, but was captured. She is very close to the queen, but is useless when it comes to acting as someone who can remonstrate with her. Since she has no rare skills and there was no particular reason to tame her, Jin did not tame her.

Name: Mestialka

Gender: Female

Age: 570

Race: Mermaid

Titles: Queen of the Mermaids, King of Rebellion

Notes: The Queen of the Mermaid Country. She harbors hostility toward Jin, who does not bow despite her arrogant attitude. However, she did not actually take action, so it was safe. Extremely rare. She became queen after killing the mother of Leila, the former labyrinth ruler. She is the type who thoroughly removes anything that displeases her from her sight.

**Crimson Empire**

Name: Strawberry Crimson

Gender: Female

Age: 17

Race: Human

Title: Crimson Empire Imperial Princess

Notes: Scarlet’s daughter and the second imperial princess of the Crimson Empire. She came to the Regalia Beastkin Kingdom to apologize for the incident where Scarlet struck Sharon in the Elgant Theocracy. Since she is Rouge’s niece, she can call Rouge “Aunt.” Doing so makes her teary-eyed, so she calls her “Big Sister” instead. She possesses extraordinary physical ability inherited from her father (non-skill). Though she is ignorant of the world, most things work out thanks to her innate power.

Name: Milfy

Gender: Female

Age: 15

Race: Human

Notes: An attendant assigned to Strawberry, and also Scarlet’s daughter. As a child of a concubine, she has no right of succession to the throne. Like Strawberry, she is slightly lacking in common sense.

**Regalia Beastkin Kingdom**

Name: Sharon (Faron)

Gender: Female

Age: 15

Race: Beastkin (White Tiger, Reincarnator)

Titles: Queen of the Regalia Kingdom, Dual Personality

Notes: One of the central characters of this volume. A dual personality in which twin souls reside within a single body. Of the two, the personality that originally belonged to the body is a reincarnator and was once Jin’s pet cat. Because her goal was “to speak with Jin on equal footing”, she is, unusually, very unusually, a friendly royal woman who has not become Jin’s subordinate even after her main story concluded. Still, she harbors a wavering desire to become Jin’s subordinate, just a little.

Name: Leopardo

Gender: Male

Race: Beastkin

Title: Eight Vassal Beast

Notes: First seat of the Eight Vassal Beasts. His epithet is “King Beast.” Though a direct descendant of the previous king, he narrowly lost to Sharon (with Faron inside) in the battle to decide the monarch. Since then, he has held hostility toward Sharon at every turn. Ultimately, he aims to usurp the throne as the figurehead of the Leopardo faction. After various misdeeds that incur Sharon’s wrath, he dies following a public execution in the form of a duel with Maria.

Name: Sein Burse

Gender: Male

Race: Beastkin (Wolf)

Title: Eight Vassal Beast

Notes: Second seat of the Eight Vassal Beasts. His epithet is “Swift Traverse.” An old (wolf) butler-type powerhouse. Though he yields the first seat to the royal Leopardo, in terms of actual ability he surpasses the first seat. He has served the longest among the Eight Vassal Beasts and was a friend of the previous king. He is sometimes spotted running across rooftops. Officially, he is part of the Sharon faction.

Name: Mercy

Gender: Female

Race: Beastkin (Sheep)

Title: Eight Vassal Beast

Notes: Third seat of the Eight Vassal Beasts. Her epithet is “Twin Ramparts.” Sharon’s secretary and bodyguard, confident in her defensive capabilities. A close attendant who also accompanied Sharon to the Elgant Theocracy, firmly of the Sharon faction. She is also Sharon’s childhood friend and knows about her dual personality. Slightly, subtly yuri.

Name: Sarad

Gender: Male

Race: Beastkin

Title: Eight Vassal Beast

Notes: Fourth seat of the Eight Vassal Beasts. His epithet is “Mage Hunter.” Formerly of the Leopardo faction and ultimately becomes Sharon’s slave. Though Leopardo’s lackey, he is not without ability. He is the type to side with those in power, and while doing so, he is reasonably competent. However, he is also a fool who failed to notice the extent of Sharon’s power.

Name: Goris

Gender: Male

Race: Beastkin

Title: Eight Vassal Beast

Notes: Fifth seat of the Eight Vassal Beasts. His epithet is “Mighty Arm.” Formerly of the Leopardo faction and ultimately becomes Sharon’s slave. A musclehead of a level representative of a muscle-brained nation. Since Sharon valued intelligence to some degree, he joined Leopardo’s faction, which adhered to a purely muscle-brained ideology.

Name: Papit

Gender: Female

Race: Beastkin

Title: Eight Vassal Beast

Notes: Sixth seat of the Eight Vassal Beasts. Her epithet is “Star Strike.” Formerly of the Leopardo faction and ultimately becomes Sharon’s slave. A self-made fighter from the slums and well-versed in the downtown areas. A transistor-glamour type, with the catchphrase “Death.” She followed Leopardo because it was disadvantageous not to. Her motto is “One Shot Turnaround.”

Name: Caruto

Gender: Male

Race: Beastkin

Title: Eight Vassal Beast

Notes: Seventh seat of the Eight Vassal Beasts. His epithet is “Sprint.” A small fry who tried to pick up Maria and was killed by Kuroneko. Effectively the weakest man among the Eight Vassal Beasts.

Name: Unknown (Alias: Kuroneko)

Gender: Female

Race: Beastkin (Black Cat)

Title: Eight Vassal Beast

Notes: Eighth seat of the Eight Vassal Beasts. Her epithet is “Black Shadow.” A ninja with an unknown real name and a versatile tamer-type character. She ends her sentences with “gozaru.” An intelligence agent who serves as Sharon’s eyes and ears, firmly of the Sharon faction. Because she does not engage in head-on combat, her seat ranking is low, but in an anything-goes fight, she is said to be on par with the second seat. One of the few members of the human races in this world who possesses a means of flight.

# **Side Story 12: The Hero of the Heavenly Eye Stands Upon the Earth**

**AN:** I am very sorry, but I did not make it in time, so please let me tide things over with a short side story.

This is the story from when Asai was summoned as a Hero.

It collects some foreshadowing, scatters some more foreshadowing, and touches on things not explained in the main story.

---

My name is Yoshinobu Asai.

Until yesterday… no, until about five minutes ago, I should have been a perfectly ordinary high school student.

This morning, I woke up to my alarm clock and was getting ready to go to school.

Today I was supposed to join morning practice as a substitute for the baseball club.

I remember waking up earlier than usual, quietly eating breakfast so as not to wake my little sister, Hijiri, then returning to my room and changing into my uniform.

The next moment, I was standing in an unfamiliar place… Where is this?

It feels like the great hall of a Western-style castle. Dozens of people are surrounding us.

“Ohhh, success! We have successfully summoned two Heroes!”

An old man who looks like a mage, wrapped in robes, is shouting.

From my situation and the old man’s words, I understood what had happened.

No, maybe understood is not the right word. Normally speaking, this is something you would refuse to understand.

A blonde, blue-eyed girl who looked about eight years old walked up in front of me.

“Heroes, welcome. My name is Sylphine. I am the princess of the Kingdom of Sanokia. We wish for you Heroes to defeat the Demon King and save this world.”

…I see. So this is what people call an isekai summoning.

According to Sylphine, this was indeed another world, and they had summoned Heroes to defeat the Demon King.

The ones summoned were me and one other person, an ageless-looking man.

At a glance, he looked about high-school age, but it would not feel strange to be told he was an adult. He was not wearing a uniform either, so it was hard to judge. Even with my own eyes.

For now, we were asked to introduce ourselves.

“My name is Yoshinobu Asai. I’m a high school student.”

“A high school student! That is one of the most common occupations among Heroes!”

Sylphine raised her voice happily.

It became clear that Hero summoning was not something that had happened just once or twice.

Then it was the ageless man’s turn.

“Me name is Koda da Yo! My favorite things are little girls and little girls wetting themselves, and also dried squid da Yo!”

…

The air froze.

“Um, Koda-sama… your given name is…?”

“Koda is Koda! That’s fine da Yo!”

He did not seem inclined to give any more of his name.

I was calling him “Koda-san” because I wanted to keep my distance. Honestly, I did not want to get close to him.

“Then, Asai-sama, Koda-sama, is there anything you would like to ask?”

“Can we return to our original world?”

I immediately asked Sylphine.

For me, this was the most important thing of all.

“I have heard that you can return. The summoning of the Heroes was done by divine revelation. According to the goddess, once you defeat the Demon King, she will convey the method of return through another revelation.”

“How did the previous Heroes return?”

Defeating the Demon King aside, relying entirely on the goddess for the return method felt risky.

If possible, I wanted a backup plan.

“…There are no stories of Heroes returning. It is said that all Heroes remained in this world.”

“All of them? Doesn’t that seem strange?”

“I am very sorry. The details have not been passed down.”

“I see…”

It sounded unnatural, but it did not feel like a lie.

If that was the case, then defeating the Demon King was the only option…

“Me can ask question too OK?”

“Y-yes. What is it?”

Sylphine seemed a bit intimidated when Koda-san spoke up.

His self-introduction must have left an impression.

“Me and him are peaceful people from peaceful country da Yo? Me only knows self-defense, and fighting someone called Demon King who sounds dangerous is impossible da Yo?”

“U-um, when Heroes are summoned, they receive a Blessing from the goddess. With that power, it is believed you can fight the Demon King. Please bring out the orb.”

At Sylphine’s call, a man nearby brought over something like a crystal ball.

“This is called the ‘Blessing Orb’. It allows us to examine your Blessings.”

“Convenient item da Ne! Me can go first da Yo?”

“Yes, please.”

When Koda-san touched the ‘Blessing Orb’ after hearing the explanation, it shone brightly.

“Me Blessing is \<Creative Ingenuity> da Yo! Looks like Me can make lots of items da Yo!”

In game terms, that would be a production-type skill.

However, it did not really suit the word Hero.

I also placed my hand on the ‘Blessing Orb’.

“Then it’s my turn. My Blessing is \<Heavenly Eye>. It seems I can see various things.”

“…That is rare.”

Sylphine frowned slightly.

“Among past Heroes, at least one always had a combat-oriented Blessing. From what I hear, neither of you has a Blessing that directly increases combat ability.”

Indeed, having two support-type abilities felt questionable.

Or perhaps there was a reason we did not need boosted combat power.

“It is also said that Heroes grow strong easily regardless of their Blessings. We would like you to stay in this kingdom for a while and undergo training.”

Even if we were Heroes, we were originally just Japanese people. Training would be necessary.

“Right. May I ask one more thing?”

“Yes, what is it?”

It was a bit hard to ask, but it would be bad not to.

“Are our enemies only the Demon King? Are demons also enemies?”

“…The Demon King is the king of the demon race. Naturally, demons are also enemies of humanity.”

Sylphine answered, seeming a bit hesitant.

“Then why are there two demons here right now?”

“…”

“W-what!?”

“We weren’t told that!”

Sylphine fell silent, but the people around us cried out in shock.

They looked around in confusion.

This must be the effect of \<Heavenly Eye>. I could see people’s information like a game status screen.

And I noticed that two people here had their race listed as demon.

“Oh, you mean Sylphine-chan da Yo?”

“…”

“Impossible!”

“Princess Sylphine!?”

At Koda-san’s words, the commotion grew even louder.

People backed away from Sylphine.

“You noticed?”

“No! Me didn’t know she was demon da Yo. She looks like little girl, but her mannerisms felt like old woman da Yo! In Koda’s book, loli-baba is not little girl. Objections accepted da Yo!”

This lolicon is dangerous.

“The other one is NINJA stuck to the ceiling da LO!”

“You noticed that too…”

The other demon was clinging to the ceiling like a ninja, but her presence was hidden like optical camouflage.

I could see her, though.

“Oh, yes! She is real little girl da Ne! Me can tell by smell da Yo!”

This lolicon is seriously dangerous.

He exposed the secret I uncovered with my Blessing using his lolicon powers.

“Kukukuku…”

Sylphine, who had been silent, suddenly started laughing.

“Kuku, I let my guard down, thinking you were freshly summoned Heroes. That’s right. I am a demon. My name is Romarier. One of the Demon King’s Four Heavenly Kings, ‘Romarier of Falsehood.’”

Romarier, who had been disguised as the princess, released her transformation.

What appeared was a purple-skinned woman in her late twenties.

“Just as expected, BBA da Yo…”

Koda-san muttered something.

“A Four Heavenly King!?”

“Impossible! Why are you here!?”

“Demons shouldn’t be able to enter the place where Heroes are summoned!”

It seemed there was a safety measure to protect newly summoned Heroes.

But the fact that demons were here meant it had failed.

“There are exploits in this world. Remember that. And obviously I came to get a front-row seat to the Hero summoning, right? Ahh, what a shame. I thought I could easily assassinate the only two Heroes.”

This Romarier definitely has a bad personality.

“Is the real Princess Sylphine alive?”

“Who knows? Ah, you can relax. Since I stole her appearance, that means she’s still alive. Though I can’t guarantee she’ll stay that way forever.”

At least that was good news.

“You should worry about yourselves instead. Since you’ve been found out, I’ve decided to kill you both… Londrine, help me.”

“It can’t be helped.”

The ninja jumped down next to Romarier, deactivating her camouflage.

She looked about ten years old and was dressed in ninja garb.

According to Koda-san, her appearance matched her real age.

“With two of us, we can kill you almost simultaneously, and you won’t get stronger. Now, die!”

“‘Phantom Londrine’, here I go.”

Londrine rushed at me with a short blade, while Romarier drew a longsword from somewhere and attacked Koda-san.

“I’ll recieve your life!”

Londrine ran at inhuman speed, aiming her dagger at my heart.

At the same time, she activated her invisibility ability.

To normal people, it would look like she suddenly vanished, but it was nowhere near enough to fool my eyes. Don’t underestimate someone who can face two monsters with just his eyes.

“Oops.”

“What!?”

I shifted my center of gravity and avoided Londrine’s charge.

“Tch! You got lucky…!”

“Don’t lump me together with Jin.”

Ignoring my displeasure, Londrine attacked again.

Since I had the chance, I decided to use another effect of \<Heavenly Eye>.

In that moment, my viewpoint increased by one.

Like a TPS (third-person shooter), I could see myself from above.

They don’t call it a third eye for nothing.

“There.”

“Why!? How can you dodge an attack from behind!?”

I avoided Londrine’s attack without looking at her.

“Die! Die! Die! Why can’t I hit you!?”

I dodged her attacks again and again.

No matter how fast she was, as long as I could see her, she was no threat.

In battle, being able to ‘see’ is the most powerful weapon of all.

“Looks like I can fight well enough.”

“Don’t mock me!”

Enraged, Londrine’s attacks became slightly sloppy.

That was a mistake.

“Got you!”

“Too bad!”

I deliberately dodged Londrine’s charge at the last possible moment and swept her legs at the edge of timing.

“Sorry.”

“Gyah!?”

She thought she had hit me. She never imagined I would dodge.

Londrine lost her balance and fell hard.

“Ugooooo…”

She rolled around on the floor in pain.

“What about Koda-san…?”

Since Londrine was not as much of a threat as expected, I checked on Koda-san.

“Gaah…”

There, I saw Romarier with a hand protruding from her back, blood spilling from her mouth, and Koda-san with his hand stained in blood, having pierced Romarier’s heart with a knife-hand strike.

“I-impossible…”

“Shut up da Yo. BBA.”

Koda-san mercilessly pulled his hand out.

Romarier collapsed and died.

“R-Romarier… Damn it! I’ll remember this!”

Recovered from her fall, Londrine fled, leaving behind a parting threat.

“Alright, then we need to hurry da Yo!”

Koda-san started running.

Curious, I followed him.

Once we left the great hall, I realized this was a detached part of the royal palace.

“Koda-san, you were strong.”

“Just self-defense da Yo!”

He answered casually while running.

That was not the self-defense I knew.

“Oh, right. Asai-kun, thank you da Ne.”

“? You don’t need to thank me for anything.”

“At the end, you tripped Londrine-chan da Lo? I saw her panties then da Ne. Purple panties at that age were sexy da Ne! Thanks!”

“…”

What should I do? I have no confidence about working with this person from now on.

“And also, thanks for not killing Londrine-chan da Yo! It would have been easy for you da Lo?”

“Well, if you ask whether I could have, I probably could have. But is that something to thank me for?”

I did not like killing, but if I had to, I could have done it.

“A little girl’s death is a loss to the world da Yo! Asai-kun deserves praise for choosing to let her live da Lo!”

“The wall of common sense is thick…”

We could understand each other’s words, but it felt like we were not communicating.

“By the way, where are you headed, Koda-san?”

“Isn’t it obvious da Lo? To the real Sylphine-chan da Yo!”

“You know where she is!?”

Even with my Blessing, I could not find her location.

“Of course da Lo! Sylphine-chan is imprisoned by BBA da Yo! That means she can’t go to the toilet and has wet herself da Yo! If it’s a little girl’s wetting, Me can track it within one kilometer for sure da Ne!”

Officer, it’s this one.

“Here da Ne.”

Koda-san took a key from his pocket and opened a locked door.

“That key?”

“Me borrowed it from BBA da Yo.”

Thorough.

Inside the room was the real Sylphine, bound in her underwear and weakened.

Just as Koda-san said, her underwear was wet, showing signs she had wet herself.

“Are you okay da Yo!”

Ignoring the mess, Koda-san picked Sylphine up.

Looking closely, the hand that had been bloodstained earlier was now clean.

“Y-you are…?”

After removing the gag, she asked in a hoarse voice.

“We are the summoned Heroes da Yo! We defeated the demon who disguised herself as Sylphine-chan and came to save you da Yo!”

“Ah, ah! Thank you… thank you very much!”

Sylphine was deeply moved and cried.

“Thirsty da Lo? Hungry da Lo? Here is drink and chocolate da Yo! Lick the chocolate without biting da Yo!”

“Y-yes…”

Koda-san took out a cheap drink and a round chocolate in wrapping and gave them to Sylphine.

Normally I would not think much of it, but given Koda-san’s past behavior, the fact that he had children’s snacks made me uneasy.

I should avoid bringing up topics from our original world with Koda-san as much as possible.

After rescuing Sylphine, we were once again welcomed as Heroes.

It was a turbulent start to Hero life, but after that, nothing major happened.

The two of us stayed in the Kingdom of Sanokia for a while, learning about this world and training.

Then, with sufficient equipment and attendants, we set out on a journey to defeat the Demon King.

Looking back, perhaps the reason we did not receive combat-oriented Blessings was because our base combat power was already more than sufficient.

My \<Heavenly Eye> was not specialized for combat, but it was extremely useful as support, and Koda-san’s \<Creative Ingenuity> could create weapons, helping expand our fighting strength. In hindsight, it was probably just right.

As Koda-san and I traveled around the world, we gained even more strength and eventually defeated the Demon King, but that is another story.

That the accompanying Sylphine became pregnant at the mere age of ten is also another story.

Officer, please come to this other world.

---

**AN:** In storytelling, the author appearing directly is a forbidden move, close to a taboo, and unless done extremely well, it makes the entire story fall flat. Perhaps bringing a guest character from a past story a little closer is just barely acceptable?

Well, there is absolutely no relation between Koda-san and the author.

Their hobbies and tastes are of completely different people.

**Editor’s note:** I thought this was an April fools…
