# **159: A Relaxed Schedule and Substitutes for Special Powers**

**AN:** A new arc.

Volume 11: The Adventurers Guild Arc … (provisional) begins.

---

The Adventurers Guild is a neutral organization that exists across nations around the world, managing adventurers.

In principle, the Adventurers Guild proclaims neutrality and holds as a rule that it does not involve itself in conflicts between nations. Of course, there are exceptions. I know that much.

While it does not take part in disputes, its ties with nations are close. High-ranking adventurers are treated on par with nobles, and there are various considerations shown by states toward adventurers (and the Guild).

The land where the Adventurers Guild Headquarters is located is called the “Guild Federation District.”

Its land area is larger than that of a small country, but since it is, in name at least, a neutral organization not belonging to any nation, it goes by the name of a federation district.

The Guild Federation District lies south of Castal, beyond several countries. Being an inland country… no, an inland district, sea travel is impossible, so getting there normally takes quite a lot of time.

Of course, if you use air travel, that is a different story.

As an aside, our Advance Trading Company has not expanded into the Guild Federation District.

Distance is one reason, but the biggest reason is that I anticipated events related to the Adventurers Guild would likely occur there, so I instructed them to avoid it.

Places where events are likely to happen sooner or later, such as the Crimson Empire or the Elf Village, are areas where I have them hold back on expansion and information gathering. I want to save the fun for later.

Back to the topic.

The Adventurers Guild Headquarters in the Guild Federation District is led by a guildmaster called the Guild Grandmaster.

The Guild Grandmaster is the de facto top of the Guild Federation District and all guilds throughout the world.

The Guild Grandmaster is said to be the strongest S-rank adventurer, and rumors say she is apparently a woman.

Hey, you there. Do not say things like, “She is basically like a female royal, so you are guaranteed to become her subordinate.”

What if she is elderly?

The Guild Federation District and the Adventurers Guild Headquarters are a holy land for adventurers, and the top destination adventurers want to visit at least once.

It is also a place frequently visited by many high-ranking adventurers.

However, S-rank adventurers from abroad surprisingly do not go there often. Many S-rank adventurers are eccentric, and more often than not they completely ignore common ideals of admiration.

“We did not intend to go to the Adventurers Guild Headquarters, since there was no benefit for us.”

Right now, I am receiving a report from Claude, an S-rank adventurer, at my residence in Castal.

“Eh? What a waste. Even though Claude and the others are an S-rank adventurer party with incredible buzz…”

Mio voices her dissatisfaction.

Many S-rank adventurers are strong-willed, and it is rare for S-rank adventurers to form parties with each other.

Cases like Claude’s, where a single party consists entirely of S-rank adventurers and has stayed together since before reaching S-rank, are extremely rare. Apparently, there is no precedent.

“But you were talking about going to the Guild Federation District, were you not?”

It seems Sera heard a bit before the report.

“Yes. We had no plans to go ourselves, but they asked us to come. It was a proper named request… Please read this.”

I read the request document handed to me by Claude.

“Let me see. A summons from the Adventurers Guild Headquarters. The Guild Grandmaster has taken interest in a very rare S-rank adventurer party. Using a Lesser Wind Dragon, you are to come to the Adventurers Guild Headquarters immediately… That is the gist of it.”

It is written a bit more politely in reality, but that is the summary.

“Yes. Since it was a direct named request from the Guild Grandmaster herself, we were strongly pressured by the Guild staff not to refuse. In the end, we accepted the request and will be heading to the Guild Federation District.”

This is exactly the kind of pressure that makes people avoid becoming high-ranking adventurers.

“When do you leave?”

“Including preparations, we will depart within today or tomorrow. We will be using the Lesser Wind Dragon you gave us, Jin-sama.”

“Is the Lesser Wind Dragon proving useful?”

“Yes, it has been a tremendous help.”

I gave it to them to in celebration for reaching S-rank. I am glad it is useful.

…If they could use ‘Portal’, it would be instantaneous, but that would be hard to keep secret.

“That aside, why did you come to report to me in the first place? Until now, the only times you came to report were when something major happened in your adventuring activities.”

Was there some kind of problem or event?

You do not seem flustered, so it does not feel urgent, but…

“I apologize for taking your time.”

Claude apologizes.

“No, it is not that it is bad. I was just curious if something happened. It is not a problem?”

“No, it is not a problem. Along with the request letter from the Guild Grandmaster I mentioned earlier, there was an enclosed free pass for the hot springs, which are a tourist attraction in the Guild Federation District. I thought I could present it to you, Jin-sama, since you enjoy sightseeing, so I asked for your time.”

“Go on.”

I straighten my posture and listen.

According to Claude, the land where the Guild Federation District is located has many volcanoes and is also famous as a hot spring region.

As expected of the holy land of adventurers, the hot springs have effects like enhanced healing of injuries and fatigue recovery, all things adventurers would appreciate. It is no wonder adventurers want to visit at least once.

Missing such an obvious tourist destination was a painful mistake.

I regret not gathering information on the Guild Federation District.

The Guild Grandmaster is the top of the Guild Federation District. In other words, she is also the top of the hot spring region.

Apparently, as a service, separate from the request fee to Claude and the others, free pass tickets for the hot springs (lodging not included) were enclosed.

“Please accept the hot spring free passes.”

“Well, that reaction is only natural.”

Mio nods in agreement.

The others show similar looks of understanding.

“I am sorry, but I do not intend to take them. I have no intention of taking away rights you earned as rewards, and I do not want to put myself in a position where I owe a debt to someone I do not even know.”

“I… I see…”

If I, who am not a direct party to the request, use the free pass, it could create a debt to the Guild Grandmaster.

It might be an exaggeration, but I dislike it, so that is that.

“That said, the information about the hot spring region was appreciated. I might go myself…”

Looking around, no one looks displeased.

“Alright. Then the next destination is the Guild Federation District.”

“Yay! A hot spring episode!”

Mio is especially happy.

A hot spring episode is fine, but Mio is the one being seen, you know? She may not have sex appeal, but there is demand.

“Jin-sama, how will we head to the Guild Federation District?”

Maria asks, so I think for a moment.

Lately, I have often acted as the Queen’s Knight Gene, but there is no need for that this time.

Rather, I will be in the position of Claude’s mentor. In other words, it is been a while since Shindo Jin mode.

“We have two options. Ride on a dragonkin and accompany Claude and the others, or have them set up a Portal and head there directly.”

“Blue-chan will definitely say she wants you to ride her.”

The 100% dere Sky Dragon would defintely say that.

However, the problem is that Blue has started to be recognized as Gene’s mount.

If Jin rides Gene’s mount, my identity would obviously be exposed.

Well, I have said this before, but at this point, I would not really mind if my identity were exposed. Still, I would hate such a pathetic way of being found out…

But it is also a problem that I cannot ride Blue as Jin. I should think of something.

“This time, ‘Portal’. Claude and the others would not be able to relax if I were with them, right?”

“It is true that we would be nervous. Though there are girls who would be happy…”

Probably the dog girl and the perverted girl.

Roro has decent development and an unbelievable amount of sex appeal for someone around elementary school age, so I privately call her the perverted girl in my head.

In terms of development, Maria is not losing, but for some reason I do not feel much sex appeal from her. Probably because her believer component is too strong.

“If it is a net negative overall, then it is better not to accompany them.”

“Coco and Roro will get angry…”

“Tell them I will accompany them if they can convince everyone.”

“Understood.”

If everyone truly wants it, I would not mind going along.

Claude leaves the room, so now it is a discussion with the main party.

“Raise your hand if you do not want to go to the hot springs.”

No one raises their hand.

“Then there is no problem with everyone accompanying us.”

“If we do not accompany Claude and the others, there will be some time until we arrive at the Guild Federation District, right? What shall we do during that time?”

“Relax as usual.”

“Master’s customary relaxation mode, huh.”

《Relax!》

“Though when you say relax, it usually ends up involving a surprising number of incidents.”

The members who know my habit of relaxing nod in agreement.

“More accurately, relaxing includes going to the hot springs. It is unlikely that hectic events would happen at a hot spring resort.”

“Master? Why are you deliberately raising a flag? Hot spring resorts are practically treasure troves of events. Something will definitely happen.”

I know.

“Jin-sama. For protection, may I accompany you, Master?”

“That is unusual. You usually come along as a guard without saying anything.”

It is rare for Maria to ask.

That is because she always comes along by default.

“Would it be acceptable for me to accompany you to public baths?”

“…Ah, I see.”

So that is it. If Maria accompanies me, that means entering the men’s bath.

“In a dangerous space like a public bath where one must be unguarded, I cannot mentally endure leaving Jin-sama alone. Please allow me to accompany you.”

“Do you not feel resistance to entering a space with naked men?”

“? I feel no particular resistance. Serving Jin-sama is the most important thing.”

Maria has zero interest in outsiders.

“That said, I want Maria to enjoy the hot springs too…”

“If Jin-sama says so, then after Jin-sama finishes bathing, I will entrust protection to Sera-chan and enter the bath.”

Her resolve does not waver in the slightest.

“You understand that a woman entering the men’s bath is a problem, right?”

“I will use \<Non-Attribute Magic> to become invisible and hide my form. With \<Barrier Arts>, I will also suppress my presence and scent.”

Maria is a professional pervert.

I never thought Maria would misuse \<Non-Attribute Magic>.

“Still… How about having Tamo-san act as guard instead? Can you not give up?”

I cannot bring myself to put Maria into a public bath that is not mixed.

Tamo-san has no gender, so no problem.

“Tamo-san… Let me think for a moment.”

Maria thinks for a while.

“…If Tamo-san is guarding you, then I will enter the women’s bath. However, in an emergency, I will immediately rush to Jin-sama.”

“Understood. That will do. …I really want Maria to be able to relax in the hot springs.”

As long as she is away from me, that is probably difficult.

“Master, Master.”

“What is it?”

Mio calls out.

“If you wear swimsuits and go into a mixed bath, everything is solved.”

“…That is an option!”

It is a hot spring resort, so there are probably mixed baths (Probably).

If it is a mixed bath, then Maria and I entering the same bath is no problem. No problem.

In the end, Coco and Roro failed to convince everyone, so it was decided that we would not accompany them on the aerial journey.

That means we will be in relaxation mode for the next few days.

First, I went to visit Ulysses, the High Elf “Princess Shrine Maiden” who had joined the Advance Trading Company’s magical tool development division.

This time, only Maria accompanies me. The others will relax however they like.

“I came to check on things.”

“Oh, Jin-san, good day. I am so happy you came in the morning.”

“Good morning.”

“Good day to you as well, Maria-san.”

When I drop by the Advance Trading Company base in the capital of the Kingdom of Castal, Ulysses approaches with a beaming smile.

I am completely hands-off when it comes to managing the company, so this is hearsay, but apparently the magical tool development division was officially launched recently thanks to Ulysses joining.

As an aside, due to the highly confidential nature of the work, the development room is located quite deeply within the company grounds (which are fairly large).

Ordinary spies would be unable to infiltrate this far.

Until now, the Advance Trading Company had not dealt with magical tools.

The reason lies in the special nature of the \<Magical Tool Creation> skill.

First, the \<Magical Tool Creation> skill alone does not allow for the creation of many magical tools.

At low levels, you can only create magical tools akin to daily necessities. Even if you raise it near the maximum level, you can hardly create anything beyond an item box.

In fact, the special magical tools I collect require derivative skills in addition to \<Magical Tool Creation>.

In this world, the existence of skills is not easily recognized.

However, there are many professions where “innate talent” plays a major role. Magical tool crafters are famous among such professions as a rare occupation that can earn stable income.

Moreover, discovering that talent is easy. You just need to have a child touch a magical tool.

If they possess \<Magical Tool Creation>, they apparently feel something.

Those with \<Magical Tool Creation> are often sent out to work immediately.

Trading companies also try to secure anyone with \<Magical Tool Creation> right away.

In other words, there are very few hidden \<Magical Tool Creation> holders in the wild.

Among my subordinates, there is none except one.

Derivative skills of \<Magical Tool Creation> can only be acquired rarely by those who were born with \<Magical Tool Creation>.

Even if I grant Magical Tool Creation later, they cannot learn them.

The subordinate who originally had \<Magical Tool Creation> does not seem to enjoy making magical tools as a hobby either…

What I am saying is that Ulysses, who has Magical Tool Creation LV10, its derivative skill \<Forest Wisdom>, and the production-boosting \<Earth Memory>, is an extremely important figure in magical tool production.

By the way, \<Forest Wisdom> is among the highest-grade derivative skills.

“So? Have you gotten used to the new environment?”

“Yes, I am fine. Compared to the sealing crystal, any place is paradise.”

“…That is true.”

If you compare it to 6,000 years of being sealed, anywhere would be better.

“Still, there was no exaggeration in what you said, Jin-san. There are truly an astonishing number of incredible people here.”

Ulysses says, impressed yet slightly frustrated.

“Standing next to you must be truly difficult. Well, I have all the time in the world, so I will take it slowly.”

“A High Elf’s slowly is really slow. Will I not die before then?”

“Eh? Do you die with a normal human lifespan?”

“Probably…”

I am not very confident.

“Even if you do die with a normal lifespan, I will stay with you until the end, so do not worry. I will never age, so I will stay by your side in my young form forever.”

“O-okay…”

You can glimpse the weight of her love in her words.

And she is not even a believer. How mysterious.

(I am envious.)

Maria mutters softly.

That one is heavy too. But she is a believer.

“So, what did you come for, Jin-san? If it is just to see me, I would be delighted.”

“As I said at the start, I came to check on things. You have already started making magical tools, right? Collecting interesting magical tools is my hobby.”

Not just any magical tool, only those I find interesting.

The troublesome part is that even I do not have a clear standard for what I find interesting.

“That is perfect timing. I have tried making a few things over the past few days. I hope you like them…”

She shows me the magical tools she created.

The first is a crystal ball like one used by fortune-tellers.

“This is a magical tool for long-distance communication. It does not show images, but it has a wider effective range than the Far-Seer Twin Mirror and does not take up space. Its magic stone consumption is moderate.”

She immediately brought out something that shatters common sense.

This world has difficulties with long-distance communication and transport.

Any magical tool capable of long-distance communication is almost always managed at the national level. They are large and require massive amounts of magic stones.

“Each one has a unique number assigned, so you can tell who is calling, and you can refuse if you do not want to communicate.”

“A phone!”

It was a rough retort, but it really was nothing other than a phone.

“Denwa? What is that? Did it not suit your taste? I was quite confident in it…”

“It is amazing, but it resembles something from my original world… too much, so I reacted.”

Visually, they are not similar at all, but functionally they are very similar.

“Really? Was it widespread in your original world?”

“Yeah. It was probably one of the most widespread tools in the world.”

“In Jin-sama’s world, there was one in every household.”

Maria adds, but… how does Maria know?

A: She heard it from Mio.

Right, Maria had heard all sorts of stories about my original world from Mio.

“Then it should be fine to sell this.”

“Wait. The impact is too big. We need to think carefully.”

This is not something that should be spread thoughtlessly.

“If you say so, Jin-san, then I understand. Originally, I do not have the authority to decide sales anyway, since I do not know the current era. It will be decided through discussions with the upper management of Advance Trading Company.”

“That is good, but…”

There is a 6,000-year gap, and she is a High Elf who had little interaction with the world to begin with. I cannot expect common sense.

The good sense of the company’s upper management is required.

I am technically the top, right? Good sense… I am not confident.

“Next is this.”

Next, she brings out something like a mat.

“If you place this in two locations, it allows for bidirectional teleportation.”

“That is just ‘Portal’!”

“Unfortunately, it is not as convenient as ‘Portal’. The magic stone consumption is significant, it only allows one-to-one teleportation, and there is a limit to the distance.”

Listing the drawbacks makes it sound unimpressive, but in reality it would have enough impact to break the world’s common sense.

Still…

“I want to ask one thing. Is it a coincidence that you keep bringing out magical tools with effects I have seen somewhere before?”

“No, it is intentional. More specifically, they are substitutes for your and Sakura-san’s Special Powers. To put it bluntly, they are decoys to obscure your powers. Advance Trading Company rose to prominence through your powers, right? But if we keep those powers secret, we need alternative means. My job is to create magical tools that substitute for your abilities.”

I have heard that Advance Trading Company is rumored to possess teleportation-type magical tools.

If Special Powers cannot be made public, then they decided to make the rumors into fact.

Apparently, she discussed with the company members and roughly decided on the direction of magical tool creation.

“I see. That really is a job only you can do.”

Since there are no other derivative skill holders, it was inevitable that Ulysses would take the lead.

“Yes. First, I decided to start by building a track record. The hurdle to accompany you on your journey is high, but I have time, so I will start slowly and do what I can.”

It seems her desire to accompany my journey has not changed.

“Next, my goal is to stop or slow time inside item boxes.”

So the next target is \<Infinite Storage>.

This is also one of Advance Trading Company’s trump cards.

“Do you have a lead?”

“Yes. It will certainly require trial and error, but it does not seem completely impossible.”

I cannot really use \<Magical Tool Creation> myself, so I do not know the sensation, but Ulysses seems to see a general direction.

“Ultimately, I want to be able to provide the same level of service without relying on your powers. That way, there will be no risk of information about Special Powers leaking from Advance Trading Company.”

“Now that you mention it, Advance Trading Company uses Special Powers pretty much without restraint…”

Normally, it would be nearly impossible for a company to rise this far in such a short time.

That feat was largely due to being able to use Special Powers almost without limitation.

The risk of information leakage that Ulysses worries about is low, but there is another concern.

Rising through Special Powers means that if Sakura or I were to disappear, or if Special Powers became unusable, most operations would collapse.

We have no plans to disappear for now, but considering risk, securing alternatives is essential.

“It seems Ulysses’ work is even more important than I thought.”

“Yes. Leave it to me. I will definitely be useful to you, Jin-san.”

“Yeah. Do your best.”

I was the one who decided to have Ulysses make magical tools.

At first, I just thought it would be fine if she made interesting ones, but before I knew it, it had become quite an important operation.

Unexpected.

Later, I learned that Sakuya’s intentions were mixed into this policy.

If Ulysses made magical tools normally, the magical tools Sakuya had prepared as “compensation to me” would lose value.

Thinking that would be bad, Sakuya apparently came up with various pretexts to have her make magical tools that would not compete with the ones she collected.

Sakuya is surprisingly busy working behind the scenes.

Once the discussion settled, I asked something that had been bothering me.

“…This is a late question, but why is Midori here?”

In fact, the Dryad Midori is in the same room.

She has not moved at all, so I thought she was a green ornament, but upon closer inspection, it was Midori.

“She is also part of the magical tool development division.”

“Why?”

I do not understand.

It would be difficult for Midori to make magical tools.

“Actually, the \<Magical Tool Development> Division is also called the ‘Special Powers Substitute Development Division’ behind the scenes. It is also a measure to avoid using the word ‘Special Power’ openly.”

From the earlier discussion, I understand the importance of preparing substitutes for Special Powers.

While I personally want interesting magical tools, it is understandable that the division’s main purpose becomes substitute creation.

“In that sense, she is my senior. After all, the ‘Divine Medicine Soma ‘substitutes for Sakura-san’s magic ‘Revive’.”

“Ah, that happened.”

There was a time when we pretended that limb regeneration by ‘Revive’ was due to ‘Divine Medicine Soma’.

“Some other secret medicines also substitute for Special Power effects, so I had her join just in case. Additionally, the dwarf Mimi-san, who can create special products, has also joined. She is usually at the forge, so she rarely comes here.”

“I see. They are all people who can make special items.”

Ulysses with magical tools, Midori with secret medicines, Mimi with holy swords and demonic swords.

All require special skills and produce extraordinary effects.

“Of course, secret medicines and holy swords still require secrecy about the creator and method, similar to Special Powers… but that is better than exposing Special Powers, right?”

“Yeah. They are rare or unique skills, but not something absolutely no one else can do. It is better than Special Powers.”

Exposing Special Powers would be bad.

Well, in the sense that Orihara already knows, it is too late, but still…

Even though she is being discussed nearby, Midori shows no interest at all.

“She really does not move…”

Midori, with her reclusive nature, is still spacing out in a poorly lit spot.

Despite being a plant monster, she prefers shaded areas.

Spacing out is plant-like, so that is fine.

“I have basically never seen her move beyond the bare minimum. She does move a bit when she has a quota for secret medicines, but voluntary action is mostly limited to moving between spots.”

“What is a Spot?”

“Apparently she has spots that are good for spacing out. I do not know the details…”

As an aside, she only moves via Portal.

Telling a plant monster to exercise or she will gain weight would be meaningless.

“…”

Midori, who had shown no interest in us until now, shuffles over.

《After a long time… Jin’s magic power… give me?》

She came straight to beg for magic power, MP.

I understand that MP is needed for \<Secret Medicine Compounding>, so I have given Midori plenty of MP and \<MP Auto-Recovery>.

However, it seems absorbing it from others via \<MP Absorption> is the tastiest and most pleasant, so I hear she occasionally begs the mansion staff.

Midori prefers secluded shady places, so she has very few opportunities to come into contact with me.

Even if she wanted my MP, she did not have the chance. Going out of her way to ask was probably never an option to begin with.

“I do not mind giving MP, but the visual is…”

Midori’s MP drain is done through the mouth.

The safest body part to put in her mouth is a finger, but the visual is not safe.

Midori is a monster, but her appearance is that of a young girl. Having a young girl lick my finger is bad.

What is worse is that among bad visuals, this one is comparatively mild.

How many times have I said bad…?

《Please…》

“Well, fine. I am used to bad visuals. …I should not be getting used to them…”

Recently, the strongest was “making a naked high school girl erect.”

I give permission, so Midori shuffles closer again and puts my finger in her mouth.

I feel my MP being steadily absorbed. That said, it is so little that Maria does not stop it. If it were enough to affect me, she would have intervened immediately.

《Mm… mm… Jin’s… thicker…?》

“State the subject.”

Midori, absorbing MP, says it with a blissful expression.

She omitted the subject ‘magic power’, making not just the visual but the scene itself bad.

What does it mean that magic power is thick?

I do not know the reason or basis, but I have far too many ideas.

The badness index is bad, so let us finish quickly.

I manipulate the flow of MP in my body and imagine pushing it toward Midori.

《Mm…! Mm…!? It is… strong… ah, it is overflowing… leaking… do not look…?!》

The next moment, Midori jumped somewhere via Portal.

The lines were bad until the end, but what happened?

On that day, a new secret medicine called “Dryad’s Drop” was added to Midori’s repertoire.

# **160: Racial Mutation and Angels**

**AN:** This chapter is labeled as the Guild Arc, but in reality it is divided into three major parts.

1. Before going to the guild, matters related to my subordinates.

2. The Guild Union District.

3. ???

4. After struggling with the chapter title, I ended up using the most straightforward one: part 2.

---

There are countless skills in this world, among them some possessed by only a single person in the entire world, so-called Unique Skills, as well as race-specific skills.

One of my hobbies is collecting such rare skills.

There are broadly three ways to collect rare skills.

The first is killing monsters or enemies and taking them.

The second is collecting them from subordinates such as slaves or tamed monsters.

The third is taking just one point from someone who owes me a favor, turning it into two points, and then returning it.

Naturally, I use \<Life and Death Authority> for all of them.

Collecting skills is fine and all, but as mentioned earlier, there are quite a few skills, including race-specific ones, that have restrictions on who can use them.

In those cases, I leave the skill with the person instead of taking it.

I am a collector, but I am not particularly attached to what I collect. You could say that collecting itself is the hobby, rather than owning them afterward.

“Welcome, Jin-sama.”

“Yeah. How are things?”

“Everything is calm at the moment.”

After receiving Alta’s report, Maria and I came to Castal’s mansion, specifically the maid dormitory.

We walk a short distance through the dormitory toward the room where the girl in question is.

“This is the room. Please, go ahead.”

I enter the room and check on the young girl sleeping on the bed… Shion’s condition.

It seems she is sleeping on the bed.

Shion was an orphan in the Kingdom of Estea. I saved her when she was about to be killed inside the labyrinth by the orphanage director, and she became attached to me, so I brought her back with me. Hearing only that part, it sounds like kidnapping.

And she had one mysterious, probably rare skill.

This is it.

\<Branch of the Genealogy Tree>

When unlocked, the user’s race randomly changes (human-type). After that, this skill automatically disappears.

To put it in extremely simple terms, it is a gacha.

Until the skill is unlocked, even Alta cannot determine its details, which is astonishing.

Since such an astonishing skill had been unlocked, there was no way I would not come to see it.

“A new species was definitely unexpected, though…”

“Jin-sama, is something wrong?”

“No, it’s nothing.”

Answering Maria, I look again at Shion sleeping on the bed.

Shion is lying face down on the bed. On her back, wings like those of a white bird have grown.

This is Shion’s status.

Name: Shion  

Gender: Female  

Age: 5  

Race: Angel  

Title: Jin’s Slave, Progenitor of Angels  

Skills: \<Flight LV1> \<Transformation LV1> \<Holy Magic LV1> \<Contract of Heaven LV >  

· Maid-related skills omitted.

When I saved her, she was definitely “Race: Human”, but the moment the skill was unlocked, it changed to “Race: Angel.”

And as I muttered earlier, “Angel” does not exist among any known races. It is a completely new race. Since Alta said so, there is no doubt.

Additionally, \<Holy Magic> is apparently a race-specific skill unique to angels that has never existed before.

Oh, and \<Contract of Heaven> is simply a pure Unique Skill.

“U-uun…”

At that point, Shion slowly woke up.

With her long blonde hair, the angel wings suit her extremely well. As a feathered little girl, does she overlap in character with Dora?

“Where… am I?”

Shion squirms and gets up from her face-down position.

With bird-like wings, she cannot sleep on her back. Dora also sleeps in her human form when resting. Except when she’s used as a body pillow (in dragon form).

“Ah, master!”

Still a little unsteady, she gets up, spots me, and immediately breaks into a smile.

For some reason, Shion is very attached to me.

“How’s your body? I heard you collapsed from the strain.”

“I’m okay!”

“That’s good.”

Even if she accepted it herself, hearing that she collapsed is still worrying.

“So, how was it?”

“Yeah, it was more interesting than I expected.”

“Yay!”

Just the fact that her race changes randomly is interesting enough, but becoming a completely new species is an even better result than I had expected.

“Then, as promised, will you tell me about it?”

“Yeah!”

Naturally, I explained \<Branch of the Genealogy Tree> to Shion.

Shion understood and accepted the racial change caused by the skill.

\<Branch of the Genealogy Tree> is a special skill. It is an innate skill, and only the original owner can unlock it.

In other words, even if I were to take the skill from Shion, someone else could not unlock it.

Incidentally, the condition for unlocking it is “the owner turning five years old.”

A change in race places a heavy burden on both body and mind.

The mental burden can be prevented with \<Multiple Existence>, but that does not mean it is without danger.

I told Shion that if she disliked pain or danger, she did not have to keep this skill, but Shion chose to possess \<Branch of the Genealogy Tree> and unlock it.

The reason was “because I get to talk with you.”

For most of my maid subordinates, time spent talking with me is apparently so valuable that it cannot be exchanged for money.

That is also why we regularly hold small social gatherings.

In any case, knowing that I had a strong interest in this skill and that I would personally interview her once her race changed, Shion apparently did not hesitate.

Even so, the physical burden was too much for a five-year-old body, and she lost consciousness the moment the skill was unlocked.

According to Alta, when both physical and mental strain are present, a five-year-old cannot endure it, and most would die.

And so, as promised, I began gathering information about “angels” while talking with Shion.

Since this is a completely new race, it seems even Alta needs time to gather information. Also, I think it is best to hear about sensory aspects directly from the person herself.

“Flying in the sky is hard.”

“My body feels light.”

“If I try hard, I think I can put my wings away.”

“But right now, I can’t.”

“I can use magic.”

“Bad kids feel pain.”

“Liars feel pain.”

Since she is a little girl, it cannot be helped, but it is really all very sensory…

Well, I got the general idea.

First, since she has wings and the \<Flight> skill, she can fly. Even though her race just changed, Shion already started flying around.

She wobbles dangerously, but she seems to be getting used to it quickly.

With \<Transformation>, she can apparently take on a human form, but it seems difficult for now.

Since she was originally human, taking on a human form should not be that hard.

\<Holy Magic> is not simple attack magic. To put it simply, it is magic that is highly effective against “evil things.”

It deals massive damage to evil beings such as demons, evil spirits, and undead.

At skill level 1, the only spell she can use is “Divine Punishment”, which envelops a single target in light.

From the look of it, the power is nothing to scoff at. I tried having her use it on the Reaper, the boss of the 40th floor of the Estea Labyrinth, and it died instantly.

Shion leveled up a lot.

“Yay!”

\<Contract of Heaven> is a Unique Skill with the effect of enforcing contracts.

Any contract made using this skill cannot be broken. If one tries to break it, intense pain occurs, and in the worst case, death. Of course, the same applies if the skill user breaks the contract.

…However, there is one problem. I tried making a promise with Shion and then breaking it, but it was only itchy at most.

Apparently, it is classified as mental damage, which gets caught by the mental protection of \<Multiple Existence>. In other words, I can lie as much as I want. …I do not think that is right.

Though the fact that it managed to make me “itchy” despite the mental protection might be impressive in its own way.

Fair and intolerant of evil. That is probably the nature of the race “Angel.”

Still, is it kind of sad that there is an exception standing right in front of her from the very beginning?

And then, I also received Alta’s seal of approval.

A: I have checked thoroughly, and there is nothing that would suggest involvement with the Goddess. The race known as angels has no relation to the Goddess.

Good. That eliminates my biggest concern.

Honestly, given the race name, I was worried about involvement with the Goddess.

I have no intention of openly opposing the Goddess of this world, but my favorability with her is extremely low.

I really do not want to get carelessly involved.

In the worst case, if there had been any relation to the Goddess, I was prepared to use the magic “Rebirth”, created by Sakura, to turn her back into a human.

A: However, another small problem has come to light.

Oh no, Alta just said “problem”! That is scary!

A: Angels seem to be classified as monsters.

?

A: They are categorized as humanoid monsters, like the Dragonkin.

??

Isn’t \<Branch of the Genealogy Tree> supposed to be human-type, meaning humanoid races like humans, beastfolk, elves, and so on? Does it include humanoid monsters too?

A: Fundamentally, there is not a large difference between “humanoid races” and “certain humanoid monsters.” Humanoid monsters like Dragonkin and angels that do not possess magic stones are only classified as monsters for categorization purposes.

So they are classified as monsters, but in practice are no different from humans?

A: Yes. The difference is both large and small. For example, to make someone submit, humanoid races require \<Slave Arts>, while humanoid monsters require \<Monster Taming>. However, even humanoid monsters can register as adventurers if they do not have magic stones. The boundary is quite ambiguous.

Come to think of it, Dora was treated as a monster, yet she could register as an adventurer.

On the other hand, even though they were humanoid monsters, harpies like Chocolat, who had magic stones, could not become adventurers, so I made them mercenaries.

So, Alta, do you understand the logic behind that classification?

A: Unknown.

…In other words, something related to the Goddess. The will of the Goddess, perhaps.

There might be some meaning behind it. But even if I think about it now, I doubt I can reach the truth.

A: I apologize.

It is not your fault, Alta, so do not worry about it.

Still…

“Shion, do you like me?”

“I like you!”

She answered instantly, without a moment of hesitation.

“Do you regret becoming my slave?”

“I don’t!”

“Then, how about becoming my familiar?”

“Familiar?”

“It’s kind of like being a slave.”

“I will!”

Since I obtained her consent, I activate \<Monster Taming>.

You have tamed an Angel.  

Please name the Angel.

I could not suppress my curiosity and tried taming her, but I had not thought about the name.

“Shion, do you like your name?”

“I don’t really like it!”

“If I give you a new name…”

“Please!”

She did not even let me finish.

As usual, boom.

”Name her ‘Shion’”  

”Name her ‘Ange’”  

”Name her ‘Yukari’”

That is basically a single choice.

“Your new name is Ange. Nice to meet you.”

“Okay!”

Alright, her new status.

Name: Ange (Shion)  

Gender: Female  

Age: 5  

Race: Angel  

Title: Jin’s Slave, Jin’s Familiar, Progenitor of Angels  

Skills: \<Flight LV1> \<Transformation LV1> \<Holy Magic LV1> \<Contract of Heaven LV >  

· Maid-related skills omitted.

Oh, the slave title and familiar title are overlapping.

I talked with Shion, now Ange, until she was satisfied, then entrusted her to the maids once she started to look sleepy. It seems her stamina has not fully recovered yet, so I cannot push her too hard.

Thanks to Ange, I learned a lot of interesting things.

Alta, from now on, make sure to secure owners of \<Branch of the Genealogy Tree> whenever possible. My intuition tells me that skill cannot be left unattended.

A: Understood. I will inform the maids as well.

Oh, and forcibly separating them from their parents is a no-go.

Secretly enslaving them or anything like that (which would be vile in its own way) is also not allowed, handle it carefully.

A: I understand.

The next day.

A: We have already secured a child with \<Branch of the Genealogy Tree>.

Wow, that was faster than I expected.

Are there really that many people with \<Branch of the Genealogy Tree>?

A: No. Even one every hundred years would be considered many.

…Could it be because I got involved?

A close friend once complained to me that probability theory does not apply when I get involved.

But this time, whether I am involved or not should not matter, right? The child with \<Branch of the Genealogy Tree> must have been born before I came to this world, age-wise.

Well, there is no point overthinking things that cannot be helped…

So, what was the situation?

As I said yesterday, I assume you did not forcibly separate him from his parents.

A: Correct. He was a normal abandoned child. He is four years old, a boy.

A normal abandoned child, huh…

By the way, where was he?

A: In a country master has never visited. When Advance Trading Company expanded there to support master’s tourism, they happened to find him. He was in a hard-to-find place, so he likely would have starved to death by today.

Just in time.

A: Considering the possibility that his race may change in the future, it would be difficult to raise him publicly. He is currently entrusted to the orphanage in the Estea Labyrinth, but I recommend letting them raise him there.

Ah, the labyrinth orphanage.

That is where children abandoned in the labyrinth are gathered and raised. Since they are all considered dead children by society anyway, raising him there the same way is probably best.

So, for now, I decided to at least go check on him (with Maria).

The 51st floor of the Estea Kingdom’s labyrinth is a residential area for those related to the labyrinth.

Among them is the orphanage in question, run by labyrinth guardians and maids. Since the labyrinth is self-sufficient, it is highly rated that operating funds are essentially unnecessary.

That said, I generally try not to get too close.

The reason is…

“Hii!”

“Ah, ah…”

“(Tremble)”

The moment most of the orphans see me, they freeze like stone statues.

Apparently, the maids have educated them very strictly, so that they will absolutely never make a mistake in front of me.

Even the children who had gotten somewhat used to me when the orphanage was first established are the same. I went through all that effort to get them used to me with food…

It seems that when it comes to me, the usually kind orphanage maids become expressionless and jokes no longer work.

I can easily imagine how terrifying that is for children.

I was once told in my original world that children are surprisingly attentive to their parents’ expressions.

I do not want to be feared either, so I try to stay away as much as possible, but sometimes the maids ask me to come check on things.

Apparently, clearly establishing hierarchy from childhood is effective.

Isn’t that overdoing it?

As I mass-produce stone-statue orphans, I walk through the orphanage.

Seriously, isn’t this overdoing it?

…Unfortunately, the number of orphans increases every time I come.

The Kingdom of Estea is generally a good country, but due to the nature of the labyrinth, it is easy for orphans and abandoned children to be born, which is not good.

As the true ruler of the labyrinth, I considered revising the labyrinth’s rules.

However, aside from orphans, parents who would abandon their children just because there is an easy place like the labyrinth to do so do not seem capable of making their children happy anyway.

In that case, it is far better to take the children in, educate them, and turn them into capable individuals.

As a result, I decided to maintain the status quo while saving children and placing them in the orphanage.

That said, the fact that the number of orphans has increased to the point that the first orphanage is getting cramped can only be described as a dark side of the Kingdom of Estea.

East, I do not want to say this to you, dead as you are, but could you not have tried a little harder with your national character?

Anyway.

When I enter the room where the boy with \<Branch of the Genealogy Tree> is, the orphans inside all freeze at once.

“Huh? Huh?”

Only the boy in question, who has not yet been educated, looks confused by the situation around him.

He really does have \<Branch of the Genealogy Tree>.

And it seems his fifth birthday is closer than I expected. In other words, the skill’s unlocking is near.

He does not know about the skill yet, right?

A: Yes. However, please rest assured. It is already confirmed that his race will change.

Why?

A: When we protected him, without telling him about the skill, we asked, “Are you okay with experiencing pain at least once?” and obtained his consent.

So you got him to sign a blank check without explaining the details. …That is pretty harsh.

Well, it is better than dying.

For now, I confirmed that he seems healthy, and that his race changing is almost certain.

The orphanage is somewhat flustered by my sudden visit, but my purpose is fulfilled, so I will head back.

I am Shindo Jin, a big fish in a small pond when dealing with my own people.

What? I act pretty freely even when not dealing with my own people?

As I was about to return from the orphanage via teleportation (a Dungeon Master ability), I spotted a girl who was neither an orphan nor a maid, so I stopped.

“Good morning, Jin-sama. Good morning to you as well, Maria.”

“Yeah, good morning.”

“Good morning.”

The one greeting me was a short-haired girl with pale pink hair, the former King of the Kingdom of Grants, Zenon, also known as Non-chan.

Non-chan is wearing something like a tank top and knee-length shorts.

It is the kind of outfit that a tomboyish girl would stereotypically wear.

Perhaps because she has not fully shaken off her sense as a man, her tastes are rather masculine.

Also, she apparently dislikes skirts.

“Are you studying at the orphanage today?”

“Yes, I was on my way back.”

Because of the first king, Non-chan never received a proper education, so she is currently studying general knowledge at the labyrinth orphanage.

In a sense, she is like an orphan, but she does not live at the orphanage and instead works as a maid.

If I recall correctly, her affiliation is…

A: She works under the noble maids of the Eldia Territory.

Our maids have already gone beyond the realm of housekeeping.

Earlier I said “working as a maid”, but is that really accurate?

“There is a meeting about the territory’s budget today, so they let me keep my studies short.”

Currently, Non-chan is involved in politics under the noble maids, making use of her experience from her time as Zenon.

Perhaps because she watched Zenon work as a king for so long, she has quite a lot of knowledge.

“In the end, all I have left are the memories and knowledge from my time as Zenon…”

She mutters self-deprecatingly, as if she guessed what I was thinking.

From birth, Non-chan’s body was taken over by a possessor, and even after being freed, she only had one (from her perspective) useless Unique Skill.

Her status values were at the minimum, and all other skills were zero, making her a weak character.

Until I gave her skills and status via \<Life and Death Authority> and brought her up to a normal level, she was weaker than a baby.

For Non-chan, almost everything she has was given to her by me. As a result, she lacks confidence in herself. In short, she does not have a firm sense of “self.”

Aside from what I gave her, the only things Non-chan has are Zenon’s memories and knowledge.

After thinking it over, Non-chan said she wanted to use that knowledge to be useful to me.

I have no intention of affirming Zenon’s methods, but even so, he supported a small kingdom for dozens, even hundreds of years. His abilities are not something to scoff at.

Alta thought that if Non-chan possessed even part of Zenon’s knowledge, we could expect her to have political aptitude.

Non-chan gladly agreed if she could be useful, which is how things came to be.

“I hear you are being quite helpful.”

“I hope so…”

I have many subordinates, but few are seriously studying politics.

The noble maid in charge of the Eldia Territory is more of an administrator than a politician at heart. Non-chan’s knowledge will not go to waste.

“If there is something else you want to do, you can change your affiliation…”

Our motto is the right person in the right place.

Those with talent should do things that make use of that talent.

And even if someone has talent, we do not force them to do things they do not want to do (with some exceptions).

“No, if anything, I want to be more involved in politics.”

However, Non-chan seems to like the world of politics more than I expected.

“Actually, I have finally decided on a goal.”

Among my subordinates, there are quite a few who suddenly lost what they were doing, lost their goals, or were thrown into incomprehensible situations.

For such people, I let them start by doing what they can, and once they decide what they truly want to do or what their goal is, I make sure they can shift over to that.

“Can you tell me what it is?”

“Of course. My goal is to become a politician and ruler greater than the possessor.”

That is an unexpectedly interesting thing to say.

“Right now, all I have are the powers Jin-sama gave me and Zenon’s knowledge. By studying politics, I want to reduce the proportion of Zenon within me. In the end, I want to be able to say that Zenon’s knowledge is nothing more than a stepping stone.”

“You are going to treat someone who ruled the Kingdom of Grants for several hundred years as a stepping stone? That is good.”

Someone who prolonged his life by sacrificing his descendants being treated as a stepping stone by those very descendants.

That is rather amusing.

“Since you have a goal, I will help you.”

“Ah, it is fine. Lady Sakuya has agreed to help me. I was able to make this decision thanks to Lady Sakuya’s encouragement…”

It seems that the Queen of Castal and the former King of Grants have gotten along well without my knowledge.

“Lady Cattleya is also helping.”

The Princess of Estea is involved as well.

“Jin-sama’s mansion is amazing. An abnormal number of royalty come and go…”

“Yeah.”

Technically, you are one of them too, you know?

**AN:** Shion, now Ange, appeared in Chapters 65 and 66.

In this chapter, several plot threads are set up, and several are rather roughly resolved.

# **161: Dragon Extermination and a Decision**

**AN:** Sorry about the strange mistake last time.

We still are not going to the guild. Claude is in transit.

---

“Just under ten thousand, I guess. Looks like it will be over in about an hour.”

I mutter as I look at the swarm surrounding the barrier.

“Quite a lot gathered, huh? They really do hate the Dragonewts.”

《Dora hates dragons too!》

Responding to Mio’s words, Dora lets out a cute “Hiss!” and threatens them.

We are currently at the “Dragonewt Hidden Sanctuary.”

Our objective is the extermination of the dragons that have gathered in the dragon habitat, the “Dragon Forest”, which completely surrounds the Dragonewt Hidden Sanctuary.

When we first visited the Dragonewt Hidden Sanctuary, we killed around fifty thousand dragons that lived in the Dragon Forest, but after a while they started gathering again.

Originally, dragons rarely spawn in the Dragon Forest (not zero, but close).

Most of the dragons here were born elsewhere and gathered for the sole purpose of killing Dragonewts.

“My blood is boiling! No matter what, I will take first place in kill count!”

《Dora will do her best too!》

“If Master and Maria-chan aren’t participating, that gives us a chance.”

“Sera-chan, Dora-chan, Mio-chan, please do your best…”

There is no concern that the barrier of the Dragonewt Hidden Sanctuary I manage will be broken, but they are a nuisance, so this event is a competition to hunt the gathered dragons and compare kill counts.

For the record, the three of us, me, Maria, and Sakura, are not participating and have decided to just watch.

The Estia Kingdom explorer group led by Cynthia, the monster-girl Atto Confederation mercenary group, and maids from various regions are participating in the dragon hunt.

The Castal adventurer group is also participating, but since their leaders, including Claude, are currently moving to the Guild Union District, they are somewhat weaker as a force.

In addition, several Dragonewts besides Dora are participating. They are the martial-artist Dragonewt maids who trained outside the barrier. …In the end, they are maids too!

This extermination operation is being conducted in the remote Dragon Forest, and the enemies are reasonably powerful monsters, dragons, so we have allowed participants to use their usually-restrained stats without holding back.

However, the main party’s stats are too high, so they have restrictions. Even so, they still have a considerable advantage due to skill levels and equipment performance.

When the operation start time arrives, the participants head outside the barrier one after another via “Portal.”

“Sorry to Sera, but Dora is the sole favorite to win.”

“I figured Jin-kun would think so…”

When Dora teleports to the ‘Dragon Forest’, the dragons that had been endlessly attacking the barrier nearby all react at once.

Then they rush toward Dora, each trying to get there first.

《Fire!》

Dora intercepts the dragons with \<Dragon Magic>.

Every time she releases \<Dragon Magic>, dragons from other locations also head toward Dora.

And so on, endlessly. Ah, but the enemies do have a limited number of lives.

Dragonewts, and \<Dragon Magic>, have the property of attracting dragons.

The higher the level of \<Dragon Magic>, the stronger this property becomes.

Due to various reasons, Dora’s \<Dragon Magic> level has risen, and is currently level 8. This is the highest in the ‘Dragonewt Hidden Sanctuary’.

Even Sera probably cannot compete with Dora, who has the strongest dragon-collecting function.

《Special Fire!》

Oh, more than a hundred dragons were turned to charcoal in a single blow.

Alright, it’s about time to look not only at Dora, but at the other participants as well.

As expected, the participants besides Dora are also hunting dragons one after another.

Dragons instinctively want to head toward Dora, but they do not ignore enemies right in front of them. If they are already in combat, that naturally takes priority.

In this extermination operation, party-based hunting is also permitted (kill counts are divided by number of members).

Because this is valuable real combat experience against dragons (excluding the infinitely spawning fire dragons in the labyrinth), many people wanted to test their abilities with their usual companions without worrying about kill counts.

In fact, the majority are participating in parties.

Of course, those confident in their skills are hunting dragons solo.

A good example is the human Hero from the explorer group.

“I will kill you!”

-Mekyo!-

Cynthia leaps at a dragon and punches it squarely in the face with full force.

The dragon’s face caves in.

“I killed it!”

At first, Cynthia used \<Staff Techniques>, but she has trained close-combat techniques using gauntlets with \<Martial Arts> up to a practical level.

Since this is a battle unrelated to labyrinth conquest (and there will be no more dragon battles in the labyrinth), she left the labyrinth-conquest party and chose to participate solo. It seems to be a pure test of ability.

Oh yes, there was another “good example” alongside Cynthia.

Rico the Dwarf, another locally-produced Hero like Cynthia.

“…”

In contrast to the shouting Cynthia, Rico continues solo combat in silence.

Rico’s combat style is high-speed mobility and concealed weapons… assassination.

Even now, she approached a land dragon from behind and stabbed a poison knife into its neck.

The land dragon collapses with a thud and stops moving. …This is strange. How did it come to this?

Originally, Rico’s combat style was distinctive.

She possesses a precognition skill and was trained primarily as a bodyguard. By the way, the VIP in question is me.

She does not fixate on a main weapon, skillfully using multiple concealed weapons hidden in her maid outfit, and throws them if necessary.

As a Dwarf, she is small and nimble, and to make use of her precognition skill, she consciously raised her speed stat.

She compensated for her weakness, low attack power, by accurately striking vital points with her dexterity.

So far, so good.

Because of her precognition skill, surprise attacks are ineffective against Rico, so she basically abandons defense. With precognition and mobility, she just needs to dodge everything.

In addition, the shorter the combat time, the better for a bodyguard. The longer a battle drags on, the more danger the protected target faces, which is only natural.

Someone who abandons defense, lacks confidence in attack power, has confidence in speed, and wants to shorten battle time as much as possible. What combat style should such a person choose?

Yes, an assassin (objections accepted).

Thus, the small, pet-like girl transformed into an assassin-type girl.

A bodyguard and an assassin… aren’t their purposes completely opposite?

As an aside, using poison is one way to compensate for low attack power.

Another aside: not talking unnecessarily during combat is the result of assassin training. She is usually a cheerful child, but it seems she has a switch that flips only during combat.

…How did it come to this?

This time, she participated as training to successfully assassinate large monsters.

Cynthia with frontal breakthroughs, Rico with rear assassinations.

Why are locally-produced Heroes always such extreme people…?

Ah, the most extreme one is right next to me right now.

Earlier than expected, in about thirty minutes, the army of roughly ten thousand dragons was wiped out.

《Dora wins!》

“I have lost!”

As expected, Dora finished with a landslide victory in kill count.

“Well, it couldn’t be helped. If I could use the map, I could have used my finishing combo…”

“That would obviously be cheating.”

Mio’s mythical-grade bow has an auto-tracking function.

When combined with the map, it completes an outrageous combo that automatically tracks and shoots any target you like on the map. That is obviously not fun at all, so it cannot be allowed.

For that reason as well, this time we completely prohibited the use of Special Powers. Things like the map, telepathy, and Alta’s support.

“Everyone, good work. Dora, do you feel refreshed?”

《Yeah!》

Just as dragons hate Dragonewts, Dragonewts also hate dragons.

For Dora, dragon hunting is good stress relief. Apparently, just having dragons nearby is stressful for her.

《Dora will never lose to dragons!》

Oh, Dora is fired up.

…Come to think of it, do calamity dragons count as dragons? Probably not, but…

A: They are treated separately from dragons.

Mm, that’s good.

If Dora developed a rivalry toward calamity dragons, I would have no choice but to stop her.

They are too dangerous.

“Then, when dragons pile up again, let’s kill them all, okay?”

《Kill them all!》

“Master, Master. That’s bad for Dora-chan’s education, you know?”

Mio is right.

We should avoid statements that are bad for Dora’s education.

“You’re right. Dora, correction. Let’s blow them away, okay?”

《Blow them away!》

“Just barely safe, maybe? It’s borderline…”

Mio tilts her head.

I didn’t use a dangerous word like “kill”, right?

A: Master. A total-extermination bonus monster has spawned in the ‘Dragon Forest’.

While we were chatting, Alta reported the bonus spawn.

In monster territories, when the number of monsters in an area is reduced, rare monsters are more likely to spawn. There are several conditions, but if you completely wipe them out, the first one is almost guaranteed to be a rare monster.

Since we wiped out all monsters in the Dragon Forest this time, a total-extermination bonus monster should spawn.

Whether we defeat it or tame it, it would not hurt to take a look.

…This is bad.

When I saw the total-extermination bonus rare monster displayed on the map, I wanted to clutch my head.

Feather Dragon (Rare)

LV1

\<Dragon Arts LV1> \<Flight LV1>

Notes: A dragon with wings covered in feathers. Extremely rare and extremely delicious.

Yes, it was a dragon of the same species as Dora’s dragon form.

“…Master, what are you going to do?”

“Wait. I’m thinking right now.”

I spin my brain at full speed.

Dragonewts have a human form and a dragon form, and the dragon form takes the same shape as real dragons.

Dora’s dragon form is a Feather Dragon. It is rare, but not something that can never be encountered.

However, perhaps because we had never encountered one before, I had not thought at all about what to do when we did.

The choices we can take regarding monsters are basically either “kill” or “tame.”

However, I know that “tame” cannot be chosen.

I tried before, but when a Dragonewt is nearby, it is impossible to tame dragons.

Simply put, dragons will continue attacking Dragonewts until death and will not accept taming. Do they really hate Dragonewts that much…?

Then, the remaining choice is “kill”, but…

Do we kill a dragon that looks exactly like Dora in front of Dora?

Even if she hates dragons, she would not feel good about it.

I would like to avoid that as well.

How about the hidden third option, “let it go”?

It would definitely die in the next extermination operation. It’s already started attacking the barrier of the Dragonewt Hidden Sanctuary…

“Dora, what do you want to do?”

Unable to choose from the options, I decided to honestly ask Dora.

《Defeat it and eat it!》

“Eh?”

Dora answered without hesitation, and now I’m the one confused.

《Because it’s delicious, right?》

I have indeed heard that Feather Dragons are delicious.

I’ve heard that, but…

“It looks the same as Dora’s dragon form. Is that really okay?”

《That’s not Dora! And it’s a dragon, so I hate it!》

Dora-chan is surprisingly dry!

Was Dora’s name derived not from “dragon”, but from “dry”?

Come to think of it, she was fairly dry in her reaction even when the ‘Dragonewt Hidden Sanctuary’ was in danger.

“If Dora is okay with it, then there’s no problem…”

《Master should eat it together with me!》

“Let me think about that.”

《Eh…》

Even if she says that sadly, this is something I cannot compromise on.

It’s good that Dora has decided it will be defeated.

However, eating it makes me uncomfortable. Not only eating it myself, but also letting Dora eat it.

《Ah, that’s right! Mio is the best at cooking, so Mio should cook it, okay?》

“Eh? …Eh!?”

Mio is shocked.

“You want me to butcher and cook a creature that looks exactly like the child I use as a body pillow…!?”

《Yep!》

That’s the biggest problem.

Even if it’s not Dora herself, telling someone to kill and eat something that looks exactly like something they dote on daily is a bit too high a hurdle.

As expected, Sakura also has a pale face.

She definitely would not eat it.

Incidentally, Maria and Sera look surprisingly fine. They must be able to compartmentalize.

“…No, that’s not happening. No matter how I think about it, I can’t bring myself to eat a Feather Dragon. If possible, I want to avoid killing it as well.”

This might be an unusually passive opinion for me.

However, I can’t help but imagine “cannibalism.”

For personal reasons, “cannibalism” is NG for me.

As for a hint about those “personal reasons”, it’s Orihara.

Alta, is there a way to erase hostility from dragons toward Dragonewts?

A: Like the Progenitor Divine Dragon, if you kill, absorb, and reconstruct it, the hostility will disappear. Alternatively, you can destroy its mind first, then tame it, and repair it. Using the level 9 effect of \<Life and Death Authority> and the level 7 effect of \<Multiple Existence> would be acceptable.

There are surprisingly many methods.

Since we’re here, maybe I’ll try the \<Life and Death Authority LV9> and \<Multiple Existence LV7> combo.

I haven’t had a target to use it on until now, so I haven’t tested it.

“For now, I’ve decided to tame the Feather Dragon.”

《Eh!?》

Dora raises a voice of protest at my decision.

“Phew… Cooking it was really impossible…”

“I’m glad…”

Mio and Sakura show relieved expressions.

“That is most unfortunate…”

Sera seems like she was fully prepared to eat the Feather Dragon. No.

《I hate dragons!》

“I understand how you feel, Dora, but please endure it this time. We don’t like it.”

《Mmph…》

Since Dora is sulking, I carefully stroke her to soothe her mood.

Gradually, Dora’s mood improves.

《At least, Master, please don’t be the one to tame it…》

After her mood recovers somewhat, Dora says that.

“Alright, I understand. Mio, can I ask you?”

“Okay! A candidate for my personal body pillow!”

Listening to Dora’s request, I decided to leave the taming to Mio.

Following the map, we arrive at the Feather Dragon that is attacking the barrier.

“Kyui! Kyui!”

As soon as the Feather Dragon sees Dora, it attacks without hesitation.

A wind-element \<Dragon Arts> flies toward us, which I casually smack away and blow apart.

“Even such a small dragon still has the same hostility toward Dragonewts.”

《Mmph!》

Dora also clearly hates the dragon.

“Kyuu!”

Seeing that \<Dragon Arts> is ineffective, it flies up and tries to ram us.

“There.”

“Kyumugu!?”

I grab the flying Feather Dragon in a way that blocks its mouth, preventing it from moving or using \<Dragon Arts>.

To avoid killing it, \<Restraint> is being fully activated.

“Alright then, let’s try the \<Life and Death Authority> and \<Multiple Existence> combo.”

“I look forward to witnessing Jin-sama’s new power.”

Maria’s attitude is different.

“Ah, Master. Is it okay not to use \<Monster Training> beforehand?”

“It should be fine to do it afterward, right?”

A: It is fine.

“Alta’s seal of approval too. Let’s activate it right away!”

I use \<Life and Death Authority LV9> and \<Multiple Existence LV7> on the Feather Dragon.

“Mugu!? Mugugugu…?”

The Feather Dragon thrashes about.

Its struggles gradually intensify.

After some time passes, its movements weaken. Then, the Feather Dragon wets itself. Drool drips from the corners of its mouth, tears flow from its eyes, followed by bloody tears.

In the end, it loses the strength to struggle and only twitches weakly.

“Alright, that went well.”

“…Eh? That counts as going well?”

Seeing the Feather Dragon hanging limply from my grip while leaking various fluids, Mio asks with slight apprehension.

“Yeah, there should be no hostility toward Dragonewts left anymore. You can tame it.”

“O-okay…”

Hesitantly, Mio activates \<Monster Training>.

The taming circle hits the Feather Dragon while it is still being held.

“…It tamed without any resistance.”

“Does it look like it could resist?”

I ask while showing the completely limp Feather Dragon.

“Probably not…”

“Regardless of the process, the Feather Dragon was tamed by Mio. Here, take it.”

“Thanks…”

I hand the Feather Dragon to Mio.

Since it had been leaking various things, I cast “Purification” once.

“Up you go. …It’s female.”

Mio lifts the Feather Dragon and checks between its legs to determine its sex.

When it comes to animal sexes, Mio checks fairly straightforwardly without hesitation.

“What should we name it?”

“Shiro is not allowed.”

That would overlap with my cat from my original world, who is the previous life of Sharon, the current queen of the Regalia Beastman Kingdom.

“There’s no way I’d give such a simplistic name.”

“Sorry for being simplistic.”

I’ve publicly stated that my naming sense isn’t great.

“Alright. Let’s call her ‘Blanc.’”

“And the reasoning?”

I can’t think of it immediately, so I ask.

“From a white dragon flying in the sky, ‘blank’. I tweaked it a bit to ‘Blanc’.”

“Where did the ‘k’ go?”

“It died.”

It died…

Anyway, the Feather Dragon’s name is now ‘Blanc’.

After a while, the Feather Dragon, now Blanc, wakes up.

“Kyuu!”

“Oh, so fluffy!”

She seems to understand that she has been tamed and jumps onto Mio.

…Something suddenly comes to mind.

“Come here.”

“Kyui!?”

When I call out, Blanc hurriedly flies over to me and lies on her back in front of me.

She shows her belly and crotch while trembling slightly, displaying no hostility and indicating obedience.

“S-she’s submitting…!”

“Probably a side effect of \<Multiple Existence LV7>.”

“Again… I’ve been cuckolded…”

Mio slumps her shoulders.

Previously, when I petted Mio’s familiar dog and cat, they became infatuated with me.

Once again, it seems I have captured its heart more than its owner Mio.

“My only ally is the wolf…”

“Hey, Mio, can I pet Potechi next time?”

“D-o-n-t!”

Apparently, Potechi’ fur is coarse, so I’m not that interested anyway.

That night, Sera came to my room.

She asked for privacy, so I had the Progenitor Divine Dragon, Sky Dragon, and Ash Person who were playing in the room leave.

Dora, meanwhile, is being used as a body pillow by Sakura.

“I have something to report… or apologize for, Master.”

“Which is it?”

Is it a report? An apology?

“I believe it likely falls within Master’s acceptable range, but it is something I cannot be certain about without actually asking.”

“Alright, let’s hear it for now.”

When I prompt her, Sera begins speaking awkwardly.

“The truth is, I have eaten Feather Dragon meat before.”

“…Could it be that when I forbade eating the Feather Dragon earlier, you looked disappointed because you had eaten it before and found it delicious?”

She was the only one who reacted differently during that conversation.

“Yes, that is correct. When I was doing a food tour before, I came across a dish made with rare ingredients, and though I felt sorry toward Dora, I gave in to my curiosity and ate it.”

“Well, it is a rare ingredient, and it is understandable to eat it if you encounter it…”

For Sera, it would be difficult to ignore a delicious and rare monster.

“If Master were to say, ‘Absolutely do not eat Feather Dragons’, then I would already be in violation of that order, so I wished to apologize to Master.”

“I have no intention of blaming you for something you did before any such order, and in the first place, I never intended to give such an order. I simply didn’t want Feather Dragons to die in front of me or Dora. I have no interest in Feather Dragons that died in places we didn’t see.”

To be blunt, if subordinates kill Feather Dragons in places neither Dora nor I see, I would not complain.

Well, subordinates who know about Dora’s existence would probably hesitate anyway…

“Of course, I will not allow you to lay a hand on the Feather Dragon tamed by Mio, alright?”

“I am not that depraved.”

When I joke, Sera counters with a wry smile.

“So, was the Feather Dragon delicious? I don’t plan to eat one, but I’m a bit curious.”

In my mind, Feather Dragons are already out of the food category.

I don’t plan to eat them in the future either, but I’d like to hear about it.

“Yes, it was very delicious. The texture is like poultry, but even without seasoning it has more than enough flavor, and it is delicious simply grilled, and even when cooked, the flavor asserts itself strongly.”

At the very least, it is clear she has eaten both “simply grilled” and “cooked” versions.

“However, while it was delicious, the guilt did not disappear. If Master and Dora-san had approved of eating Feather Dragons, I could have eaten them openly, so I felt regretful.”

It seems she wanted the atmosphere that it was okay to eat them, rather than specifically wanting to eat them on the spot.

Food-related puns…

“If it’s in a place where neither Dora nor I will see it, I will not forbid eating them.”

“Really!?”

Sera reacts dramatically.

“Yes, but only if you eat already-cooked food outside. I want you to avoid bringing it as an ingredient and having maids butcher it.”

“It is a little disappointing that I cannot eat maid-made cooking, but understood. In other words, do not bring it into the mansion at all, correct?”

“Exactly. However, I am not forbidding you from bringing maids with you.”

“!?”

Sera’s eyes widen.

“Since Mio-san dislikes butchering Feather Dragons, we will need another cooking maid. Perhaps I should ask Nino-san. Ah, but Nino-san also interacts with Dora-san, so she may dislike butchering them as well. I will need to find a cooking maid with a relatively high \<Cooking> level who has not interacted with Dora-san.”

She’s seriously considering this…

---

Blanc: “…”

K: “Kill me.”

A new form of “kukoro.”
