# **162: God’s-Eye View and the Truth of the Demon Race**

**AN:** A rather sloppy, spoiler-filled chapter.

---

One of my Special Powers \<Clairvoyance>, allows me to acquire virtually all information within the map.

I can view the skills and statuses of everyone inside the map, and if I feel like it, I can even grasp what they are saying.

However, the sheer volume of information is overwhelming, so I generally leave the processing to Alta, and low-priority information is not reported.

In the first place, Alta manifested as a Special Power because of the need to process map information.

The map function allows me to check from the current area out to three adjacent areas. Since a single area is at least several kilometers across (with some exceptions, such as small villages), taken together I have a complete grasp of information within roughly a five-kilometer radius.

Additionally, not only my own location, but also the locations of my subordinates are treated as active areas.

In other words, I can obtain information within a five-kilometer radius of wherever my subordinates are.

And my subordinates exist all over the world, as members of the Advance Trading Company or as adventurers.

With that much coverage, I can usually predict most events before they even occur.

Yes, just like how I could already foresee what was about to happen when Claude, currently on an expedition, entered the Guild Federation District…

This is the Adventurers Guild Grandmaster who summoned Claude and the others this time.

Name: Yurisuzu  

Gender: Female  

Age: 3110  

Race: High Elf  

Titles: Elf Princess Shrine Maiden, Elf Royalty, Living Sacrifice, Adventurers Guild Headquarters Grandmaster  

Skills:

Martial Arts  

\<Swordsmanship LV10> \<Spear Technique LV10> \<Shield Technique LV10> \<Archery LV10> \<Unarmed Combat LV10>

Magic  

\<Spirit Arts LV10> \<Spirit Magic LV10> \<Sealing Arts LV >

Technical  

\<Magical Tool Creation LV10> \<Wisdom of the Forest LV >

Physical  

\<Physical Enhancement LV10>

Other  

\<Ageless LV > \<Shrine Maiden Succession LV > \<Will of Hellfire LV > \<Spiritual Rank Sight LV >

*Numerous skills below LV10 omitted.

And sleeping deep underground beneath the volcanic mountain range, at the hot spring source, is this.

Calamity Dragon Volcano  

Race: Disaster Dragon  

Titles: Anti-Existence, Sealed Calamity

This is far beyond something that can be brushed off with the word “spoiler.”

The ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’ who is currently sealing a Disaster Dragon summoned Claude’s party, that is to say, she summoned Yulia, another High Elf ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’.

There is no way an event involving a Disaster Dragon would not occur.

What makes it even funnier is that Yurisuzu has a habit of talking to herself.

It seems she verbalizes her thoughts to explain her situation… yes, everything was completely audible. I finished listening to Yurisuzu’s objective in full.

To put Yurisuzu’s objective in one sentence, it is to retrieve Yulia and carry out a generational replacement of the ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’.

…That was really short.

From what she said, Yulia, who had amnesia, was apparently the missing next-generation ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’.

Not of the ‘Calamity Dragon Volcano’, but ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’ of the ‘Wind Calamity Dragon Tempest’.

Another Disaster Dragon just got added out of nowhere…

Although she is not currently in the Guild Federation District, Yurisuzu seems to have connections with the ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’ sealing the ‘Wind Calamity Dragon Tempest’, and she had been asked to search for the missing Yulia.

Under those circumstances, if a newly promoted S-rank adventurer party included the missing ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’, you would have no choice but to summon them, even if it meant offering excellent conditions.

Now I understand why the summons sent to Claude and the others were so desperate.

The ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’ of the Wind Calamity Dragon Tempest has already lived for a very long time and wishes to pass her role on to Yulia. If necessary, she is prepared to take her back by force.

Using force against an S-rank adventurer. That is quite the confidence.

“…That is why we would like to hear your policy, Jin-sama.”

I consider my response to Claude’s question.

After learning Yurisuzu’s objective, Claude and the others decided to seek my judgment.

Claude, the leader, and Yulia, the concerned party, returned via ‘Portal’, while the remaining members are waiting in the Guild Federation District.

“As for Disaster Dragons, my basic stance is to leave them alone. If there is a necessary reason, I will defeat them, but without such a reason, I have no intention of getting involved.”

Disaster Dragons are essentially my enemies, but the world has continued without incident until now.

I have no intention of taking risks without a compelling reason.

“So, what does Yulia want to do? Do you want to inherit the role of ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’?”

When I asked her, Yulia shook her head.

“No. Unless it is Jin-sama’s order, I have no intention of becoming such a thing. At the very least, not in my current state, with my memories still lost…”

Conversely, it seems that if I were to order her to become a ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’, or if she were to regain her lost memories, there is a possibility she would accept the role.

Incidentally, thanks to the mental protection provided by \<Multiple Existence>, the greatest burden of being a ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’, mental contamination, can be prevented. So becoming a ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’ itself is not a major problem.

“Then are you going to stop going to the Guild Federation District? It sounds like they are prepared to take you by force.”

“In that regard, we have a request for you, Jin-sama.”

“Go on.”

Claude speaks with a resolute expression, and I straighten my posture as well.

“We will go to the Guild Federation District. And we will refuse, head-on, to hand Yulia-san over. In the worst case, our S-rank qualifications may be revoked, and we may become enemies of the Adventurers Guild. We know this is selfish, but we ask for your permission.”

“Fine.”

“”Eh?””

They asked for permission, so I granted it. I do not know why they are staring at me blankly.

“Did I say something strange?”

“N-no, you answered so quickly, without even thinking, that it surprised us a little.”

No, this does not even require thought.

“The reasons I became an adventurer were twofold. Because it was ‘expected,’ and because it was convenient. The reason I had you become S-rank adventurers was because I wanted the influence that comes with the title.”

“‘Expected’ things are important, after all.”

Mio, who had been quietly listening until now, nods repeatedly.

She must have really wanted to say that.

“No matter the reason, anyone who plans kidnapping is not sane. If their blade is pointed at someone close to me, there is no need to hesitate about becoming their enemy. If it were me, I would crush them without hesitation.”

“Ah, I see. So that is why Eldia was destroyed.”

“Now that you mention it, this really does resemble how the Kingdom of Eldia was destroyed.”

Sera and Mio murmur in understanding.

Eldia, whose leadership attempted kidnapping and then declared war on Castal, which had become family to me, was destroyed by my hand, exactly as I just described. (Though the direct cause was the war, not the kidnapping.)

A man of his word, Shindo Jin.

“If Claude and the others have decided, I do not mind you becoming enemies of the Adventurers Guild. The title of S-rank adventurer is a bit of a waste, but when you think of it as a title belonging to an organization whose leader plans kidnappings, its value plummets anyway.”

After hearing Yurisuzu’s story, I was surprised at how easily my interest in the Adventurers Guild vanished.

Maybe I do not even need to renew my adventurer license anymore.

“Ah, Master has completely lost interest.”

“Jin-kun really does become utterly indifferent once he loses interest…”

“The gap between interest and disinterest is truly extreme.”

Everyone says what they like, but I cannot refute them. Nor do I intend to.

“Oh, right. This might become troublesome, so make sure you do not kill Yurisuzu.”

I remembered and added that note.

If you kill her, the ‘Calamity Dragon Volcano’ will emerge.

And on top of that, the Adventurers Guild itself would likely fall into dysfunction. Or rather, it definitely would.

That is because the guild cards, proof of belonging to the Adventurers Guild, are magical tools created by Yurisuzu herself.

They require the ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’-exclusive skill \<Wisdom of the Forest>, so no one else can make them.

“We had no intention of going that far to begin with.”

“As long as you understand that, do as you like. I will permit you to go as far as half-killing.”

“That permission itself is troubling…”

Even if they become enemies, and even if they do not half-kill anyone, Claude and the others are kind.

Among my subordinates, they are the moderate faction. Incidentally, the most radical faction is the maid corps (the largest faction).

After Claude and the others returned via ‘Portal’, we also began preparing to head to the Guild Federation District.

It is certain that Claude and the others will run into trouble involving the Adventurers Guild, but putting that aside, we are still going sightseeing at the hot springs.

The plan is for them to call us once they get a bit closer to the Adventurers Guild headquarters.

“If a Disaster Dragon revives, the Guild Federation District will vanish, after all. If there is risk involved, it is better to sightsee sooner rather than later.”

“You say some pretty outrageous things so casually…”

Mio looks a little taken aback, but this is my honest feeling.

Even if Claude and the others have no intention of killing Yurisuzu, the mere fact that this land houses a Disaster Dragon means it unquestionably carries enormous risk.

If, for some reason, the Disaster Dragon revives, the calamity will certainly swallow the Guild Federation District.

It is a tourist spot. I would like to enjoy it at least once before it is destroyed.

“To be honest, I would hate for a tourist spot to disappear, but I also hate the idea of protecting someone we are (scheduled) to become enemies with.”

There are two ways to prevent damage from a Disaster Dragon.

Protect the ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’, or defeat the Disaster Dragon itself in subspace.

I do not feel like protecting an enemy ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’, and defeating a Disaster Dragon sealed in subspace requires the cooperation of a ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’.

There is no way around this.

“To begin with, Master does not need to protect anything, right? After all, it has been fine for thousands of years. There is no way things will suddenly change so easily today or tomorrow.”

Mio speaks optimistically, but I do not see it that way.

“Normally, the seal would not break so easily. However, the Guild Federation District is land I am about to visit. Since I am going, one or two events are guaranteed to occur. One of those could very well be the release of the seal.”

According to Orihara, ‘getting caught up in trouble is both the right and duty of a protagonist.’

Whether or not I am a protagonist is another matter, but it is true that I have a constitution that easily causes trouble, or easily gets caught up in it.

“That is strangely convincing. As expected of the ‘Knight of Turmoil’…”

Mio speaks my epithet.

It is a nickname given because lands I become involved with tend to experience upheavals large enough to shake nations.

As far as Alta can tell, there are no other events on the horizon that would destabilize the Guild Federation District.

Which makes it all the more likely that an event involving the Disaster Dragon’s seal will occur.

“What you are saying makes no sense, yet when Jin-kun says it, it somehow becomes convincing…”

“Come to think of it, most of the seals and barriers in places Master has visited have been broken, have they not?”

As Sera says, special seals and barriers in places I go are fated to disappear.

It is what you would call a template.

Off the top of my head, there is the barrier of the ‘Dragonkin Hidden Land’, the seal of the Oni God in the Izumo Wa Kingdom, the Demon God of the Atto Confederation, the ‘Spirit Realm’ in the desert, and the barrier stone of the Elgant Theocracy.

Should I include the ‘Earth Calamity Dragon Earthquake’ as well? I ignored the seal itself, but still…

If memory serves, the only one still intact is the barrier of the Mermaid Kingdom.

“Then if Master does not go, nothing strange will happen?”

“No, once I have recognized it, it is already too late. It is just a matter of sooner or later. And if it is later, there is a chance we will not get to enjoy the hot springs. Therefore, we should go early.”

“That is basically a curse…”

“I am not troubled by it, so there is no problem!”

Even if it were a curse, as long as it does not present a disadvantage or risk to me, there is no problem. There is no need to worry about it.

While we were talking like that, I received a telepathic message from Claude.

《Jin-sama, we apologize. It seems calling you to the Guild Federation District will be delayed.》

《I do not mind the delay, but did something happen?》

《Yes. We helped a carriage that was being attacked by monsters and will be escorting it to a nearby town. It will likely be difficult to call you today.》

《…Understood. Contact me again once your schedule is set.》

《Yes, excuse us.》

I end the telepathic call with Claude.

“Claude is really going through a textbook template himself.”

“Master has hardly ever experienced those kinds of events, after all.”

The template event, ‘Carriage in Peril.’

Claude encounters it frequently, yet I have almost never encountered it myself.

If I had to name one time, it would be when I saved Princess Strawberry of the Crimson Empire the other day?

“In that sense, Claude really does have a trouble-prone constitution too. And a fairly orthodox one…”

“Master’s is just way too unorthodox.”

“I cannot deny that.”

The unorthodox trouble magnet, Shindo Jin.

I do like the orthodox route too, you know!

“So then, what shall we do now? The plan was to go to the Guild Federation District today…”

“Let me think…”

I consider our schedule in response to Sera’s question.

I have no intention of complaining to Claude and the others, but I was fully prepared to go to the Guild Federation District today.

It is only a little past noon, so changing today’s plans is not an issue.

I would rather not think that this schedule change will cause the Guild Federation District to collapse.

This is not a flag!

One option would be to have Claude and the others set up a ‘Portal’ somewhere appropriate, and then head to the hot spring by carriage from there.

However, since we had planned to travel by carriage this time, aiming for the capital from their current location would take too long, so I would prefer to avoid that.

“Let us just behave ourselves and kill time locally.”

By locally, I mean a ‘Portal’ destination… which might be a rather broad area.

“And so, we have arrived at the Kingdom of Sanokia.”

At Alta’s recommendation, we came to the Kingdom of Sanokia.

“We did not set up the ‘Portal’ ourselves, but does it really count as local?”

“Well, for me, it really is my homeland…”

Sera, who answers Mio’s question, is from the Kingdom of Sanokia.

It seems she has no good memories here at all, though.

“Welcome. The Shippouin-sama and the others are waiting in a separate room.”

“Understood. Lead the way.”

The one who welcomed us was the Queen of the Kingdom of Sanokia, Ekaterina.

For clarification, Ekaterina is my slave, and also a believer of my childhood friend Saki.

There should have been four other women in the same position, but the only one present here besides Ekaterina is a single woman wearing knight attire.

Sanokia has several ‘Portals’, but most of them were installed not by me, but by members of the Sanokia royal family, including Ekaterina.

This time, we used the ‘Portal’ near Ekaterina’s office.

…From a national security perspective, it seems questionable, but it is fairly common (in Castal’s case, it connects directly to the queen’s private chambers), so I have nothing to say.

“Understood.”

Guided personally by Ekaterina, we head toward the room where Shippouin and the others are.

“We have arrived. Shippouin-sama, Jin Shindo-sama has arrived.”

“Please, come in.”

When Ekaterina calls out, Shippouin responds from inside.

Ekaterina opens the door and gestures for us to enter.

“It has been some time, Shindo-sama.” x17

As soon as I enter the room, Shippouin and sixteen other women bow in unison.

Their perfectly synchronized movements make me recoil slightly.

“A-ah, yes, it has been a while.”

These seventeen women are heroes… or rather, former heroes who were summoned to this world alongside me and Sakura.

They abandoned being heroes in the Elgant Theocracy (and abandoned their lives once), becoming my slaves.

More than that, even in our original world, they were my believers.

“Come to think of it, you never come to my mansion at all.”

At the very least, the last time I saw them was when we returned from the Elgant Theocracy.

Of course, I have never forbidden them from visiting my mansion.

“You may not mind, Shindo-sama, but we do. Approaching you before we have even proven useful to you is simply unforgivable.”

The other sixteen nod vigorously.

For some reason, these seventeen have an extremely strong bond and an abnormal level of unity.

“W-well, if that is how you feel, I am not going to force you.”

I, I value the autonomy of my subordinates.

“Amazing. Master is actually backing away.”

“Jin-kun acts a little differently around them, does he not…”

“Master is not used to being treated like this.”

“…”

《Maria? Your face looks scary. What’s wrong?》

“It is nothing. I am fine.”

Even I find it hard to tease my own ‘believers’.

Maria presents herself primarily as a slave and guard, so it does not bother me, but Shippouin and the others never deviate from their attitude as believers.

“But according to Alta, today is different, right?”

“Yes. At last, we have achieved results we can report to you, Shindo-sama. …It is not something we can boast about proudly, but we would be happy if it proves that we are not useless.”

The slightly self-deprecating phrasing is likely because, up to now, the heroes have achieved little in terms of results against the demon race.

“…So, is that the result lying collapsed back there?”

“Yes. We defeated and captured one of the Demon King Army’s Four Heavenly Kings, the ‘Phantom Londrine’.”

Pulled forward by one of the believers was a demon girl who had been bound tightly and left rolling in the corner of the room.

In truth, Shippouin and the others had successfully captured… apprehended one of the Demon King Army’s Four Heavenly Kings.

All demon race members who have faced me have died (including in the mental sense), so this is the first time a Four Heavenly King has been captured alive.

My basic policy is to exterminate the demon race, but based on the example of the Naruse mother and daughter, former demons and reincarnators, I had wanted to investigate the demon race, or rather, the Demon King Army’s Four Heavenly Kings.

However, since I had not encountered another Four Heavenly King since the Naruse mother and daughter, the opportunity had not arisen.

“Well done. This is more than sufficient results.”

“Th-thank you very much!”

When I praise them, all seventeen light up with joy.

“So, where was she?”

“Yes. Rather than being there, she came to this country. It seems she judged us to be the core combatants among the heroes and came to investigate. She had stealth-type curse marks and was hiding, but… she was caught on the map normally…”

Ah, yes.

Stealth abilities really do become tragic when there is a map.

After that, they simply beat her up and it was over.

Indeed, not something to boast about grandly.

And, as expected, it seems the Demon King Army’s Four Heavenly Kings are still increasing.

She is the fifth one I know of. ‘Romalie of Falsehood’, defeated in Castal. ‘Zelvain of the Great Host’, defeated in the Estea Labyrinth. ‘Crownliese of Metamorphosis’ and Carielius, the Naruse mother and daughter defeated in Eldia.

Carielius lacks a title because he lost his mind from Alta’s counterattack before he could announce it.

A: He was apparently called “Carielius of Corruption.” The demons in Eldia used that name.

Thanks for the supplement.

In any case, now that a fifth has appeared, it is confirmed that the term ‘Four Heavenly Kings’ cannot be taken at face value. Do not mess with me.

“So then, is it true that Shindo-sama will be conducting the interrogation this time?”

“Yes. I just acquired a very suitable ability.”

By ‘suitable ability’, I mean the combo of \<Life and Death Authority LV9> and \<Multiple Existence LV7>.

It is an ability that seems tailor-made for situations like this… no, not really. It is just absurdly versatile. Truly a ridiculous ability.

“Then, we apologize for troubling you, but we leave her to you, Shindo-sama. She did not break under our torture…”

Ah, so they did torture her…

“Excuse me for a moment.”

I say that and grab Londrine’s head.

Activate \<Life and Death Authority LV9>. Followed immediately by \<Multiple Existence LV7>.

“A-ah… aaaaaaahhhhhhh!”

Five minutes pass from the start of ability activation.

“Alright, that is enough. I found out quite a few interesting things.”

When I release my grip, Londrine collapses, her body leaking all kinds of fluids.

Given this state, will Londrine eventually be added to my subordinates?

“That may be fine, but as always, it is brutal. Blanc looks traumatized.”

Blanc refers to Mio’s tamed Feathered Dragon.

I erased its hostility toward Dragonkin using the same method just before taming it.

“Yes. It is undeniably useful, but it is a bit unsightly.”

“A bit…?”

Sakura looks at Londrine in confusion.

At a glance, Londrine is in a state where she does not even look alive.

“No, she is alive with all limbs intact. She is just leaking a little.”

“That is true. Compared to how I was at the slave trader’s, this is mild.”

Maria, who was in a far worse state at the slave trader’s, agrees.

No missing limbs, not starving. This is more than mild.

“Please do not remind me of unpleasant things.”

“I remembered unpleasant things too…”

And thus, the slave group gets hit by stray bullets.

Their lives at the slave trader’s still are not good memories. As if they could be.

“Shindo-sama, so what exactly was discovered?”

“…Let us get back on track.”

Shippouin steers the conversation back after it derailed.

“First, as we suspected, the Demon King Army’s Four Heavenly Kings are inhabitants of our original world.”

“That was expected.”

“Master, is that reincarnation? Or transfer? From what we heard about the Naruse mother and daughter, their last memory was being hit by a car, so I thought it was reincarnation…”

Mio asks a sharp question.

“As Mio said, it is reincarnation. The Demon King has a curse mark called \<Fourfold Appointment>. When this curse mark is used, those who died in our world are reincarnated, and a personality suitable for the demon race is overwritten onto them.”

“You are casually dropping several huge revelations. Just by examining a Four Heavenly King, you can even learn about the Demon King’s curse marks?”

“Yes. This curse mark seems to be directly connected to the Demon King, so I was able to learn various things through something like reverse tracing. Though it was cut off midway by the Demon King.”

“As always, you are doing incredible things…”

I did investigate everything that needed investigating in the brief time before it was cut off.

“Those appointed as Four Heavenly Kings receive a set consisting of a personality suitable for the role and a curse mark. There are more than four such sets. These sets do not function without a connection to the Demon King. Only four connections can be maintained at once. …That is what proves someone is a Four Heavenly King. The Demon King can roughly grasp the status of the Four Heavenly Kings, and it seems the Naruse mother and daughter had their connections severed the moment their memories returned.”

In fact, the Naruse mother and daughter still possess the curse marks from their time as Four Heavenly Kings, but once their memories returned, those marks became meaningless empty skills.

I once tried to have Naruse Megumi show me her chuuni curse mark, \<Existence Addition>, but failed. A sad memory.

This time, after Londrine was subjected to \<Life and Death Authority LV9> and \<Multiple Existence LV7>, the Demon King judged her beyond recovery and severed the connection.

Of the Four Heavenly King slots, Crownliese and Carielius took the slots vacated by Romalie and Zelvain.

After their connections were severed, Londrine filled one of the newly opened slots.

In other words, there are still two unseen Four Heavenly Kings. In addition, two new Four Heavenly Kings should be added.

“If the Four Heavenly Kings change according to the Demon King’s will, was capturing her a wasted effort?”

Shippouin asks, looking slightly disappointed.

“No. Activating Fourfold Appointment is also a considerable burden for the Demon King. It should not be an option he can use lightly. It also seems to come with various restrictions.”

Where there are restrictions, there are loopholes, but let us leave that for now.

“I am glad we could be of even a little use.”

“Rest assured. Just learning this much is a major achievement.”

“Yes, thank you very much.”

All seventeen show relieved expressions.

This unity…

“There is one more important thing. If a Four Heavenly King is killed by a Hero, it becomes impossible to add a replacement… it seems the slot itself is destroyed. Going forward, it would be best to leave killing Four Heavenly Kings to you.”

“Understood.”

In the worst case, I could leave it to Maria.

“That covers the major discoveries. There were other minor things, but nothing worth presenting here.”

Having Alta inform the relevant parties should be sufficient.

A: Understood.

“As for our future policy, Shippouin and the others should continue to grow stronger, defeat demons, and if possible, Four Heavenly Kings, and eventually advance into demon territory.”

“Yes, understood.” x17

All seventeen nod in unison.

I really want these fake heroes to defeat the Demon King.

“By the way, will this incident be made public?”

I ask Shippouin and the queen.

“From a national standpoint, it would be preferable to make it public, but it is not important enough to take precedence over Shindo Jin-sama’s convenience. Please feel free to decide as you wish.”

Ekaterina may be queen, but she does not seem particularly attached to the Kingdom of Sanokia.

She is only doing this because Saki told her to, apparently.

“In this case, the Four Heavenly King was operating in secret. To make it public, we would need her corpse. Should we kill her?”

“…No. That will not do. I am sorry, but please do not make this public.”

I plan to remove Londrine’s demon personality and restore her original personality.

If her original personality turns out to be problematic, I will not make her a subordinate, but I will not execute her as a demon without hearing anything either.

“Very well. As long as we can show our results to you, Shindo-sama, that is enough for us. What will you do with Londrine?”

“I will take custody of her. Is that acceptable?”

“Of course.”

And so, the demon girl Londrine has been entrusted to me.

“‘Purify’.”

Since she was leaking fluids, it was necessary.

---

Side Story

_* Behind-the-scenes notes and extra tidbits._

– \<Fourfold Appointment>

A curse mark exclusive to the Demon King, used by successive Demon Kings to create the Four Heavenly Kings.

Its effect is to reincarnate those who died on Earth (with a body identical to the one they had at the time of death), and overwrite that body with a personality and curse mark suitable for a Demon King Army Four Heavenly King.

The overwritten personality disappears once the new personality fully settles in. Before it fully settles, it is possible, with an extremely strong shock, to restore the original personality (normally impossible).

The personality and curse mark come as a set, and more than ten such sets exist. These sets are shared across successive Demon Kings.

However, even if a set used by a past Demon King is reused, the newly overwritten personality does not retain memories from the previous overwrite.

Maintaining the personality and curse mark requires a connection to the Demon King.

A maximum of four such connections can be maintained. Hence, the Four Heavenly Kings.

When a Four Heavenly King dies, a new connection can be created, but if a Four Heavenly King is defeated by someone bearing the title ‘Hero’, the maximum number of connections decreases.

One of the Demon King’s curse marks, and the one that has inflicted the greatest harm upon humanity.

It goes without saying that the current Demon King has been forced to use \<Fourfold Appointment> the most.

---

**AN:** The boss enemy revealed before the protagonist even arrives.

The Demon King’s skill revealed without the Demon King appearing.

Sloppy.

+++

# **163: Dungeon Conquest (Final Version) and Conquest Rewards**

**AN:** I added a hidden side story at the very end of the previous chapter. If you have time, take a look.

This work will, without hesitation, trample over one of the taboos of creative writing (in a certain sense).

---

As evening fell, the four members of the Estea Kingdom dungeon exploration team, Cynthia, Kate, Karen, and Soura, arrived.

“Master! We want you to come to the dungeon!”

《Cynthia, you need to explain things a bit more clearly, or Master will not understand, you know?》

Kate admonished Cynthia, who had opened with an unexplained demand.

From the start, I would rather hear things from the intellectual Kate. Cynthia the puppy, back to your kennel.

Perhaps sensing the meaning behind my gaze, Kate continued.

《Actually, our party has finally reached the 50th floor of the dungeon, right in front of the boss.》

“So you finally made it to the 50th floor boss. Well done.”

Cynthia and the others have been aiming to conquer the 50th floor.

I had heard that they were getting close, but it seems they had already reached the boss room without me noticing.

《No, if anything, we feel sorry that it took us this long.》

“The 30s were tough, right, Karen?”

“The 40s were tough too, right, Soura?”

“It’s been quite some time since Master cleared the 50th floor.”

From the 30s onward, the killing intent jumps to an entirely different level, so you cannot proceed with the same mindset as the 20s.

Taking time is only natural, and in the first place, no other explorers have even made it that far.

It is not that Cynthia and the others were particularly slow.

It is simply wrong to compare them to me.

《Master, if you do not mind, would you watch our final battle in the dungeon?》

“I’ll do my best!”

I see, they want me to witness the moment they accomplish the dungeon conquest I ordered.

…Or rather, even if they did not ask, I would want to watch if possible.

When Claude and the others became S-rank, I was on an expedition to the Elgant Theocracy, so I could not see it directly (I was watching on the map, though).

This time it is the Estea Dungeon, in other words, my home dungeon, so going to watch is no trouble at all.

If anything, as the dungeon ruler, it is something I should watch.

“Very well. I will watch you from the dungeon ruler’s exclusive space. …But even if things get dangerous, I will not help you, understand?”

Even if they are my subordinates, that is that, and this is this.

《Of course.》

“We will do it!”

“”We will do our best!””

That said, if by some chance Cynthia and the others were to lose to the boss and die, I would retrieve them and revive them.

However, I would never let them act as dungeon explorers again.

Publicly, they would be treated as dead, and they would live quietly behind the scenes of the dungeon.

Saving dead explorers is not completely fair, but there are lines I cannot cross even as the dungeon ruler.

While Cynthia and the others prepared to head into the dungeon, I entered the Dungeon Core Room as well.

Inside the Dungeon Core Room is the Dungeon Core, and only the dungeon ruler may enter. However, while the dungeon ruler has not been decided, the Chief Dungeon Protector, in other words Caro, can also enter.

Not even Maria may enter, so I had Maria wait outside, in the post-dungeon-clear space.

I told her she could go back, but she insisted on staying no matter what…

This is beside the point, but Maria waiting in the space you go to after clearing the dungeon makes her feel like the true final boss, does it not?

The dungeon has no intention of letting you clear it…

By the way, this is the real boss.

Of course, it is neither the Fake Azuma I fought, nor Maria.

Demon King Lucifer

LV150

Skills:

Martial Arts

\<Spear Technique LV10> \<Throwing Technique LV10> \<Martial Arts LV10>

Magic

\<Fire Magic LV10> \<Water Magic LV10> \<Ice Magic LV10> \<Dark Magic LV10> \<Parallel Chanting LV10> \<Chantless Casting LV5>

Physical

\<Physical Enhancement LV10> \<Flight LV10> \<Levitation LV10>

\<Physical Attack Resistance LV10> \<Status Ailment Resistance LV10> \<Magic Resistance LV10>

Other

\<Inversion LV10> \<Dungeon Adaptation LV10> \<Gatekeeper LV10> \<Rebellion LV10> \<Black Ring LV10>

Notes: The one who rules all demons within the dungeon.

Since it has been a while, I will explain. On the 40s of the dungeon (floors 41 to 50), the area becomes a heaven-like zone (in appearance) during the day, and a hell-like zone at night (the difficulty is hell either way).

Due to the \<Inversion> skill, the final boss becomes a Demon King in hell mode, and a Grand Archangel in heaven mode.

I did not touch the structure up to the 50th floor at all, so this is entirely the taste of the previous dungeon ruler, Azuma.

Strengthening the heaven – angels and hell – demons imagery across the entire area, then placing a fallen angel with duality as the final boss. It is a well-balanced, beautiful thematic area.

Conversely, the Fake Azuma I fought sticks out a bit. Where did the harmony go…

As an aside, both angels and demons have flat, mannequin-like faces just like the other angels and demons of the 40s.

Aside from their faces, however, they wear dignified clothing with lavish decorations, unlike ordinary angels and demons. If everything were identical, there would be no sense of specialness.

Their weapon is a massive spear. When you think demon, you think spear. The angel version uses a greatsword.

Their size is also modest, around three meters, smaller than bosses on other floors.

Azuma apparently had no taste for making things needlessly huge just because they were the final boss. Of course, small does not mean weak.

If you look at the skills, you can see that this is essentially the culmination of the angels and demons encountered so far. In other words, if you have been thinking carefully and fighting properly until now, you should already have the necessary countermeasures.

The fact that it sneakily tries to kill Heroes with the \<Rebellion> skill is also a nice touch.

…Huh?

I just realized, but is not the name Lucifer the same as the demonic god from the Final Trial that Sera defeated before?

It cannot be the same individual… But is there some kind of connection?

A: It is just a name overlap.

Azuma… What an anticlimactic blunder at the very end…

Well, he probably just did not know about the demonic god’s existence…

While I was reminiscing about a departed friend, Cynthia and the others arrived in front of the boss room.

Hmm, they are better equipped than I expected.

It has been a while since I watched Cynthia and the others conquer a dungeon, but it seems almost all of their equipment is unified at secret-treasure class or higher.

As she showed back in the ‘Dragonkin Village’, Cynthia has completely shifted to close-combat, using gauntlets as weapons and minimal armor with very little metal.

No, she is quietly using a dragonhide breastplate and such, so her defense is probably not as low as it looks. She must have obtained it separately from the recent dragon hunt.

Also, her gauntlets seem to be legendary-class equipment. The common type that adds magic power to attack power.

On top of that, she is equipped with the “Undead Wings”, the first-clear reward from the 40th floor boss. It seems their policy is to give aerial mobility items to Cynthia, who fights on the front lines.

Karen and Soura have not changed their combat styles significantly. Karen uses a spear, and Soura uses sword and shield.

Unlike Cynthia, they wear light orichalcum armor that does not hinder movement. Was that orichalcum something Cynthia and the others collected?

Karen uses \<Fire Magic>, and Soura uses \<Ice Magic>, so they are equipped with multiple magic tools that assist spell activation.

To put it bluntly, unlike Cynthia and Kate, these two are not overwhelming geniuses, so their equipment is grounded and practical.

The most outrageous equipment setup belongs to Kate.

She has no intention of engaging in physical combat and is fully specialized in magic.

Her weapon is just a short rod for magic assistance. It does not look usable as a bludgeoning weapon at all.

She wears almost no armor, having decided that attacks will be avoided entirely.

This is a decision only Kate, who sees the world through a detailed map via \<Clairvoyance>, can make.

In exchange, she carries a huge number of magic tools and takes full responsibility for magic assistance and ally support.

After holding a final meeting in front of the boss room, Cynthia and the others steeled themselves and opened the door.

The door closed, and Lucifer appeared.

《As expected, it is a demon-type monster.》

“Kate-chan’s prediction was spot on!”

It seems Kate had predicted the nature of the final boss to some extent.

She brought plenty of appropriate magic tools. Correct.

“All right, let’s go!”

As always, Cynthia charges in first.

They made it to the 50th floor, but Cynthia’s nature never changed.

Lucifer swings his great spear to intercept, but Cynthia dodges swiftly and lands a blow to his side. Lucifer is blown back.

…Even for a final boss, engaging in close combat with current Cynthia is a losing proposition.

Lucifer creates distance and switches to \<Chantless Casting> magic attacks.

Lucifer’s \<Chantless Casting> is LV5, meaning he can cast up to LV5 spells without chanting. MP consumption increases, but there is no way the final boss has a low maximum MP.

Just as Lucifer tries to fire the LV5 \<Dark Magic> “Dark Javelin” at Cynthia, the “Ice Bullet” Kate had pre-cast lands, throwing the spell far off course.

Predicting Lucifer’s movement and disrupting his actions is one of Kate’s signature feats.

Even though a LV1 spell like “Ice Bullet” cannot cancel out a LV5 “Dark Javelin”, it can disrupt it if it hits before activation.

As Lucifer staggers from the magical hit, Karen and Soura follow up with thrusts and slashes.

The damage is not large compared to Cynthia’s blow, but it will certainly accumulate.

《Fall back!》

The moment Kate gives the order, Karen and Soura leap away.

The next instant, Lucifer swings his spear in a wide horizontal arc, launching an area attack.

Unfortunately for him, no one is within the attack range.

“Take this!”

Instead, Cynthia, who had moved through the air using the “Undead Wings”, slams down from directly above Lucifer.

Cynthia is not as dexterous as Maria, but she is still skilled enough to fully master the “Undead Wings.”

Five minutes into watching the battle between Cynthia’s party and Lucifer.

The flow of the battle has not changed much since the initial exchange.

Karen and Soura use balanced teamwork to deal steady damage and support Cynthia’s heavy-hitting attacks.

Lucifer’s attacks are either dodged or shut down by Kate before they are unleashed.

The party’s combat style is fundamentally evasion-focused, with Karen and Soura tanking only those attacks that absolutely cannot be avoided.

…Ah, did they enter a pattern?

A: They did.

That was faster than I expected.

In fact, most monsters in this dungeon are configured to follow fixed action routines based on specific behaviors.

Despite being called monsters, they lack anything resembling emotion and are closer to robots in a sense.

This is not Azuma’s taste, but a fundamental dungeon specification.

Interestingly, bosses have fewer action routines.

Because they only fight in fixed-condition boss rooms, there is no need to specify overly complex routines.

Think about it.

What happens when “Kate, who excels at action prediction”, is paired with “a boss that only has relatively simple action routines”?

Exactly. Before Kate, most bosses have their actions read and are crushed without being able to do anything.

The final boss is no exception, it seems…

With \<Physical Attack Resistance LV10> and \<Magic Resistance LV10>, it will take time, but it is ultimately only a matter of time.

Kate’s meticulous preparation even extended to starting the boss fight at 7 PM.

As mentioned earlier, the 40s switch between heaven mode and hell mode depending on the time. The boundary is 7 AM and 7 PM.

When the mode switches, all monsters in the dungeon undergo \<Inversion>, and the final boss Lucifer also inverts into Lucifel at 7 AM (HP remains the same).

By starting the fight at 7 PM, Lucifer remains unchanged for 12 hours, eliminating the need to fight two patterns. It is a long-term strategy that ensures the battle stays in the same mode.

Carefully prepare and win without risk.

This is Kate’s, or rather the party’s, fundamental policy.

Explorers do not fight just one battle, they must continue fighting over time. A narrow victory is equivalent to a loss when considering what comes next.

Kate and the others have thoroughly strengthened their sustained combat capability and stamina.

An evasion-focused style also reduces weapon wear compared to blocking.

Against Lucifer, who has many resistances and guarantees a long fight, Kate’s approach worked exceptionally well.

Against such a perfectly matched opponent, there is almost no way they could lose.

Four hours later, Lucifer fell.

…Kate really is terrifying.

Watching the demon disappear as its HP hits zero, I think that once again.

To be honest, when I gathered companions to conquer the Estea Dungeon and form the explorer party, I thought the Hero, Cynthia, would ultimately become the central figure.

However, before I realized it, the center and leader of the party had become Kate.

It was clear from the first battle (the great rampage) that Cynthia lacked leadership aptitude, but I did not expect Kate to grow this much.

Using her innate \<Spatial Perception> and \<Calculation>, she became a command tower who grasps the situation, predicts actions, and issues orders and support from the rear.

To defeat the final boss with almost no damage taken… This is truly a welcome miscalculation.

“We did it!”

“”We won!””

《Everyone, good work.》

“”Good work Kate!””

“Good work!”

After completely sealing the boss, Cynthia and the others sit down and praise each other.

Even so, there is no denying it was a long battle, and fatigue shows on their faces.

Then, from the boss’s spawn point, a pillar of light appears. A warp point.

Beyond the warp point lies the post-dungeon-clear space.

《We should not keep Master waiting. Come, let’s go.》

“I want to rest just a little…”

“Just one minute.”

“Even 30 seconds is fine.”

《…Very well. Just a little. Master, we are sorry.》

I am not going to complain about a short rest.

Alta, tell them they can rest for one minute or five minutes, whichever they want.

A: Understood.

All right, I will go congratulate them myself.

Leaving the Dungeon Core Room, I return to the post-dungeon-clear space.

A pillar of light is rising here as well.

“Maria, sorry to keep you waiting.”

“No problem. Did Cynthia and the others win?”

From the post-dungeon-clear space where Maria was waiting, the boss battle is not visible.

Seeing that she is a bit sweaty, it seems she was training alone.

“Yeah, it was an easy victory.”

“That is good to hear. Things went exactly as you wished, Jin-sama.”

So she says “good” not because Cynthia and the others were safe, but because things proceeded conveniently for me.

Maria really never wavers.

Of course, it is not that she feels no relief over Cynthia and the others’ safety…

– Bwoom –

As I was talking with Maria, the four of them appeared from the pillar of light with a teleportation sound.

“Master, we won! Cynthia won!”

《Cynthia, please do not run ahead!》

“”Excuse us!””

Once everyone passed through, the pillar of light burst and vanished.

The break was shorter than I expected, but everyone seems fully recovered.

“Good work. That was a good fight.”

“””《Thank you very much!》”””

Some might say it lacked excitement or spectacle, but I believe winning safely through strategy is also a “good fight.”

To put it bluntly, facing a boss you know is there and still being put in danger means either insufficient preparation or poor prediction.

“All right then, I will give you the dungeon clear rewards.”

“We did it! Lesser Wind Dragon!”

“No, the Lesser Wind Dragon is not a dungeon clear reward.”

I correct Cynthia’s misunderstanding.

“It is not?”

“No. The Lesser Wind Dragon is a gift I plan to give you as Queen’s Knight Gene. What I am about to give you is the clear reward as the dungeon ruler.”

More precisely, these rewards were prepared by the previous dungeon ruler, Azuma.

I received the Dungeon Core by becoming the dungeon ruler through a hidden route, but Azuma also prepared rewards for those who cleared it via the normal route.

I intend to largely inherit Azuma’s policies regarding the dungeon, so I decided to use the rewards as-is.

“There are two main things I will give you. One is the normal clear reward, and the other is the first-clear reward for defeating the final boss. The area bosses had first-clear rewards too, right?”

“The ‘Undead Wings’ are useful, but flying for a long time is tiring.”

Humans are not built to fly, after all.

It is like forcibly using a function you were not designed for, so it places a mental burden.

“For long-distance flight, the Lesser Wind Dragon will be your best option. …Anyway, the final boss also has a first-clear reward. This is it.”

I show them the stone in my hand.

《Is that… a Phase-Shift Stone?》

It looks almost identical to the Phase-Shift Stones used for dungeon return and re-entry.

However, its effect is entirely different.

“Close, but not quite. This is called a ‘Teleport Stone’. Simply put, it lets you teleport to any location above the dungeon. Unlimited uses, unlimited distance. It is similar to my dungeon ruler teleportation authority.”

It is not a two-way stone. Just a teleport stone.

Which also means it has no unnecessary restrictions.

“That is amazing! Gathering requests will be so much easier!”

“We do not even take gathering requests.”

“We only did dungeon conquest.”

《Saying that ‘Portal’ already covers this would not be appropriate, would it?》

That is a surprisingly lukewarm reaction.

Well, compared to us who teleport constantly, its value probably feels diminished.

Well then, let’s strengthen it.

“…Actually, there is a hidden meaning to ‘any location above the dungeon’. Kate, what is above the dungeon?”

《The Kingdom of Estea… wait, do you mean!?》

“Yes. Anywhere within the Kingdom of Estea. Dungeon or surface, you can teleport anywhere you like.”

With this, you can teleport anywhere within the Kingdom of Estea.

The royal castle, a vault, anywhere.

“Wait, Master, does that mean you can also teleport anywhere in the Kingdom of Estea?”

“Did I not tell you? I can.”

I answer Cynthia.

“This is the first I have heard of it.”

If it can be turned into an item, there is no reason a dungeon ruler cannot do it.

I have been using it whenever traveling between the dungeon and the Estea estate.

Thinking about it, this country is the one I have the most complete control over.

Other countries are controlled by placing their leaders under me or by economic dominance, but only this country has every land and resource fully under my control.

I hold life-and-death authority over the entire country. I just do not do anything with it.

《It is convenient… but owning it could get you targeted.》

“That judgment is up to you. I will give you four Teleport Stones, but only one person can be registered per stone. Ownership transfer is possible, but re-registration is not. You can threaten someone to take it, but you cannot kill them to steal it.”

Azuma clearly understood the danger and built in several safety measures.

《Understood. We will discuss how to handle the Teleport Stones later.》

“It is a dangerous item, Karen.”

“It is a troublesome item, Soura.”

“Convenient items should be used!”

The problem is that it is too convenient.

Even for a first-clear reward, this is overly generous.

“Also, the normal clear reward is choice-based. There are quite a few options, such as a bundle of limited drops from previous bosses, or a bundle of first-clear bonuses.”

The first-clear bonus bundle contains four first-clear rewards from previous area bosses, including the “Undead Wings.”

The limited drop bundle includes extremely rare drops such as the “Divine Medicine Soma”, which restores lost body parts, and the ultra-rare ore “Hihiirokane.”

Either would be worth a fortune if sold. Almost no one sells them.

“There are also a limited number of legendary-class equipment collected by Azuma that you can choose from. …Honestly, explorers capable of reaching this point probably already have legendary equipment, so it might feel a bit late.”

When I conquered the dungeon and became the dungeon ruler, I gave legendary equipment to Maria and Dora.

Those were actually from Azuma’s collection.

Even though they did not defeat the boss, I judged that effectively clearing the dungeon warranted the reward.

“Master, is the reward one per party?”

“Yes. However, you can receive up to four pieces of legendary equipment.”

After all that effort, one legendary item would be too little, but giving one per person would also be unreasonable.

So Azuma used the standard four-person party as a baseline and allowed up to four items per party.

“Choose carefully!”

《Indeed. First, limited drops are off the table. Thanks to the Teleport Stones, boss hunting is now easy. If we really want them, we can teleport near boss rooms. Thanks to Master sharing his luck, drop rates should not be an issue. Next, legendary equipment is also not particularly important. While these are exclusive to this dungeon, legendary equipment can be obtained elsewhere. We already have multiple legendary items, so increasing the number of equivalent gear has limited benefit. That leaves the first-clear reward bundle as the strongest option. It is useful for dungeon conquest and highly versatile. The ‘Toughness Ring’ from the Fire Dragon was excellent, and I hear the first-clear rewards from the Elder Treant and Minotaur were also useful. Above all, being able to re-acquire the ‘Undead Wings’ is huge. Currently Cynthia is using the first one, but if we obtain a second, I should use it. If we only have one, Karen and Soura’s coordination could be disrupted. In other words, we can finally match Master! That alone makes it worth obtaining!》

“N… okay…”

Kate had thought so far ahead that even Cynthia was taken aback.

《Cynthia, Karen, Soura, I would like to choose the first-clear reward bundle from the previous bosses. Any objections?》

“No.”

“”None.””

She asked for opinions, but after that display, no one was going to object.

《Master, we would like the first-clear reward bundle.》

“All right.”

I hand the four first-clear rewards to Cynthia and the others.

《Ufufufufufu…》

As discussed, Kate will use the “Undead Wings.”

She looks extremely happy… Or rather, her eyes are a bit unsettling. She is rubbing her cheek against the “Undead Wings” with vacant eyes.

“Oh, right. There is one thing I would like to ask.”

《Please ask me anything.》

When I speak up after remembering something, Kate immediately responds, snapping back to sanity.

She agrees before even asking what it is…

“I want the four of you to keep my existence secret. This time, since it was an internal challenge, I handed you the rewards directly, but normally this is the role of the Chief Dungeon Protector, Caro.”

“Is that so?”

Normally, the dungeon ruler never appears before challengers.

Just like when we cleared the dungeon, Caro is supposed to explain things to the conquerors.

“Caro, come out.”

“You called? Pyon.”

When I call out, Caro appears in her bunny-girl outfit (formal wear).

Her forcibly tacked-on verbal tic remains intact.

“This is Caro. Have you met her before?”

《Yes, we have met her several times at the Estea estate.》

“Cynthia has met her too.”

“”We have as well.””

I have too many subordinates to keep track of who knows whom.

If I drew a relationship chart, it would be absurd.

“Since you know each other, that saves time. Caro, sorry, but could you give Kate and the others the proper ‘explanation for conquerors’? Kate, you will use that explanation as the official account, without mentioning me.”

As the first ever dungeon conquerors, they will surely be asked for explanations in appropriate places.

To answer publicly without revealing my existence, they need to hear the proper explanation from Caro.

This was also Azuma’s policy.

《Understood. Caro, please explain.》

“Yes. I will explain from the beginning, pyon.”

“Cynthia does not need to listen?”

《You need to listen carefully. We must ensure our stories align.》

Cynthia, who was about to leave, gets caught by Kate.

“Okay…”

Cynthia reluctantly prepares to listen.

Caro’s explanation will be almost identical to mine, so it will probably bore her.

“Well then, I will head back first. …Oh, right. This is secret information, but the final boss respawn cycle is one year. Exactly one year from today, the final boss will appear again, so look forward to it.”

That is right.

Just like other area bosses, the final boss also respawns. Since there is a first-clear reward, they could have guessed.

A one-year respawn cycle might sound long, but considering the guaranteed clear rewards, it is overly generous.

“I am looking forward to it!”

《”Undead Wings”… a third one!?》

“We cannot tell anyone, Karen!”

“We cannot tell anyone, Soura!”

Most notably, if there are no other conquerors, the first conqueror can defeat it repeatedly.

And if you know the respawn cycle, you can snipe it. If it does not get out, you can obtain rewards over and over… Am I spoiling them too much?

Leaving the still-excited Cynthia and the others to Caro, I return to the estate.

Or rather, it is already late at night, so I am going to sleep. I am sleepy.

Oh, right. I should probably hold a dungeon-clear celebration party for Cynthia and the others tomorrow or the day after…

“Fwaaah…”

---

Settings

– Relationship between miasma and monsters

In this world, miasma refers primarily to stagnation of sufficiently dense magical power.

Magical power exists evenly throughout the world (excluding the area around the former Spirit World) and circulates (excluding the former Spirit World area), but most magical power stagnates to some degree.

The causes of stagnation vary, but the main cause is disruption in magical circulation (around the former Spirit World, it was not just stagnation but a blank zone).

When this stagnation becomes strong and dense beyond a certain threshold, monsters begin to spawn in that region. Regions where monsters spawn are called “Monster Domains.”

Miasma stagnation is equalized on an area basis as recognized by Jin, and spawn frequency is determined per area. The higher the density, the higher the frequency.

Monsters within a “Monster Domain” generally do not leave the domain that spawned them unless under special circumstances (such as a monster rampage).

When all monsters spawned in a “Monster Domain” are wiped out, rare monsters spawn as a bonus.

However, after wiping them out once, simply wiping out a few newly spawned monsters will not trigger a rare spawn. They must increase to saturation again before wiping them out has meaning.

Strictly speaking, monsters are not born from miasma. Stagnated magical power becomes a magic stone, which then transforms into a monster through mysterious forces. In other words, monster bodies are not made of miasma.

Additionally, monsters spawned in “Monster Domains” always possess magic stones within their bodies.

Some monsters have magic stones, and some do not, but monsters with magic stones almost always originate from spawning within a “Monster Domain” (they may reproduce afterward).

---

**AN:** In creative works, you rarely see overlapping character names.

Outside of naming children after related people, coincidences are almost nonexistent.

Realistically, if you transfer schools, names would overlap, right?

When people move across regions, it would not be unnatural for identical names to exist.

However, because it is inconvenient to address them, if the same name appears, one of them will always die (or be wiped out).
