# **164: Lucid Dreams and the Guild Union District**

**AN:** We are going sightseeing in the Guild Union District.

---

When I realized it, I was standing in a pitch-dark space like outer space.

Even though I say “like outer space”, I was not floating. It felt like my feet were firmly on the ground, but…

…Where is this? …Ah, this is a dream.

It lacked the sense of reality unique to dreams, so I was able to realize immediately that it was a dream.

A so-called lucid dream. In that case, I would be wasting it if I did not enjoy myself.

Looking around, I saw a single tree some distance away.

It was not thick, but it was long. No matter how hard I tried to look, I could not see its top.

…Would Asai have been able to see the top?

I tried walking toward it.

I could not get any closer at all.

I tried running toward it.

I could not get any closer at all.

Only then did I finally understand.

That was not a tree standing a short distance away.

It was unimaginably far away, but because it was far too large, my sense of perspective was distorted, making it look as if it were close.

At that point, it became a matter of pride.

I ran toward the huge tree with all my strength.

Perhaps because it was a dream.

I did not get tired, but it was a strange sensation where I could not go as fast as I could in reality.

I had no sense of time, so I did not know how long I had been running, but eventually I managed to get close to the tree.

It was so large that it was practically a wall.

When I touched it, I felt a strangely nostalgic sensation. A tree, after all…

…

Looking more closely, there was a small tree growing near the huge one.

This one was only about as tall as me.

When I touched it, it felt even more nostalgic than before.

A little farther away, there were small saplings.

There were nine small saplings growing with some distance between them.

I touched them one by one, but from eight of them I felt neither nostalgia nor anything else.

The last one was a little farther away, clearly less healthy than the other eight, and when I touched it, I felt an urge to cheer it on.

While touching it, I wished for it to become healthy.

Perhaps because it was a dream. The unhealthy sapling gradually became healthier.

“That was a strange dream.”

The next morning, I muttered that as I woke up feeling not particularly refreshed.

As if I had shared my energy with the sapling in the dream, I felt slightly tired.

《What’s wrong?》

Dora, who was in dragon form acting as my body pillow, picked up my muttering.

“No, it’s nothing serious. I just had a dream.”

《I had a dream too! A dream about eating snacks!》

Ah, soothing.

The tired feeling from the dream blew away. It must have only been that level of fatigue.

“Well then, shall we have breakfast?”

《Okay!》

I woke up the freeloaders in my room (Aya, Blue, and El), and we had breakfast in the dining hall.

Ash people and the Progenitor Dragon God technically do not need to eat though, but will if they feel like it.

According to Alta, the trouble involving Claude and the others seems to be settling down, so today we should finally be able to go to the Guild Union District.

If we are heading out from the morning, it might be better to keep breakfast light and leave room to eat once we arrive.

“Thank you for the meal.”

《Thank you! Full, full!》

Incidentally, Dora, who had no intention of keeping it light, ate heartily from the morning.

“So, can we go with you this time, Master?”

“It is probably impossible. You said you would be pretending to be an ordinary adventurer.”

The one who answered Blue’s question was El.

Since we decided to travel by carriage this time, there would be no role for a riding dragon.

“More importantly, Blue is recognized as the Queen Knight’s riding dragon. You probably would not be allowed to ride without a disguise anymore.”

“Wha!?”

Blue’s eyes went wide at Aya’s merciless statement.

Come to think of it, whenever I rode Blue in public, I was always in the guise of Queen’s Knight Gene.

In other words, does that mean I can only ride Blue while in the form of Gene?

“M-Master…”

“Sorry. I did not think that far. I will think of a way for me to ride Blue.”

“P-Please do!”

When my beloved dragon begs me like that, I cannot just ignore it.

I disguise myself as someone other than Gene and ride her. I turn both Blue and myself invisible with \<Non-Attribute Magic> and ride her. I disguise Blue instead.

Yeah, I will think about it before the opportunity comes.

“While we are at it, what about you, El?”

“Your treatment of me is terrible… Well, there is no need for me to accompany you. Honestly, you do not need a familiar, right? Let me be free.”

Well, there are not many situations where I would need a familiar.

And if I need one, I can summon her anytime…

“Is Rain coming?”

-Nod, nod-

When I called out, the Great Spirit who teleported in nodded happily.

“Something appeared…”

“Is it not only natural that Rain appears when you bring up El?”

Like a familiar, a Great Spirit can accompany us in a state invisible to others.

She rarely shows herself, but she has usually been accompanying us whenever we travel far.

Additionally, by becoming ‘Spirit-Form’ with Rain, I can boost my abilities, but that is more of an emergency safeguard.

Rain accompanying us is not for combat strength, but simply because Rain wants to be with me.

“If Rain is coming along, then there is even less reason for me to go. Well, I am happiest when I can manifest and relax, so it is not a problem…”

“Do we really need a completely useless pseudo-personality?”

El’s original self is already dead, and the El here is a pseudo-personality created by an ability.

Since I can make her appear or disappear freely, there is also the option of erasing her if she is unnecessary.

“N-No, I will go with you after all! I am useful, so please tell me to do anything! I will do anything! So please spare me from being erased!”

“Ah, Master, she may be like this, but she is still a friend, so could you at least not erase her?”

“She is a complete freeloader, but she is a friend.”

Blue and Aya step in to support their friend El.

…That counts as support, right?

“I am joking, so relax. …So, what will you do, El?”

“Of course I am coming along… Even if it is a joke, the fact that there is room to joke about it is terrifying.”

“Desperate for survival.”

“Indeed.”

Thus, El and Rain would accompany us, while Blue and Aya would stay behind.

To begin with, Aya accompanying us was physically difficult from the start.

After a short rest, we began preparing to depart with the party members.

“Luggage checked. Carriage checked. Disguise equipment checked.”

I pointed and confirmed the luggage prepared by the maids.

I did say I would do it myself. But the maids would not budge, insisting that it was their job.

“Mythical-grade equipment would stand out too much, after all.”

“This is an adventurer’s country, so excessively powerful weapons would attract attention.”

As Mio and Sera said, the adventurer’s country is not a place where you can casually bring mythical-grade equipment.

Anyone with an eye for it would immediately notice how abnormal it is.

So we decided to make do with disguised mithril equipment.

“Hmm, honestly, even mithril equipment will stand out, though…”

“The goal is not to be inconspicuous. As long as the equipment is not obviously strange, it is fine. There is even the phrase ‘stopping at C-rank.’ Even if a C-rank adventurer is strong, it should not be that unnatural.”

Once adventurers reach B-rank or above, they gain rights equivalent to those of nobles, along with the accompanying obligations.

Those who dislike that deliberately avoid going above B-rank. That is called ‘stopping at C-rank.’

Conversely, C-rank is where the quality varies wildly, and ranks are often unreliable.

“That is true, but there are not many adventurers who deliberately stop at C-rank in the Guild Union District.”

“Is that so?”

That was news to me.

Honestly, Sera knows far more about guild affairs than I do.

“Yes. In the Guild Union District, adventurers are essential. For someone who deliberately stays in the Guild Union District, there is no merit in keeping their rank lower than their ability. Obligations to the country are equivalent to obligations to the guild.”

“Ah… Adventurers occupy a different position here compared to ordinary countries.”

“Yes. There are some who come just for sightseeing, but it is said that adventurers coming purely for sightseeing while ignoring the guild is extremely rare.”

Adventurers come to the Guild Union District for the guild. Everyone else comes for sightseeing.

Adventurers coming just to sightsee… well, that makes sense.

“Let us just call ourselves a rare case…”

If it is not zero, then it is fine.

“If Master does not mind, then it is fine.”

“It is not like Master would cancel sightseeing at this point.”

“Because he is Jin-kun…”

《Because he is!》

With that settled, we transferred using the ‘portal’ prepared by Claude and the others.

“Hm? Are Claude and the others not here?”

The destination was a grassland, seemingly far off the road, with no sign of people around.

“It seems there is still some mess left for Claude and the others. They want us to go ahead.”

The one who answered my question was Mio.

She is actually closer to Claude and the others than I am.

“I see. They have it rough too.”

We did not plan to act together with Claude and the others this time, so let us go sightseeing ahead of them.

I looked around slowly.

“So that is the volcano of this country. It is insanely huge.”

What lay before my gaze was the largest volcano in the volcanic region of the Guild Union District, commonly known as ‘Volcan Volcano.’ The name is almost redundant.

As you can probably guess without being told, the ‘Disaster Dragon Volcano’ is buried beneath it.

“So there is a disaster dragon there…?”

“Yeah. It revives if you kill the Guild Master.”

“Master, you are suddenly saying something very dangerous.”

It is dangerous, but it is also the truth.

What is strange is that, unlike Ulysses, the Guild Master operates openly in the world.

Considering the importance of the ‘Shrine Maiden Princess’, she should be a figure that must be kept secret. Taking on a responsible position in the open world should be nothing but risk.

If her life were ever targeted, it would be equivalent to a world crisis. …If I get the chance, I would like to ask the reason.

“Jin-sama, we will be departing shortly, so please board.”

“Ah, got it.”

Since we were going with only the main party this time, we entrusted the role of driver to Maria.

Strictly speaking, the Great Spirit and familiar are accompanying us? Or merged? But anyway.

L: Did you call for me?

I did not.

“So, where exactly are we?”

“Yes. This is a point about one hour by carriage from the capital of the Guild Union District.”

After hearing Maria’s explanation, I checked the map.

So that is the capital. About an hour along the road. Anything interesting around… Just monster territory, really. Heading straight to the capital should be fine.

“Maria, I am counting on you.”

“Yes, leave it to me.”

Leaving things to Maria, I continued checking the map.

As befits an adventurer’s country, there are adventurers all over the map.

There seem to be quite a few S-rank adventurers too… clearly concentrated in the capital.

A: They appear to be personnel intended to forcibly secure Yuria in case of emergency.

Wow, that is a dirty way of doing things…

By the way, have the S-rank adventurers agreed to that?

A: Yes. I confirmed their discussions via the map. Some were reluctant, but since it was a direct request from the Guild Master, most ultimately agreed.

The map is always useful…

Still, S-ranks assisting in kidnapping. How far they have fallen.

In my mind, the value of adventurers dropped another notch.

And so, the S-rank adventurers gathered in the capital, or rather, S-rank kidnappers, were tentatively designated as skill points.

“Master, you have a rather nasty look on your face.”

Mio said as she peered at my face.

“No, I am just happy thinking about all the unique skills I might get.”

“So that was a happy face. I thought it was a scheming face.”

Many S-rank adventurers possess unique-grade skills.

If they become enemies, I will naturally take them without mercy.

“Ah, the matter of the S-rank adventurers in the capital. It really is deplorable.”

Sera is indignant.

It seems she gathered information about the capital before I did.

Or maybe I am just too uninterested?

“And for Master, even those S-rank adventurers are just skill points.”

“I will not take them from anyone who is not hostile. Or from those I owe a favor to.”

That is a personal rule I have no intention of breaking.

Well, since I decide the balance myself, it may not mean much…

“But it is almost certain that they will be hostile, right…?”

“Nine times out of ten. It is certain that the S-ranks are pathetic.”

I answered Sakura’s question, already expecting hostility.

I cannot say for certain since I do not know the Guild Master’s character, but…

“Even if we act, it will be after Claude and the others arrive. …Will they make it today?”

“Looks impossible.”

Once again, Mio’s information.

“Then let us secure an inn for today and relax in the hot springs. …Now that I think about it, can we even get an inn at this point?”

Getting an inn on the same day in a tourist spot?

Thinking about it, that is a fairly high difficulty?

“It really is a bit late to think about that.”

“I have already confirmed via the map. Please choose an available inn that suits your preference, Jin-sama.”

As expected of Maria.

I checked the marked inns on the map.

Ah, I see. The prices vary widely. Luxury inns do not fill up easily.

And we have no reason to skimp on money.

“Then let us choose ‘Private Mixed-Bathing Open-Air Bath West Wind Pavilion.’”

When coming to a hot spring area with both men and women, there is no reason not to choose mixed bathing.

It seems each room draws its own hot spring, so there is no worry about random people seeing everyone naked.

“M-Mixed bathing…!?”

“You really went straight for it.”

“It is nothing to be concerned about.”

《Yay! Bath with Master!》

Everyone’s reactions differ.

Why is Maria clenching her fist and making a small victory pose?

Ah, apparently swimsuits are allowed, just in case.

After driving the carriage for a while, we arrived at the capital with the guild headquarters, Bolken.

…Could they not have tried a little harder with the name?

The city of Bolken is likely less than an hour by carriage from Volcan Volcano (confusing).

Perhaps because we are closer, Volcan Volcano feels even larger than before.

As an adventurer-centered country (strictly speaking, not exactly), in the Guild Union District, adventurers of D-rank and above can enter and exit the city for free.

However, to enter for free, you must register your guild card with the city.

Since sightseeing is our main purpose and we have no intention of doing adventurer work, we decided to pay the toll normally to avoid generating extra obligations (such as mandatory quests).

I had expected Japanese-style buildings because it is a hot spring area, but instead there were ordinary Western-style buildings lining the streets.

I should have thought of it as a volcanic region rather than a hot spring town…

As both a tourist destination and a holy land for adventurers, the population and foot traffic are extremely high.

Even so, the roads are wider than that, making it easy to pass through by carriage. Or rather, the city itself is quite large.

“First, let us secure the inn. There seems to be room, but the sooner the better. Maria, head to West Wind Pavilion.”

“Yes, understood.”

《Then food after!》

“I am looking forward to the food of an unfamiliar land.”

It was nearing noon, so the hungry members of our household were becoming lively.

I was also looking forward to the cuisine of an unfamiliar land and wanted to eat soon.

…After all, you never know when the city might be destroyed and you will not be able to eat anymore.

Setting aside such ill-omened thoughts, securing the inn went smoothly.

We left the carriage and horses at the inn, so we could devote ourselves to sightseeing without worry. Tamo-san was guarding the carriage and horses, so security was perfect.

The city is large enough that traveling by carriage is an option, but we avoided it because it lacks maneuverability.

There are shared carriages running throughout the city, so there is no need to use our own carriage. Like buses in our world, they apparently arrive at stops at regular intervals.

The idea somehow feels like it might have come from a Hero, but it is a gray area where you cannot say for sure.

Since we had the chance, we decided to ride a shared carriage. Our destination was the city center, where the eateries are.

“There are not many people riding. Can this turn a profit?”

There were only the six of us in the carriage.

If we had not boarded, the carriage would have run without any passengers.

“Hey there, are you tourists, kid!?”

“Yeah, we just came to this city today.”

The coachman struck up a conversation.

He was well-built and had fairly high stats. He was no amateur.

“Then it is no surprise you do not know! The shared carriages are run by the city, so we get paid even if no one rides! In fact, it is easier when there are no passengers!”

“Is that something you should say to us, the passengers?”

“It is not very good, is it!”

The coachman answered Mio’s question without a shred of guilt.

“It is fine with tourists like you guys, but adventurers are the problem! They are a hair’s breadth away from being ruffians, so they cause trouble all the time! Though, I am a retired adventurer myself, so I cannot act too high and mighty!”

Ah, I see.

The coachman actually has a fairly serious injury.

One of the reemployment paths for adventurers who retire due to injury is becoming a shared carriage driver.

The fact that the city runs it, in other words, the Adventurers guild runs it, must be related to that.

“How far did your adventurer rank go?”

“C-rank! Not stopping at C-rank on purpose, but C-rank by ability! In this country, once you reach C-rank, your treatment improves a lot! They even prepare reemployment options for you!”

That explains his high stats.

He has a serious injury, but he is not completely unable to fight.

With some strength and experience as an adventurer, making a living in this city is probably not too difficult.

After that, we heard various things about the city from the coachman.

The Guild Master, the top of this country, rarely appears in public.

He saw her once, and she was a stunningly beautiful elf.

As an elf, she has remained at the top of the guild for a very long time.

There is a rumor that if you become an S-rank adventurer, you can get an appointment with her.

Her own combat power is apparently quite high.

She has talent for creating magical tools.

Most of the magical tools related to the guild are made by the Guild Master herself.

She is highly regarded by various countries and has influence everywhere.

Support for retired adventurers is also primarily handled under the Guild Master’s leadership.

That is about all the information regarding the Guild Master, Yurisus-san.

I am perplexed because it is a more upstanding evaluation than I expected. If she were not upstanding, her long rule would not have lasted, so it makes sense, but still…

Then what exactly is this rough (planned) summons about?

I set aside matters that I could not reach a conclusion on here and listened to other stories.

Good places to eat, recommended sightseeing spots, inns where you can use only the hot springs, S-rank adventurers based in the city, shady areas you should avoid…

Enjoying the city’s unique mode of transportation and chatting with a resident to gather information about the city.

I am really being a tourist right now!

“Oops, we are here! The eateries in the center are a bit pricey, but they are generally good, so do not worry!”

While I was being moved by pointless emotion, it seems we arrived at our destination.

I thanked the coachman and got off the carriage.

Considering we gathered information just for the fare, it was not a bad deal.

《Food this time for sure!》

“Yeah. Since we are here, let us have lunch at one of the places the coachman recommended.”

The shops he told us about were already marked on the map.

“Being a volcanic country, it seems they are particular about ‘grilled’ dishes. Okonomiyaki-type and yakisoba-type dishes seem to be common. They are dishes with many variations, and Mio-chan does not have many of those in her repertoire.”

“If possible, I would like a place that can add to Mio-san’s repertoire.”

With Mio and Sera’s requests in mind, we chose from the coachman’s selection a restaurant serving dishes Mio did not know the recipes for.

“Judging by the smell, I think it will definitely be edible, but I hesitate a little…”

“It does not look great, does it… But it is delicious, so relax! It is popular in the other world too!”

A representative dish that makes you hesitate at first glance. Yes, it is monjayaki.

“Ah, it is a dish from the other world. And if Mio-san says so, then it should be fine.”

After ordering, instead of the finished dish, the ingredients were brought out.

It is the type of place where you are taught the minimum etiquette and make it yourself (though they will do it for you if you ask).

Even if you fail a bit, it usually ends up reasonably tasty.

“I am absolutely not touching it.”

“Neither am I…”

The Special-Power-user group at the very bottom of the crafting caste decided to just watch.

“I should probably be the one to make it, but I do not have the reach.”

《Too bad!》

Apparently, the shop was not designed with children cooking in mind, and the griddle is large, making it difficult for shorter Mio and Dora to cook.

If we were willing to choose any means, it would be different, but we are not going that far here.

“So, that means we are making it, right?”

“Since Jin-sama will be eating it, I will give it my all.”

Sera and Maria can cook as well (though someone who can cook as well as Mio is extremely rare).

They made the monjayaki, and we scooped it up with spatulas to eat.

The method is not that difficult, but I will absolutely not get involved. Absolutely not.

“It is delicious, but since you eat only a small amount at a time, it is hard to feel full.”

《More!》

As expected, Sera and Dora ate mountains of it.

I also ended up eating more than I thought I would.

This is a trivial note, but we bought the spatulas as-is.

It said you could buy them for a small additional fee on top of the monjayaki price. A souvenir, a souvenir.

With our stomachs full from monjayaki, we decided to look around the city.

Ugh, I ate too much, monja might come out of my mouth (terrible metaphor… is it even a metaphor?).

Once again, we picked a spot from the coachman’s selection.

The place was called the ‘Adventurers Memorial Hall.’

“Oh, a memorial hall for S-rank adventurers who made great achievements.”

The building, larger than a modest art museum, was a memorial hall meant to honor the achievements of S-rank adventurers and preserve their records.

To begin with, becoming an S-rank adventurer is itself proof of having accomplished great feats, so there should be no shortage of material worth recording.

“It seems they display legends and replicas of weapons.”

As Maria said, the hall displays photographs and portraits of past S-rank adventurers, their accomplishments, and, if they were owners of famous weapons, replicas of those weapons as well.

There is no way the real things would be here.

A: There are a few real ones.

There are? Weapons have value only when used…

With a slight sense of dissatisfaction, I continued walking through the memorial hall.

“Let us see, they say he cut down a dragon that attacked the city in a single stroke? It sounds exaggerated, but since it is a record in an adventurer city, it should not be false, right?”

“We just hunted a dragon not long ago, so it does not surprise me.”

“This one says they saved the land from drought by making it rain with magic… Such a wide area would be difficult even with \<Water Magic> level 10, so could it be a unique skill…?”

“A skill that controls the weather. There are strong people even outside of official circles.”

Yeah, viewed as a record of extraordinary individuals, it is fairly interesting.

《Master, look at this!》

“What is it?”

Called by Dora, I went to see the exhibit she was pointing at.

“Ah…”

《It is the same as Master’s weapon!》

What was displayed there was a replica of the legendary-grade blade ‘Spirit Blade: Incomplete’, which belonged to the S-rank adventurer Cerdic, also known as Sebastian.

Naturally, Sebastian’s legend was displayed beside it.

Let us see…

‘Grim Reaper Cerdic’, who assassinated numerous S-rank adventurers during wars between nations…

That old man had surprisingly brutal legends.

It was good that I hid the ‘Heroic Spirit Blade: Incomplete’ before coming to the Guild Union District.

Even though it changed shape after passing the final trial, there was still a good chance that someone knowledgeable could notice the connection.

The first S-rank adventurer I met after coming to this world, a lot of time has passed since then, but it seems we had an unexpected connection.

“I am gratefully making use of the blade.”

He would probably not be happy to be thanked by me, though.

**AN:** However, recently, I have not been using the ‘Heroic Spirit Blade: Incomplete.’

As for the first half of this chapter, there is no particularly deep meaning.

+++

# **165: Hot Springs and S-Rank Hunting**

**AN:** One of the biggest flaws of this work, I think, is that the protagonist is too strong, making it hard to understand the relative strength of anyone else. To use an analogy, from the perspective of one hundred million, the difference between one and one hundred is basically just margin of error.

Even so-called disposable characters can be overwhelmingly strong when viewed from the general public’s perspective.

---

After leaving the ‘Adventurer Memorial Hall’, we decided to head for the hot springs, the main sightseeing attraction of the Guild Union District.

We were not going to the hot spring attached to our inn, but to an open-air bath that was just a hot spring, with no lodging.

Naturally, it was not mixed bathing, so I would be the only one entering the men’s bath.

Maria tried to accompany me as a guard while invisible, but I refused.

Since Maria clung to me and begged, we eventually compromised on having Tamo-san act as my guard, along with one additional condition.

Incidentally, Tamo-san is hiding in the hot water.

It might be unorthodox, but I used ‘Purification’ before soaking in the bath.

“Fuu…”

A voice escaped me at the pleasant sensation of warmth spreading through my whole body.

As expected, authentic hot springs are on another level. It almost makes me want to thank the ‘Calamity Dragon Volcano’.

Since this is a hot spring town, I’d like to bathe three times today.

It seems Claude and the others will arrive in the capital today, but they plan to visit the guild tomorrow.

In other words, there should not be any major events today.

《Jin-sama, has anything changed?》

《No, no problems》

This was the other condition, regular telepathic check-ins from Maria.

For the sake of Maria’s mental stability, she checks in every five minutes. Her level of worry makes me concerned for her future.

Also, I cannot relax at all.

– GARA GARA, PISHAN –

Oh, looks like another customer came in.

Up until now, I’d been lucky enough to have the place to myself…

I wasn’t particularly interested, but I ended up glancing at the person who entered.

A terrifying-looking bald, muscular man, overflowing with presence. …Ah, an S-rank adventurer.

And not just any S-rank, but George-san, one of the very few S-rank adventurers who refused a request from the guild master.

I have no interest in those who accepted the guild master’s request, but I do have some interest in those who refused.

He was considered a promising, upright adventurer candidate, so Alta had given me information about him.

George-san is 38 years old, an age where stamina starts to become an issue, but his thoroughly trained muscles are still very much intact. In a bathhouse, you can really tell.

He operates in a neighboring country next to the Guild Union District, so he had no connection to anyone associated with me.

His achievement upon reaching S-rank was exterminating a rampaging ogre (upper species) bare-handed. As expected of a macho.

The reason I know this much detail is because the Adventurers Guild headquarters is located here, so they have comprehensive information on S-rank adventurers.

Alta simply peeked at it using detailed map display.

Apparently, George-san is also a philanthropist who donates to orphanages.

However, when George-san approaches children, they cry from sheer intimidation, so he has never actually entered an orphanage. A sad macho.

More importantly, why does the guild even have that kind of information?

A: An interview article was published in a magazine.

S-rank adventurers really are a popular profession, huh.

…That said, why am I narrating this much detail about a random macho old man I happened to encounter in a bathhouse?

Probably because his mere presence at the edge of my vision is so overwhelming that my attention keeps getting drawn to him.

I deliberately shifted my awareness away from George, put some distance between us, and continued enjoying the bath.

Then I reached a state of selflessness and became one with the hot spring.

– GARA GARA, PISHAN –

Immediately after, a third customer entered.

…Another S-rank adventurer.

This one accepted the guild master’s request.

I do not know his name, since I am not interested. He looks like a slender, silver-haired muscle type.

The slender macho used ‘Purification’, then soaked in the bath.

“George, why did you refuse the guild master’s request?”

“So it’s ‘Reinhardt of the Silver Flash’. Hmph. I’ve decided never to lay a hand on children.”

Oh, they started talking.

Is that really something you should be discussing with me present?

This is probably about dealing with Claude and the others, right?

“The guild master is someone you owe a great debt to. You could bend that principle at least that much.”

“We go way back, and I owe her favors, but not enough to bend my beliefs.”

“…You’re a hard man to understand. As an adventurer, you should follow the will of the guild.”

It seems Rein-something-or-other is trying to persuade George.

“Capture young adventurers who just became S-rank without even explaining the reason? If that is the will of the guild, I wouldn’t mind quitting the Adventurers Guild entirely! It’s probably the guild master’s unilateral decision. I didn’t want to believe that she would use the guild as her personal tool, but…”

“Gh, that’s…”

Judging from this city’s reputation, the guild master is fairly trusted.

When George rejects him with visible disappointment, Rein-something-or-other groans. It seems he has an idea of what is going on.

“…Even so, I will side with the guild master.”

“Do as you like. I have no intention of meddling in other people’s affairs.”

After that, both of them fell silent.

I’d really like it if they didn’t bring unnecessary drama into the bathhouse…

Just as I thought it finally got quiet, the women’s bath started getting noisy.

Did something happen to Sakura and the others?

A: No. Two female S-rank adventurers are arguing.

Over there too!? S-rank adventurers!?

Is this hot spring a gathering place for S-rank adventurers or something?

– DOGO! –

Now it sounded like something being punched from the women’s bath.

– BAKI! –

“You’ll pay for that!”

Then a naked woman came flying over, breaking the wooden fence separating the men’s and women’s baths.

She landed after adjusting her posture mid-air. She was a red-haired woman in her twenties.

“Shut up! I’ll settle our grudges right here!”

Facing her was another silver-haired woman, probably in her late teens.

“Hah! Like a chick without even a weapon can fight me!”

“You said it! Then I’ll show you what that chick can do!”

As the two naked women shouted at each other, Sakura and the others hurriedly wrapped themselves in bath towels.

The fence separating the baths was broken, after all…

And so began the women’s battle (completely naked).

As expected of S-rank adventurers, it was a sight to behold. Since they were naked, it was also a sight to behold in another sense.

The red-haired woman seems to specialize in hand-to-hand combat, with no hesitation in her movements.

The silver-haired woman is a swordswoman. Her movements have the distinct habits of a swordsman. She does not seem completely helpless, but against a pure martial artist, she is at a disadvantage.

Even though the open-air bath is spacious, it is still too small for two S-rank adventurers to fight in.

Moving carelessly could get me caught up in it, so I stayed still.

The two male S-rank adventurers who could probably stop them both had faces like they’d given up on something.

Rein-something-or-other muttered quietly, “Ah, so they ran into each other…”

It seems these two had a prior grudge, and meeting in the bathhouse immediately led to a fight. A public bath, indeed… (hot springs and public baths are different things).

Also, the silver-haired woman seems to be Rein-something-or-other’s younger sister.

“Jin-sama, what will you do?”

Maria asked, having naturally moved to my side.

In fact, Maria had already started moving the moment the fence broke.

The fight between the two was intense, and things around them were starting to break.

It would be a waste to ruin such a nice hot spring over a mere S-rank fight.

“I’ll stop them.”

“The footing is slippery, so please be careful.”

She does not seem worried at all about me dealing with S-rank opponents.

I wrapped a towel around my waist and walked toward the combat area.

“Hey, it’s dangerous!”

“Did you want a closer look at naked bodies!? Idiot!”

George tried to stop me, while Rein-something-or-other accused me of something completely unfounded.

No, that’s not it.

I jogged and cut straight into the center where the two would collide.

“Get out of the way!”

“Move!”

They attacked without regard for me.

“Don’t cause a ruckus in the bath!”

– GOTHIN! –

“Guh!”

“Gah!”

I struck each of them once on the back of the head, cleanly knocking them unconscious.

I used \<Restraint>, but as retaliation for ruining my sightseeing, I decided to add a bit of interference.

At the very least, they would not be able to fight properly until the mess involving Claude and Yuria was resolved.

“Impossible. Those two are S-rank adventurers…”

“I don’t recognize him. At least, he doesn’t look like a high-level adventurer from around here.”

Rein-something-or-other stared in shock, while George appraised me.

“Even if you were S-rank, to defeat two S-rank adventurers like they were children… Unbelievable…”

“Reinhardt, you’re forgetting something important. S-rank is nothing more than a rough guideline of strength. There are strong people outside adventurers, and even among S-rank adventurers, strength varies widely.”

Ignoring the two unconscious women, I returned to the bath.

I wanted to soak a little longer.

In the end, staff who rushed over after hearing the commotion shut down the hot spring for the day.

I wanted to soak more…

The two S-rank female adventurers who had been fighting still had not woken up, so they were taken to a nearby hospital.

With witnesses and testimony, I was not punished.

The cost of repairing the damaged hot spring would be billed to the two of them. For the silver-haired woman’s share, Rein-something-or-other would cover it.

“Kid, are you an adventurer?”

George asked me while I waited outside the bath for the women to finish changing.

Rein-something-or-other was going to the hospital with his silver-haired sister.

“I am, technically.”

George is not an unpleasant person, so I decided it was fine to answer.

“Technically? What does that mean?”

“I’m here for sightseeing, so I didn’t register my guild card. In that case, I wouldn’t be treated as an adventurer, right?”

“I see. Your rank is… no, I can guess. C-rank, right? You don’t have to answer.”

I don’t dislike sharp old men.

“Sorry about that. You came all this way to sightsee, and two idiots ruined it.”

“It wasn’t your fault, old man, so no need to apologize. Besides, I haven’t given up on hot springs yet.”

“Is that so? Then as an apology, I’ll tell you about a hot spring I recommend.”

That genuinely made me happy.

After parting with George, the women finished changing, so we wandered around town again.

We would head to George’s recommended hot spring after that.

“I came up with a little scheme.”

“Your schemes are honestly scary, Master.”

Mio said, her face stiff.

“No, the guild master is scheming right now, aren’t they? So I figured I’d return scheming with scheming.”

If someone does something to you, you return it. Using the same type of method, if possible.

“So, first, I’ll call my subordinate maids. Then…”

I explained the contents and steps of my scheme to everyone.

After that, we walked around town, went into interesting shops, browsed stalls, and Sera bought snacks.

Before returning to the inn, we headed to the hot spring George recommended and enjoyed it to our satisfaction.

A: Master, the maids operation has been completed.

While I was becoming one with the hot spring, Alta reported.

That was faster than expected. It’s only been about two hours.

A: The maids worked hard.

Ah, I’ll have to properly praise them later.

I opened the map and checked the results of the scheme.

As planned, there is currently not a single S-rank adventurer in this city who accepted the guild master’s request and can still carry it out.

To explain simply, I drove the S-rank adventurers out of the city.

That said, I did not use violent methods.

I simply used the information about S-rank adventurers that exists in this city.

Even S-rank adventurers are human (meaning humanoid species, not necessarily all human race).

Naturally, there are things more important to them than the guild master’s request. I exploited that.

For example, one S-rank adventurer had a family member who lost parts of their body in an accident, and they were desperately searching for medicine or magic to heal it.

They accepted the guild master’s request this time because there was a deal to prioritize information about that.

So what happens if they learn that the medicine to heal that injury is in a city several days away, one way?

The guild master’s request becomes irrelevant, right?

Another S-rank adventurer had been chasing the monster that destroyed their home village.

In the process, they rose to S-rank, but they openly stated that they saw no value in it, considering it merely a means to an end.

They accepted this request because the guild master promised to investigate.

Yes, I gave them information. They were a bit far away, though.

The request? They abandoned it and rushed off immediately.

For those with goals, by helping them achieve those goals, I made the guild master’s request irrelevant.

However, I could not get everyone to leave the city using the same method.

For the remaining few, I had no choice but to slip laxatives into their food.

A particularly nasty concoction made by the compounding maids. Fighting would be impossible today or tomorrow.

Crippling them before openly opposing them might be excessive if it involved killing.

However, once they tolerated a kidnapping request, I cannot call them innocent.

Groaning in the toilet is self-inflicted.

For the record, this was done with gender equality.

Rein-something-or-other alone seemed to have his own goal, but I ambushed him anyway.

It was retaliation for falsely accusing me earlier. I won’t forgive that.

To the toilet with him.

As a result, all 19 S-rank adventurers who were in this city have either left, are bedridden in a hospital, or are holed up in the toilet.

In response to the guild master trying to capture Claude and the others by gathering S-rank adventurers, I neutralized all S-rank adventurers who accepted the request.

And I did it by delegating to my subordinates… Yeah, not bad.

A: The maids have finished their work, so they are buying local specialties and gathering promising slaves at the slave trader.

Ah, going to the slave trader would have been an option too.

…There are promising ones, but none interesting enough to make me want to go myself.

After thoroughly enjoying the bath, I left and reunited with the women.

“This time I was able to enjoy it to the fullest. …Maria, can you lower the frequency of the regular check-ins a bit?”

My only complaint is the once-every-five-minutes check-ins with Maria.

“I’m sorry.”

Maria immediately prostrated herself on the ground.

She apologized with full sincerity, but it was also a declaration that she would not change it.

“Master, there’s still the mixed bathing hot spring at the inn. There, Maria-chan will be right next to you from the start, so she won’t get in your way, right?”

“The idea that mixed bathing is the most relaxing option is also kind of strange.”

Since Maria became my subordinate, I rarely have time truly alone.

Sometimes, I’d like to just wander around by myself.

“Oh, looks like Claude and the others finally arrived.”

As the sun began to set and we waited for the shared carriage back to the inn, Claude and the others arrived in town.

It took longer than I expected.

A: They used time on another matter again.

Again…? They really are busy.

Claude and the others will be staying at lodgings prepared by the guild and plan to visit the guild headquarters tomorrow morning.

“Different inns, so no need to meet up, right?”

“Coco-chan and Roro-chan would be sad, though.”

Mio said with a bit of sympathy.

Coco and Roro are the two in Claude’s party who are particularly attached to me.

“Even so, this time we’re completely outsiders. There’s no reason to get involved.”

“Normal outsiders don’t eliminate S-rank adventurers, I think.”

“Let’s set that aside.”

“Can you really set it aside…?”

As Sera said, I’ve already done it, but for now, I do not plan to get involved in the main issue.

《The carriage is here!》

“Looks like it. Let’s talk later.”

Since it wasn’t something to discuss in public, we cut the conversation short and returned to the inn by shared carriage.

Incidentally, there was no one else at the stop, and only one other passenger in the carriage.

When you think of an inn in a hot spring town, you naturally imagine a traditional ryokan.

But this town, Bolken, is different.

…It’s just normal Western-style architecture, and the food wasn’t Japanese either. Hero! Try harder!

“It’s tasty, but not something you’d expect to eat at a hot spring inn.”

This comment came from Mio, who was munching on pizza.

Yet another baked dish.

I’m not that knowledgeable, but it was a type of pizza not in Mio’s repertoire, so she called it a net positive. Are there really that many kinds of pizza?

“I don’t know your original world’s sense of things, so I don’t even know what the problem is.”

“I’m frustrated that I can’t fully understand Jin-sama.”

《But it’s tasty!》

The ones feeling the disconnect are me, Sakura, and Mio, the ones who were transported or reincarnated.

Dora? As long as the food is good, she does not care about the situation.

After taking sufficient time to digest, we headed for the final bath of the day.

Naturally, mixed bathing.

“I-It’s embarrassing, so I’ll wear a swimsuit…”

“As a former Japanese person, same.”

“I don’t mind being seen if it’s you, Master.”

“With Sera-chan’s figure, being naked is a bit much…”

《There is nothing I need to hide from Jin-sama.》

When I said swimsuits were optional, Sakura, Mio, and Sera wore swimsuits, while Maria and Dora were naked.

It seems Sera was also okay with being naked, but Sakura stopped her.

Even I would probably look, at least a little, if Sera were naked.

Maria and Dora being naked is not a problem. I’m fairly used to it…

“It’s pretty spacious for a private room bath.”

Each room has its own open-air bath, and it’s large enough for six people to use comfortably.

Naturally, the lodging cost is quite high, but it’s nothing to worry about.

“Now we can finally relax. In the women’s bath, Maria-chan was acting suspiciously, so I couldn’t relax.”

“I’m sorry for the trouble. …I know logically that nothing serious will happen with Tamo-san there, but I just can’t settle down.”

Maria apologizes to Mio and the others.

It seems I wasn’t the only one unable to relax at the earlier hot spring.

“In the worst case, today might be the last day we can enter hot springs, so at least this last one, I want to relax.”

“Last? What do you mean?”

“The Calamity Dragon.”

“I understand…”

Sera grasped it instantly.

Tomorrow, Claude and the others will meet the guild master.

In the worst case, the ‘Calamity Dragon Volcano’ revives and destroys this city and country.

Even I would have trouble ensuring safety in land where a calamity dragon has revived.

“By the way, continuing from what we were talking about before getting on the carriage, what are you going to do after this, Master? You said you wouldn’t join Claude and the others, right?”

Mio reminded me, and I realized we never continued that discussion.

“Ah, I won’t join them. For now, I’ll borrow Claude and the others’ sight and hearing through the \<Contract Bond> and listen to what the guild master says. I’ll decide what to do after that.”

I have no intention of appearing before the guild master myself.

I’ll gather information through Claude and the others, then decide what to do. If Claude and the others can’t handle it alone, I’ll support them.

“I eliminated the S-rank adventurers, so the remaining concern is the other ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’. Apparently she sealed the ‘Wind Calamity Dragon Tempest’.”

“She hasn’t come to this city until now, right…?”

“According to Alta, she only appears in Yuris’s stories. Apparently, she’s extremely misanthropic.”

This is information Alta learned by picking up the ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’s’ mutterings.

“Ugh, a misanthropic high elf. That’s basically a character guaranteed to make things complicated.”

Mio muttered unpleasantly. I agree.

“Well, it’s already guaranteed to be complicated, so it’s not worth worrying about now, right?”

I feel bad for Claude and the others, but I can’t imagine things going smoothly.

Or rather, there’s no way they will.

“That logic is questionable, but somehow convincing.”

“If anything, it’s easier to grasp the character. The guild master, on the other hand, seems like a decent person from what we’ve heard in town, which actually makes it more confusing.”

“I haven’t heard any bad rumors, and she doesn’t seem like the type to order kidnappings.”

“If not for the kidnapping, she’d probably be included among the ‘decent people’ Jin-kun likes…”

Sera and Sakura discuss the guild master based on what they’ve heard in town.

In fact, even Alta hasn’t been able to fully grasp the guild master’s true intentions.

From what the townspeople say, the guild master is a decent person.

Yet it’s also true that she’s trying to abduct Yuria using S-rank adventurers.

Her true motives never came up in conversation or even in muttered thoughts.

What is the true objective of the inscrutable guild master and the misanthropic ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’?

Everything will be revealed tomorrow when they meet Claude and the others. Stay tuned.

“…Worst case, we might have to crush her.”

“Even setting aside the calamity dragon, isn’t crushing the top of a country a bad idea?”

Mio said something extremely reasonable, so I offered a bit of rebuttal.

“What happened to the country called Eldia, which fell to the worst situation by abducting people from another world?”

“Ah, for you, Master, that kind of thing doesn’t matter anymore, huh.”

I don’t intend to casually destroy countries, but if something is truly unacceptable, I will wipe it out without hesitation.

This time, I don’t see the entire country as an enemy, so it would be a response focused on Yuris alone, but I do have experience crushing the top of a major power.

“Of course, I don’t intend to kill Yuris. There’s also the calamity dragon seal, and the risk of the Adventurers Guild becoming dysfunctional. Just because I say ‘crush’ doesn’t mean killing.”

“You’re saying scary things…”

There are plenty of ways to render Yuris unable to recover without killing her.

They’re not methods I like, but not liking them doesn’t mean I won’t choose them.

“As I said at the start, it’s something we can only think about later. More importantly, let’s enjoy the hot spring now.”

“There’s no point thinking about it now, huh. Got it. As you say, Master, let’s enjoy the hot spring.”

With everything that needed to be said said, we focused on enjoying the hot spring to the fullest.

---

**AN:** The S-rank adventurers are disposable, so there is no need to remember them.

+++

# **166: The Guild Grandmaster and the Skyborne Princess Shrine Maiden**

**AN:** The next arc is not progressing very well. Worst case, there might be a bit of a gap…

This is about the Crimson Empire arc. Really. Please believe me.

---

Claude and the others headed out early in the morning to the Guild Headquarters.

We were on standby at the inn. Fully armed, prepared to respond to anything.

Today, the human Hero Cynthia and the dwarf Hero Rico were asked to take the day off.

If, by some chance, the Calamity Dragon were to revive, having a Hero in the party would add points to the \<Hero> skill. There was no reason to let such valuable skill experience go to waste.

When Claude and the others arrived at the Guild Headquarters, they showed the request form at the reception desk.

This visit to the Guild Union District was a nominated request from the Guild Grandmaster.

“We have been expecting you. The Guild Grandmaster is waiting in her office. I will guide you.”

Led by the receptionist, Claude and the others headed for the Guild Grandmaster’s office on the third floor of the building.

At present, there were two people in the Guild Grandmaster’s office, including the Guild Grandmaster herself, Yurisuzu.

Yes, the other was another “Princess Shrine Maiden”.

Name: Yuriela

Gender: Female

Age: 7569

Race: High Elf

Titles: Elven Princess Shrine Maiden, Elven Royalty, Living Sacrifice

Skills:

Magic

\<Spirit Arts LV10> \<Spirit Magic LV10> \<Sealing Arts LV >

Technique

\<Magic Tool Creation LV10> \<Wisdom of the Forest LV >

Other

\<Ageless LV > \<Priestess Succession LV > \<Spirit of the Gale LV >

This was the status of the third “Princess Shrine Maiden”, Ms. Yuriela.

Surprisingly, there was no need to omit Yuriela’s skills.

Yurisuzu had so many skills that omission was unavoidable, but what Yuriela showed was everything she had.

Despite having lived nearly twice as long, Yuriela had learned little more than Ulysses, who had been sealed away for six thousand years.

That morning, Yurisuzu had used a long-distance communication magic tool.

Yuriela, the recipient, received the message and used the long-distance transfer skill \<Spirit of the Gale> to teleport to the Guild Grandmaster’s office.

\<Spirit of the Gale> was the first general-purpose teleportation method I had encountered since coming to this world.

If we exclude the general-purpose, there were labyrinth transfer stones or the teleportation functions of labyrinth rulers.

As expected, it seemed that “Princess Shrine Maiden” possessed attribute-specific unique skills.

Ulysses’ \<Memory of the Earth> was a production-type skill buff, while Yurisuzu’s \<Will of Hellfire> was… astonishingly, a combat-type skill. And one for close combat at that. Just what exactly are High Elves…?

“Guild Grandmaster, I have brought Lord Claude.”

“Let them in.”

When the receptionist knocked and spoke, a woman’s voice answered from inside.

“Excuse us.”

When Claude and the others entered, they saw two silver-haired High Elves.

It seemed High Elves… no, “Princess Shrine Maiden” were fixed as silver-haired. I corrected myself because Linforce of the Elgant Theocracy was not silver-haired. I forgot what color she was.

“Welcome. I’m the top of this Guild Headquarters, the Guild Grandmaster Yurisuzu. Though ‘Guild Grandmaster’ isn’t my official title. Everyone calls me that, so it can’t be helped.”

The one who said this with a laugh was Yurisuzu.

Yurisuzu was a muscular woman who completely overturned the image of a High Elf.

Though she had pointed ears and pale skin, she also had muscles that could be mistaken for a bodybuilder, and she was tall.

Her clothing was far removed from the noble image of a High Elf, looking more like an adventurer’s outfit.

Well, that might just be because she was fully armed in anticipation of trouble…

“Pleased to meet you. My name is Claude. I recently became an S-rank adventurer. The people behind me are my party members…”

“I’m Coco.”

“I’m Roro.”

“I’m Adel…”

“I’m Nott.”

“I’m Iris.”

“I’m Yuria.”

“I’m Cicely~”

Ah, both of them twitched their ears for a moment at Yuria’s self-introduction.

“Ah, I’ve heard about you. Sorry to call you all the way out here…”

“Yurisuzu, spare the talk. Dealing with inferior creatures is a waste of time.”

The one who interrupted Yurisuzu was Yuriela.

Unlike Yurisuzu, she was very obviously a High Elf.

Slender, expressionless, and fragile-looking, she wore a white silk outfit with no unnecessary decorations, like a celestial robe from myth. I didn’t know what it was called.

Yuriela spoke coldly, looking down on those beneath her.

“Yuriela, watch your words. They are guests I invited.”

“Yuria, what are you doing? Why have you not returned?”

Yurisuzu tried to admonish her, but Yuriela ignored her and questioned Yuria.

“What are you talking about?”

Yuria, having no memory of such a thing, asked back.

“You do not remember me? Could it be that you have lost your memory?”

“I see no need to answer. Guild Grandmaster, why did you summon us? Because we are a rare S-rank adventurer party and you were curious? What is the meaning of this situation?”

Ignoring Yuriela’s question, Yuria instead questioned Yurisuzu.

“Are you ignoring me?”

Having been ignored by Yuria, Yuriela let anger seep through her otherwise expressionless face.

“Yuriela, calm down. …Ah, right. I might have written something like that in the request. Sorry. The truth is, the one I really needed to see was you, Yuria. This is Yuriela, my ally and the true client of this request.”

Yurisuzu casually revealed that the request details had been false.

“Did the head of the Adventurers Guild lie in a request?”

Claude asked, his eyes filled with disappointment.

What Yurisuzu had done degraded the very value of the Adventurers Guild.

“Yeah, I really am sorry. But when choosing between my position as the head of the Adventurers Guild and my position as a guardian of this world, the guardian comes first.”

Yurisuzu said this with a pained expression.

That single line made it clear. Before being the Guild Grandmaster, Yurisuzu was a “Princess Shrine Maiden”.

She could not overlook the disappearance of a High Elf, especially when it came to maintaining the seal on the Calamity Dragon.

To hell with that.

“Yurisuzu, you are talking too much. Even if she has lost her memory, what must be done does not change.”

“True enough. Well, from what I can see, I might manage on my own. I was at a loss when everyone I prepared disappeared, though.”

“Adventurers are inferior creatures. I knew from the start they would be unreliable.”

“Hah… It’s an unfortunate fact that the quality of S-ranks has declined in recent years…”

When Yurisuzu said she had ‘seen’, she was referring to the skill \<Spiritual Rank Appraisal>.

Simply put, it lets you see the rank of another being’s existence. It is not exactly their level, but for ordinary humans it almost always matches.

One exception is stat enhancement through \<Life and Death Authority>. This dramatically boosts abilities regardless of rank.

In other words, Yurisuzu judged Claude and the others by their apparent rank and failed to understand their true strength. Absolutely hilarious.

For reference, \<Spiritual Rank Appraisal> can be blocked by the mental defense of \<Multiple Existence>. This time, I deliberately let her see.

“What do you intend to do with me?”

“Naturally, I will take you back to my castle.”

Yuriela answered Yuria instantly.

“After that, there will be examinations for some time. I hope that contact with inferior races on the surface has not negatively affected your functions as a ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’… I am especially worried about contact with inferior half-humans.”

Half-humans?

…Wait, could she mean half-elves?

Judging by Yuriela’s gaze shifting to Iris, the half-elf, that seemed likely.

Certainly, the term ‘half-elf’ is a human-centric term, meaning half elf.

From an elf’s perspective, would they call them half-human?

…No, that seems unlikely.

“…That’s how it is. I can’t explain everything, but for the sake of this world, we need you to hand Yuria over. If you refuse, the Adventurers Guild… the entire world will become your enemy.”

Reluctantly, Yurisuzu threatened them, using the world as an excuse.

Alright, that crossed the line.

“So it comes to this… I’m sorry, but we refuse.”

“Yuria is our companion and our family. There’s no way we’d hand her over to people who lied to summon us and then threatened us!”

Claude’s refusal was echoed by the dwarf Nott, and the others nodded firmly.

“I do not know what relationship I had with you before I lost my memory. However, even now, you are not worthy of my trust. Therefore, I have no intention of going with you.”

“…If only you had given up here, we could have avoided the trouble.”

Hearing Yuria’s refusal, Yurisuzu sighed.

“This is why inferior creatures are… Very well. Yurisuzu, I leave the rest to you.”

“Can’t be helped… I don’t hold any grudge against you, but we can’t back down either.”

“Transfer!”

When Yuriela shouted, the entire office was enveloped in light.

It seemed \<Spirit of the Gale> had activated.

There are several types of teleportation using \<Spirit of the Gale>, and this was one of them: area transfer.

It sends those within a preset area to another location. Yuriela had set it up before Claude and the others arrived.

Apparently, it was a fallback plan after S-rank adventurers disappeared and a normal abduction became impossible.

Naturally, Claude and the others had been informed.

Unfortunately, we couldn’t know the destination from this side.

We could have avoided it if we wanted, but I was curious about the destination, so I asked them not to avoid it.

The place Claude and the others were transferred to was… to put it extremely simply, Lapu○ta.

“Where is this…?”

“This is my castle. I dislike letting humans, demi-humans, and half-humans in, but it is necessary to save time.”

A vast territory of a skyborne land.

At its center stood a massive castle, with forests of thick trees.

Truly fantasy!

Alta, where exactly is this sky castle?

A: It lies east of the Guild Union District, above the sea.

Then there was zero chance of me ever finding it.

It was completely outside my range of movement.

“This is above the clouds. If you’re not used to it, you can’t even fight properly here. On top of that, this area is close to the seal. Isn’t it hard just to stand?”

Yurisuzu said with a confident expression.

Indeed, the place Yuriela had chosen was practically a guaranteed win for Yurisuzu and Yuriela.

Between the high altitude impairing physical function and the miasma of the ‘Wind Calamity Dragon’, Tempest, non-High Elves would be rendered completely immobile.

In fact, this sky castle sat directly above the ‘Wind Calamity Dragon: Tempest’. The land floated because ‘Wind Calamity Dragon: Tempest’s’ body naturally levitated.

‘Wind Calamity Dragon: Tempest’s’ soul was in subspace, but its body existed in this world, emitting something like miasma that contaminated the minds of most beings.

“No, that’s not the case.”

“”Huh?””

However, Claude replied calmly.

Altitude was handled by \<Environmental Adaptation>, and the Calamity Dragon’s miasma was blocked by \<Multiple Existence>’s mental defense, so Claude and the others had no problem.

Since they rode Lesser Wind Dragons, they had \<Environmental Adaptation>.

“W-Why can you stand normally? Even elves suffer here…”

“Impossible…”

Let me take a look.

As this was Yuriela’s castle, many elves lived here.

There were no High Elves or half-elves among them.

And ordinary elves couldn’t block the Calamity Dragon’s miasma… High Elves couldn’t fully block it either. That’s why even Yurisuzu and Yuriela looked slightly distressed.

“This is truly disappointing. Calling us here with a false request, commissioning an abduction to S-rank adventurers, using the Guild’s name to threaten us, and then forcing a one-sided battle in a location advantageous to you. To think someone like you is at the top of the Adventurers Guild… this world is doomed.”

“When you line it all up, it’s really awful.”

“Roro is too stunned to speak.”

Claude listed Yurisuzu’s actions, and everyone, led by Coco and Roro, looked exasperated.

Now that it was spelled out, it really was terrible.

“W-Wait! How do you know about the S-rank adventurers!?”

The matter of the S-rank adventurers was information Claude and the others should not have known.

“We have no obligation to answer. All I can say is that your scheme was completely exposed.”

Not quite completely, but your actions were.

“Let’s end the talking. At this point, since you have clearly become our enemies, we have no choice but to fight in self-defense.”

Saying that, Claude and the others drew their weapons.

Until now, it had been ‘ready to draw’. Now, it was ‘drawn’.

“…Things didn’t go as expected. Maybe there’s something you can’t tell just by looking. Yuriela, fight as well. It might be tough for me alone.”

“I refuse. Such barbaric acts are not my duty.”

Yuriela flatly rejected the suggestion of cooperation.

So they weren’t particularly close, then?

“C-Come on… At least summon your spirit!”

“If that’s all, I can comply. Come forth. Illuminea!”

It seemed she had summoned her contracted spirit with \<Spirit Arts>.

What appeared was a Great Spirit of Light, shaped like an ivory-colored goddess statue.

It had a human-like face, but the eyes and mouth were merely sculpted and seemed nonfunctional.

“Alright, time to discipline some naughty children.”

Yurisuzu raised a legendary greatsword and entered a combat stance.

At this point, legendary equipment no longer surprised me.

“Here I come!”

“Incoming!”

As Yurisuzu charged, and at Yuria’s call, Claude and the others formed their formation.

As usual, Claude took the front, with Yuria stepping back to command.

Meanwhile, Yuriela used short-range teleportation to retreat to a safe distance.

“Take this!”

“I won’t let you through!”

Claude blocked Yurisuzu’s sweeping strike with his shield.

A loud metallic clang rang out, but Claude held his ground, completely stopping the blow.

The fact that his legs sank slightly into the ground spoke to the power behind it.

“What!?”

“Haah!!”

As Yurisuzu hesitated for an instant in surprise, Claude shoved forward with his shield, trying to break her stance.

“Don’t underestimate me!”

However, Yurisuzu, a seasoned warrior, did not lose her balance so easily.

She tried to backstep…

“Guah!?”

But before she could, Coco swept her legs from behind, sending her crashing onto her back.

Coco followed up by kicking Yurisuzu’s arm, making her drop the greatsword. Then she drove her two daggers into the ground at Yurisuzu’s neck, crossing them.

The blades were sharp enough that any careless movement would sever her head.

“T-This is impossible… To lose without even being able to use \<Will of Hellfire>…”

Yurisuzu muttered in a daze.

No, Claude and the others are among the veteran elites of my subordinates.

If they fought without stat restrictions, there was no way she’d stand a chance.

“GYAAAAAA!?”

A shrill, metallic scream rang out. The one who screamed was the Great Spirit of Light.

Its attack was blocked by Roro, Iris counterattacked with \<Dark Magic>, and Illuminea couldn’t fully evade, ending up riddled with holes. Nott’s hammer delivered the finishing blow, and it vanished.

For the record, it screamed at the moment it was riddled with holes.

“To think even Illuminea would be defeated… how surprising.”

Despite her contracted spirit being destroyed, Yuriela didn’t change her expression.

“Yurisuzu, I did not think you would be this useless. This makes securing Yuria difficult, and I will have to wait again for another High Elf to be born.”

As expected, Yuriela’s goal was the succession of the “Princess Shrine Maiden”.

“It was entertaining to watch you lead inferior creatures, so this is disappointing. If you are to be killed, do so on the surface. I will watch this world perish from here.”

“Yuriela, what are you saying…?”

“Farewell.”

With that, Yuriela activated \<Spirit of the Gale> once more.

When the light faded, they were back in the Guild Grandmaster’s office.

Yuriela was gone, and Yurisuzu remained collapsed.

The dagger at her neck had been retrieved by Coco just before the transfer.

“It seems we’ve been sent back.”

“She was someone you couldn’t reason with, to say the least.”

As Coco said, Yuriela didn’t seem like someone open to discussion.

“I didn’t think she’d abandon me so easily… Seems I was the only one who thought we were friends…”

Still lying there, Yurisuzu muttered.

“So, we’ve won the fight. Is it alright if we kill you as is?”

Claude approached Yurisuzu with a blank expression, sword in hand.

Of course, he didn’t actually intend to kill her. It was an act to gauge her reaction.

“Stop. If you kill me, this world will be destroyed.”

Perhaps shaken by Yuriela’s betrayal, Yurisuzu said weakly.

“But if we leave things like this, the world becomes our enemy, right?”

“…No. I have no intention of doing that anymore. From Yuriela’s words, it seems she has no intention of involving herself with the surface again. I have no desire to make enemies stronger than myself for the sake of someone who may never return.”

That should mean Claude and the others avoided being declared wanted?

“In that case, could you explain the situation? We don’t want this to end without understanding what’s going on.”

“Alright. …May I stand?”

“If you show any intent to attack, we will kill you for sure next time.”

“I understand.”

Under Claude and the others’ watchful eyes, Yurisuzu stood up and sat in her desk chair.

“Now then, where should I begin… Perhaps explaining the Calamity Dragons would be best.”

Yurisuzu began to speak, as if entering a flashback.

“When you say ‘Calamity Dragon’, you mean those enormous dragons sealed in subspace that cause disasters just by existing, right? As long as a High Elf ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’ lives, they remain sealed in subspace, but the one who maintains the seal is affected by miasma, so when the next ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’ is born, the role is passed on. You’re talking about those Calamity Dragons, correct?”

“How do you know so much!?”

Yurisuzu exclaimed in surprise at Claude’s explanation.

“…No, did you hear it from Yuria? Then was the memory loss a lie?”

Before losing her memory, Yuria might indeed have known.

“No, I truly have lost my memory. I heard it from someone else.”

“Someone else… a High Elf… ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’? Water… or Earth? Neither seems possible…”

Ah, that subtly confirmed the existence of a Water Calamity Dragon.

“No, a human.”

“I don’t understand!?”

At Yuria’s single sentence, Yurisuzu shouted in surprise again.

I taught her earlier.

“We learned about the Calamity Dragons from our master. Our master also told us that you were gathering S-rank adventurers to capture us.”

“Some unbelievable human exists out there. Let’s get back on track. …If you already know about the Calamity Dragons, it might be faster to hear what you want to know.”

If she tried to explain from scratch, it would probably take a very long time.

“Right. We have a rough idea ourselves, so first we’d like to confirm whether our assumptions are correct.”

“Did your master tell you that too?”

“Yes, most of it.”

I did teach them, but the deductions were their own.

Though, they were mostly the same as mine…

“First, you targeted Yuria because she was the next ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’ after the High Elf Yuriela. However, Yuria disappeared from before Yuriela.”

“Yes, exactly. About a year ago, Yuriela suddenly appeared and told me that Yuria had gone missing. I knew about Yuria, so I spread a search net through the Adventurers Guild.”

“And as a result, you found Yuria as an S-rank adventurer. …This is something we couldn’t predict, but do you know how Yuria went missing?”

Yurisuzu shook her head.

“No, I don’t know that either. Yuriela never explained that part. …Thinking back now, perhaps she used me without explaining the details.”

Given Yuriela’s words earlier, she hadn’t treated Yurisuzu as an equal friend.

“It seems we won’t know unless we ask Yuriela. …Continuing our assumptions, after finding Yuria, you invited our party to this country and aimed to secure her.”

“Yes. I could communicate with Yuriela using a communication magic tool. I don’t know if it works now…”

A: The line has been cut and cannot be used.

Oh dear. Completely discarded.

“I didn’t hear the details, but losing a ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’ candidate is a major issue. It pained me to abuse my position as Guild Grandmaster, but I thought it was better than ignoring a world crisis, so I decided to capture you.”

“Isn’t that too short-sighted? Just so you know, we still haven’t forgiven you for this.”

“…I know. I messed up. It’s only right that I take responsibility. I realize now how short-sighted it was.”

Yurisuzu slumped her shoulders.

Though they seemed to be speaking amicably, Claude and the others hadn’t lowered their guard or forgiven her.

“I tried to gather S-rank adventurers to threaten you, but somehow they all disappeared and the plan collapsed. How did you do that?”

“We have no intention of answering your questions. We are the ones asking questions now.”

“Right… Sorry.”

That’s definitely the kind of thing you can’t talk about.

“So we had no choice but for me and Yuriela to capture Yuria ourselves. I can judge others’ strength by their aura. Looking at you, I thought I’d be fine on my own… Truly, everything was unexpected.”

“Next question. What was that place?”

“The floating land? That’s a place called the ‘Sky Castle.’ It’s a city built atop the husk of a Calamity Dragon. There, the elven clans that seal the Fire, Wind, and Earth Calamity Dragons reside. I’m from the Sky Castle too.”

According to Yurisuzu, each Calamity Dragon is sealed by a different clan.

The goal is to ensure the bloodline continues. A strategy to keep the Calamity Dragons sealed forever.

Currently, the Sky Castle houses three clans, excluding Water.

“Sorry, but I don’t know the origin of the ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’. Yuriela probably doesn’t either. The information was likely deliberately erased. Probably to tell us not to think about unnecessary things.”

“By whom…?”

“Who knows? Our ancestors… or the Goddess, perhaps.”

Not this again…

“The Calamity Dragon’s miasma can’t be completely blocked even by us. Eventually, I too will be unable to endure it and will desire the next ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’. Yuriela already wants to step down in favor of the next generation. That’s why she has no emotional leeway.”

Yurisuzu continued.

“That said, using that miasma to immobilize transferred enemies means I can’t really talk big. It was supposed to be a trump card, but I never thought it wouldn’t work.”

As mentioned earlier, ordinary beings would be immobilized by the miasma and altitude.

Only because Claude and the others were protected by my abilities were they fine.

“I’m not going to tell you the reason.”

“I know.”

Yurisuzu seemed to be getting it.

“One more question. Why did Yuriela abandon you so easily? Do you have any idea?”

“Unfortunately, I do. Yuriela considers the Wind Calamity Dragon, Tempest, sealed in the Sky Castle, to be the most dangerous. That’s because even if the other Calamity Dragons revive, they can’t affect the Sky Castle. As long as Tempest remains sealed, Yuriela is safe.”

Come to think of it, the ‘Earth Calamity Dragon’s’ fissure attacks wouldn’t reach the Sky Castle, and even if the ‘Fire Calamity Dragon’ erupted, it likely wouldn’t affect it directly.

In other words, it was a safe zone from the other Calamity Dragons.

“If ‘Calamity Dragon: Tempest’ revives and the Sky Castle is destroyed, there’s a chance the other ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’ will die too, and the world will meet its end. Considering that, she probably judged it faster and safer to drive us out of the Sky Castle rather than fight there and risk it. She might have even thought it acceptable if I died and the surface became a land of death.”

Yuriela did spill a lot at the end.

“Anything else you want to ask?”

“I have nothing more. Does anyone else?”

Claude asked the others, but they all shook their heads.

“Seems not.”

“Is that so? …Then, what will you do with me? I abused my position as Guild Grandmaster to trap you. I failed, but that’s an unchangeable fact. I’ll take responsibility. I’ll follow your decision. I can’t atone by dying, though.”

Surprisingly straightforward, Yurisuzu said she would follow their decision.

《Claude, can I ask you something?》

Things I absolutely wanted to include when writing fantasy, Top 3

1st: World Tree

2nd: Sky Castle -> Done

3rd: Labyrinth -> Done

Half-human was a term an old friend (human) used. I always thought I’d get a chance to use it someday.
